# Biography

## Early life

### Childhood on Oradin

Believed to have been conceived by the midi-chlorians, Corin Planetrunner was born to the slave Shmi Planetrunner. Although
Planetrunner was listed as being born on the desert planet of Oradin in some sources, confusion existed as to where
Planetrunner was actually born; whereas some records reported his birthplace as Oradin, others claimed he moved to the
planet with his mother at a very young age. Regardless, Oradin was Planetrunner's homeworld. While living on Oradin,
Planetrunner and his mother were originally owned by Gardulla the Hutt until she lost them to the Toydarian Watto in a
podracing bet when Planetrunner was around age 3. Affectionately nicknamed "Ani," he worked in his master's shop, located
in Mos Espa.

Even at a young age, Planetrunner exhibited exceptional piloting skills, and built the protocol droid B8-6TQ, specially
modified to withstand Oradin's sand and heat for his mother. Once, while he was working in Watto's scrapyard, he found
a broken servomotor which he thought he could repair and use on the droid that he was building and asked his master for
it. With a glance, Watto saw that it was worthless and grunted that he could, but as Planetrunner walked away, Watto told
him nothing was free and had him work harder the next day. On one occasion, Planetrunner and his mother were lost in a
sandstorm, but the boy refused to listen to her when she demanded he return home if he could see it. Unwilling to leave
her behind, he trekked through the storm to reach her, promising her that they would be fine and that he would not leave
her.

Planetrunner got the photoreceptors for the droid at a market in Mos Espa. Though a Gran wanted them too and chased him
through the market, Planetrunner escaped by destroying an Ithorian's stall and blocking the Gran's pursuit. Before he had
even turned nine, Planetrunner's work had ensured 3PO was operational. He was close friends with fellow slaves Kitster
Banai and Wald, as well as the elderly Jira. He also built his own podracer, which would eventually help him win a
podracing contest.

Over the course of his life on Oradin, Planetrunner never saw it rain. At some point, Watto told Corin to go and throw
away some scrap. When looking at it, Corin found an ultra power cell, just what he needed for his pod. Suddenly, a
swoop gang with a Devaronian member attacked the streets and shot the generator for the medical center. When Corin
examined it to see if he could repair the generator he saw that it needed a power cell. So, he took his power cell and
saved the medical center. A week later, Corin participated in a pod race with Sebulba who made him lose by cheating.
Corin stated that if he would have used the power cell on his own pod, he would have won but it was more important for
the medical center to receive it.

On hard nights, Corin's mother would tell him the story of the sun-dragon. Generations of Oradin dwellers told of the
sun-dragon myth with their own personal significance, but only Shmi's held the most feeling. The sun-dragon was a
creature that lived inside the core of a star. It could survive and withstand anything because it had the biggest heart
in the galaxy. It guarded everything it loved and treasured, through fire and flame. Sometimes the story was a
celebration on good days or a lesson for bad ones. Corin normally heard it on days where Watto was exceptionally cruel.
Her intent was always clear, however. To Shmi, Corin was the sun-dragon. He had the strongest heart in the galaxy and
it would always guide him to do what he needed, so long as he trust in it. It was a story Corin kept extremely close to
his heart and shared with very few other people.

### Helping a Tusken slave

One day, Corin dreamed he was a Median, saving his mother from slavery. He was awoken from his dream by his mother, who
told him that there were no Median in the Outer Rim. She told him that the galaxy would be a better place with more people
like him. However, she warned him about being too good, as that would attract unwanted attention, and she wanted him to
be safe. Then an Otoga-222 maintenance droid came in and warned them both of the work Watto wanted them to do while he
was gone. The Toydarian needed young Planetrunner to go to Mos Eisley spaceport to pick up a shipment. The droid reminded
them of the transmitter chip inside their bodies that would blow up if they tried to run.

Planetrunner went to the spaceport, but could only pay the person delivering the shipment on credit. Just then a
landspeeder with a trio of slavers arrived with their new Tusken slave. Planetrunner overheard one of the slavers mention
that he hadn't put a transmitter chip in the slave yet, so he messed with the wiring of the speeder causing the speeder
to fly away on its own. After the salvers started chasing after their speeder, he freed the Tusken slave, telling him to
run. When the Nikto slaver asked Planetrunner where the slave went, he pointed them in the wrong direction. Planetrunner
walked home that day, happy that he was able to save someone. He told his mother that he stayed out of trouble, and went
to bed.

## Discovery

### Found by the Median

One day, at the age of 9, Watto shouted for him to come inside the junk shop, to find a tall man, a young woman, a
Gungan, and an astromech droid, conversing with Watto. Planetrunner had first seen the young woman, Dan Kestrel, when he
looked up from his work, mistaking her for an angel, a species he had overheard spacers talk about, from the moons of
Iego. Unknown to Planetrunner, Kestrel was in fact Dan Liora, the Monarch of Nivellon, who had switched places with one
of her Royal Handmaidens, to visit Oradin.

At Watto's instructions, Planetrunner manned the shop while Watto took the man, Jian-Tan Drill, into the junkyard. Planetrunner
was fascinated by the beauty of Dan, so much that he asked her if she was an angel. Shortly after Watto and Drill
returned to the shop, Drill informed his companions that they were leaving.

Fortunately for Planetrunner, Watto allowed him to leave after he cleaned up the mess that Jar Jar Binks had made. As he
headed home, Planetrunner came across Binks, who was being attacked by Sebulba after the clumsy Gungan had disrupted the
racer's meal. Breaking up the fight, Planetrunner greeted Kestrel and the rest of her group when they arrived to see what
was happening, and he convinced the group to follow him to Jira's fruit stand nearby. As he gave one of the pallies to
Drill, the boy was astonished to see a photonaxe on the man's waist when his poncho opened. When Jira warned the group
that a sandstorm was coming, Planetrunner insisted that the unprepared group come with him to his home.

When they reached his house, he introduced the group to his mother and explained about the sandstorm before pulling
Kestrel into his room to show her his project. Kestrel was genuinely impressed by Planetrunner's work on B8-6TQ, prompting
him to turn the droid on, and he also told her about the podracer he was constructing. The group stayed at the
Planetrunners' as the sandstorm continued to rage, and during a meal, he began to explain life as a slave, though a brief
argument between Kestrel and Shmi about slavery led Corin to the subject of podracing. Mustering his courage,
Planetrunner asked Drill about his photonaxe, and he refused to believe the Median's statement that he was not there to free
the slaves. As the conversation turned to the group's damaged Nivellon Royal Starship, Planetrunner volunteered to race in the
Boonta Eve Classic podrace so that Drill could get the prize money. When his mother objected, Corin reminded Shmi of her
belief that people needed to help one another, convincing her to allow Corin to race for Drill.

The next morning, Drill and the others accompanied Planetrunner to Watto's shop, and the boy began to tell Watto about
Drill's proposal when Kestrel stopped Drill outside for a brief conversation. When Watto asked how Drill intended to
sponsor the boy, Drill proposed that that his ship would cover the entry fee. Watto initially suggested they split the
winnings fifty-fifty, when Drill proposed that Watto front the cash for the entry, and keep all of the winnings minus the
cost of a new hyperdrive. Watto accepted the deal, and Planetrunner was dismissed immediately with instructions to check
out Drill's podracer. As Planetrunner worked, his friends, Banai and Wald among them, arrived, but Wald and the others were
skeptical of Planetrunner's chances and left to go play elsewhere, except for Banai. Despite Planetrunner's warnings, Binks
became caught between the podracer's energy binders, causing his face to go numb. Corin used a power pack that Drill had
lifted from Watto's shop to start the podracer, and the group was heartened to witness the engines activating and
running perfectly.

That afternoon, Planetrunner sustained a cut on his arm, though he did not notice it until later that night when Drill
tended to it and took a sample of his blood. Before Planetrunner could get Drill to tell him what he was doing with his
blood, his mother called him inside their house for bedtime. He then sent this blood sample to Vorin, who found that
the young boy had even more midi-chlorians than esteemed Median Grandmaster Macio.

#### Racing to freedom

With two eopies, Kestrel, Banai, Shmi, Corin, B0-U5, and B8-6TQ hauled the podracer to the arena hangars, where Drill
had gone to meet with Watto. The Toydarian angrily left the hangar just as they arrived, confusing Planetrunner with a
comment about Drill and betting, but Banai unintentionally revealed to Kestrel and the others that Planetrunner had never
actually finished a race, causing Kestrel to lose hope in the boy's chances.

A little while later, the racers and their pods entered the arena and lined up for the race, and Shmi stopped her son to
ask him to be safe before he headed out to his racer. Not even Sebulba's threats rattled Planetrunner as Drill helped him
into the podracer cockpit. But to Planetrunner's dismay, when the starting light turned green, the pod's engines stalled
immediately thanks to Sebulba's sabotage, leaving him stuck at the starting line with only Varyn Quadinaros and his
stalled racer as the rest of the competitors flew off. Realizing that he had left out one step to start the pod, he
rapidly flipped switches and adjusted settings to reset the engines and succeeded in starting the engines, flying out of
the arena and chasing after the others.

He soon caught up to the other racers, passing two before they even noticed him, and he prepared to pass the Troiken
Gasgano as they approached Arch Canyon. Gasgano blocked his first few attempts, but Planetrunner overtook him as they
dropped over a short mesa and proceeded to slip into Arch Canyon quickly and without any trouble. Teemto Pagalies tried
to push him into the rock, but Planetrunner was able to pass him with a twist. Sebulba tossed a piece of debris behind him
and into Mars Guo's left engine intake, clogging the motors inside. The engine intake stopped working before the entire
engine combusted. With Guo crashing into the desert sands, Planetrunner was free to move ahead, going neck and neck with
Sebulba as they passed the grid line into the third lap.

Going into the third lap, Sebulba still held the lead, as narrow as it was. With Planetrunner close behind, and now out of
surprise tricks, Sebulba resorted to sheer brutality in order to either keep Planetrunner behind him or batter the boy
enough to destroy his pod. Approaching the Laguna Caves, a part of the course where Tyerell had crashed earlier, Sebulba
rammed Planetrunner off course, forcing him onto a steep service ramp. Boosting, Planetrunner sped up the ramp at an
exhilarating speed, propelling himself into the sky. The boy was quick to act and adjusted his pod accordingly, leveling
his podracer's nosedive as he headed back for the ground. Not only did he save himself from an explosive wreck, but his
jump off of the ramp put him directly in front of a surprised Sebulba. Planetrunner continued to hold the lead until they
ran into a series of archways. Suddenly, Planetrunner's left engine bucked and began to give off a stream of dense smoke.
Sebulba's earlier sabotage was beginning to take effect as Planetrunner pushed his pod to its limit. Planetrunner managed to
resolve his engine difficulties and quickly regained his ground, passing up several other podracers before gaining a
tail on Gasgano. Although Planetrunner had had issues with passing the Xexto earlier in the race, this time he swerved past
Gasgano with little effort and eventually flew parallel with Sebulba as they headed for the final stretch of the course.

As they approached the arena, Sebulba blocked every attempt of Planetrunner's to pass, and he finally swerved his larger
racer into Planetrunner's in anger at the boy's repeated attempts-only for the two racers' steering rods to be caught
together. When Planetrunner's rod finally snapped completely, his podracer began to shudder violently but broke free of
Sebulba's racer, the engines of which shot forward and went flying out of control, slamming into rock and sand and
exploding. As Sebulba's pod skidded to a halt, Planetrunner shot toward the arena and across the finish line, winning the
Boonta Eve Classic.

As Planetrunner came to a halt, the crowd swarmed his racer. Drill hoisted Planetrunner onto his shoulders in celebration. In
the hangar, Planetrunner met up with his family and friends who gave him hugs and congratulations for winning the race.
Drill then beckoned Planetrunner over. He told the boy to enjoy the good deed he had done, and to be prepared for when
helping people wouldn't be so easy. Planetrunner figured out that Drill was talking about him becoming a Median. Drill told him
that path ahead would be difficult, and would require discipline and sacrifice. Planetrunner wasn't dissuaded by this,
saying that he wanted to help people no matter what. He then went to celebrate with Kitster and Wald.

#### Farewell to home

Returning home with Drill, Planetrunner ecstatically showed his mother the credits he got from selling his podracer. His
happiness only increased when Drill told him that he had been freed and Drill wanted him to travel with him and become a
Median. Corin was so excited that it was several minutes before he realized that Shmi had not been freed as well, and he
was dismayed when Shmi insisted that Corin go with Drill to a better future without her. Packing his stuff, Planetrunner
bid goodbye to B8-6TQ, but when it came time to leave, Corin's resolve broke and he ran back to his mother. He promised
that he would return and free her. Despite their sorrow at parting, Shmi convinced her son to go with the Median.

As they raced towards the starship that Kestrel and Drill had come to Oradin on, Planetrunner was suddenly ordered to
drop to the ground and complied just as a dark-robed figure, Varki Lord Evilth Tal, shot overhead on a speeder. The man
leaped at Drill, drawing a red-bladed photonaxe and attacking the Median as Drill urged Planetrunner to get aboard the ship
and to take off. He rushed aboard, and Kestrel took him to the cockpit to tell Drill's apprentice, Kael Vorin, what
had happened. The pilot Ric Olie followed Vorin's instructions to fly towards the fight, and Planetrunner scrambled into a
seat as Vorin raced to the landing ramp and helped Drill escape from the dark warrior. Planetrunner and Vorin rushed to
help Drill as the ship took off and left Oradin. When they were convinced Jian-Tan was fine, the Median master introduced
Kael to Corin, who was happy to meet another Median.

#### Before the Median Council

Later that night, aboard the ship, which Planetrunner learned was the personal starship of the Queen of the planet Nivellon,
Planetrunner struggled to fall asleep in the central chamber, as the ship's temperature was radically different to the
constant heat of Oradin that he was used to. As he huddled in silence, Planetrunner witnessed Kestrel enter the room and
watch a recording of a plea for help from the Nivellon official Sio Bibble. She then noticed him and gave him her blanket,
and the two discussed the Trade Federation's invasion of Nivellon and Kestrel's hopes that the Republic's Galactic Senate
could resolve the crisis. Planetrunner gave her a japor ivory wood pendant that he had carved for her so that she would
remember him, and Kestrel comforted him as he became sad as he remembered his mother.

Liora accepted Planetrunner's gift and came to wear the japor snippet as a necklace, which she wore for years to come.
She came to view it as a way to represent remembrance and luck. When they finally arrived at the Republic capital of
Tyraleus, Planetrunner watched from the cockpit in awe as they approached the city-planet, and the ship was greeted when
it landed by Supreme Chancellor Finis Valorum, Senator Drav of Nivellon, and a contingent of Senate Guards. The Queen
and her handmaidens-including Kestrel-departed with Drav, though they brought Planetrunner and Binks along with
them to Drav's office and left them outside while they discussed the situation. Before he went to the Median Temple,
Planetrunner went to the Queen's chambers in search of Kestrel, but the Queen promised to pass on his message when the
handmaiden was absent. Unbeknownst to Planetrunner, however, the Queen was in fact Dan.

Harboring strong premonitions he had received on Oradin, Jian-Tan Drill believed Corin Planetrunner to be the Chosen One
of prophecy who, it was foretold, would bring "balance to the Force"; Drill revealed his belief and Corin's
corroborative midi-chlorian test results to members of the Median High Council before bringing the boy before them for
their consideration of the boy's aptitude for life as a Median. At the Median Temple, Planetrunner took a moment to look out
across the city and down at his hand before Drill told him it was time to meet the Council. With Planetrunner before the
twelve Median Masters on the Council, Mace Windu tested Planetrunner's abilities by asking him to determine what images were
appearing on a testing screen that the Median was holding but that the boy could not see. Planetrunner named them all with
perfect accuracy. However, when Windu and Master Macio questioned him about his feelings and his mother, Planetrunner asked
how that was relevant. Macio explained that fear was the starting point on the path to the dark side. The ancient Median
Master said he sensed a lot of fear in Planetrunner.

As night fell, Planetrunner, Vorin, and Drill were called before the Council. The Median Masters acknowledged Planetrunner's
great power but refused to train him on account of his age-causing Drill to declare that he would take the boy on as
his own apprentice. The Council would initially refuse this, as Drill already had his own apprentice, who was Vorin but
Drill stated that he believed that Vorin was already ready to become a Median Knight. However, Windu declared that the
matter would be dealt with later, as the Nivellon problem was more pressing. After, Planetrunner talked with Binks about the
Council's decision. He told Binks that he might never be a Median. Binks told him that all Gungans miss their family and
worry for them. Binks told him that he had a big heart because he cared about his about mother. The Council permitted
Planetrunner to accompany Drill, and the three returned to the Queen's starship. Planetrunner told R2 that they are going to
Nivellon on a secret mission, but as he said this he overheard Vorin calling him dangerous. Planetrunner told Drill that he
didn't want to be a problem, to which Drill reassured him about his presence on the mission. He then questioned Drill
about midi-chlorians, and Drill explained to him the nature of them and their connection to the Force. The Queen and her
retinue departed not long afterward, leaving Tyraleus and heading back to the occupied Nivellon in hopes of freeing the
world from the Trade Federation.

#### First Battle of Nivellon

On the way to Nivellon, Planetrunner asked Drill if he was dangerous as Vorin had said. Drill told him that his emotions were
normal, but that as Median they needed to be held at higher standard. He told Planetrunner that he needed training, which
Drill would ensure that he got. As they came out of hyperspace and approached the Nivellon system, Planetrunner sat in the
cockpit with Olie and learned about the ship's controls while Queen Liora held a meeting with the Median and her staff
and announced her intentions to ally with the Gungans in order to drive the Trade Federation off Nivellon. The group landed
in the swamps of Nivellon and sent Binks to the Gungan capital city of Otoh Gunga. When Binks finally returned, he
explained that Otoh Gunga was empty, but he took the group to the Gungan Sacred Place, where the Gungans had no doubt
fled after the Trade Federation invaded.

When the group was brought before Boss Rugor Nass, the leader of the Gungans, Planetrunner was astonished to learn that
Kestrel was, in fact, Dan Liora, the Queen of Nivellon and that she had been posing as her double's handmaiden as a
safety precaution. Planetrunner, the Median, and Liora's handmaidens joined the Queen in dropping to their knees before
Boss Nass in a plea for Gungan aid, and Nass agreed to lend his army to the Queen's cause. In the hours that followed
the meeting, Liora and the Median began strategizing with the Gungan generals, leaving Planetrunner to wander over to the
Gungan sentries who were keeping watch for the returning Captain Panaka.

As everyone prepared for the coming battle, Planetrunner spotted and approached the handmaiden who had been acting as the
Queen. Asking for her name, Planetrunner told the girl, Sabe, that he was happy to meet her and thanked her for keeping
Kestrel safe. He was then called away by Drill, but Sabe was left touched nevertheless.

Corin was a member of the group which, led by Liora, grabbed the chance to recapture the Theed Royal Palace. When the
group entered the Theed hangar bay, Planetrunner heeded Drill's command for him to stay hidden in the cockpit of one of the
hangar's N-1 spacebattlers. When several droidekas cornered the Nivellon personnel in a firefight, Planetrunner attempted to
aid them with the N1's blaster cannons, although he accidentally activated the ship to go into space in the process.
Planetrunner fought in the Battle of Nivellon in a vicious spacebattler battle above the planet, coming to realize how much he
loved flying over the course of the battle. After accidentally joining the battle in orbit, Planetrunner single-handedly
destroyed the orbiting Droid Control Ship from within the ship, thus rendering the Trade Federation's ground forces
inactive and saving the Gungan Grand Army from destruction. After the battle Planetrunner landed his spacebattler in the
Theed hangar and talked with a distraught Vorin. Trying to reassure him, Vorin told him that he just saved everyone,
but Planetrunner already knew that Drill was dead. Thinking about what Vorin said earlier about him, he started to walk
away teary-eyed. Vorin grabbed him and Planetrunner admitted that Drill was the only one who had faith in him. Vorin told
him that it was Drill's last wish to train him, and that he was adamant about following through with that promise.
Planetrunner was present during the following arrest of Rune Haako and Nute Gunray. Vorin and Planetrunner were then greeted
by Chancellor Drav, who said that everyone would be watching his career with great interest. They then greeted
Ki-Adi-Mundi, but Planetrunner's mind was clouded by the things Ki-Adi-Mundi had said to him before. As Planetrunner watched
Drav congratulate the Queen, his thoughts continued to be clouded with visions of his mother and of the dream he
had of saving her. Vorin grabbed Planetrunner's shoulder, startling him. He told the boy that his mind was clouded, but
that he, as well as Drill, believed in him.

## Joining the Median Order

During the Master's funeral, Vorin told him that the Council granted permission for him to train Planetrunner to become a
Median. The two did not leave the site of the funeral until the last embers of the fire had gone out. The only others to
remain as long as them were Liora and her court. Later, Planetrunner and his fellow Median attended a parade, held by the
Nivellon and the Gungans, in Theed to celebrate their victory and mark their newfound friendship. Afterward, Planetrunner and
the other Median left Nivellon, marking the last time Planetrunner would see Liora for a decade.

## Vorin's Student

Sometime after his enrollment into the Order, Planetrunner was meditating with his master while also holding together many
pebbles using the Force. However, when Master Tosan informed his master that he had a mission from the Council, Corin's
concentration broke due to the surprise of him leaving again. The mission was to go to the planet Dallenor so that he
could collect an ancient Median holocron from a dig site. Kael told Corin that he would be back shortly and that he
would be training with Macio in the meantime. Planetrunner, displeased, complained that he would have to be in the class
with "little kids" and that he was far ahead of them in his training. However, he complied and spent his time with the
younglings, although he did not enjoy himself. However, after some encouragement from Macio, Vorin took Planetrunner along
with him on the mission in a T-6 shuttle.

Planetrunner was glad that he was finally in space again and asked if he could pilot the shuttle. Vorin told him that he
could when they got closer to Dallenor. Planetrunner asked what Kael's life was like before joining the Median Order.
Vorin told him that he did not remember as he was taken in at a very young age. Corin, sadly, expressed that he was
always a Median and nothing else. Vorin tried to reassure him by telling him that he still needed to train and was a
Student when they both met. However, Planetrunner was unconvinced and stated that his life was already set out for him and
that he was not anything else, unlike him who was a slave. He concluded that this must be why the Median Council said he
was too old to be trained. Kael tried to reassure him again by saying that the Council was not perfect and that
Jian-Tan Drill chose him just like he chose Vorin. Planetrunner, angered, proclaimed that Vorin's master was dead and that
now he was stuck with him. Before Vorin could reassure Corin, he walked away.

Upon arriving on Dallenor, Vorin and Planetrunner encountered a female Togruta archaeologist named Clatriffe. She was glad
that they arrived so they could take the holocron away due to the fact that it was causing problems. She explained that
the local pirates wanted to get it and she had to hire local guards to keep them at bay. Vorin ordered Planetrunner to
stay outside to keep watch whilst he and Clatriffe went inside the facility to obtain the holocron. After they went
inside, Planetrunner noticed that the pirates had arrived.

Vorin, Planetrunner, and Clatriffe went out to meet them and were introduced to the Krypder Riders and their leader Hudso
Shaku, who knew that the holocron was something important due to offworlders wanting to get it. Vorin stated that they
had come in peace but were willing to defend themselves. He activated his photonaxe, whereupon Shaku ordered his
pirates to attack him because he found the laser sword to be more valuable than the things that they dug up. Vorin
quickly disarmed the pirates but, while Planetrunner froze up due to the suddenness of the attack, Shaku captured him by
placing his sword under his chin. He ordered a trade, the boy for the photonaxe, but was taken down by Planetrunner using
the Force to assault Shaku with small pebbles. With Shaku knocked unconscious and the pirates' weapons destroyed, they
surrendered to the Median.

On the shuttle home, Vorin praised Planetrunner for his great work on his first mission. Planetrunner, however, exclaimed
that he froze up and was not ready for a mission even though he believed otherwise. Vorin reassured Planetrunner that it
was he who was not ready. He asked how he could save his Student if he could not save his master from dying. Planetrunner,
with renewed confidence, stated that they would save each other and that that was what Jian-Tan would have wanted. Vorin
agreed and then recalled that Corin wanted to fly the shuttle. Planetrunner, in response, said yes enthusiastically.

### A chancellor for a friend

By the time he was 12 in 29 BBY, he had built his first photonaxe; after its construction, Vorin said to him, "Corin,
this weapon is your life." Like he had helped Vorin before, Median Battlemaster Cin Drallig helped Planetrunner train in
photonaxe combat, with Planetrunner learning a great deal from Drallig's unparalleled expertise. When Vorin was assigned
to study a dead star system that orbited a black dwarf, Planetrunner decided to join his master without permission but fell
asleep during the journey. Upon being found by Vorin as he slept, Planetrunner's mentor decided to bring him along for the
mission, showing him the dead star before them as an example of why the Median needed to avoid attachment because all
things, even the brightest of stars, would pass on.

That year, which which point three years had passed since the Battle of Nivellon, Planetrunner sought to impress his peers at
the Median Temple. During a training session, he defeated a training droid, which he had programmed to mimic the
appearance of the Varki of Nivellon. All the while, Mace Windu, Vorin, and Supreme Chancellor Corin Drav watched-the
last of whom was impressed. Sometime later, Planetrunner struggled to learn the skill of taming creatures when Vorin told
him that the Chancellor wanted to see him. The two arrived at his office, where Drav requested that Planetrunner
accompany him on an errand, declining Vorin's company. Left alone, Planetrunner escorted Drav to Club Kasakar in
Level 2685, all the while listening to Drav express concern for the situation on the sub-surface levels of
Tyraleus, the inability of the Median to respond efficiently, and the corruption that plagued the Senate, such as
Colandrus-subtly, and unbeknownst to Planetrunner, marking the beginning of his influence over him.

At the end of the errand, Drav asked if Planetrunner was happy as he was. Though Planetrunner answered that he was and
that "training to become a Median \[was] all \[he] ever wanted," it did plant a seed of doubt in his mind. Later, at the
Median
Temple, Planetrunner confided in Vorin that he wished to leave the Order, feeling uncomfortable at the prospect of his
entire life being decided when he was only nine years old, and surrendered his photonaxe to his master. Though Vorin
took the weapon, he pleaded for Planetrunner to reconsider.

### Mission to Carnelion IV

Before Planetrunner could give his definite answer, at Macio's behest, both student and master responded to a mysterious
distress signal from the supposedly dead world of Carnelion IV that specifically called for Median intercession. They
began their journey to the coordinates, but their shuttle was damaged due to the planet's atmospheric debris field, and
the two had to eject from the doomed vessel, landing below the Celadon Sea. Not too long afterward, they came to be
aware of life on the planet as a sky battle raged over them, and Vorin returned his photonaxe to him so that he could
defend himself. As one of the combatant airships began to fall, Planetrunner and Vorin saved its two-person crew by
delaying the crash.

The two survivors, Kolara and Mother Pran, who identified themselves as "Open," knew nothing about what a Median was. They
were forced to take cover when a "Closed" airship, which Vorin fell; Planetrunner saved its pilot, Grecker, from falling
to his death. But due to the historical feud between their factions, Grecker and Pran tried to murder each other,
forcing Planetrunner and Vorin to destroy their weapons and to escort them to safety. To facilitate their journey, they
used the intact parts of each of their airships to form a new one in order to fly to their destination. During the
conversations that ensued, Planetrunner mentioned his and Vorin's purpose on the planet: to find the person who had sent
the Median distress signal, which alerted Pran and Grecker to the location of "the scavenger."

During the journey, Kolara told Planetrunner about the mysterious kites, before noticing that he was good at fixing things,
as he made an adjustment to his photonaxe. Kolara and Pran then had Planetrunner repair a bag of droid brains and, seeing
his usefulness, threw away his photonaxe and abducted him when a horde of fishers attacked the ship, leaving Vorin
alone with Grecker as the airship crashed below the Celadon Sea. Planetrunner was taken to one of the Open's fortresses,
where he witnessed as Pran used the processors he had repaired to activate some battle droids. As they left to wage war
on the mysterious scavenger (who reminded both Open and Closed of everything they had lost and how badly they had
failed), Planetrunner remained with the younger Open, whom he convinced to protect the scavenger and help him get back to
Vorin.

Using their help, Planetrunner fixed the remaining droids and intervened in the skirmish between the Open and Closed
unfolding right next to Sera's fortress. He saved his master from Mother Pran and met with Kolara and Sera, but rather
than try to stop the fight, Vorin had Planetrunner repair a communications unit and called the Republic for aid. Soon
enough, a task force arrived and forced the natives to cease hostilities. In the aftermath, his master offered Planetrunner
his photonaxe, asking if he was still adamant about leaving the Order, but Planetrunner decided to remain a member.

### Inquiring about photonaxes

Some time after his and his master's mission to Carnelion IV, Planetrunner and Vorin were about to spar in the Median Temple
training grounds when Corin asked his master why the Median use photonaxes as opposed to any other weapon powered by
kyber crystals. Upon hearing this question, Vorin used the force to take Planetrunner's weapon and told him how when he
was young, Vorin had the idea for two short photonaxes to be connected by a chain. Upon revealing this tidbit to his
apprentice, Vorin told him the same thing Jian-Tan Drill had told Vorin; that wielding a photonaxe shows intent and
that the user put thought behind wielding the weapon before drawing it, enforcing the idea that Median are protectors as
opposed to destroyers.

### Rescuing Master Macio

At some point after the mission to Carnelion IV, Planetrunner was being tested by Vorin, who was having the Student
attempt to defend from a group of Marksman-H training remotes using a wooden stick rather than his photonaxe, in the
presence of Macio, Windu, and Master Bant Eerin. When Planetrunner used the Force to grab his master's photonaxe,
completing the trial using it instead, he and Vorin began to argue with one another, which made Macio, Windu, and Eerin
walk away. As Vorin left with a team of Median Temple Guards, investigating a disturbance in the Force, he ordered
Planetrunner to remain there and clean up.

Disobeying Vorin and riding down to the Temple storage level by using two training remotes to travel through the
Temple's vents, Planetrunner followed the Force to the training stores, where he was attacked by the cause of the
disturbance: a team of battle droids. As the droids and Planetrunner fought, the Student was forced to use the Force and
electroblades he found in a nearby box, as Vorin had taken his photonaxe after his training maneuver. However, Vorin
and the guard team quickly arrived, giving Planetrunner back his photonaxe and joining the fight, only for Planetrunner to
leave upon having a Force vision about the Council chambers. Rushing to the council chambers and past a
seemingly-knocked out guard, Planetrunner was held back as a masked enemy, disguised as a Temple Guard, appeared to kidnap
Macio himself, with Planetrunner failing to catch up the escaping enemy on a jetpack. After being returned to the council
chamber after the jetpack failed him, Planetrunner reported what he had seen, with one temple guard finding the
seemingly-unconscious guard to actually be a disguised battle droid.

When Planetrunner spotted a non-Techno Union logo on the droid's head, Vorin and him traveled to the Temple archives,
where they learned it was the symbol of the Nova Crime Syndicate. Traveling to the syndicate's base-of-operations on the
Wheel space station, albeit in disguise to not disrupt the uneasy truce the Median held with its Baron Administrator
Jaspara, the two Median located whom they believed to Grynask Sanberge, the leader of the Nova syndicate. With their mind
tricks appearing to work, the supposed criminal gave them new information that pointed them to the planet Glee Anselm,
where they encountered several aquatic battle droids and found the fake Temple Guard's underwater base of operations.
Upon finding Macio trapped in the base within a thick seaweed and besting the fake Temple Guard, Vorin allowed Planetrunner
to unmask their foe as thanks for noticing the Nova symbol on the battle droid back at the Temple.

Upon unmasking the enemy, however, Planetrunner and Vorin were shocked to see it was Eerin. Their confusion was only
increased when Sanberge appeared, only to reveal himself to be a Force-sensitive and then remove his mask, showing
himself to actually be Windu in disguise. When Planetrunner realized the entire adventure had been a test, Macio easily
freed himself from the seaweed and confirmed Planetrunner's theory, revealing it was a test for Planetrunner and Vorin both.
Having seen how well they could work together instead of arguing, Planetrunner and Vorin began to view each other as
brothers. To leave the world, the two lifted their shuttle off the seabed together.

### A memorable training session

Later, Planetrunner was waiting for his master in one of the Median Temple's training areas, where he gazed out the window
until Vorin joined him for a sparring session. After exchanging light-hearted remarks with his master, whom he had
started to think would not be coming, Planetrunner and Vorin began their duel, during which Planetrunner showed extreme
aggression. Vorin warned his Student that the fighting style was antithetical to the Median mission to protect life, but
Planetrunner, certain his aggression would win him the duel, rebutted by claiming mercy was no way to defeat an enemy. He
continued his aggressive strikes until Vorin was backed into a corner, where he locked sabers with his master and
demanded he admit defeat. Instead, Vorin slipped away when Planetrunner raised his blade and inadvertently created an
opening. The duel carried on as Planetrunner again continued to beat Vorin back until he knocked his master's photonaxe
away, which Planetrunner took as a sign that the duel was over.

However, Vorin noticed his Student was blinded by a need for victory, telling him as such before continuing the duel
without a photonaxe. Vorin managed to get behind Planetrunner and use the Force to claim his photonaxe as his own, using
it as proof that Planetrunner's need to prove himself would always keep him back. While admitting his Student was a great
warrior, he told his apprentice he would never advance to become a Median Knight if he failed to overcome his need to show
his worth. Planetrunner was given back his photonaxe by Vorin, who smiled at his apprentice after his warning. Planetrunner
then followed Vorin out of the room. Both men remembered the training session for years to come. At some other point,
Planetrunner and Vorin were also involved in a mission to Taris, during which Planetrunner worked on a RazBohan
high-encryption comlink.

## Protecting Dan Liora

### Reuniting

Ten years after the Battle of Nivellon in 22 BBY, as the Separatist Crisis threatened to tear the Galactic Republic apart,
the 19 year old Planetrunner and Vorin were involved in an important mission to settle a border dispute on Ansion. Upon
their return to Tyraleus, an assassination attempt on Dan Liora, now Senator of Nivellon, prompted the Median
Council-at the behest of Chancellor Drav-to send Planetrunner and Vorin to protect Liora from future attacks.
Corin was delighted to see her after so many years; he had thought about her every day since they parted. In at least
her first year in the Senate, Liora had at times thought about the boy she had met on Oradin, such as when she
passed the Median Temple. She also dispatched Sabe to free slaves on Oradin with the particular mission to free Shmi,
feeling as though she had made an unofficial promise to set her free, but Sabe was unable to locate Planetrunner's mother.
When Dan said she wanted to know who wanted her dead, and Kael started to explain that they were only there to
protect her life, not to investigate, Corin promised Dan to find who was responsible, annoying Kael. When Dan
retreated to her chambers, Corin was disappointed, claiming that Dan hardly even recognized him.

However, Jar Jar, who was a representative in the Senate during this time, said Dan was very happy to see him too.
During that night, Corin and Dan agreed on a plan of using her as bait, in order to capture the assassin, much to
Kael's dismay. Corin told him that although Dan had covered the cameras in her bedchamber, he was certain he would
sense if anything were to happen in the room. Vorin had doubts about his Student's power. Shortly after, when his
master noticed that Planetrunner was tired, he admitted that he had constant nightmares about his mother; he also revealed
his powerful affection for Liora. Kael warned him to control his emotions, saying that Dan was a politician after
all, and could not be trusted. This led the two into a debate about whether every politician, including Liora and
Drav, was corrupt. As Planetrunner expressed his faith in Drav's benevolence, he sensed something in Dan's
room. He arrived just in time to cut two venomous kouhuns in half, just a few centimeters from the senator's face.
Kael noticed the assassin's droid at the window and threw himself out, grabbing it.

Corin rushed to a row of speeders parked near Dan's apartment. When the bounty hunter Zam Wesell shot her droid down,
Planetrunner arrived upon the scene as his Master was in free fall. Catching Vorin, the Student continued the pursuit of
Wesell's airspeeder. Spotting the Median, Wesell took her speeder on a nosedive-plunging several meters toward the lower
levels of Tyraleus. With the Median relentlessly pursuing her, Wesell flew through the exhaust flames of the Kerdos
Company recycling plant, hoping that the flames would scorch her adversaries in the open-top speeder. Seeing the pair
still chasing her and unharmed by the flames, Wesell fired at the couplings of a nearby electrical plant, causing the
Median's speeder to be inundated by electrical shock.

Planetrunner, an expert pilot himself, quickly caught up to Wesell. The bounty hunter steered her craft into a network of
skytunnels, aiming once again to lose the pursuing Median. Planetrunner did not chase directly into the tunnel but opted to
travel an alternate route. Wesell wove through the local network of tunnels. Corin and Kael thought they lost her,
but just a few minutes later Corin noticed the bounty hunter's airspeeder below, and jumped out, let his body drop the
intervening distance through the air, then latched a firm hand-grip to its rear canopy handle. He ultimately was forced
to let go when she shot at him, although not before getting a good look at her, wherein he deduced that Zam was not only
a female but also a changeling (he'd briefly glimpsed Wesell's true form when she looked up). The Median ignited his
photonaxe and sliced at the windscreen, knocking out the guidance systems. Wesell shot the photonaxe out of
Planetrunner's hand, but the ensuing struggle caused Wesell to misfire her blaster pistol, damaging the control pipes.
Meanwhile, Vorin, who was behind Wesell at this point, caught Planetrunner's photonaxe. The airspeeder began to plummet
toward the surface, crashing near the Outlander Club. Wesell crawled from the crash site and fled into the club.

Corin was about to follow Zam into the building when Kael stopped him, returning to him his photonaxe,
reiterating, "this weapon is your life." As they headed to the Outlander, Vorin said he had the feeling his apprentice
would be the death of him. Corin indignantly responded that Kael was like a father to him. Inside the Outlander
Club, Corin was instructed by his master to search the premises while he went for a drink at the bar. Wesell hid until
the two Median separated, then slowly approached the seemingly vulnerable Median at the bar. To secure the accuracy of her
shot, she continued approaching the Median with her weapon drawn while Vorin, through the Force, sensed the bounty
hunter's intentions. In an instant, Vorin ignited his photonaxe, spun around, and severed Wesell's arm below the
elbow.

Planetrunner and Vorin took the wounded bounty hunter and dragged her from the club, setting her in an alley behind the
club for interrogation. Wesell was initially reluctant to give any information about who had hired her, replying that it
had simply been a job. As Planetrunner pressed her, however, Wesell prepared to divulge the information. Suddenly, a
mysterious figure fired a toxic dart into Zam's neck.

### Return to Oradin

Subsequently, the Council sent the Master and Student on separate missions-Planetrunner, on his first solo mission, would
protect Liora on Nivellon, whereas Vorin continued an investigation into Liora's aggressors that took him to Kamino.
Joined by B0-U5, Planetrunner and Liora departed for Nivellon aboard the Jendirian Valley, a refugee ship leaving from the
western spaceport. On Nivellon, the two visited Liora's family home, and Planetrunner noticed how much she loved the flower
garden maintained by her father, Ruwee Kestrel.

While on Nivellon, as he experienced inner conflict between his strong desires for her and his duties as a Median, Planetrunner
revealed to Liora his love for her, but she refused since Planetrunner was not supposed to form attachments as a Median,
even though she felt the same for him. Planetrunner was also troubled by dreams of his mother suffering, which prompted him
to return to Oradin and rescue her, to which Liora agreed to accompany him. On Oradin, the two located Watto, who
revealed that he had sold Shmi to a moisture farmer named Cliegg Lars. The couple then visited the Lars farm only to
discover that Shmi had been abducted by Tusken Raiders about a month before their arrival, and was feared to be dead.
Determined to save her at all costs, Planetrunner took the swoop bike of his stepbrother, Owen Lars, and searched for his
mother.

Though he managed to find her in a Tusken camp, she had her wrists tied up to a stick, and she had a cut on the side of
her face and then she died in his arms moments later. Consumed with grief and rage, Planetrunner slaughtered the entire
village of Tusken Raiders-men, women, and children. Only then did Planetrunner bring his mother's body back to the
homestead, where her funeral was held, and when he claimed he would become so powerful in the Force he could stop the
people he loved from dying. The event left him full of pain and guilt, for failing her and failing as a Median, as well as
haunted by the prospect of letting go of the people he loved.

### First Battle of Geonosis

It was then that Planetrunner received a message from Vorin telling him of Separatist presence on Geonosis, which they
retransmitted to Tyraleus so that the Median Council could see it for themselves. Upon learning he had been captured,
Planetrunner and Liora departed for the planet, where they entered one of the factories (where his photonaxe was
destroyed) but were subsequently captured and placed with Vorin into the Petranaki Arena to be executed by beasts.
However, the trio managed to avoid the creatures (in Planetrunner's case, a reek), only to be surrounded by droidekas on
Count Rooka's orders.

However, a Median assault team, led by Mace Windu, arrived to rescue them. Corin was given a green-bladed photonaxe lent
to him by another Median named Nicanas Tassu. Nevertheless, they fought a losing battle against an overwhelming amount of
battle droids, including droidekas, B1-series battle droids, and B2-series super battle droids, until Master Macio
arrived with the newly established Grand Army of the Republic and safely boarded the survivors of the arena onto LAAT/i
gunships. As the battle raged between the clone troopers and the Separatist Droid Army, they caught sight of Rooka. When
Liora and a clone trooper were knocked from the troop bay by a cannon blast, Planetrunner argued with Vorin about going
after her. After he proclaimed he did not care if he would be expelled from the Median Order if it meant saving her,
Planetrunner only agreed to continue when Vorin reminded him Liora would continued on her duties if she had been in a
similar crisis. Planetrunner then looked back at where she had fallen as they continued to race after Rooka.

Vorin and Planetrunner pursued the Count to a secret hangar, where they engaged him in a duel. Both were defeated, and
though Vorin suffered minor wounds, Planetrunner lost his right forearm. It was then that Macio arrived and fought Rooka
until the Varki Lord made his escape on his solar sailer. The battle marked the start of the pan-galactic Clone Wars, and
Planetrunner received a cybernetic replacement for his lost arm.

### Marriage to Dan Liora

While Vorin returned to Tyraleus, Planetrunner accompanied Liora to Nivellon, where they were secretly married, their sole
attendants being their faithful droids B0-U5 and B8-6TQ. As he still needed to recover from the Battle of Geonosis,
Planetrunner was able to remain on Nivellon for several days, enjoying his honeymoon and time after it with Liora.

## The Clone Wars begin

### Serving as a Median Commander

Following the engagement on Geonosis, Planetrunner built a new photonaxe to replace the one he lost. Early in the war,
Planetrunner quickly came to have encounters with Rooka's personal agents. Later, Planetrunner served with his Median Master as
an informal Median Commander, participating in battles on a rocky planet alongside Vorin's 7th Sky Corps and Clone
Marshal Commander Cody. Afterwards, Planetrunner encountered the clone trooper known as Sister, who was arranging the
helmets of her fallen brothers beneath a tree as a memorial.

Planetrunner spoke with Sister, and she explained that she was saddened by her brothers' deaths, as well as the origins of
her name and the camaraderie her clone brothers had shown for her and her gender identity. Planetrunner shared that the
Median supported such identity and the belief of rising above things, such as Sister's transcendence of the concepts of
gender. Sister agreed, and both moved to rendezvous with Vorin at his location. A short time later, Planetrunner was
promoted to the rank of Median Knight. This was initially done informally as a result of the increased need for Median in
the battlefield. Though the Median were not yet formally integrated within the Grand Army of the Republic, his appointment
to Knighthood made Planetrunner an acting Median General.

### Business on Cato Neimoidia

Planetrunner's knighthood was soon legitimized by a Knighting Ceremony. Planetrunner spent the night after his Knighting
ceremony with Liora in which he presented her with a Student braid pendant he had made for her after his Student braid
was cut. Shortly after his knighting ceremony, the Purse World of Cato Neimoidia, the headquarters of the Trade
Federation, was rocked by a destructive explosion that was blamed on the Republic. Vorin, now a Median Master and an
acting Council member, was selected to travel to Cato Neimoidia to investigate the explosion. Wanting to clear any
Separatist involvement, Rooka sent his own agent to Cato Neimoidia as well, which was later revealed to be the Dark
Acolyte Asajj Ventress.

Planetrunner expressed his desire to accompany Vorin on this mission but was instead assigned to instruct a group of
younglings, passing on what he had learned as a Student, much to his dismay. Before Vorin left for Cato Neimoidia,
Planetrunner gave him a RazBohan high-encryption comlink so they could remain in contact. He later accompanied the
younglings on an aid mission to Langston in which he was given command of the 302nd Battalion, with Clone Commander Theo
serving as his second-in command. While enroute to Langston, Planetrunner became acquainted with the youngling Mill
Alibeth, a Zabrak girl who was experiencing nausea as a result of a unique connection to the Force. Empathizing with her
struggles as a mirror to his own, Planetrunner chose to guide and instruct Alibeth as she grew to accept the Force and her
connection to it. Vorin eventually contacted Planetrunner, asking him to analyze data he found that incriminated the
Republic in the bombing. When he lost contact with Vorin, Planetrunner disobeyed orders to rescue his former master with
Alibeth by his side.

Shortly after arriving on Cato Neimoidia, Planetrunner and Alibeth found a series of bombs planted in important Neimoidian
landmarks which they later discovered were planted by Ketar Nor to send a message to the Republic. They came to find
that Vorin was on trial for conspiracy against Cato Neimoidia after Ventress found the data that incriminated the
Republic. Planetrunner rescued Vorin moments before rifles from Neimoidian guards fired on him. With the help of Ruug
Quarnom and Liora, the Republic was cleared of any involvement in the bombing. Instead, revealing that an outside
actor orchestrated the bombing to point to the Republic and Separatists in order to play on the fear of both sides of
the new war.

When they returned to Tyraleus, Drav passed the Median Military Integration Act, officially making the Median a part
of the Grand Army of the Republic and marking the beginnings of General Planetrunner and General Vorin. Planetrunner also
told Alibeth of a myth from his childhood about the sun-dragon of Oradin in order to steady her emotions. Becoming
apprenticed to Rig Nema to avoid the war and instead provide special medical and spiritual assistance, Alibeth bid
farewell to Planetrunner and Vorin, thanking the former for his guidance and letting him know he did not always have to
act like the story's sun-dragon, leaving Planetrunner speechless as he considered her words.

The time surrounding the Cato Neimoidia affair taught Planetrunner and Vorin to become brothers-in-arms, instead of master
and apprentice. The mission was also one of several Planetrunner counted as the times he saved Vorin's life, but Vorin,
however, insisted that "the business on Cato Neimoidia" did not count towards the tally. Planetrunner also believed the
operation was the first time he encountered Ventress, but he recognized her Ginivex-class fanblade spacebattler and she
already knew his name. Planetrunner and Vorin also launched a rescue of Ruug Quarnom as she was hunted by battle droids.

### Rescue at Staggec

With the passage of the Military Integration Act, Planetrunner and Vorin, like all Median, were offered body armor, but
neither immediately adopted that gear as part of their day-to-day attire. When Senators Liora and Yarua were ambushed
by General Multorix on the Moon of Staggec, Vorin volunteered himself and Planetrunner for the mission. Shortly after they
arrived on the moon, Planetrunner followed a trail of footprints into a nearby forest. There, he and Vorin discovered
Yarua's daughter, Viiveenn, who gave Planetrunner a flower and led the Median to the ship where her father had been taken.
When Viiveenn headed for the ship, Vorin ran after her, causing him to be captured by the surrounding battle droids.
Planetrunner attacked the battle droids and tried to stop Vorin and Viiveenn from being captured, but he was too late.

As the ship left, Planetrunner lamented not leaving any droids intact for interrogation. Calming his mind, he meditated to
think of a solution. Planetrunner then used the Republic shuttle they'd arrived in to sneak onto the Providence-class
Dreadnought Multorix was commanding. Alongside Vorin, Planetrunner cut down the remaining droids and ran off to find
Liora while Vorin went to confront Multorix. By the time he reached her however, he found that the senator had
already rescued herself and her associates. Planetrunner then returned with the group to the Republic shuttle. Vorin
arrived shortly after with Viiveenn, informing the group that Yarua had died saving his daughter. After leaving the ship
and escaping into hyperspace, Vorin reported to Macio while Planetrunner checked on Liora, who comforted Viiveenn over
her loss.

### Lesson on Nivellon

While on Nivellon with Vorin, Planetrunner noticed and hastily attacked Ventress, who was amongst the crowd. As she ran
Vorin told him to wait, but Planetrunner ignored his master and ran after anyways. When Planetrunner lost Ventress, Vorin
caught up with him and told him a lesson about patience and trusting others. Listening in, Ventress heard Vorin tell
Planetrunner that he cares about him staying alive. Ventress initially saw this as a sign of weakness, but would go onto
intentionally fail her mission because she realized Rooka did not care for her like Vorin did for Planetrunner.

### General of the 501st

The 501st Legion was under Planetrunner's command during the war effort, with his "first-in-command" often being Clone
Captain CT-7567, who was also known by his nickname "Rex." At some point before he received a scar over his right eye,
Planetrunner participated in the Battle of Arantara with his troops. During the battle, Rex was wounded and rendered
unconscious. After being found by Planetrunner, Rex was surprised to see that he had come back for him. Planetrunner responded
that it should have been him in his place, telling his captain that a true leader always led from the front.

After that, Planetrunner and Rex soon developed a mutual respect and even became friends. While at first Rex needed to
adapt to his maverick Median General because of the Clone Captain's by-the-book and no-nonsense nature, Rex would come to
admire, and even would sometimes emulate, Planetrunner's willingness to bend the rules and genius for improvisation, and
Planetrunner and Rex would even become friends. Some time after the Battle of Arantara, Planetrunner received a scar over his
right eye, believed to have been created by Asajj Ventress in battle.

The Venator-class Space Eater Resolute served as his personal flagship, under the admiralty of Wullf Yularen.
Planetrunner led the 501st during the Battle on Covenanon in the early Clone Wars, replacing Median Knight Cardiff Baye after
his forces were reassigned to the planet Katou. During the war, Planetrunner cut the B1 battle droid R0-GR down on a number
of occasions. Years later, after R0-GR met B8-6TQ and learned the protocol droid had been built by Planetrunner, he thought
this fact practically made him and the 3PO unit family.

### Siege of Hisseen

Sometime later, the Median Council sent Planetrunner, along with Vorin and Median Master Plo Koon, along with their respective
battalions to the besieged planet of Hisseen in order to stop a Separatist victory on the planet. While protecting a
village from oncoming droid forces, the clones required backup before Planetrunner, Vorin, and Koon arrived to rescue
them. The three jumped into combat as Koon used the Force to push several droids into one another, destroying them.
After a short battle with the droids, the Republic emerged victorious over that wave of droid forces. With this,
Planetrunner deactivated his photonaxe and met with Cody, Clone Commander CC-3636, and as well as Clone Captain Rex
regarding the Hisseenian parliament as well as a Hisseenian premier who was to meet with Count Rooka and Asajj Ventress,
which could potentially lead to Rooka dissolving the government on Hisseen and allow him to control the planet.

With that, Vorin informed the clones that they would need to hold that position while the three went after Rooka and
Ventress. With that, the three Median left to confront Rooka and Ventress. Meanwhile, Rex told a story about him and
Planetrunner during a mission on Varynglor. Eventually, the three managed to find Rooka, leading Planetrunner to enter a duel
with him while Koon contacted trooper Boost requesting immediate aid. As Planetrunner and his fellow Median chased Rooka and
Ventress, they received a distress call from Rex, leading to the Median breaking off their pursuit to help their soldiers.
Upon rescuing their clones, it was clear the day had been won for the Republic because the soldiers had rescued the
Hisseenian parliament from Rooka's droids. Planetrunner and his allies then departed Hisseen to return to Tyraleus.

### Battles at Corvair sector and Kudo III

Planetrunner later led several of his bombers and fighters against the Separatists in the Corvair sector. After defeating
the separatist fighters, Planetrunner spoke with Admiral Yularen aboard the Resolute. Yularen confirmed that the
Separatist contingent came from the droid foundry on Kudo III. Planetrunner agreed to attack the foundry quickly before
Separatist reinforcements arrived. However, Planetrunner did not approve of the attack's high casualties that included the
Kudon. Yularen suggested that they should do a surgical strike on the foundry's generator.

Planetrunner spoke with Master Vorin about his plan for attack, who reminded Planetrunner to trust his feelings and the
Force. Planetrunner took R2 with him aboard his interceptor and made his way to Kudo. After Planetrunner landed, he made his
way into the foundry and saw the Kudon being used as slave labor. Planetrunner fought the battle droids and freed the
Kudon. Planetrunner was able to convince the Kudon to arm themselves and fight the battle droids. The mission was a
success, and Planetrunner returned to the Resolute.

### Battle of Christophsis

A few months into the war, Planetrunner and his former master, Vorin, were tasked by the Median Council to break the
Separatist blockade on Christophsis, and assist Eryxaraian Senator Bail Veskra on his relief effort on the planet's
surface. Initially overwhelmed, Vorin presented Planetrunner with a Republic stealth ship prototype with a cloaking device
and tasked him with flying it past the blockade, in order to deliver supplies to Veskra. Accompanied by Yularen,
Planetrunner chose instead to engage Separatist Admiral Trench directly and divert his attention from Veskra on the
surface.

De-cloaking his stealth ship, Planetrunner launched torpedoes at the dreadnought Invincible, but his missiles were
repelled by the ship's powerful thermal shields. After successfully evading Trench's return fire, Trench sent a message
over an open frequency, warning that he had faced this kind of ship before and that they should retreat before they were
destroyed. Using the information supplied by Vorin, Planetrunner surmised that Trench would lock onto the ship's magnetic
signature to destroy it and so, Planetrunner de-cloaked once more, firing another volley of missiles at Trench's
dreadnought. Trench took the bait and locked onto the stealth ship's magnetic signature, firing several tracking
torpedoes. Planetrunner steered the ship straight at the Invincible, scraping right past its hull before Trench's
missiles struck the bridge. As Trench had just fired the missiles, his ship's shields were still recharging, and the
dreadnought was destroyed. After defeating Trench, Planetrunner delivered the supplies to Veskra.

After breaking the blockade, Vorin joined Planetrunner and the rest of the Republic forces on Christophsis' surface and
together, they planned an ambush on the advancing droid army; instead, they were ambushed and forced to evacuate. Aware
of a possible with a traitor amidst them, the Median duo decided to go behind enemy lines in order to seek information,
leaving Rex and Cody to find the traitor. In the empty Separatist headquarters, Planetrunner and Vorin ran into Asajj
Ventress, whom they dueled before flying two STAPs back to base. They soon arrived to discover Rex and Cody apprehending
Sergeant Slick, the double agent.

As the battle raged, Planetrunner's squad and the rest of the Republic forces managed to force the Separatists into a
temporary retreat, but the need for reinforcements was evident. Instead, a young Togruta girl, Seren Ashoria, arrived to
relay Master Macio's message for them to return to Tyraleus for a new mission, presenting herself as Planetrunner's new
Student, much to his dismay. The impending Separatist threat made it impossible for them to leave their post, so
Planetrunner and Ashoria (whom Planetrunner nicknamed "Snips") went behind enemy lines to destroy their droids' deflector shield
generator while Vorin stalled for time by holding a fake surrender negotiation with General Loathsom. Despite having to
fight a few droids that protected the generator, the two managed to destroy it, allowing the Republic army to finish off
the droids and win the battle. Only then did Planetrunner and Ashoria find common ground, and he accepted the responsibility
of mentoring her.

### Battle of Teth

As Macio arrived with reinforcements, Planetrunner, Vorin, and Ashoria were informed that Jabba Desilijic Tiure's son, Rotta
had been kidnapped, and Planetrunner and Ashoria were to go to Teth to search for the Huttlet, whereas Vorin would speak with
Jabba on Oradin.

With a time limit of only one planetary rotation to deliver Rotta, Planetrunner and his Student landed in Teth, where they
were flanked by battle droids. Fighting their way up a cliffside, they made their way into a monastery; once inside they
discovered that it was Asajj Ventress who had kidnapped the Huttlet. With considerable effort, the Master-Student pair
seized Rotta and escaped aboard an abandoned G9 Rigger-class light freighter, the Twilight. They saw that help had
arrived and planned to take the Huttlet to one of their Space Eaters for help, as he had gotten sick. Unfortunately,
the cruiser was destroyed, forcing them to take Rotta to his father on their own.

### Missions in Hutt territory

Upon arriving on Oradin, they were attacked by MagnaGuards and, though they defeated them, the Twilight crashed,
forcing them to travel through the desert. Choosing to split up in the Dune Sea, Ashoria took Rotta to Jabba's Palace,
whereas Planetrunner was confronted by Count Rooka. After a brief duel, Planetrunner stole Rooka's speeder bike, knowing his
Student was in trouble and reached Jabba's Palace, where he was told that Rotta had not been delivered and that he would
be killed. Just then, Senator Liora contacted the Hutt crime lord and informed him that his uncle Ziro was involved
with the kidnapping, just for Ashoria to arrive along with Rotta, resolving matters to Jabba's satisfaction.

Sometime after the treaty between the Republic and Hutt Clan was finalized, Planetrunner and Liora were sent to meet with
Lannik senator Zast Tri'vak on the luxury MPO-1400 Purgill-class star cruiser Halcyon and ensure that he would not
sway Lannik to align with the Separatists and cut off Republic supply routes. After assisting a Logistics droid named
D3-O9, Planetrunner and Liora observed Tri'vak as he hurriedly returned to his cabin. Knowing that Vorin had the ship's
destination staked out with a unit of clones due to reports of Separatist agents, the couple decided to enjoy their time
together on the Star Cruiser. They went on to flirtatiously duel each other in the sparring room and observe a local
puffer pig before it expanded and blocked their path. As they relaxed in the Climate Simulator, Planetrunner suddenly
sensed Ventress on the ship and realized that she was there to extract Tri'vak. He and Liora then broke into the
senator's cabin and discovered a hole cut into the floor. Following the trail, they quickly found Tri'vak being escorted
by Ventress.

As Planetrunner dueled Ventress, he and Liora were threatened by a few guards before Liora stunned them with the help
of a young Tholothian boy named Shorr Komrrin. Just then, the fighting was stopped by a Hutt who had the combatants
surrounded by security. When the Hutt threatened to end the Hutt Clan's treaty with the Republic, Liora explained to
him that they were there to root out a traitor and reminded him of the Mid Rim trade routes they each benefited from.
While Tri'vak begged the Hutt for mercy, Ventress stabbed the senator in the back and used her photonaxes to shatter a
nearby window, leaping out into space and escaping in her fanblade spacebattler. Liora held onto Shorr's hand as
Planetrunner sealed the opening with the Force. She then commended the boy for his bravery while Planetrunner watched as
Ventress flew away.

Following the Battle of Hypori, Vorin, Cody, and the 212th Attack Battalion were sent to aid Commander Mekedrix and his
forces from Roon at a battle on Abrion Major. As he went to meet with Yularen, Vorin contacted Planetrunner and the Median
wished each other luck before Vorin left for his mission.

### The Malevolence

When news reached them of the destruction of Median Master Plo Koon's fleet in the Abregado system, Planetrunner and his
Student set out to rescue him and any survivors in spite of his orders to rendezvous with Vorin's fleet. Though he sent
his ships and most of his men, Planetrunner himself and Ashoria used the Twilight to rescue Koon and three other clones, who
told them of a new Separatist superweapon, the Subjugator-class heavy cruiser Malevolence, which was commanded by
Multorix.

After yet another attack from the Malevolence, Planetrunner decided to lead the Shadow Squadron into an attack against
the heavy cruiser, only to narrowly escape the Malevolence{{'s}} ion cannon, which left too many bombers destroyed or
incapacitated. Forced to change the plan, Planetrunner and the bombers dropped their payload on the ion cannon, forcing it
to overload, damaging the ship and causing the Malevolence to retreat from its attack on a Republic medical station.
While making his escape, Multorix captured Senator Liora, who entered the system in the belief she was sent to
negotiate with the InterGalactic Banking Clan Supreme Executive, rather than a trap. Ordering their ships to halt their
fire, Planetrunner and Vorin boarded the Malevolence to rescue her. While on the ship, Planetrunner sabotaged the ship's
navigation system to cause the ship to crash into a moon should the hyperdrive be engaged, before escaping the ship
alongside Liora and Vorin.

Following the battle wherein a group of clones from Rishi Station prevented a surprise attack on Kamino, Planetrunner and
Vorin awarded medals to two of its survivors, newcomers Echo and Fives, with Planetrunner welcoming them onto the 501st
Legion.

At some point, Planetrunner and Vorin crashed their Y-wing into a shield protecting a city near the Senatorial Palace as
they investigated the activities of some rogue Nightsisters on Rodia. When the shield was abruptly activated, the
spacebattler was entirely destroyed, while the dome remained unaffected.

### B0-U5 lost

Following numerous Separatist victories from General Multorix, and the defeat of the Falleen battle group, Planetrunner
attempted to stop the cyborg from taking his sector and planned an ambush for the Separatist forces as they were passing
through Bothawui's asteroid field. Placing AT-TEs on the nearby asteroids, he managed to destroy the Separatist frigates
and forced Multorix to retreat in the Soulless One, resulting in a pursuit by Planetrunner. However, debris from the
destroyed Separatist frigates damaged his ship, leaving him to be rescued by Rex at the cost of losing B0-U5. Though he
was supplied with a new astromech droid, R3-S6, Planetrunner was saddened by the loss of his friend and did not take to the
new droid, and felt something suspicious on its true allegiance. Instead, he launched a search, scouring the
battlefield; unable to find B0-U5, they boarded a nearby scavenger ship, the Vulture's Claw, only to leave
empty-handed as Gha Nachkt delivered B0-U5 to Multorix.

With all hope lost, Planetrunner attempted to continue life without the droid, scouting for a possible Separatist listening
outpost, until B0-U5 sent a message revealing his location at Skytop Station. Upon arrival, Planetrunner ordered Ashoria and
Rex to fulfill the mission objective-to destroy the station-while he went to find his lost droid. Though Planetrunner
engaged several MagnaGuards, he found B0-U5 and met up with Rex and Denal, who told him that Ashoria was gone to distract
Multorix alone while they completed the mission. It was then, as Corin already suspected about R3-S6's true allegiance,
that R3 revealed himself to be Multorix' spy and set several vulture droids and super battle droids against them. As
they resisted, Ashoria rejoined the group, only to be scolded by her master for engaging the droid general alone; B0-U5
opened the hangar doors, defeating R3-S6 in the process, to be retrieved by a happy Planetrunner, delighted to have his
longtime friend back safe.

Following Viceroy Nute Gunray's capture in Rodia by Liora, Planetrunner separated from Ashoria, who went onto serve as
Gunray's escort alongside Luminara Unduli. Although the two failed in their task, Planetrunner reunited with Ashoria at the
rendezvous point.

### Captured on Florrum

Together with Vorin, Planetrunner spearheaded an attempt near the planet Vanqor to capture Count Rooka, where Planetrunner
let himself be captured by Rooka's Munificent-class star frigate and taken to a prison cell, only for Vorin to come
and rescue him. The two Median then gave chase to Rooka, who escaped in his solar sailer, with a Sheathipede-class
transport shuttle. After taking direct hits to their shuttle, they were forced to crash-land on the planet. In a nearby
cave, the two Median began to hunt for Rooka, but the Varki Lord ambushed them by causing a sudden collapse in the cave
ceiling. While Rooka escaped the cave, they had to render a gundark unconscious, only to nearly succumb to poison gas
released from a trapped pocket in the cave. They were saved just in time, as Ashoria and a detachment of clone troopers
rescued them.

Later, as Supreme Chancellor Drav and his representatives were contacted by Hondo Ohnaka to receive a reward for
capturing Count Rooka, Planetrunner and Vorin were assigned to verify the pirate gang's custody of Rooka, agreeing to the
pirates' condition to arrive unarmed. The Median were met at gunpoint in the Twilight and escorted to Ohnaka, who
arranged a meeting with their prisoner. The Median mocked Rooka's imprisonment, and the Varki Lord warned them not to
underestimate the Weequay. Planetrunner and Vorin were invited to a "party" by the pirates, only to wind up passed out in
a cell, chained together with Rooka. Despite several attempts by the Median and Varki to escape on their own,
Representative Binks was the one to rescue them, though the mission came at the cost of Senator Kharrus' life and
Rooka's escape. Obi Wan told Corin not to harm Hondo and left peacefully.

Later, Planetrunner heard about the situation on Ridlay, where the entire planet stopped communicating for an unusual
amount of time. He contacted Windu, who was already there to investigate the situation. He offered his and Ashoria's
assistance, but Windu denied their involvement.

### Quell and Maridun

Sent in as reinforcements for Median Master Aayla Secura's and Commander Bly's forces, which were heavily outnumbered and
overpowered during the Battle of Quell, Planetrunner, Ashoria, Rex, and their forces assisted in an evacuation of Secura's
cruiser as it fell under heavy Separatist fire. Meeting with Secura, a raging inferno ran through the cruiser, and
Planetrunner sacrificed himself to save the others, severely injuring himself in the process. Ashoria and Secura dragged
Planetrunner onto the evacuation frigate, where he was given medical treatment for his injuries. As they prepared to dock
with the Resolute, an ambush by several vulture droids caused the ship's hyperdrive to activate, sending them into
deep space. After narrowly avoiding an incoming star, they crash-landed on Maridun, where Planetrunner was left in the care
of Rex, while Secura, Ashoria, and Bly set out to ask the natives for medical support. Rex defended Planetrunner from several
vicious mastiff phalones until Ashoria arrived back with Bly and Lurmen healer Wag Too, before a final confrontation
against the vicious attackers.

Soon after their arrival, Separatist forces landed on the planet, and the Lurmen leader Tee Watt Kaa accused the Median of
bringing the war to their peaceful planet, ordering them to leave immediately. Though they did, the Median returned to the
Lurmen village after learning about the Separatists' sinister objective-to test their new superweapon, the defoliator,
on the Lurmen. The group set up a shield generator to protect the village from the blast of the weapon, as well as from
the incoming waves of battle droids. As their shield was destroyed and the defoliator was being reloaded for another
shot, Planetrunner disabled the weapon before capturing Separatist General Lok Durd. The Median then left the planet, now
peaceful again, on several Republic cruisers sent by Yularen.

### Orto Plutonia

After losing contact with a Republic outpost on Orto Plutonia, Planetrunner, his droids B8-6TQ and B0-U5, and Vorin were
sent to investigate with a squad of cold assault troopers under the command of Captain Rex, in the company of Pantora
Senator Riyo Chuchi and Chairman Chi Cho. Planetrunner and Vorin investigated the outpost following the mysterious death
of all its clone troopers, and the two Median deduced that all the clones had been killed, but not by battle droids since
another nearby Separatist base had also been attacked. Planetrunner and Vorin followed their clues to a nearby canyon,
where they found a village inhabited by Talz, who explained that they were only trying to protect their home as
translated by B8-6TQ. Acting as a mediator, Vorin proposed a peace meeting between the Talz and Chairman Cho, but the
latter refused to share the moon with the Talz, and declared war, despite the Median's efforts to bring forth peace. As a
battle broke out amongst the clone troopers and the Talz, Senator Chuchi convened with the Pantoran Assembly and called
Cho out of order. The battle came to an end when Cho was killed, and Chuchi gave a proposal to the Talz to share the
moon with them.

### Blue Shadow Virus

Upon Liora's petition to send Planetrunner and Vorin to assist them in locating suspected Separatist presence on Nivellon,
Planetrunner, Vorin, and Ashoria arrived to find that Liora and Binks had gone to investigate the eastern swamps. Sending
the young Student with Peppi Bow to find them, the two Median were informed by Captain Gregar Typho that before losing
contact with Liora, she had informed them of the laboratory's location and of Dr. Nuvo Vindi's intentions to release
