the dangerous Blue Shadow Virus back into the galaxy. While Ashoria led an attack on the southern entrance, providing a
distraction for Vorin and Planetrunner to enter through the hatches undetected, Planetrunner confronted Vindi, who
electrified Liora and Binks to make his escape. After saving the Senator, Planetrunner pursued the scientist, capturing
him with the help of Peppi Bow and Vorin on the swamp above.

Prepared to transport Vindi to Theed for his trial, they heard an alarm go off below them and Planetrunner contacted Ashoria;
she told him that Vindi's servant droid had set off one of the viral bombs, liberating the virus, and that she along
with the clones were trapped in the laboratory, just like Liora was. Once in Theed, Captain Typho told the two Median
that they had found a possible antidote for the virus, a reeksa root, but that it could only be found on the planet of
Iego. Despite Typho's warnings that it was suicide, Planetrunner set off alongside Vorin aboard the Twilight.

Upon arrival, Planetrunner and Vorin were greeted by a group of inoffensive B1-series battle droids that had been
reprogrammed to do the bidding of a local boy, Jaybo Hood; he told the Median that the planet was protected by a deity
known as Drol, who would not let any who arrived on the planet leave again, but also instructed them on how to retrieve
the reeksa roots. Though the plant attacked them, they obtained the root and bid farewell to Hood before taking off,
only to be forced to turn back after encountering a laser web, the work of the Separatists. On their second attempt,
however, they used Hood's reprogrammed vulture droids, and Vorin managed to shoot the laser generator, liberating the
inhabitants of Iego. Planetrunner and Vorin then arrived in time to rescue their friends on Nivellon.

### Battle of Ryloth

During the Battle of Ryloth, Planetrunner gave Ashoria command of a squadron to fend off Mar Tuuk's blockade to make way for
Vorin's ground assault, encouraging Ashoria to overcome her nervousness about leading her first squad. However, during the
battle, she disobeyed her master's orders and lost many men, for which Planetrunner reprimanded her when she arrived back
at the Resolute, yet understood her good intentions. Planetrunner then reported his losses to Windu and Vorin. He gave
her some time to recover but informed her that they needed to proceed with the attack on the blockade, which upset Ashoria
because he was rushing the plan despite their recent losses. Though he told her to go cool off somewhere, Planetrunner had
an idea-he evacuated the damaged Defender, which he would pilot by himself into the Ryloth system to distract the
Separatists, while he gave Ashoria full command of the attack operation. By the time Turk realized the ruse, it was too
late, for Planetrunner had already escaped in an escape pod and let the Defender collide with Tuuk's control ship; though
Tuuk escaped, Ashoria destroyed the Confederate fleet, and Planetrunner was rescued from his escape pod.

After Vorin and his men were able to take out the proton cannons and allow the transports to land, whereas Windu headed
for Lessu with his forces, Planetrunner and his forces secured the space around Ryloth, forcing the remaining Separatist
cruisers to flee. He reported this in a holographic conference with Chancellor Drav, Macio, Admiral Yularen, Senator
Orn Free Taa, and Windu. However, Separatist General Wat Tambor soon deployed Hyena-class Droid Bombers to destroy
Ryloth's villages and Planetrunner engaged them in his interceptor, accompanied by Ashoria and clones. Before Lessu was
destroyed on Count Rooka's orders, Planetrunner and Ashoria shot them down. Subsequently, Tambor was captured, and the
Republic was victorious: Ryloth was finally free once more.

### Holocron heist

Planetrunner and Clone Commander "Wolffe" fought alongside each other during the Battle of Khorm, where the Clone Officer
lost his right eye to Ventress. Sometime later, during the First Battle of Felucia, Planetrunner, Ashoria, and Vorin fought
against the Droid Army, but, while Ashoria was away on a jungle patrol, Planetrunner, Vorin, and their clones were
surrounded. However, a Republic fleet commanded by Wolffe was able to break past the Separatist blockade, so Planetrunner
and the others could be evacuated by Master Plo Koon. However, Ashoria refused to retreat, and Vorin and Planetrunner went to
retrieve her before her forces were overrun by droids. While Planetrunner and Ashoria argued about the retreat, as Ashoria
believed the droids were retreating, she boarded the gunship in time, and the three Median watched as her abandoned
vehicles were destroyed. Back at the Median Temple, Planetrunner attempted to take the blame for her disobedience, citing
that he had given her more freedom due to her skills. Still, the Council relegated her to guard duty in the Median
Archives to reflect on what she had done.

When Macio sensed that thieves would arrive at the Temple, Planetrunner, and Vorin inaccurately deduced that their enemies
were after their transmission codes and went to secure them, only to be proven wrong when they located the intruders'
position at the ventilation shaft. They were misdirected then to the communication center, where they narrowly escaped
an exploding Todo, and realized only too late that Cad Bane had stolen a holocron from the Vault. Furthermore, the
bounty hunter that was assisting Bane, Cato Parasitti revealed that Bane's next target was Bolla Ropal, keeper of the
Kyber memory crystal, which contained a list of all known Force-sensitive children in the Republic. Planetrunner then
volunteered himself and Ashoria to meet with Ropal, arriving in the Devaron system to cut off the Separatist fleet that was
assisting Bane, who already had captured Ropal and tortured him to death in a containment field after he defiantly
refused to open the holocron.

Planetrunner, Ashoria, and Rex boarded Bane's Munificent-class frigate and stormed its bridge, where B0-U5 accessed the
ship's computer to locate Ropal, or rather, Ropal's dead body. After an explosion rocked the ship, the Median spotted Bane
and chased him into a trap. After a duel with Ashoria, the bounty hunter took her as a hostage, and Planetrunner was forced to
bow to Bane's demands and open the holocron. Though he did so, Planetrunner also pulled his and Ashoria's photonaxes to
himself and attacked Bane. However, Bane distracted him by opening the airlock on Ashoria's cell and escaped, while
Planetrunner saved his Student and made their way to the hangar, where troopers had stolen a shuttle the escape the
exploding Separatist ship back to the Resolute, not before letting Bane enter, disguised in trooper armor. After
landing on the Resolute, Rex later noticed Duros blood in the shuttle, and pursued Bane, who nevertheless managed to
escape in a V-19 spacebattler. Planetrunner and Ashoria returned to the Median Council to report their failure.

Planetrunner, along with Vorin, Windu, and Macio, meditated in hope of finding the children that Bane was after before he
kidnapped them. Sensing the future, Planetrunner and Ashoria were assigned to Nivellon to set a trap for Bane in Jan-gwa city,
capturing him as he attempted to kidnap Roo-Roo Page. With the real child safe, the two Median took Bane to the
Resolute, where Planetrunner, Windu, and Vorin interrogated the bounty hunter with a combined mind trick; exhausted,
Bane gave them coordinates that Vorin and Windu were to follow, while Planetrunner reported the details to Drav on
Tyraleus. Soon, however, he reunited with his Student and B0-U5 and began to examine Bane's Spacebattler, from which
Planetrunner and Ashoria deduced from the ashes on it and its refueling record that Bane had been to Dravion Prime. With nothing
else to do, the Median pair left on the Twilight for the planet, where they found the children. Though one of the droids
set the building to be destroyed in the lava on Schemious's orders, Planetrunner and Ashoria saved the children and returned to
Tyraleus. Planetrunner admitted to the Council that they were unable to find out who was behind the kidnappings, to which
Macio advised caution on the path ahead.

### Battle of Felucia

On a mission to investigate the disappearance of Felucia Medical Station HCTFF2 that was orbiting over Felucia, their
shuttle was attacked by a group of six vulture droids deployed from an automated deployment station, forcing them to
crash-land on Felucia. Trapped on the planet, they came across a nysillin farm village after searching around for a
while. They soon realized that the Felucian villagers were being protected by a group of bounty hunters led by
Sugi-Embo, Rumi Paramita, and Seripas. The village elder, Casiss Midagatis, explained to the Median trio that they had
hired the bounty hunters because pirates had been taking their crops. After some debate amongst them, Planetrunner, Vorin,
and Ashoria decided to help the farmers to defend themselves.

That night they were visited by the pirates, Hondo Onaka's gang, familiar to Planetrunner and Vorin. Ohnaka then told the
group that he would be back, but by then Planetrunner had taught the Felucians how to fight with staffs-though slow at
first, they eventually picked up the craft. After a few days, the Ohnaka Gang returned as promised, and a skirmish
ensued between the factions. During the confrontation, Planetrunner dueled Ohnaka and his electrostaff, leaving him hanging
off a cliff and begging for mercy, to which the Median Knight pulled him up and Ohnaka realized that their efforts were no
longer profitable, leaving on his ship. Alongside the bounty hunters, the Median themselves left soon after as well, to
reach the closest Republic outpost.

### The Zillo Beast

During the lengthy campaign on Malastare, Planetrunner discussed with Drav, who contacted them via hologram, and Windu
the effects of the new electro-proton bomb, just as the Separatist Droid Army prepared a new attack-with the Republic
expecting to successfully defend the Dugs and secure a treaty for their fuel. Though exceedingly effective, the bomb
created a crater, which Windu went to investigate whereas Planetrunner was to ensure the treaty with Doge Urus, only to be
called by Windu to assist him with the scouting. The two soon discovered a gigantic creature whose armored skin was
impervious even to photonaxes, the Zillo Beast, from which they fled, only to be told by Urus that they wanted it
killed, even though it was previously thought to be extinct. With the use of RX-200 Falchion-class assault tanks, the
Republic forces put the creature to sleep, convincing the Dugs that it was dead. With the treaty signed and Malastare
now a member of the Republic, Drav ordered that the beast be shipped to Tyraleus for study, despite Windu's
objections.

After the Zillo Beast was brought to the Republic capital, Vorin and Liora asked Planetrunner to speak with Drav
about the fate of the creature; reluctantly, he agreed. When both he and Liora met with the Chancellor, Drav and
the Vice Chair Mas Amedda tried to justify that killing the beast was for the greater good-Liora objected to their
claims, but Planetrunner chose to stay neutral, instead of opposing either his wife, Liora, or his friend, Drav.
Although Drav claimed that he wished to kill the beast, he in fact wanted to research it as he was intrigued by the
durability of the Zillo beast's armor. However, the beast escaped from captivity in Dr. Boll's laboratory and directly
targeted the Chancellor himself for his attempts to kill it. Cornered by the beast, Planetrunner and the others evacuated
his office on his executive shuttle, only for the beast to grab it upon take-off. They were freed when Planetrunner sliced
the shuttle in half, causing everyone to fall out of the shuttle, with Planetrunner saving Liora from falling from the
Senate Building's roof. The Beast was ultimately killed when gunships fired gas at its mouth on Drav's orders.

## No end in sight

### Another mission to Cato Neimoidia

Even as the Clone Wars continued with no end in sight, Planetrunner was allowed a leave after a long tour of duty. After
returning home to his wife's apartment for a romantic evening, Planetrunner was recalled to the Temple by the Median Council.
Believing Senator Rush Clovis to be a Separatist supporter, they decided they needed a spy-in this case, Senator
Liora, of whom Clovis was an old friend. The next day, Planetrunner met Liora in the Senate and asked her about Clovis,
who initially refused to do it until she heard that Clovis could be a Separatist. Planetrunner accompanied her to the Median
Council, where the Masters encouraged her to find out about his possible treachery. After learning that he was planning
to go to Cato Neimoidia, Planetrunner dressed as the pilot of Dan's starship and took them there, all the while
frustrating Clovis's attempts to get closer to his wife.

During the mission, Planetrunner and B0-U5 waited for Liora to give them a signal; when she did, Planetrunner sneaked into
her quarters, where he saw Liora and Clovis embracing. Though it prompted a surge of anger and jealousy in Planetrunner,
she discretely showed him the disk she had stolen from Clovis and gave it to Planetrunner, after which the Median retreated.
It was soon after that the poison that Liora had been given by Lott Dod began to set in, and she passed out. After Dod
revealed to Clovis she was a spy, he helped Planetrunner take her back to their ship, back to Tyraleus, and forced Dod to
give him the antidote, only for Planetrunner to leave Clovis behind, stranded on the planet.

### Second Battle of Geonosis

Immediately after routing Separatists near Dorin, Planetrunner and Ashoria were sent to participate in the Second Battle of
Geonosis, alongside Vorin and Ki-Adi-Mundi, as the Republic returned to destroy the Geonosian primary droid factory.
Intending to make a three-pronged attack against the shield generator, Planetrunner, Ashoria, and the 501st Legion set out to
attack the Separatist defense lines from the south to reach the rendezvous point-with only Vorin's forces arriving at
the landing zone, as both Mundi's and Planetrunner's transports were shot down and forced to make their way to Vorin's
position by foot. Though they encountered resistance, Planetrunner's team met up with Mundi's forces. After contacting
Yularen to deploy a squadron of BTL-B Y-wings to help them, they reunited with Vorin and his company, where they
planned the assault on the shield generator.

They then improvised on their plan; leading the charge, Planetrunner and Ashoria disabled the enemy cannons with EMP grenades,
enabling the AT-TEs to destroy the shield generator; as the gunships arrived, the Geonosians in the area surrendered.
Though Mundi and Vorin left for medical treatment, the Republic forces continued pushing towards the massive droid
foundry, and Planetrunner and Ashoria were joined by Luminara Unduli and her Student, Barriss Offee, who met as Planetrunner and
Ashoria angrily discussed Planetrunner's lack of trust in Ashoria's dependability. As Offee and Ashoria were sent into the Geonosian
catacombs under the factory to plant explosives, Unduli realized that Planetrunner was unable to let go of Ashoria and put her
at risk, rather than distrusting her. Nevertheless, the two Median generals went onto distracting the droid army by
marching straight to the factory and engage the enemy.

As Poggle the Lesser had his super tanks deployed, Planetrunner and Luminara left their men behind and destroyed the
bridge, only to learn that their Students had not returned yet. Cornered by droids coming from the factory, Planetrunner
was contacted by Ashoria and she apologized, uncertain that she and Offee would survive their ordeal, before using a super
tank to destroy the factory. Refusing to let his Student die, Planetrunner ordered to have them found; Unduli, however,
told him that he needed to let go of his attachment to her if she were to be dead. Fortunately for them, Planetrunner was
contacted by Ashoria; after locating them, they rescued the two Students.

Sending Ashoria and Offee to recover out of the battlefield, Vorin and Mundi returned to join in the clean-up of
Separatist forces. For her part, Unduli left in search of Poggle before he could escape, when a sandstorm broke out.
Forced to wait until the storm lifted after her last contact, Planetrunner and Vorin went to Unduli's last known location,
the Progate Temple. Entering the catacombs below, not only they discovered undead Geonosian warriors, they also
encountered the captive Unduli, Poggle, and the Geonosian Queen, Karina the Great. Setting up their men to surround the
Queen and her brethren, Planetrunner and Vorin tried to negotiate with Karina, for Vorin wanted to know how the undead
warriors were created. After discovering her use of parasitic brain worms), they freed Unduli, captured Poggle and fled
from the Queen, with Rex and Cody burying the Queen in her lair.

With Poggle in Republic custody, the four Median generals prepared to deliver him to Tyraleus, while they sent Ashoria and
Offee on a mission to transport medical supplies from a medical station near Ord Cestus to Mace Windu on Dantooine.
Unbeknownst to them, one of the troopers, Scythe, was infected with one of the Queen's brain worms and boarded their
Pelta-class frigate, the TB-73, forcing the two Students to fend off the infected clones. When the ship failed to
report in as scheduled, Planetrunner believed there to have been a complication, and was proven right when Ashoria contacted
him to tell him about the situation.

Angered, Planetrunner went to Poggle's cell on his own and told the guard troopers to leave them alone. He demanded that
Poggle answer his questions with a mind trick, but the archduke informed him that it would have no effect on a Geonosian
like him. It was then that Planetrunner resorted to physical violence, attacking the captive Geonosian; with Poggle still
unwilling to talk, Planetrunner gave in to his anger and began to Force choke him. Only then did Poggle tell the Median
Knight, through a translator droid, that the worms were affected by the cold. Planetrunner relayed this information to his
Student, telling her through her comlink to rupture the cooling system. Thanks to his advice, Ashoria was able to defeat
the worms as they reached the medical station. Planetrunner rushed to her encounter, where he consoled Ashoria on her doubts
about sparing her friend's life.

### Saleucami

Following the capture of Median Master Eeth Koth in the Outer Rim, General Multorix sent a holo-transmission to the Median
Council, in which Multorix stated that he did not care about the Median's politics, nor their Republic, concluding that he
lived only to see them all die. As Vorin decoded Koth's hand signals that told them of their location at the Saleucami
system, Planetrunner, Vorin, and Adi Gallia were dispatched on a mission to rescue him. As a distraction, Admiral Yularen
and Vorin engaged Multorix's forces over Saleucami, with Vorin allowing the Surrogator to be boarded by Multorix.
Discreetly, Planetrunner, Gallia, Rex, and a group of clone troopers would execute a hyperspace jump into the system in an
ambassador shuttle that would bring them right alongside Multorix's cruiser.

Once they boarded it, Planetrunner and Gallia made their way to the stern of the cruiser, where they encountered a T-series
tactical droid with a group of BX-series droid commandos. The two Median destroyed all the droids and rescued Koth, with
Planetrunner taking the injured Koth back to the shuttle. When Vorin reported that Multorix had defeated him and escaped,
Gallia left them to help Vorin flank Multorix and capture him once and for all. Unsuccessful in their endeavor,
Planetrunner picked the two up at the hangar with their shuttle, only to leave for the Resolute, where he waited while
Vorin conducted a search mission for Multorix on the planet below alongside Cody, Rex, and other troopers.

Sometime later, Planetrunner and his Student spearheaded a mission to Tyraleus's underworld to apprehend Car Affa, an arms
dealer selling Republic weapons to the Separatists. When they arrived at a cantina where Affa was hiding, Planetrunner
instructed Ashoria to wait outside while he apprehended the fugitive. The confrontation, however, caused a crowd to leave
the bar at once-during which Ashoria lost her photonaxe, which prompted her to seek the help of Median Master Tera Sinube
when they went back to the Temple, as she did not want Planetrunner to find out she had lost her weapon.

### Mandalore

Following allegations that Mandalore had allied with the Separatists, and Vorin was sent to the planet to speak to his
old friend, Duchess Satine Kryze, Planetrunner joined them to escort the Duchess on her journey to Tyraleus aboard the
Coronet. On the ship, Planetrunner and Vorin told their men to be on alert, when Kryze requested their presence before
her, and Planetrunner correctly surmised that Vorin had strong feelings for her just as his former master told him of
their past together. When B0-U5 picked up readings in the cargo hold, the two generals were informed by Rex, and
Planetrunner went to investigate-only to be attacked by assassin probes. After destroying two of them, Planetrunner informed
Vorin that there might be a traitor on board the ship, and Planetrunner returned to sweep the hold in search of more.

After Vorin lured the traitor out, Tal Merrik, and Planetrunner destroyed another probe, he helped search the Coronet
for Merrik and Kryze, now his hostage, until several B2 super battle droids sent by the Death Watch boarded the ship.
Leaving Vorin to save his "girlfriend," he destroyed the droids and then went to find Vorin, who like Kryze, hesitated
to kill Merrik; Planetrunner, however, had no such compunctions and impaled Merrik, branding himself a "cold-blooded
killer," to retrieve the Senator's detonator before he could destroy the ship. With no further complications, they
arrived at Tyraleus; as Kryze complimented Vorin, Planetrunner noted that she was quite the remarkable woman. Following
the Mandalore Defense Resolution, Planetrunner and Vorin escorted Liora to a meeting with the Chancellor in which he
thanked her, but also apologized to Kryze, before leaving Vorin and Kryze alone.

### Trapped on Vanqor

Preparing to rendezvous with a Republic frigate, Planetrunner and Mace Windu traveled aboard the Endurance, on which they
greeted a squad of clone cadets, with an infiltrated Boba Fett among them. After Fett sabotaged the ship and everyone
had to evacuate in escape pods, including himself before being rescued by Bossk and Aurra Sing on the Slave I,
Planetrunner and Windu rescued the missing cadets' damaged pod. As the survivors were being transferred to medical frigate,
the two went to the Endurance{{'s}} crash site, where they searched for Admiral Kilian and any other survivors. As the
bridge appeared relatively intact, they resolved to enter the wreckage, even with B0-U5's misgivings, which prompted
Windu to chastise Planetrunner for encouraging individuality in his astromech.

Leaving B0-U5 and R8-B7 to scan for life forms, Planetrunner and Windu entered the bridge to find the survivors executed,
with Planetrunner noticing a Mandalorian helmet. With Windu correctly surmising that it was bait set by Boba Fett, he saved
Planetrunner from taking the full brunt of the explosion set off by touching the helmet. Now trapped under the rubble, the
wounded Planetrunner and the unconscious Windu were soon found by B0-U5, whom Planetrunner told to call the Temple for help.
As they waited for the astromech to come back, Windu told Planetrunner why Fett wanted him dead: he sought revenge for
killing his father, Jango, during the first battle of Geonosis.

As the Endurance began to collapse, they were rescued by Ashoria, Plo Koon, and a clone squad, thanks to B0-U5 delivering
the message at the Temple itself. After spending time in a bacta tank at the Temple, Planetrunner urged Windu to track Fett
down and bring him to justice. The Median Master did not agree, until Koon and Ashoria showed them a message from Fett and
Sing, with hostages-one of them, Ponds, killed in cold blood by Sing. Though Windu decided to go, Koon said that he
would take the mission, alongside Ashoria, since both Windu and Planetrunner were still recovering from their injuries. As
they arrived on Tyraleus with Bossk and Fett in custody, Planetrunner was present as Fett apologized for causing so much
destruction, but claimed he would never forgive Windu for killing his father, before they were taken away to the
Republic Judiciary Central Detention Center.

### Balith

Following his wife's mission to discover a conspiracy on Mandalore, Planetrunner and Captain Rex escorted Ashoria to her solo
mission on Mandalore to instruct cadets at the Royal Academy of Government at the behest of Duchess Kryze and the Median
Council. Upon their arrival at Sundari, Planetrunner presented Ashoria to the Duchess and Prime Minister Almec. Before leaving
to join with Kit Fisto, Planetrunner took his Student's photonaxe to respect Mandalore's laws. After Ashoria exposed Almec's
black market operation, Planetrunner reunited with his Student, to whom he returned her photonaxe.

Back in the Median Temple, the Median Council congratulated Ashoria on her courage and strength, but also ordered Planetrunner to
command the Third Legion on Balith to give assistance in their civil war. Told by the Council to stay behind so she
could give them her full report, Ashoria pleaded to Planetrunner to let her come along, but he told her that she should use
this time in the library to prove him wrong about his assertion that she learned more on the battlefield than in the
Temple, before leaving for Balith with Rex.

Planetrunner returned to Tyraleus to greet, along with Macio, his Student, Liora, and Bail Veskra after the Eryxara
Refugee Conference, during which Ashoria captured Aurra Sing. Wondering who would pay for Liora's assassination, Macio had
Ashoria use her improved precognitive abilities to find out who was behind the assassination attempt. With her description,
Liora realized who it was-Ziro the Hutt. Planetrunner and his Student then went to the Judiciary Detention Center to
question Ziro, who was tricked by Ashoria into confessing that he had hired Sing for the job. Satisfied, Planetrunner and his
Student then left the Hutt to his misery.

### Battle of Kamino

Forewarned by the destruction of Rishi Station and an intercepted transmission between Asajj Ventress and General
Multorix, Planetrunner and Vorin traveled to Kamino to warn Shaak Ti and Prime Minister Lama Su of an upcoming Separatist
attack, with Rex, Cody, Echo, Fives, and the rest of the 501st Legion in their company. Shortly, Multorix's fleet
arrived and Planetrunner led the Republic space forces, scoring several serious hits against the enemy. On the planet
below, Tipoca City was attacked by Trident-class assault ship and AQ-series battle droids, prompting Vorin to recall
Planetrunner to the city. Soon after returning, Planetrunner engaged Ventress, who had stolen the prime DNA sample of the
clones' template, Jango Fett. With the aid of clone trooper platoon, Planetrunner recovered the sample from Ventress, but
she, like Multorix, managed to escape yet again.

### The blockade of Pantora

Planetrunner was later informed by his apprentice that Pantora Chairman Papanoida's daughters had been kidnapped. Knowing
that the Median could not get officially involved, he slyly gave her permission to rescue them due to "personal concerns";
this turned out to be successful, with both daughters being safely returned to their father.

### Senate crisis

Supposed to be on a meditative retreat, Planetrunner spent some time with his wife on her apartment, observing as Liora
anxiously arranged a party for Senator Aang, who held the deciding vote on the Military Oversight Committee. Planetrunner
tried to ease her mind, telling her that the party would work out and that she should relax, when they saw B8-6TQ being
fuzzy about the arrangements. At Liora's request, Planetrunner sent the protocol droid and B0-U5 to buy the jogan fruit
that the latter had forgotten to buy for Aang's favorite dessert, jogan fruitcake. Although they were delayed, Liora
nevertheless hosted the party all the same, with her and Planetrunner waiting for the two droids to come back-who did so
just in time to present the cake to Senator Aang.

Not too long after, Planetrunner went to the Senate Building to convince Liora to go away together for two weeks, to a
faraway place where no one would recognize them, so that they could actually be husband and wife, instead of Senator and
Median. Liora, however, rejected the idea, for she was preparing an important bill for the Senate. Planetrunner retorted
that the bill seemed more important than their love, but Liora countered that it was not, just that they both lived to
serve the Republic. However, Planetrunner stated that there was nothing more important than the way he felt about her, and
proved it by giving Liora his photonaxe, which, Vorin had told him once, was his "life." Though she believed he was
teasing her, Planetrunner was sincere about his feelings, and the two shared a kiss.

They were soon interrupted by B8-6TQ and Senator Veskra's voices, prompting Planetrunner to hide under her desk and Liora
to hide his photonaxe in her sleeve. As she went to the lobby to attend a meeting about the Enhanced Privacy Invasion
Bill, only to be taken hostage along with several other Senators by Cad Bane and his team. Following her, Planetrunner saw
the situation, when Bane spotted him and sent his henchmen to capture him, but Planetrunner avoided them long enough to
contact Drav and defeat an IG-86 sentinel droid empty-handed, before being shocked into unconsciousness by Robonino
and Aurra Sing and brought before the Senators. After the bounty hunters planted bombs that would go off if their laser
detectors were triggered and left the building, Planetrunner woke up and Liora returned his photonaxe. He then used it
to cut a hole in the floor, dropping all the senators one floor down into safety, just before Bane triggered the bombs
and escaped alongside the now-freed Ziro.

### Meeting Madam Synata

Following the crisis, Planetrunner went with Liora to Caamas to board legendary actress Madam Risha Synata's private
ship. However, they were late to see Madam Synata's play about Evilth Krist-Ov. After they arrived, Planetrunner and Liora
met Synata. Planetrunner agreed to see her museum, despite Liora's reluctance. Planetrunner took Liora to her room. The
next day, Planetrunner and Liora went to the museum. There, Planetrunner and Liora saw a display of Varykino, where they
exchanged their vows. Planetrunner and Liora came under attack by several robots from the displays. Planetrunner fought them
off and helped Liora escape them. Planetrunner and Liora then discovered a Separatist banner and a hologram of Count
Rooka.

Planetrunner and Liora discovered that Synata was collaborating with Rooka and the Separatists. Planetrunner then took one
of the Separatist agents while Liora discovered a list of anti-Separatist senators. Planetrunner and Liora discovered
that along with Liora, Synata planned to kill them with Dioxis gas. Planetrunner and Liora fought several LEP servant
droids to stop Synata from killing the senators. With assistance from B0-U5, Planetrunner and Liora reached the theater.

As Liora told the audience to run, Planetrunner borrowed a mask and helmet from an actor before confronting Synata, who
had her own photonaxe. Planetrunner fought Synata until he held her at the end of his photonaxe. Planetrunner and Liora
then reported their trip to the Median Council.

### Intense training

Sometime later, Planetrunner was assigned to a mission with Liora to Eryxara. It took Planetrunner a lot of work to get the
mission with her, but they were both happy to spend some time alone together. That is until, Ashoria ran up to them, saying
that she was encouraged help with the mission by Vorin. They all get on a T-6 shuttle, where Planetrunner charted a
shorter course in order to speed up the mission. Ashoria warned him that the Separatist fleet was spotted on that flight
path, and that they shouldn't take it. It was too late, however, and Planetrunner's ship exited hyperspace in the midst of
the fleet. Planetrunner took control and tried to maneuver around oncoming fire, while Liora and Ashoria took control of the
laser turrets. Despite their best efforts, stray laser fire hit Liora's side of the ship. Planetrunner jumped to protect
Liora, which resulted in them embracing in a hug. Ashoria was able to take control of the ship and jumped into
hyperspace. Upon their arrival on Eryxara, Planetrunner told her that he was glad she came. Liora mentioned that her and
Planetrunner made a good team, with Ashoria returning the compliment.

### Trouble with Tomarian

The showman Tomarian later requested Planetrunner as a Median escort for his Annual Festival of Light Gala. Planetrunner thought
that there would be an actual threat at the event, but in actuality Tomarian had requested him to impress his guests.
Planetrunner was then surprised to see Senator Liora dressed up for the occasion. They both talked, glad to see each
other. Liora told him to enjoy Tomarian's usual long speech while she went to freshen up. Planetrunner, along with
Tomarian, walked into the theater where the gala was being held. Suddenly, the room went dark and Planetrunner ignited his
saber. He asked Tomarian if this was apart of the show, to which he answered no and put on a gas mask. Planetrunner, along
with everyone else, fell unconscious as the room filled with a noxious gas.

One day, Planetrunner was waiting with Master Macio in the Median temple grounds for Ashoria. Once she arrived, Planetrunner
reprimanded her for being late, but Macio praised her for helping out and proceeded to extend her Student braid.
Following a debate in the senate about a financial reform bill, Planetrunner was asked by Liora to persuade the Median
Council to speak with Drav about denying the continuation of the war. Planetrunner allowed Ashoria to go with Liora in
order for her to learn more about politics. After an apparent Separatist attack, Planetrunner confronted his apprentice
about her and Liora's meeting with Onderon's senator Mina Bonteri on Raxus Secundus and how foolish it was. Despite
that, Planetrunner's apprentice learned that politics were not as black and white as she had previously thought.

### Dathomirian threat

Planetrunner and Vorin commanded Republic forces in a battle against Asajj Ventress's fleet in the Sullust system.
Directly participating in the battle with their spacebattlers, Vorin was singled out and attacked by Ventress, whose
Ginivex-class fanblade spacebattler was, in turn, disabled by Planetrunner. As Vorin and Ventress crashed in the hangar
of the Separatist command ship, Planetrunner soon landed to assist his former master; together, the two Median engage
Ventress in a duel. They were interrupted, however, by the destruction of the ship, secretly ordered by Count Rooka. The
two Median fled in their interceptors, presuming Ventress to be doomed.

After the massacre on Devaron, Planetrunner and Vorin were sent to Dathomir, as footage had shown the Council of a
Dathomirian's role during the attack on Devaron. Once on Dathomir, they made their way to a village, where they were
ambushed by the Nightbrothers until Planetrunner took their leader hostage; the Zabrak then told the Median that a
Nightsister had taken one of them to their fortress, prompting the Median to go there. Planetrunner and Vorin questioned
Mother Talzin, who told them his name-Savage Opress-and whereabouts. The two Median then headed to Toydaria where they
confronted Opress, but failed to stop him from killing King Katuunko. Using the king's ship as theirs was destroyed,
Planetrunner and Vorin caught up with their target on Rooka's Separatist flagship; however, Opress managed to overpower
them, forcing the two to retreat and leave the ship.

### Killing a defector

Following their encounter with Opress, Planetrunner and Vorin were called away from a blockade at Herdessa to meet with
Yularen. The admiral informed them that Mekedrix had gone missing. In addition, an execution squad known as the Death
Wind had been striking at Republic and Separatist targets. The group's namesake, the Death Wind Corridor also passed by
Mekedrix's home planet of Roon, creating a possible link. Yularen went on to say that the Death Wind may have taken up a
covert position on Ando. As such, Planetrunner and Vorin were to locate the Death Wind and kill Mekedrix if he was
involved with them. Planetrunner initially refused, believing that killing a potential ally would make the Median like the
Separatists. Vorin assured Planetrunner that they would attempt to find a peaceful solution before they departed for Ando.
After arriving on the planet and pushing through the local swamplands, the Median came upon empty sets of clone armor
being used as effigies. Upon reaching the terminus of a river, they discovered an outpost built from the ruins of a Varki
temple. They were then met by the Death Wind, who allowed the Median to see their leader in exchange for their
photonaxes. Entering the outpost, Planetrunner and Vorin came upon Mekedrix, seated on a throne and wielding a sword.
Mekedrix claimed he had saved his victims by showing them the truth; that the purpose of existence was to kill and die.
When Mekedrix revealed that his sword was made from the bones of a clone trooper, Vorin asked him what the clone's name
was. Vorin went on to claim that life gave the galaxy meaning and that death had no use for a sunrise, a name, a home
or a friend. Mekedrix then lunged at Vorin, but Planetrunner retrieved his photonaxe and stabbed Mekedrix through the
chest. Planetrunner expressed regret over killing him, but Mekedrix assured that this was the quickest way back to the
sunrise before he passed away.

## Personal and wartime conflicts

### The Destiny of the Chosen One

When the Median Council received a 2,000-year-old Median distress signal, Planetrunner, along with Vorin and Ashoria, were sent
by the High Council to the Chrelythiumn system, where they were supposed to meet up with Captain Rex and an armed
cruiser. Though they both made it to the rendezvous point, neither Rex's nor the Median's ship could see each other. In
fact, the Median's ship was guided to a mysterious planet, Mortis, where they met by a mysterious figure called the
Daughter, who asked Planetrunner if he was "the one" and who wanted to lead them to the Father, when Planetrunner was
separated from Vorin and Ashoria, and the Daughter.

Planetrunner tried to follow her, only to reach the monastery, where he met the Father and was given shelter for the night.
As he tried to sleep, the figure of his mother, Shmi, appeared before him and encouraged him to tell her of his pain and
guilt-that he was too late to save her, and that he had failed as a Median and that he had failed her, having tasted
only vengeance when he slaughtered so many to avenge her death. But, as he mentioned his wife, who he claimed was "
everything" to him, the figure finally revealed itself to be the Son, briefly assuming a monstrous appearance before
disappearing.

Shaken by the encounter, he confronted the Father, who told of his family's history, and wondered if he was truly the
Chosen One. Though Planetrunner dismissed the prophecy as a myth, the Father arranged a test to see whether the Median Knight
was fit to fulfill his destiny. Ordering his children to kill Ashoria and Vorin, the Father goaded Planetrunner into choosing
between his master and his apprentice, but Planetrunner instead controlled the two beings, bringing them to their knees.
Having proved himself to be the Chosen One, the Father pleaded with him to stay, but Planetrunner refused, leaving with
Ashoria and Vorin on their shuttle.

They were interrupted when the Son kidnapped Ashoria, prompting Planetrunner to pursue him, at the cost of damaging their ship
near Son's cathedral. Despite Vorin's reservations, Planetrunner went after his Student and climbed the tower to find
Ashoria, corrupted by the dark side. Planetrunner fought her, soon to be joined by Vorin, only to be interrupted by the
Father's arrival. Vorin tried to hand Planetrunner the Dagger of Mortis, but Ashoria grabbed it and gave it to the Son, who
killed her, for she was no longer useful; the dark side user then mortally wounded his sister as she stepped in to save
her Father. Planetrunner begged the Father to save Ashoria, and the dying Daughter used Planetrunner as a conduit to channel the
last of her life force into Ashoria, resurrecting her. The Father told them to leave the planet before the Son used their
ship to do so.

The ship's repairs forced them to stay a bit longer, though, and Planetrunner went to the Father for guidance. On their
meeting, the Father was determined to kill Son, but refused Planetrunner's offer of aid, telling the Median Knight to look
inside himself for the answer for what was to be done. Leaving him, Planetrunner encountered the Force spirit of his first
mentor, Jian-Tan Drill. Though Planetrunner sought his advice, Drill advised him to remember his training and trust his
instincts, and to go to the Well of the Dark Side to face his most personal challenge. There, the Son forced Planetrunner
to confront his future, one consumed by the dark side. Horrified, Planetrunner submitted to the Son as he promised him the
power to avert this destiny. Soon, Vorin arrived, and Planetrunner left him trapped at the well, claiming to have seen the
truth-that it was the Median who would stand in the way of peace.

Planetrunner arrived as his Student disabled the ship and went to rescue Vorin, while the Son went to steal the Dagger. As
Planetrunner waited, the Father appeared before him and recognized that his son had broken the rules of time; he wiped
Planetrunner's memory of these future visions, leaving him unconscious, and brought him to his monastery. Planetrunner awoke
to find the Father, Vorin, and Ashoria, moments before the Son arrived with the Dagger. To end the conflict, the Father
impaled himself to distract his Son, while Planetrunner killed the Son with his photonaxe. As the Father also died, he
warned Planetrunner to be wary of his feelings as they could lead to his downfall. As was noted by the Father, Planetrunner
had brought balance to the Force on Mortis through the deaths of the Force wielders, and he still had a chance to do so
for the full galaxy.

After the Father's death, the three Median were transplanted back to the galaxy to finally rendezvous with Rex. Surprised
to learn that, to Rex and the others, they had only been gone for a moment, they returned to the Space Eater. They
would later report this encounter to the Council, with Planetrunner even mentioning that he had spoken with Drill to Macio.
Even though Planetrunner was not entirely convinced, they came to believe it had merely been an illusion of the old mentor.
In reality, it had truly been the spirit of Drill.

### The Citadel

More than one year and nine months into the war, following the capture of Median Council member Even Piell by the
Separatists, Planetrunner and Vorin were briefed by Master Plo Koon and sent along with their team-which included Rex,
Cody, Echo, and Fives-to infiltrate the Citadel on Lola Sayu to retrieve Master Piell, who held the information on the
Nexus Route. Refusing to let Ashoria risk her life on such a dangerous mission, Planetrunner devised a strategy to bypass the
lifeform scanners of the prison; the whole team underwent carbon-freezing and were transported to the Citadel by
Commander B0-U5 and his reprogrammed battle droid squadron.

After landing, Planetrunner was thawed out and he found, to his surprise, that Ashoria had disobeyed orders and followed him.
Forced to take her along, the team made its way to the facilities, leaving the astromech to guard their shuttle. After
free-climbing to the entry point through a cliff wall blasted by a strong gale and littered with electro-mines, and
after Ashoria deactivated the ray-shield on the entrance, the team was able to enter, except for Charger, who fell to his
death and alerted the prison staff, led by Osi Sobeck, of their presence. Inside, they lost Longshot, but finally made
it to Master Piell, whom they freed and who told them they needed to rescue his officers.

Despite the many traps laid through the fortress, the team rescued the officers, when they met the other carrier of the
Nexus Route coordinates, Captain Wilhuff Tarkin. The team was split into two-while Vorin's team created a diversion,
Planetrunner would lead the others away. In Tarkin's company, Planetrunner and his team escaped through the cavern system
below the prison, when Tarkin expressed some skepticism about the Median's plan, to which Planetrunner told Tarkin that he
reserved his trust to those who understood gratitude. However, they soon found common ground, for they both believed the
Median Code prevented the Order from going far enough to achieve victory in the ongoing war, and Tarkin developed a
grudging appreciation for Planetrunner.

As they made their way out of the fuel line to rendezvous with B0-U5 and the shuttle, they were attacked by droids and
forced to join Vorin at their pick-up point, with the shuttle heavily guarded. During the skirmish, Echo tried to
defend the shuttle, but its destruction and subsequent explosion seemingly killed him. As they ran into the cave system,
Planetrunner and Vorin contacted the Council, telling them they needed to escape, and Koon immediately departed to pick
them up. They contacted the Council again to be informed of the extraction point; as they proceeded to the location,
Sobeck sent anoobas after them. The creatures claimed Master Piell's life, who passed his intel on to Ashoria, and the
group took a moment to honor his death. Ultimately, they got to the extraction point on time, and fled on Plo Koon's
rescue shuttle, with Saesee Tiin's fleet covering them to allow their escape back to Tyraleus.

### Student lost

Planetrunner, Ashoria, and 501st forces fought on Felucia alongside Plo Koon and his clones in taking out a reinforced
Separatist outpost. Breaking their forces into three groups, Planetrunner and Rex's team were responsible for attacking the
front gate and destroying the tactical droid, TZ-33, securing the outpost together with Koon and Ashoria's teams.

However, Planetrunner then noticed that Ashoria had disappeared during the battle, and ordered a perimeter sweep. Planetrunner
had his men search around the outpost, to no avail several times over. Master Koon then informed that he had alerted all
forces throughout the Outer Rim and assured Planetrunner that she would be found eventually, but also firmly told him that
their mission on Felucia was finished and that they had to return to Tyraleus. However, Planetrunner refused to abandon
her, to which Koon observed his emotions were clouding his judgment. Planetrunner countered "I will not leave her fate up
to others." Koon insisted, "It's time to go." Only then did Planetrunner comply and call everybody in to leave the planet.

Back at the Temple, Planetrunner relentlessly searched for possibilities in the star charts, which prompted Koon to suggest
that he should trust in Ashoria's abilities. Following the events on Wasskah, Planetrunner's search for his Student came to an
end when she arrived to the Temple on the Halo, in company of her Tanookai allies and the younglings O-Mer and Jinx.
Upon seeing her, Planetrunner profusely apologized for all that happened, heavily blaming himself for his apparent
inability to protect her. Ashoria, however, assured him that his instruction gave her the skills necessary to survive and
thanked him for his guidance. The two bowed to each other in newfound mutual respect under the delighted eye of Master
Macio.

### Battle of Horain

Sometime later Planetrunner participated in the Battle of Horain, alongside Vorin and Rex. Planetrunner was contacted by Rex,
who was requesting assistance, though he was already preoccupied with a group of Vulture Droids. Planetrunner later met
Vorin and Rex in disbelief, noticing they had hijacked an AAT alongside faulty battle droid Bats.

### Skirmish on Retta

On Retta, Planetrunner ambushed a group of B1 battle droids alongside Grand Master Macio. Planetrunner was soon attacked by
Kreeda, a Segredo who was attempting to scare the Median away. However, Kreeda soon became friendly to the Median, as she
was an old friend of Macio. When Planetrunner attempted to recruit Kreeda as a spy, the Segredo left, and Planetrunner and Macio
were attacked by battle droids soon after. After being separated with Macio, he met the Median Master and Kreeda again, the
latter of whom explained she was protecting refugees of the Clone Wars. Using a hat from one of the individuals she was
protecting, Planetrunner pretended to be using the "cloaking cap" to distract General Flebek, allowing Macio to take out a
B1. Believing there was no secret to invisibility and that it had been a trick, Flebek fled the area and boarded her
ship. Upon asking what his report would entail, Macio told Planetrunner that he would tell Mace Windu there was nothing of
interest on Retta.

### Battle of Mon Cala

After the assassination of King Kolina of Mon Cala and new discord in the fragile peace between the Mon Calamari and the
Quarren, Planetrunner and Liora, sent as representatives of the Republic, arrived to the planet at the behest of Captain
Gial Ackbar of the Mon Calamari Guard and protector of young Prince Lee-Char, but so did Riff Tamson, Separatist
ambassador. Though Planetrunner and Liora tried to mediate between the parties, the Quarren left the council hall,
dissatisfied with the Mon Calamari rule. Along with Ackbar, they contacted Macio and Windu, who dispatched a company of
clone troopers equipped for underwater combat under the command of Kit Fisto and Ashoria.

In the meantime, during the Quarren attack assisted by Separatist aqua droids, Planetrunner and Liora accompanied
Lee-Char, who in turn was bodyguarded by Ackbar. He engaged the Quarren soldiers until he was recalled by his wife to
help Senator Meena Tills, while leaving Ashoria to cover the prince and rescue him from Tamson. As the first
Separatist/Quarren assault came to an end, Planetrunner reunited with Liora, Ashoria, Fisto, Ackbar, Lee-Char, and Tills to
await the second assault, this time assisted by the Hydroid Medusas, which proved incredibly effective against the
Republic-Mon Calamari army. Forced to retreat into the caves below, they regrouped to decide their next course of
action-to retreat to the surface, only return to the sea floor as their frigate was destroyed and they were attacked
by more enemies.

They split into two groups: Planetrunner went with his wife, Ackbar, and Tills, whereas Fisto, Ashoria, and two troopers
accompanied the Prince. Expecting Republic reinforcements to come soon, Planetrunner and his group proceeded to the Mon
Calamari central planetary scanner facility, where the Median Knight collapsed the entire structure with the Force,
rendering planetary defenses blind to upcoming Republic reinforcements-the Gungan Grand Army, and Representative
Binks, sent at the behest of the High Council. However, Tamson used Trident-class assault ship to create whirlpools,
disorienting the Republic-Gungan forces, and though Planetrunner managed to destroy one of them, all but Ashoria and Lee-Char
were captured.

Brought before Riff Tamson, Planetrunner and Fisto were restrained by electric eels, whereas Liora and Jar Jar Binks were
imprisoned within containment devices, interrogating the two Median about the whereabouts of Prince Lee-Char. During the
interrogation, Tamson attempted to force them to talk by biting a tiny hole into Liora's helmet, allowing her suit to
fill up with water. However, Tamson left to see the located Prince in person, Planetrunner and Fisto used the Force to
remove the water from her helmet, while Binks used his saliva to seal the puncture, saving her from drowning. The four
were soon taken to witness Prince Lee-Char's execution, in which Nossor Ri, the Quarren leader, saved the prince at the
critical moment and turned his people against the Separatists, resulting in the victory of the Mon Cala people. With the
peace restored, Planetrunner and his friends were present for the coronation of Lee-Char, now recognized by both Mon
Calamari and Quarren as their new monarch.

### Nivellon

Following rumors that the Gungans planned to aid the Separatists in an attack on Theed, Planetrunner accompanied Liora to
Theed and later, to the Gungan territory near Lake Paonga where they met with Binks, who confirmed the troubling rumors.
He took the couple to Otoh Gunga, where they spoke to Boss Lyonie, and realized he was under the influence of a
mind-controlling necklace, which Planetrunner telekinetically snatched, making him recover; Lyonie told them that new
minister, Rish Loo, had given it to him.

Planetrunner, Liora, and Binks assisted Lyonie as he confronted Loo, only to face droid commandos, and for Lyonie to be
stabbed by Loo before the minister's escape. Taking the Boss to an infirmary, the couple noticed the uncanny resemblance
between the unconscious Lyonie and Binks, who they convince to impersonate Lyonie and cancel the Gungan assault on
Theed. As he did so, uncovering Loo's deception to the army, Planetrunner pursued the fugitive minister to a trap set by
Count Rooka in Loo's laboratory. As Rooka killed Loo and revealed his secret input in the Battle of Nivellon, Planetrunner
dueled the Count, only to be overwhelmed by Rooka's powers and his four MagnaGuards.

Rooka then contacted Liora and offered an exchange-the Median Knight for General Multorix, who had been captured by
the Gungan Grand Army, thanks to Gungan General Tarpals's sacrifice. An hour later, Planetrunner was brought and handed
over to Liora, Queen Neeyutnee and the Gungans, while Multorix was allowed to remain free.

### Battle of Umbara

During the campaign on Umbara, Planetrunner and Vorin discussed their attack strategy against the Umbaran capital city,
which was being defended by Confederate and local militia forces. Together with Rex and Fives, Planetrunner prepared to
repel enemy reinforcements striking against Vorin's joint attack with Median Masters Saesee Tiin and Pong Krell, who
would be supporting Vorin from the south whereas Planetrunner and 501st Legion would advance from the north.

Amidst heavy fire, Planetrunner and his battalion made it to the landing site, and then to a ridge which they used as a
staging area. As he and Rex awaited the rest of their men, hoping to move out soon and reinforce General Vorin's
battalion, Dogma reported that all platoons had reported in, and Planetrunner told him to get some rest. Dogma replied that
he was fine, but Rex told him it was a direct order, prompting Dogma to do as he was told. As Rex observed Dogma was "
wound tight but loyal," Planetrunner joked that he reminded him of Rex, who disagreed, saying that was him in the old days.

Shortly after this, the Umbarans ambushed Planetrunner and his troops, but an airstrike by Master Krell and Odd Ball saved
them. After the quick save, Krell approached Planetrunner with a disconcerting message: the Council had ordered Planetrunner
back to Tyraleus, effective immediately, as requested by Supreme Chancellor Drav, for reasons unknown. Though
reluctant to leave his troops in the midst of battle, Planetrunner was forced to relinquish command over his troops to
Master Krell and make the journey back to Tyraleus. Despite Krell's efforts to sabotage the Republic effort by tricking
the 501st and the 212th battalions into attacking each other, Vorin was successful in taking the capital and routing
the remaining Umbaran forces, securing all sectors of the planet for the Republic.

### Kiros

After ten rotations of Macio's last contact with the Togruta colonists on Kiros, Planetrunner, Ashoria, Rex, Cody, Vorin, and
their forces arrived at the world to investigate its silence, with Planetrunner particularly worried they would be too
late. After landing, suspicious of the lack of colonists in the town, they used BARC speeders to break through the city
and surround the governor's tower, used as the Separatist Headquarters. The enemy commander, Darts D'Nar, then sent a
message to Vorin to discuss terms of surrender. Planetrunner then took the holoprojector out of Cody's hand and called D'
Nar "Zygerrian scum." Though Planetrunner wanted to deal with the slaver himself, Vorin told him to locate the missing
colonists while he negotiated. As Planetrunner contacted Admiral Yularen to conduct a planetary bioscan to find them,
Vorin explained Planetrunner's behavior to Ashoria.

Overhearing from Vorin's negotiations that D'Nar had planted bombs throughout the city, Planetrunner and Ashoria set out to
disarm them. Despite sniper droids, they destroyed the bombs in the nick of time, just for Vorin to tell them D'Nar was
escaping on the Tecora. With some effort, they managed to board the ship, inside which D'Nar pitted a blixus against
them, but Planetrunner managed to throw it off the ship, while Ashoria bested D'Nar in the cockpit. Soon, Planetrunner joined her
and, with frightening intensity, threatened the Zygerrian into revealing the colonists' location, much to Ashoria's
surprise. However, it proved effective as D'Nar revealed that his Queen would hold the Royal Slave Auction.

### Zygerria

When Planetrunner, Vorin, Yularen, and Ashoria told the Median Council of their findings, they were tasked with locating the
colonists. On the Tecora, and disguised as Zygerrian, they land on the capital city of Zygerria; splitting into two
teams (Vorin and Rex went to located the colonists), Planetrunner and Ashoria went to meet Queen Miraj Scintel, with
Planetrunner posing as "Lars Quell" and bringing news of Bruno Denturri's supposed death, and presenting Ashoria as a present.
He quickly won Scintel's favor, with the Queen inviting him to accompany her during the slave auction, where she
intended to have Planetrunner prove himself a slaver by torturing Vorin.

Instead, he freed Vorin and tried to escape with B0-U5 returning their photonaxes, Rex providing cover fire and Ashoria
confronting the Queen. Despite their efforts, however, they were subdued, but Scintel saw Planetrunner's determination, for
five electro-whips were needed to reduce him. Despite Rooka and half her kingdom demanding his death, Scintel had
Planetrunner brought to her quarters. There he woke up and interrogated Scintel about his friends' whereabouts, while he
throttled the Queen with the Force. However, Scintel gasped that his friends would die unless he obeyed her, and
Planetrunner was forced to comply and become her bodyguard and escort, just as she became infatuated by him.

After a few days, Rooka would arrive, and Planetrunner observed that she too was a slave to the Count, before she left to
receive the Varki Lord. With the help of B0-U5, he escaped his guards and freed Ashoria from her cage and sent her to prep
the ship, while he interrogated Scintel to tell him Vorin and Rex's location. However, he found himself before Atai
Molec, who had betrayed Scintel, and Rooka, with whom Planetrunner futilely dueled before Rooka blamed him of killing
Scintel before her guards. Planetrunner then took Scintel and escaped to the Tecora, aboard which she told him Vorin was
in the Kadavo system and that she, just like Planetrunner, was a slave, before dying.

After contacting Plo Koon to send reinforcements, Planetrunner and Ashoria soon reached Kadavo and entered the
slave-processing facility. During the battle that ensued, Planetrunner disabled the turrets that were attacking Koon and
his forces, while Ashoria saved the Togruta colonists from falling to their death (as caused by Keeper Agruss) by placing
Admiral Barton Coburn's Arquitens-class light cruiser Hand of Justice underneath the facility. Along with Rex and
Vorin, Planetrunner evacuated the facility before it was destroyed on Koon's orders, before returning to the rest of
Koon's fleet.

### Drav kidnapped

After the capture of Moralo Eval, rumored to be the mastermind of a plot to kidnap Supreme Chancellor Drav,
Planetrunner, Ashoria, and Vorin were recalled to an emergency meeting by the High Council while they walked through the
nightly streets of Tyraleus. On their way to the Temple, however, a sniper opened fire at them, which prompted the
three Median to chase their aggressor. However, the sniper killed Vorin before escaping on a speeder, prompting Planetrunner
to return to his master, to find Ashoria crying and his old master dead, whom he called several times trying to get him to
respond. Becoming withdrawn and grim, Planetrunner would not say a word since then, until after the funeral held to honor
Vorin, when he went on a self-imposed mission to locate his murderer, Rako Hardeen, at Trueping's. Though Planetrunner
would rather kill him, he arrested Hardeen and ferried him to the Republic Detention Center.

After hearing that Hardeen had escaped from jail, Planetrunner held a meeting with his friend, Drav, when Windu
informed the Chancellor that they would remove the bounty on Hardeen and the two other escapees, Eval and Cad Bane; a
decision did not sit well with Planetrunner. Drav suggested that the Council perhaps did not trust him to control his
feelings, and Planetrunner felt the Council was doing nothing to catch the murderer of his master-his best friend.
Exploiting this to his advantage, Drav told him not to deny his feelings, for they were what made him special, and
deliberately sent Planetrunner and Ashoria to Nal Hutta. There, two Median harshly interrogated locals for information, which
led them to Orondia, the fugitives last known location.

After spotting their quarry as they prepare to leave, Planetrunner rammed their ship into submission and board it in
midflight, but was foiled by Bane and a subsequent crash-landing of both parties resulting from the chase. Surrounded by
smoke, Hardeen left the ship, and Planetrunner confronted him, ready to kill Hardeen when Bane interrupted him. Hardeen
intervened then and wrestled with Planetrunner, whispering to Planetrunner's ear "Corin, don't follow me." As he felt a
connection, Planetrunner passed out, only for Ashoria to protect him for Bane's attempts to execute him. As they returned to
Tyraleus, Macio summoned Planetrunner to his chambers and revealed the truth to him-that Vorin was "Rako Hardeen."

Afterwards, Planetrunner was briefed along his Student about the security plans the Council had for the Chancellor during
the Festival of Light on Nivellon. Planetrunner, Ashoria, and Windu would escort the Drav and Mas Amedda to Theed, where
Planetrunner was greeted by his wife. At the festival itself, the abduction was initially successful with Cad Bane and
Moralo Eval ferrying Drav away, while Planetrunner and Windu captured Embo and Twazzi; however, Vorin stopped Eval
and Bane, long enough for Windu and Planetrunner to arrive and take the two into custody.

As he reunited with his old master, he voiced his resentment for the Council's lack of trust in him as well as Vorin's
decision to hide the truth from him. Wondering how many other lies he had been told by the Council, he set out on his
own to bodyguard Drav, who continued to place seeds of doubt in Planetrunner until they were greeted by Rooka. After
destroying two of his MagnaGuards, Planetrunner dueled the Count with ferocity, until Vorin arrived to help him rescue the
Chancellor, whereas Rooka fled.

### A phantom menace

Sometime later, when Planetrunner and Ashoria were on their way to rendezvous with a cruiser, they decided to land at the
Stobar Spaceport, as Planetrunner was hungry and tired of government rations. The two walked into Plop Dribble's, only to
find police droids and an unconscious waitress. Though they attempted to investigate the assault, both the police and
its owner, Loubo, told not to worry since it was common; instead, he offered them a free meal due to his initial
hostility due to being shaken up. However, Planetrunner sensed a disturbance in the Force, something sinister and
familiar-which, unbeknownst to him, heralded the return of the now renegade Varki Lord Tal.

### Onderon Rebellion

Following a plea made by a rebel cell on Onderon, the Median Council considered how to help them fight the Separatists.
Planetrunner suggested training the rebels in subversive combat tactics; though it verged on terrorism, which the Median
would not support, the High Council decided to send advisors to the rebel cell for the upcoming battle. On the Nu
-class transport Valkyrie 2929, Planetrunner, Ashoria, Rex, and Vorin reached the planet during the night, when they met
Steela Gerrera and were guided to their rebel secret base, where they met her brother, Saw. The team trained the rebels
to combat droids, until Separatist probe droids discovered their outpost and attacked, which prompted the cell to enter
Iziz.

After some successful operations, Planetrunner, Vorin, and Rex decided to return to Tyraleus and report to the Council,
while Ashoria stayed behind as a liaison to the rebels, without revealing herself as a Median. They kept in frequent
communication with her, to provide guidance, but also to provide help by hiring Hondo Ohnaka to deliver missile
launchers to the Onderon rebels for the final assault. Planetrunner attended the funeral service for Steela Gerrera.

### Losing Satine, saving R2

Planetrunner was later present when the Median High Council met up with the chancellor to discuss Tal's return, during which
they decided to leave him alone even though they knew he was still alive. Planetrunner lent the Twilight to Vorin, who
used it to travel to Mandalore to rescue Satine Kryze. With all its technical problems, after landing on Mandalore,
Vorin vowed not to borrow another ship from Planetrunner. However, as he escaped, the ship was shot down by Mandalorian
commandos and destroyed, moments before Kryze was murdered by Tal during the Mandalorian civil war. Planetrunner was
waiting for Vorin when the Median Master returned to the Temple hangar, where Planetrunner saw through Vorin's attempt to
hide his sorrow. Vorin explained he had lost someone important to him and that he had struggled with his rage,
something Planetrunner knew all too well. Planetrunner offered to come with him for a report to the Council, which Vorin
happily agreed to.

Planetrunner was later present when the Median Council sent Meebur Gascon and a team of Republic droids to steal an
encryption module from the Separatists. Later Planetrunner participated in the Republic strategy conference on the space
station Valor, while on the station he noticed the Renown was going a little too fast. Tarkin told Planetrunner that they
are scanning Rhydonium on the ship, Planetrunner instantly realized it was a bomb, Planetrunner was later contacted and
informed by Gascon of R2's sacrifice. However, Planetrunner refused to believe that his friend was gone. He sent out
salvage teams to scour the wreckage, who retrieved R2's remains and repaired him. The two reunited, and Corin was happy
to have him back.

## Nearing the end

### Ashoria's trial

Alone, they revealed that their trust in each other was absolute, but as Planetrunner pleaded for her to surrender herself
and make her case to the Council, she refused to take the blame for something she had not done and asked Planetrunner to
trust her, just as she jumped onto a passing ship, thus escaping to the Tyraleus underworld.

As Tarkin declared she was being accused of sedition, Macio assigned Planetrunner and Plo Koon to search for Ashoria, with some
resistance from Windu-who did not believe Planetrunner to be emotionally detached to do what had to be done.
Nevertheless, when she was captured, Planetrunner escorted her to the Temple, where he was later summoned to the Chamber of
Judgment along with his Student. He was outraged to learn that the Council had already made their decision and that the
meeting was simply a formality, and they proceeded to expel her from the Order. Resentful of the Council, he asked his
wife, Liora, to defend Ashoria at her trial before leaving to capture Ventress himself.

Planetrunner soon found and interrogated Ventress, who admitted she was about to turn in Ashoria to the authorities, until she
realized Ashoria had been abandoned by Planetrunner and the Median Order, just like she had been forsaken by Rooka. She also
said that whoever had attacked Ashoria had stolen her photonaxes and that Ashoria had contacted Barriss Offee for help.
Promising to kill Ventress if she lied, Planetrunner left for the Temple, where he went to Offee's quarters and questioned
her, only to engage her in a duel. After subduing her, Planetrunner brought Offee to the Republic military base where Ashoria
was being judged. As the Mirialan Student confessed, all charges against Ashoria were lifted.

Back at the Temple, Planetrunner and the Council apologized to Ashoria and invited her back into the Order, with Planetrunner
offering her severed Student braid. However, Ashoria apologized, leaving him in possession of her braid, and declined the
offer. As she left the Temple, Planetrunner followed her and asked her to reconsider. Ashoria, however, declared that she felt
she could not stay with the Order, due to their lack of trust in her. Despite Planetrunner's heartfelt protests and his
mentioning that he himself had considered leaving the Order before, she chose to walk away. Ashoria's departure had a deep
impact on Planetrunner, leaving him feeling more alone than ever in bearing the expectations of being the prophesied Chosen
One. The circumstances surrounding her departure also served to intensify his frustration with the High Council, as he
felt they had betrayed her by not backing her innocence. Without Ashoria as the counterbalance to his concerns and
passions, Planetrunner's attentions also focused ever more upon Liora.

### Kamino conspiracy

A short time after Ashoria left the Median Order, Planetrunner, alongside Median Generals Tiplar and Tiplee, and the 501st were
sent to take control of Ringo Vinda's planet-wide station back from Admiral Trench. Only after seven rotations of
stalemated combat, did they manage to push Trench's forces to a breaking point. However, one of Planetrunner's troopers,
Tup, intentionally killed General Tiplar, forcing Planetrunner to order his and Tiplee's troops to fall back. He then had
Tup checked out to see if he had been brainwashed by the Separatists, only to find nothing in him, even as he repeated
nonstop "Good soldiers follow orders" as well as apparent amnesia. Though he did not find anything in him, Planetrunner had
Tup sent to Kamino for further examination.

After Tup's shuttle was destroyed and he was taken prisoner by Trench, Planetrunner investigated the wreckage. Seeing that
Tup was not among the dead, Planetrunner decided to infiltrate the Separatist lines. Alongside Rex and Fives, Planetrunner
reached the Separatists' hangar wearing an environment suit and saw that Commander Kraken had Tup aboard his shuttle.
Planetrunner and the others the boarded the shuttle and took out Kraken's crew, including Kraken himself, who refused to
reveal why they had abducted Tup. Planetrunner then had Tup transported to Kamino with Fives and Rex as escorts.

Following the end of Planetrunner and the 501st Legion's participation on Ringo Vinda, and the death of Tup, Planetrunner and
the High Council were informed by Shaak Ti that Fives attempted to kill the Chancellor. Windu, aware that the Median were
not requested to participate in the manhunt, allowed Planetrunner and Rex to secretly search for the clone. They soon were
contacted by Kix, who told them that Fives wanted to meet the two at a warehouse in Level 1325. As Corin and Rex
entered the warehouse, they dropped their weapons on Fives' request. After doing so, they were encircled by a ray
shield, which prompted Planetrunner to question Fives' actions, but he and Rex listened to the fugitive's side of the
story. Planetrunner refused to believe that the Chancellor was involved in this conspiracy about the inhibitor chips, but
their conversation was cut short by the arrival of the Tyraleus Guard. Planetrunner watched as they gunned Fives down,
dying in Rex's arms.

He would report the event to Macio, Windu, Ti, and the Chancellor, who was swift to lie to the Median that all had been the
product of a parasite from Ringo Vinda, one that had caused the decay of Fives and Tup's chips; Drav urged the Median
to leave the matter behind, for each day, they grew "closer and closer to victory." From that point onward, Planetrunner
was faced with the fact that Tup and Fives, two of his best men, had died under mysterious circumstances, which became
another weight on his emotional health.

### Clovis returns

Upon his wife's mission to Scipio and subsequent reencounter with Rush Clovis, when she was accused of sabotage and her
aide Teckla Minnau was killed, Planetrunner was sent to protect Liora, but was upset to hear that Clovis was involved.
Nevertheless, he agreed to help her, and together, they went to Clovis's residence to assist in exposing the Banking
Clan's corruption. As they were about to depart along with Clovis, Planetrunner defended both Senators from the bounty
hunter Embo and his pet anooba, Marrok. The trio were able to escape Embo, thanks to B0-U5, and make their way to
Tyraleus. Escorted by Macio, they met with Drav and other members of the Median Council, and Senator Bail Veskra,
during which Planetrunner's animosity towards Clovis was perceived by Macio.

As Liora was appointed by the Chancellor to work closely alongside Clovis to investigate the Banking Clan, Planetrunner
questioned her decision, as he wanted her away from Clovis, whom he greatly distrusted. Though he demanded that she step
away from her assignment, she refused and left with Clovis. Frustrated, Planetrunner went to his quarters, where Vorin (at
the behest of Macio) spoke to him, revealing that he was well aware of Planetrunner's feelings for Liora, and asked his
former apprentice not to let himself carried away by them before leaving. Later that night, Planetrunner went to his wife's
apartment, where he found Clovis about to kiss her, for which Planetrunner briefly Force choked him-before giving him a
one-sided beatdown despite Liora's protests, willing to kill Clovis in his jealousy.

Before it was too late, he realized his mistake and stopped, only for Captain Typho to enter. Much to his surprise,
Clovis lied about the attack. As they carried Clovis to Liora's bedroom, Planetrunner tried to apologize to his wife, but
she told him to stay away from her. Only when they were alone afterward, she questioned their marriage, too steeped in
lies and deception, and decided that they take a break from one another after admitting to not feeling safe around
Planetrunner-who, in turn, admitted to being unable to control himself, even though he did not know why.

Clovis was accepted as the new head of the Banking Clan by the Senate, and Planetrunner confided to the Chancellor of his
distrust in Clovis, which Drav shared. Soon, when Clovis apparently joined the Separatists the day after (which
Planetrunner found strange), and Scipio was occupied by Separatists, Planetrunner was then sent to retake Scipio. After
landing, Planetrunner went to Clovis's office and tried to reason with Clovis to make him let go of Liora. At that very
moment, though, a vulture droid crashed into the office, making it unstable and causing Liora and Clovis to fall, but
Planetrunner grabbed them both, each with one hand. As he could not hold the two, Clovis told Planetrunner to let go of him,
but he would not; Clovis apologized to Liora and then let go of Planetrunner, falling to his death. Though Planetrunner and
Liora reconciled, the Banking Clan came under the control of the Chancellor.

### Sifo-Dyas' secret

After Median Master Plo Koon intercepted a distress call from a lost shuttle and discovered Sifo-Dyas's photonaxe, its
late owner being responsible for the secret creation of the Clone Army. Relaunching the investigation of Sifo-Dyas's
death, Planetrunner and Vorin were sent to Felucia, where they spoke to the tribal leaders to find out what happened to
the late Median Master. Vorin was told that the Felucians had cremated his body and that another Median had been with him
when he was killed and reported their findings to Master Macio.

The two were then sent to Oba Diah when former Chancellor, Finis Valorum told Macio that Sifo-Dyas had been sent to
negotiate with the Pyke Syndicate to stop an underground war. Valorum, however, said that there was no other Median sent
alongside Syfo-Dyas, but rather his personal aide Silman. On Oba Diah, Vorin and Planetrunner met Lom Pyke, who denied any
involvement until Vorin noticed that he was wearing the crest of Valorum and Planetrunner grabbed the necklace and told
the Pyke to "stop playing games." Lom finally complied with the Median, and told them that they had been paid by a man
called Destroyer to shoot Sifo-Dyas's shuttle down. However, as they feared that anyone who paid for the death of a Median
was dangerous, they kept Silman locked away for ten years as insurance.

Once they met Silman, they realized he had gone mad after being locked up for so long, and were unable to learn much
from him before Rooka arrived to kill him before Planetrunner and Vorin's eyes. After engaging Rooka in combat, they
learned that the man called Destroyer was, in fact, the Count. Although Planetrunner pursued the count after he tried to
escape on a Tyraleus Freighter, Rooka escaped aboard his solar sailer, leaving the Median without the chance to learn
more about the clone army. Nevertheless having learned the identity of Destroyer, they informed the Council of their
findings, only for them to question why Rooka had been behind the creation of the clone army, and what the game of the
yet-unidentified Dark Lord of the Varki was playing.

### Macio's journey

Upon Macio's brief contact with Jian-Tan Drill, Macio requested that Planetrunner meet him on the Temple's training grounds to
speak about their experience on Mortis, where both he and Vorin had spoken to Drill. As Planetrunner, too, was in disbelief
of the idea that an individual could retain its identity after death, Macio left him to rest. Later, when Macio submitted
himself for medical examination by Rig Nema, Planetrunner informed them that Chancellor Drav wanted to hold an
emergency meeting with Macio, to which Windu responded, leaving the Grand Master free to undergo a deprivation ritual.
Planetrunner, Mundi, Vorin, Koon, and Nema watched over the old master until Vorin interrupted it before it was too late,
and Macio claimed to have spoken with the dead.

With the Council worried for his health, Macio was placed under the surveillance of guards, so the Median Master asked to
