Planetrunner to see him. Macio asked Planetrunner to help him escape, which Planetrunner did. Accompanying Macio to his fighter,
Planetrunner even lent B0-U5 to Macio to accompany him on a journey that would take him to Dagobah, a mysterious planet and
Moraband, to learn that the Median Order would not win the war, and that there was "another Planetrunner."

### An Excuse to Fight

After a skirmish against Tofen's Raiders, in which Vorin's spacebattler malfunctioned, a Republic fleet was attacked by
Separatists. Planetrunner and Vorin were present alongside the young Tanookai Viiveenn during the attack. They both argued
about who should be the one to join the fight and who should be the one to deliver Viiveenn to safety. When a missile
that entered the hangar bay exploded near the three, Planetrunner and Vorin were separated, with Vorin left with
Viiveenn. Planetrunner used the wreckage that landed in his way as an excuse to join the fight. As another explosive
entered the hangar, Vorin reluctantly took the Tanookai into his starship and told her that Planetrunner did that sort of
thing all the time.

### Mission to Batuu

#### Alliance with a Chiss "commander"

Planetrunner was told by Senator Liora that one of her former handmaidens, Duja, had found something near Batuu that she
and Planetrunner should investigate. Unfortunately, Planetrunner was unable to join her due to being sent to battle. Planetrunner
allowed her to travel to Batuu by herself. Upon his return to Tyraleus after the battle, Planetrunner could find records
of Liora's travels in the Outer Rim. After another battle, Planetrunner received a message that Liora's ship was found
on Batuu. Planetrunner, along with B0-U5, took his interceptor to Batuu. En route to Batuu, Planetrunner encountered a
freighter. Planetrunner spoke with the freighter's captain, Chiss Defense Fleet Commander Mitth'raw'nuruodo, known simply
as Thrawn. Unknown to Planetrunner, Thrawn was actually a Senior Captain. Planetrunner accepted Thrawn's assistance in finding
Liora and Duja.

Planetrunner found Liora's ship near Batuu's Black Spire Outpost. There, he stopped a group of smugglers who were angry
about the ship being in their landing spot. Planetrunner fought them until Thrawn broke up the fight. Together, they
investigated Liora's ship and learned about Duja's ship, Nomad Four. The two then went to a nearby cantina. After
speaking with the bartender, Planetrunner and Thrawn came under attack by four assailants. The two of them were able to
kill the assailants. Thrawn suspected the assailants were sent to kill Planetrunner and that there was the fifth nearby.
Planetrunner and Thrawn came up with a plan to capture the last assailant. After Planetrunner took one of the assailant's
body, he pretended to suffer engine damage in his interceptor. After landing, Planetrunner came under attack by an assassin
droid but was to destroy it. Thrawn was able to capture the assailant and found his freighter, which belonged to the
Separatists.

#### Mission to Mokivj

Planetrunner and Thrawn took out the droids guarding the freighter. Together, they found out the freighter was headed to
Cermau. As they returned to Black Spire, they came under attack by several thugs. Thrawn was able to use their speeder,
to capture the thugs. Planetrunner and Thrawn questioned the cargo inspector Oenti, who reveals that the cantina's
bartender, Janott had ties to the Separatists' Duke Solha. They learned that they were shipping supplies to a droid
factory. After learning of Duja's death, Planetrunner told Thrawn about the politics behind the Clone Wars. Planetrunner and
Thrawn traveled to Mokivj. There, they discovered that the Separatists were mining Cortosis and discovered a factory.

Following Planetrunner's and Thrawn's location of the factory, and later their change of clothing, Planetrunner contacted the
duke, to infiltrate the factory and informed him that Captain Boroklif was indisposed, that there was trouble at Black
Spire, and that the he and the others were losing. The Serennian was shocked when he heard this news and asked if the
Separatist captain and his companions were dead, to which Planetrunner replied that he did not know as he was not there at
the end of the battle.<ref name="Thrawn: Alliances />

The Median Knight offered the Separatist to bring the cargo he had lost to his factory, Solha accepted and told him he'd
open the shield when he was on the coordinates of the courtyard, that he was not stupid and he would not open it until
it was truly necessary, just when he was in position to land. Following their arrival, the Median Knight and the Chiss
commander were hailed by the Serennian duke escorted by a pair of B2-series super battle droids and two squads of
B1-series battle droids, who inquired their possession of an astromech droid that belonged to the Republic, B0-U5. In
response, the Median explained that he had found the droid and believed it could be worth something if he desired to
purchase it.

The Chiss commander and the Median Knight asked the Serennian what happened to Liora's former handmaiden, Duja. They
also told him how they acquired Boroklif's ship, the Larkrer, that they came to Mokivj because there was a preset
hyperspace course on the ship, the Serennian asked who had put in that course, to which they replied they assumed the
Separatist captain did. The duke then warned the pair that they did not have anything else to bargain with and that he
could have them shot. However, the pair told them there was another preset hyperspace course locked below the current
one, which was locked by a two-stage encryption passcode, and that each of them had one half, Planetrunner then presented
his Chiss companion as "Brix." The Serennian ordered all of his droids to lower their weapons and to escort them while
they entered the factory. The lights went off while the group was entering the building, and the Median sliced a droid
squad and threw his photonaxe to the top of the building so the duke would not be aware that Planetrunner was in fact, a
Median. Then two B2s blocked the courtyard's opening to prevent any escape.

Solha knew that there was a Median loose on the factory, however, he didn't know who Planetrunner was, he then sent Thrawn
and Planetrunner to some improvised prison cells. Calling the Median a thief, the Serennian aimed at Planetrunner from the
corridor in front of his cell with his blaster, and said that the Median wanted to be here and that he got here thanks to
Planetrunner, and for that alone he should be shot. He then revealed he was the Duke Solha of the Free System of Serenno,
to which the Median Knight replied if he should be impressed, Solha said he should be, and that he would be at some point.
One B2-series super battle droid took all of their weapons and communication devices, even taking Thrawn's small
hold-out blaster located in his boot. Solha and the droids left with R2, who was dropping oil so Planetrunner knew where
they had taken him. They left the room and locked the cell's doors.

The pair agreed on running a test, which would discover if Planetrunner's wife had been captured, if she was free or was
not on the factory by waiting two hours as Liora, and if she did not join them on the detention block, they would
break out and try to locate her. Thrawn asked the Median that if he recognized the ship in the courtyard, telling him it
was an ore carrier, which was full of ore, so this was not a staging ground but a manufacturing facility, he also told
Planetrunner where was there more activity and where was there less activity, as Chiss could see more infrared than humans,
and he noticed the heat signatures, and that where they were in was the most active section.

Following the completion of Thrawn's and Planetrunner's test, the Chiss crafted a cord from the clothing he got from the
Larkrer and unlocked their cells from the inside. Meanwhile, the senator had entered the building and was accompanied
by a group of locals, consisting of maintenance workers of the factory, Cimy, Huga, and LebJau. They had entered the
factory through the service level, which was usually unprotected and only them and the Separatists knew of. Liora had
promised the group a fortune, which would be given to them by her Uncle Corin if they helped her access the factory.
The group later arrived at the detention block, defeated the droid guards and found the Chiss and Median Knight inside.

After the Chiss was presented to the newcomers by Planetrunner, the group created a plan to retrieve Planetrunner's
photonaxe, which involved Thrawn and the senator going alone to the roof to retrieve the photonaxe. The Median was
scared of her going alone with the Chiss, but accepted it. After the Chiss and the senator left, the Median began to
wander across the factory, and found a section of the factory that produced cortosis B2 super battle droids, which was
guarded by the duke and his relatives and some droid sentries. The Serennians were protecting themselves with clone
trooper armor covered with cortosis, Planetrunner tried to confuse Solha's droids but he only achieved making the
Serennians aware of his presence. Planetrunner then left the room and began his search for the senator once again.

On the roof of the building, Liora and Thrawn retrieved Planetrunner's photonaxe, they also witnessed some spheres which
descended onto the factory, which were part of a Chiss mission to retrieve a deflector shield generator from the
factory. The senator asked the Chiss commander to continue helping them but he insisted that his mission came first.
Meanwhile, the Median, disarmed, used the Force to see where Solha and his droids sentries were, so he did not have to
fight them, while he traveled across the maze of rooms, and corridors that the factory contained. Until he met with his
wife who gave him his photonaxe, and told him that Thrawn had abandoned them. Their meeting also coincided with the
Chiss Ascendancy's raid on the factory, retrieving the shield generator. Planetrunner fought several B2s and discovered
that their armor disabled photonaxes and deflected blaster bolts. However, he used the Force and disabled them.

In the meantime, Liora evacuated the workers with LebJau before the factory was destroyed, Thrawn joined the senator
and the Median Knight who revealed that the ore was cortosis and that it deflected blaster bolts and disabled photonaxes,
thanks to its large energy absorption rate. They learned that the ore was mined in the river next to the factory and
strengthened the battle droids' armor making them invulnerable, something that could change the Clone Wars forever.
Thrawn then agreed to destroy the factory after the Chiss retrieved the shield generator.

Liora encountered the duke, who wore clone trooper armor covered with cortosis, who protected him from his husband's
photonaxe, he then told her that by using the factory he was going to build his name in the Confederacy. As he knew
Planetrunner and the senator, he rejected Liora's ultimatum to surrender and told her that he had no doubts that he'd
live and that he'd never surrender.

In another section of the factory, the Median and Chiss learned the Separatists were are also producing clone trooper
armor covered with cortosis. The Median thought they were planning to infiltrate the Republic by sending Serennian
troopers wearing clone trooper armor to Tyraleus. After the battle droids protecting the room were defeated by
Planetrunner and Thrawn, and the Serennian duke by the senator, knocking him out with her grappling hook, they left the
factory and then destroyed the factory. Planetrunner decided to destroy the mine too, so the Separatists could not start
again on Mokivj, though, Liora, Thrawn, and LebJau asked him not to do it, he ignored their petition, and he destroyed
the mine too, which gained him the anger and devastation of the already devastated Mokivj, as it caused a massive
explosion expanded by the cortosis.

#### Aftermath of Mokivj

The mission ended with a catastrophe for Mokivj and an end to Solha's career. In an effort to collapse the Separatist's
efforts to produce cortosis battle droids, Planetrunner accidentally sent lava, ash, and smoke into the planet's best
cropland and water. Planetrunner did not know the cortosis in the mine would redirect the heat of the explosions, the heat
was sent down the planet's crust, activating volcanic activity and leading to widespread devastation, deforestation, and
desertification on Mokivj, resulting in the explosive force doing more than merely collapsing the mine's tunnels.

The catastrophe forced LebJau to move to another planet as the population knew he had collaborated with the ones who
devastated Mokivj. Thrawn had warned Liora that Planetrunner's plan seemed reckless, yet she had known that he would be
unable to be talked out of it, leaving the Median and Senator to regret their actions as they looked upon the ruined
world. Thrawn had also warned Planetrunner that his theory about the clone armor being used to infiltrate the Republic
seemed unlikely based on how great the risk of discovery would be. Despite Planetrunner's shortsighted plan, Thrawn
continued to respect the man and still viewed him as an effective warrior.

### Bombing of the Temple

Planetrunner and B0-U5 were in the Median Temple prior to it being bombed by Separatist captain Rackham Sear. The bomber was
foiled by Depa Billaba and Meron Tyrax.

### Liora's departure

Prior to a mission that Liora was taking to Clabron, Planetrunner insisted that he be allowed to assist Liora, under
the impression it was a diplomatic mission to Duro. After assurance from Liora, Planetrunner agreed to remain on
Tyraleus, kissing Liora. He was startled when he realized Liora's handmaiden, Motee, had witnessed their display of
affection, though Liora assured Planetrunner that Motee understood discretion. Liora lied to Planetrunner about her
mission because of his close ties to Chancellor Drav.

### Crystal crisis on Utapau

During the last months of the war, Vorin and Planetrunner were sent to Utapau to investigate the mysterious death of Median
Master Tu-Anh. Once they landed on Pau City, Inspector Jen June led them to see the corpse at the morgue. After
examining the body, they went to the place where she had been found, only to determine she had been hit in the optic
nerve with a precision laser dart by a sniper. As they found the sniper's position, from the building's owner, Garri,
the two Median learned of the involvement of MagnaGuards and began to suspect the involvement of General Multorix, and had
Inspector June analyze some slimy substance they had found-the secretion of an Amani's skin.

Though Governor Torul Blom asked them to leave Utapau, Vorin and Planetrunner persevered and rented two dactillions to go
talk to the leader of an Amani tribe, who revealed that an Amani outcast had entered one of the caves. The two Median
entered it to find MagnaGuards. Despite some resistance, they managed to have the droids reveal the involvement of the
Sugi and went to see Inspector June once again. Soon after, the two attended the funeral for Tu-Anh.

As they reached the Amani settlement they had been looking for, the Amani scattered, leaving Planetrunner and Vorin to
follow the tracks of one that appeared to be their leader. During the hunt, Planetrunner mentioned Ashoria for the first time
since her departure, and Vorin asked if he wanted to talk about it, yet Planetrunner refused. Vorin then suggested for
them to set up a camp and rest. However, he insisted on the subject, prompting Planetrunner to tell Vorin he missed Ashoria
and to voice his anger at the High Council for turning its back on her. To Planetrunner's annoyance, Vorin stood by the
Council's authority, asserting that it had been Ashoria's decision to leave and that she had allowed her emotions to cloud
her judgment, something against the Median way. Then, Vorin suggested he rest, but Planetrunner declined so that he could
keep the first watch. Finally, he questioned Vorin on what would happen if he had turned out to be a "major
disappointment," but Vorin wanted to believe it would never happen.

However, they both fell asleep and were captured by a group of Sugis led by Chong, who brought them before Endente as
Vorin told Chong of their "intention" to buy weapons. They learned Endente was, in fact, selling a kyber crystal, and
Planetrunner prompted him to show it before they made the deal. Brought to the starship where the crystal was being kept,
they escaped from their captors, and Planetrunner eliminated all the Sugi, except for Endente, who fled. After they
discovered the massive kyber crystal inside the ship, the two Median managed to transport the crystal through Utapau's
plains until they reached Pau City, where Blom had the two Median surrounded with his men and Multorix's droids. As the
kyber crystal was loaded into a shuttle and sent to a ship on orbit, Vorin and Planetrunner stole a freighter to recover
the crystal.

During the persecution, Multorix damaged their ship, forcing them to perform a number five special; they crashed it to
disable the hyperdrive and, with their escape pods, boarded the ship where the crystal was then held. As they got
separated, Vorin was captured by Multorix, and Planetrunner recovered his photonaxe, located the crystal, and freed
Vorin. Together, they made their way to the kyber crystal at the vault, where they were temporarily trapped until a
squad discovered them. Using the crystal and the Force to knock them out, he managed to get to a hangar, where Planetrunner
stole a shuttle to escape. Meanwhile, Vorin set several AATs to shoot and overload the crystal, destroying the crystal
and the ship, while they escaped from the explosion in the nick of time and returned to Tyraleus to report to the
Council.

### Stationed on Tyraleus

Sometime later, while on a Venator-class Space Eater, Planetrunner discovered an unknown ship, the Silver Angel, in
military airspace. Planetrunner then asked Admiral Yularen who was on that transport. After he closed his eyes and sensed
Seren Ashoria's presence through the Force, he decided not to send a detachment to arrest the crew and to let Seren and
her companions leave.

### Vos and Ventress

Median Master Quinlan Vos had been tasked by the Median Council to assassinate Rooka with the help of Asajj Ventress, but
during a mission to Raxus Secundus the Median turned to the dark side due to Rooka's manipulations and Ventress's
training. Ventress staged a rescue mission, which failed and prompted her to contact the Median Council. When she arrived
at the Median Temple, Planetrunner and Vorin escorted her to the Council Chamber, where despite Mace Windu's open
disapproval, Macio dispatched Planetrunner and Vorin to go with Ventress to rescue Vos above Taris. Soon enough, Vorin,
Planetrunner, and Ventress were on the cockpit of her ship, the Banshee, to infiltrate the Separatist dreadnought from
which Vos, or rather "Admiral Enigma," was issuing orders.

Stealthily, the three boarded the ship and made their way to the bridge, where they found Rooka, instead of Vos.
Planetrunner then engaged in a duel with the Count, distracting him while Vorin and Ventress discovered a captive Vos.
Though she knew Vos was consumed by his hatred, they escaped to the Banshee, and Planetrunner joined with them to escape
the enemy ship and return to Tyraleus. Back in the Median Temple, Planetrunner saw as the Council welcomed Vos and pardoned
Ventress. That same night, Planetrunner reunited with his wife, Liora, for a moment of respite, during which Planetrunner
told her of the ordeal-after which, Liora conferred that perhaps Ventress's love could be Vos's way back from the
dark side, leaving Planetrunner at a loss for words.

A month later, Planetrunner was sent alongside Vorin, Vos, and Akar-Deshu in a mission to take over a Separatist supply
storage base and redistribute the supplies to worlds in need of them. However, their mission went awry when Vos,
unbeknownst to them, arranged the base's destruction. After another failed mission to Vos's name, he was suspected of
treason, Planetrunner and Vorin were sent to spy on Vos and Ventress as they were deployed to assassinate Rooka during the
second battle of Christophsis. When they saw Vos attempt to force the Count to lead him to his master, Evilth Schemious,
rather than kill him, Planetrunner and Vorin intervened, taking the pair by surprise and arresting them.

However, Vos and Rooka soon escaped from the Vigilance, causing the death of Akar-Deshu and Kav Bayons, and boarded
Ventress' ship, Banshee to escape Christophsis. Planetrunner had the Banshee fired on, forcing the renegades to land on
the planet below. He and Vorin pursued the three injured fugitives to a Separatist-controlled tower, where they
surrounded them. There, Planetrunner and Vorin witnessed what appeared to be Ventress' last moments, sacrificing herself
to save Vos from Rooka's fatal Force lightning. After her death, Planetrunner and Vorin were joined by the redeemed Vos,
and they tried to capture Rooka, to no avail. They then transported Ventress' body and Vos to Tyraleus, where the
fallen Median confessed his crimes and Vorin defended Ventress.

### A New Droid Army

After confiscating a Munificent-class star frigate with Squad 326, Planetrunner was joined by Grand Master Macio and
informed about the mysterious Separatist project, Operation: Titan. Hacking into the frigate's datacore, they were able
to discover that Operation: Titan was being overseen on the planet Enthenium. Together, Macio and Planetrunner traveled to a
Separatist base on Enthenium to uncover more information about the supposed "weapon" that was being developed under
Project: Titan. Once they snuck onto the base, Macio climbed through the vents, found information on the "weapons", and
confronted Multorix, who was stationed on the base. Meanwhile, Planetrunner and Squad 326 were battling battle droids as
the base went on alert. After Macio came back and aided in the fight, the team escaped before reinforcements arrived. On
the frigate once again, Planetrunner was informed by Macio that on Golatha the weapons being developed were a new army of
megadroids four times taller than a human. Planetrunner quipped that they should have expected the Separatists to
eventually make their droids bigger.

Planetrunner and Macio then informed the Median High Council via hologram about their planned mission to Golatha. Planetrunner
believed that, because the planet was small, the forces guarding the droid factory would also be small. Macio warned
against being overconfident, and suggested being more cautious. Master Windu agreed with Macio and wished them luck,
ending the transmission. Planetrunner was offended by the idea that his plan was overconfident, doing an impression of what
Macio had said to mock him. Clone Captain Cesar interrupted their brief argument and informed them that they had arrived.
On the planet's surface, Macio and Planetrunner surveyed the valley where the factory was, but found no above-surface
structure. They determined that the factory was fully underground and that an access point must be in the valley. Macio
and Planetrunner, along with Company 326 descended into the valley, and found no droid guards. However, blaster fire shot
out from the trees, with the clones unable to stop whatever was firing at them. Macio was able to stop the droid guards
firing on them and find the hidden access point, but only after Cesar and rest of the company were all killed.

They entered the facility alone, with Planetrunner noting that the size of an attacking army didn't matter anyways. After
taking out more droids, Planetrunner mentioned to Macio that he only had eight thermal detonators, and hoped that would be
enough. Upon entering the main area of the factory, they saw a massive assembly line manufacturing hundreds of
megadroids. Planetrunner didn't think they could destroy the whole thing, but Macio pointed out the central column holding
up the factory. Planetrunner asked if he thought taking out the column would take out the whole facility. Macio cheekily
responded with an impression of what Planetrunner had said earlier, with Planetrunner having to admit that the impression was
pretty good. They set the charges and escaped just in time for the factory to explode. However, a sound erupted that
wasn't just the factory caving in. A single megadroid shot out from the explosion, and landed right in front of
Planetrunner and Macio. Planetrunner mentioned that it seems to big, to which Macio replied that size was only a matter of
perspective. They try attacking it, but its durasteel coating was stronger than normal, leaving it immune to photonaxe
attacks. Macio climbed inside the megadroid, but just as the door closed, the droid shot itself into space. Planetrunner,
terrified for the Grand Master's safety, got into his interceptor and chased after the droid. To his relief, Macio
responded to his calls. Planetrunner had to stop the rotation of the droid so he could attach his ship to it, but the droid
was too big and heavy. He tried asking Macio to do it, but since the droid was disabled and the cold vacuum of space
weakened Macio, he could not. Macio instead instructed Planetrunner to do it, reminding him that there was no heavy, nor big
or small, just light. Calmed down, Planetrunner was able to stop the droid. Macio then cut his way out from the inside and
jumped to Planetrunner's ship, and he was able to get Macio to safety. On the ship Aspirant, Planetrunner told Macio that
their destruction of the Golatha factory had put the Separatists back years at least. He then asked Macio if he really
was too weak to stop the rotation of the droid on his own. Macio said he'd never tell him.

### Anaxes

Following an assault on Cato Neimoidia, Planetrunner was dispatched alongside Windu to participate in the Battle of Anaxes
to defend the Republic shipyards on Anaxes. With mounting losses on the Republic side, Captain Rex told Planetrunner and
Windu his theory that the Separatists had learned his own strategy. Considering this possibility, Windu sent Rex and
Commander Cody to take a squad, and Clone Force 99, behind enemy lines to infiltrate a Separatist Cyber Center while he
and Planetrunner held the line. The general staff was told about the possibility of sending a mission to Skako Minor, and
Planetrunner was sure the Median High Council would approve it. Clone Sergeant "Hunter" also stated The Bad Batch would go
with them. Although Rex was eager to get going, Planetrunner informed him they had a "thing" to do, and, although Rex felt
they did not have time, they both went to the barracks.

Rex remained outside on watch while Planetrunner, holding Rex's helmet, went in and contacted Liora. Planetrunner apologized
for being away for so long, but, as the two spoke, Kael Vorin approached Rex. The Clone Captain knocked on the door
to speed up Planetrunner. Planetrunner confided that he was worried about his captain, worrying that Rex was letting his
personal feelings drive him too much on the mission, although Liora believed Rex had learned that trait from him.
Outside, Rex tried to lie about what Planetrunner was doing. However, Planetrunner and her ended their conversation, and both
went on their way to Skako, although Vorin revealed he knew he had been talking to Liora by quipping that he hoped
Planetrunner at least greeted Dan for him. In response the Median stopped in his tracks, and although dismayed that his
effort to be secretive had been for naught, Planetrunner kept his composure and only gave his master a knowing glance
before walking away.

As they reached Skako Minor on the Marauder, Planetrunner was captured by the Poletec on their keeradaks, prompting Rex
and the Bad Batch to follow them to the village and rescue the Median General. They apologized and explained the
situation, and the chief helped them reach Purkoll, which they infiltrated with some effort. When they reached the
antechamber, Foreman Wat Tambor sent a transmission saying they had violated the Techno Union's neutrality, and sent
droid reinforcements. While Planetrunner, Hunter, Wrecker, and Crosshair destroyed them, Rex and Tech found Echo-alive,
but as a cyborg.

Tech managed to unplug Echo, and they escaped to the ventilation system before being vaporized by Tambor's Decimator,
after which Wrecker destroyed the Foreman's main computers with explosives. As they escaped, however, they were
surrounded by his D1-series aerial battle droids, but thanks to Tech, they rode keeradaks to the Poletec village. There,
they convinced the natives to help them against the Techno Union's forces, including their octuptarra tri-droids, with
Planetrunner effectively destroying two of them.

Following the skirmish, Planetrunner, Rex, and Clone Force 99 returned to Fort Anaxes, where Windu and Vorin were to take
the Separatist assembly complex by air, whereas Echo was to be escorted by the Bad Batch, Planetrunner, and Rex into
Trench's communications vault on a dreadnought on the planet's orbit, where he would plug himself to the dreadnought to
feed the Separatist's strategic movements. When Echo did so and deactivated the droids attacking the assembly complex,
he realized that Trench had initiated a countdown for an explosion that could destroy most of Anaxes. While Vorin
assisted in the evacuation efforts, and Windu deactivated the bomb, Planetrunner went to the dreadnought's bridge to
confront Trench, destroying his droid bodyguards. Trench refused to give the final sequence number, believing that
Planetrunner would not harm him. Planetrunner amputated Trench's prosthetic attachments, prompting the Harch to immediately
give in. After relaying it to Windu, who deactivated the bomb, Trench then tried to electrocute him; in response, Corin
thrust his photonaxe through the Harch's chest, killing him. He then took the self-destruct detonator for the
dreadnought and reunited with the rest of his team.

As they left aboard the Marauder, Planetrunner let Wrecker destroy Trench's flagship, the Invulnerable, damaging the
nearby Separatist fleet, and they went back to Fort Anaxes. Following the victory, the Republic prepared medals for the
team, while Corporal Echo joined "The Bad Batch."

## Birth of Evilth Papa

### Battle of Yerbana

At some point before the Battle of Tyraleus, Planetrunner was on Tythe and had another encounter with Rooka, yet he failed
to defeat the Count. Along with the 501st and 212th, Planetrunner and Vorin were sent to Yerbana to take down the
Separatist forces on the planet. The fight caused Planetrunner and Vorin to split their respective battalions into two
fronts.

Planetrunner, Rex, and the 501st Legion defeated the Separatist Droid Army on their front, so they left to assist Vorin
and his 212th Attack Battalion, which was suffering heavy casualties from the ongoing conflict. While Vorin and
Commander Cody were taking cover from the blasts, Planetrunner ordered his men to hide under the bridge, while B0-U5 would
tell them when to launch. Next, Planetrunner stepped into the fight and convinced his Master to follow his plan. Planetrunner
faked a surrender to draw out the droid commander, who saw through the lies of the Median Knight; however, it was too
late, as Planetrunner used his Force abilities to destroy the droid commander, allowing his 501st Legion led by Captain Rex
to make a surprising ambush on the rest of the droid army, ending the conflict.

The 212th Attack Battalion proceeded to help the 501st while Planetrunner was approached by Vorin who complimented him,
which Planetrunner answered by thanking Vorin for helping achieve victory. The two were soon contacted by Admiral Wullf
Yularen, who informed them of an upcoming transmission going under the code "Fulcrum," while the two Median thought it
might have been Saw Gerrera, Yularen confirmed otherwise saying it was necessary for the generals to attend the call
themselves.

### The last meeting of a friendship

At Yularen's ship, Planetrunner and Vorin were surprised to see Seren Ashoria and Bo-Katan Kryze were the ones that had made
the call. Emotionally shocked to see his former apprentice after several months of being apart, Planetrunner barely managed
to control himself and proceeded to talk to Ashoria, who remarked the moment was not a reunion as Tal had been located on
Mandalore and they had an opportunity to capture him.

Ashoria hoped Planetrunner and Vorin would be able to join forces with her to confront him. Ashoria, Kryze, and her Mandalorians
boarded the ship, where they were greeted by Planetrunner and Vorin. The former tried to greet Ashoria, but his former
apprentice turned him down saying they had to act immediately if they wanted to capture Tal. The group went to discuss
the possible attack, but Vorin was not willing to help Ashoria and her allies unless the Median Council gave their
permission, causing Planetrunner to unnoticeably scowl at him. While Vorin contacted the Council, Planetrunner had Ashoria
accompanying him through the complex. Planetrunner led Ashoria to a room full of the 501st clone troopers, including Rex, who
had painted their helmets as a way to honor her former Commander. Planetrunner then prepared to give Ashoria her old
photonaxes, but before he could do so, the ship's alarm suddenly went off.

Vorin rushed in and informed Planetrunner and Rex that they would be jumping to hyperspace immediately. When Planetrunner
asked if this meant the attack on Mandalore was approved, Vorin revealed that they were actually heading for Tyraleus,
where a dire situation was happening: General Multorix had launched a full-scale attack on the capital of the Republic,
and the Median Council had lost contact with Shaak Ti, Chancellor Drav's assigned protector. Planetrunner was visibly
uncomfortable about this news, but Vorin assured him that their fleet would arrive at Tyraleus very soon.

Ashoria, however, was angered by her former Masters' decision to abandon Mandalore. Vorin pointed out that they were
entering a pivotal moment in the Clone Wars, but Ashoria countered that Vorin was playing politics and that the Median Order
had lost their way by forgetting that their duty was to help people and not politicians, which was why the people, and
Ashoria herself, had lost faith in them. Planetrunner heard the argument and weighed in; so as to help Ashoria in the upcoming
siege while also taking part in the mission to rescue the Chancellor, Planetrunner promoted Rex to Commander so he could
lead the a new formation of the 501st that was dubbed the 332nd Division, assigning Ashoria to assist as an advisor due to
her being unable to hold an official military title. When Vorin agreed, Ashoria accepted the proposal. Vorin left the
room to prepare their troops leaving Planetrunner and Ashoria behind. Planetrunner gave Ashoria her new photonaxes complimenting
them as better than before.

Planetrunner then headed to rescue the Chancellor, believing the defeats of Tal and Multorix would mark an end to the war.
While he was leaving, Ashoria stopped him by wishing him good luck in his mission. Happy to have been reunited with his
apprentice, Planetrunner smiled and they both parted ways. Unbeknownst to either of them, this would be the last time they
ever saw each other as friends.

### Confrontation on the Invisible Hand

Having been away from Tyraleus for months due to the Outer Rim Sieges, Planetrunner and his Master finally returned to the
planet after leaving Ashoria, to lead the rescue of the Chancellor from General Multorix before the cyborg's fleet could
flee the besieged Capital. Assisted by a squadron of ARC-170 spacebattlers led by Clone Commander Odd Ball, the two Median
fought their way through a swarm of Vulture and tri-fighter droid spacebattlers protecting the Invisible Hand, General
Multorix's flagship. Planetrunner and Vorin headed for the ship while the clones distracted the droids, but Vorin's ship
was damaged and partially disabled by Buzz-droids. Although Vorin told Planetrunner to abandon him and complete the
mission, the younger Median refused and cleared his former master's ship of droids before escorting him to the Invisible
Hand{{'s}} hangar. After crashing landing, the two Median disposed of the few remaining droids in the hangar while B0-U5
located the Chancellor.

Once they discovered that he was being held at the top of the ship's observation spire, they concluded that they were
walking into a trap when Planetrunner sensed the presence of Count Rooka. Not long after they arrived at the top of the
spire, the Varki Lord appeared before them and the two Median engaged him in a duel. Rooka managed to gain the upper hand
and knocked Vorin out, but his taunting, intended to erode Planetrunner's morale, instead enraged him. Planetrunner unleashed
his fury on the Varki Lord, brutally overwhelming him and slicing off both of his hands. Taking Rooka's photonaxe, he
crossed both his and the Count's blades at the Count's throat, and Drav urged him to kill his helpless opponent.
Planetrunner initially hesitated, but after the Chancellor's continued insistence, he gave into his hatred of his nemesis
and beheaded Rooka. He expressed regret afterward, stating it was not the Median way, but the Chancellor assured him that
he had been right to kill the Count.

Despite the Chancellor's pleas, he carried Vorin on his back to make their escape. However, the elevators leaving the
spire had been disabled. With help from R2 and the attack taking place on the Invisible Hand by a neighboring Republic
cruiser, they were able to escape in the elevator shaft until the ship's crew was able to regain control of the ship,
restoring its gravity and turning the shaft once more into well. Vorin regained consciousness while they were hanging
on inside the shaft and together, he and Planetrunner were able to escape the shaft just as a reactivated elevator was
about to crush them. However, their good fortune failed them, and they were trapped by a ray shield and apprehended,
along with R2, by battle droids. The two Median and the Chancellor were brought before Multorix in the Invisible Hand
{{'s}} control room. The cyborg personally taunted them, derisively commenting on Planetrunner's youth considering his
reputation. Planetrunner retorted with a taunt about the General being shorter than he had expected, which angered the
cyborg general.

Eventually, B0-U5 caused a distraction, allowing Vorin to draw his photonaxe to him with the Force, freeing himself
and then Planetrunner. Once the younger Median had also summoned his weapon, they engaged and made short work of Multorix's
MagnaGuards and the battle droids holding them and the Chancellor. However, as they attempted to apprehend Multorix, he
used one the MagnaGuards' electrostaffs to shatter the viewport, depressurizing the bridge and letting the vacuum take
him. Planetrunner and Vorin caught onto nearby command consoles until security measures allowed the bridge to
depressurize. Before they could reach him, however, Multorix escaped, jettisoning all the escape pods to prevent them
from escaping. As the command crew had fled, Planetrunner took control of the damaged flagship, which had begun to enter
Tyraleus's atmosphere. Although he briefly managed to slow the ship's descent, the damage it had sustained proved too
great, and the Invisible Hand broke in half, picking up considerable speed as it fell towards the Republic capital.
Planetrunner eventually succeeded in crash-landing the Invisible Hand on a deserted landing strip, returning the
once-captive Chancellor to Tyraleus unharmed.

### Looming fatherhood

Following the ordeal, the two escorted the Chancellor to the Senate building, where they separated-while Vorin went
back to Median Temple to report to the Council, Planetrunner remained with the Senators who had come to greet the returning
Chancellor. He briefly spoke with Senator Veskra, who expressed hope that Count Rooka's death could bring a quick end to
the war. Planetrunner disagreed, saying that as long as General Multorix remained as leader of the Separatist armies, the
war would continue. At that moment, he noticed Liora behind one of the columns, took his leave from the Senator and
reunited with his wife for the first time in months. Having been away fighting in the Outer Rim Sieges, Planetrunner's
single focus was reuniting with Liora. Liora then revealed to her husband that she was pregnant. Though they were
both worried that this might expose their secret, Liora especially, Planetrunner was overjoyed and told her not to worry,
saying that it was the happiest moment of his life. The couple returned to Liora's apartment, where they began to make
plans for when the baby would be born, deciding that their child would be raised on Nivellon, in the Lake Country. Liora
also planned to head there before the birth, to prepare the room.

However, that same night, Planetrunner's happiness was marred when he suffered a nightmare of his wife dying in childbirth,
similar to the visions he had had of his mother before her death. Although Liora tried to comfort him that it was only
a dream, he was terrified that he would lose her, as he had lost his mother. Liora tried to convince him that they
needed help and suggested they ask Vorin for his assistance. Planetrunner refused, insisting that their baby was a
blessing, not a curse. The next day, at the Median Temple, he sought Macio's counsel concerning these dreams, but the Grand
Master told Planetrunner that death was a natural part of life, and to let go of all that he was afraid to lose.

### Tensions of loyalty

At the same time, tensions were rising between Chancellor Drav and the Median Council, who were concerned with his
increasing power. Matters were made worse when the Senate announced that they planned to grant him more executive powers
in order to facilitate the end of the war. When Planetrunner was informed of this by Vorin, he was supportive of the
measure, despite the reservations of the Council and Vorin's warning to be wary of Drav. He then told him that the
Chancellor had requested his presence for unknown reasons, without informing the Council. So Planetrunner met with
Drav at his office, where he told him that he was appointing the young Median to be his personal representative on
the Council, a decision that Planetrunner believed the Median Masters would never accept.

When informed of this, the Council allowed Planetrunner to sit on the Council, yet they refused to grant him the position
of Master, a decision which greatly angered Planetrunner. Planetrunner turned to Vorin, who so remained silent. Angered more
by this, Planetrunner reluctantly accepted his position and took his seat on the council. At the end of the meeting, Vorin
acknowledged to Planetrunner that his appointment had been accepted so that, on behalf of the Council, he could spy on the
Chancellor, which Planetrunner was reluctant to do. In recent weeks, Liora and other senators concerned about Drav's
expanded powers had also created the Petition of 2,000 in the name of protecting democracy, requesting he return his
emergency powers to the Senate and end the war with cease-fire negotiations. Planetrunner was manipulated by Drav into
believing Liora could have ulterior motives that she was keeping hidden.

At the Galaxies Opera House in the Uscru District, Planetrunner joined Drav in his private box while he was watching
Squid Lake. During the performance the Chancellor told Planetrunner that Clone Intelligence had located General Multorix
in the Utapau system. He began to stir Planetrunner's distrust in the Median council, claiming that the Median were planning on
taking control of the Republic and betraying him. Planetrunner felt conflicted - despite the Median's mistrust in the
Chancellor, he still felt that Drav was a good man. He confided in the Chancellor that he had lost trust in the
Median. Drav correctly guessed that it was because they had sent Planetrunner to spy on him, and that it made him feel
dishonest. Planetrunner didn't know how to respond. The Chancellor claimed that the Median were only perceived as good
because "good is a point of view," stating that the Median and the Varki were not so different. While Drav's
conflation of the two groups played to Planetrunner's devotion to his Order's ideals and helped set the stage for his
conversion to the dark side, Planetrunner rebutted by saying that the Varki were selfish while the Median were selfless.
Drav then recounted the Tragedy of Evilth Plagueis the Wise to Planetrunner framed as an "old Varki legend". In reality,
the tale was about his Varki Master and how he killed him. Drav specifically told the story knowing that Planetrunner
was having nightmares about his wife dying. The revelation that he might need to disobey the Median Order to save Liora
opened Planetrunner's mind - he wanted to learn this power. Afterward, Planetrunner bid farewell to Vorin, showing
gratitude for his teachings and said to each other "May the Force be with you," before parting ways.

### Fall to the dark side

Though horrified that he betrayed and contributed to the death of Windu, Planetrunner saw this as the final straw against
the Median Order, and as such there was no turning back for him. Desperate to save Dan, he reluctantly betrayed the Median
and pledged himself to service under his new Varki Master, Evilth Schemious. Schemious named him "Evilth Papa," a title that
he did not bestow lightly, and promised that, together, they would unlock the secret to immortality. Whereas earlier
Schemious had implied he already had that power, Planetrunner was so focused on the possibility that there was a chance to
save Liora that he did not notice the contradiction. After Schemious declared all Median enemies of the Republic, he
ordered Papa to kill the Median at the Temple and execute the Separatist Council on the Dravion Prime System. Schemious then
executed Action 256, during which the clone troopers were forcibly brainwashed into turning on their Median Generals and
executing them on the spot, while Papa led the 501st Legion to attack the Median Temple.

During the assault, Papa killed dozens of Median, such as Master Cin Drallig. In the council chamber, he found a group of
younglings trying to hide. Thinking Papa was still a Median Knight, one boy asked him what they should do, but the new
Varki Lord slaughtered the boy and the other younglings. Similarly, as he led a force of clones further into the Temple,
he encountered a group of younglings who assumed he had arrived to help. Instead, however, he cut the children down,
leaving only one survivor; after Papa stabbed her and looked her in the eyes, the human youngling Reva Sevander,
growing to be filled with rage, survived because she played dead amongst the corpses of her classmates. After the
battle, Papa manipulated the Temple's beacon to broadcast a signal telling any surviving Median to return to Tyraleus
where they could be murdered by the clone troopers stationed at the Temple.

Following the attack, he met with Schemious, who then sent him to Dravion Prime to kill the remaining mebers of the Executive
Separatist Council. Before his departure he went back home to Liora and told her much to her disbelief that the Median
Order had tried to topple the Republic and that he was about to go to Dravion Prime. Telling her that he would end the war,
they kissed and he left aboard his new green Eta-2 Actis-class light interceptor, which replaced the interceptor he
had lost in the Battle of Tyraleus.

On Dravion Prime, Papa slaughtered the entire Separatist Council, including Wat Tambor, Poggle the Lesser, and Nute Gunray,
along with their aides, his eyes now yellow and red with rage. Simultaneously, Schemious carried out the proclamation of
the New Order in an emergency session of the Senate, claiming that the Median Order had committed treason against the
Republic, and reorganized the Republic into the first Galactic Empire with himself as its Emperor. During this time,
Papa was followed by Kakan, who believed he was a Median. Papa showed his face, eyes to Kakan and chased after him to
ensure there would be no witness. During his chase, Papa ran into a cloud of Lava fumes. The fumes caused Papa to see
hallucinations his fellow Median such as Windu, Drill, Koon, Billaba, Macio, and his former apprentice Ashoria. Papa was able
to push the fumes away from himself and dismissed the hallucinations. Soon, Papa reported his mission's completion to
Schemious; on his orders, Papa sent a shutdown signal to the Confederate navy and army, effectively ending the Clone
Wars. With his mission completed, and the Separatists dead, Papa looked on from a balcony and shed a tear at the man he
had become, but knew it was too late to turn back.

## Becoming Evilth Papa

### Duel on Dravion Prime

Soon thereafter, Papa saw Liora's star skiff land and ran to meet her. She told Papa that Vorin had discovered
their secret and had also told her that Papa had joined the dark side, hoping that he'd prove Vorin wrong. However,
Papa only confirmed it to be true. Driven power-hungry by the Dark Side and declaring the galaxy was at peace, Papa
tried to convince her that they could be happy together as rulers of the new Empire, promising he could overthrow
Schemious. In Papa's ideal world, Liora would have taken his hand, believing the man before her was still her husband.
In reality, however, Papa's propositions and actions horrified his wife, who begged him to leave the dark side behind.

At that moment, Papa saw Vorin walking out of Liora's ship because he had secretly stowed away. Convinced that his
wife had betrayed him to give his old master a chance to kill him, Papa, ignoring her attempts to explain, Force-choked
Liora until Vorin demanded he let her go, by which point she had already fallen unconscious. While what he had just
done horrified him, Papa lashed out at Vorin by blaming him. Although Vorin tried to reason with his former pupil,
Papa refused to listen, as the new Empire was everything he wanted the galaxy to be. Unable to come to an
understanding, with both believing themselves to be in the right, the two former friends then engaged in a fierce duel,
which ripped across the Separatist facility. As they fought throughout the Separatist war room, their duel damaged the
computers, causing the facility shields to deactivate and allowing the building to start falling into the lava river
below.

After fighting across the crumbling building and over a lava river, the duel ended on the river banks, where Vorin
claimed the high ground and warned Papa not to attack. Blinded by rage and arrogance, Papa leaped to continue the
duel, only to have his remaining limbs severed by his former master's blade, leaving only his cybernetic arm. Crippled,
Papa slid down to the riverbank while screaming his undying hatred for his former master. Vorin, taking Planetrunner's
photonaxe, told him he had considered him his brother and remorsefully left him for dead as a flap of Papa's clothing
caught fire and he started burning. Vorin then left the planet with Liora, B8-6TQ, and B0-U5 as Papa lay screaming
and burning on the riverbank.

### Rebirth

Although Papa survived, he was horrifically scarred, both physically and mentally, and had damaged lungs due to the hot
ash in the air. Shortly afterward, the Emperor-having sensed his apprentice's peril-arrived on Dravion Prime, where he
found the severely wounded Papa and took him back to Tyraleus, in a medical capsule. As the Emperor could not afford
to lose Papa, he turned to the Republic's best scientists, among which was Cylo, who, in doing so, gained private
access to Papa's cybernetics. By the Emperor's orders, Papa was put into a life-sustaining black suit of armor and
outfitted with three new robotic limbs by numerous droids skilled in both cybernetic reconstruction and medical surgery.
Among the droids working on Papa was FX-6, an FX-9 surgical assistant who previously worked on Multorix's armor. After
what Schemious later called a "long night" of work, he was finally sealed within his new armor. His eyes showed a brief
flicker of fear before his mask and helmet locked together and he drew his first breath.

Effectively entombed within and smothered by his new life-support armor, Papa's rebirth was complete. Upon regaining
consciousness, Papa asked the Emperor what had become of his wife, and he told Papa that he had killed her in his
anger. Unbeknownst to either of the two Varki, Liora gave birth to the twins Drian and Mira before her death. Papa was
overwhelmed by his despair in the belief he had killed Liora and their unborn child, which fulfilled his prophetic
dreams of her death. Remembering that he had, indeed, attacked Liora with a Force choke on Dravion Prime, he believed
Schemious's claim. Further, he was both enraged and filled with despair that it had been his own choices that led to his
current reality, of a life imprisoned within a cybernetic suit and without Liora by his side. In his emotional
turmoil, Papa incidentally destroyed the medical droids and severely damaged the entire room through the Force. He
broke free of his bindings on the operating table and, despite struggling to walk under the sheer weight of his new
prostheses and armor, let out a cry of anger and despair over losing everything he had loved.

Papa's despair then turned to rage and he telekinetically slammed the Emperor against a wall in the surgical bay,
snarling that his master had promised to save Liora. The Emperor, as Papa attempted unsuccessfully to strangle him
with the Force, responded that in death Liora had provided Papa a gift: Pain. The Emperor continued by giving Papa a
choice; to either accept and use that gift or to die. After a moment, Papa replied that he would live. The Emperor then
immediately launched a barrage of Force lightning at his apprentice, and rhetorically demanded that Papa use the power
of his photonaxe to defend himself, but Papa replied that his photonaxe had been taken by Vorin at the conclusion of
their duel.

As he continued his barrage, the Emperor angrily shouted that the weapon Papa spoke of was not his. Rather, it had
belonged to a Median, and Papa was now a Varki. Ceasing his Force-based assault, the Emperor drew his own photonaxe. He
put the blade to Papa's throat and stated that he understood how traumatic the last few days had been for his
apprentice, but warned that should Papa ever use the Force against him again, he would finish what Vorin could not.
The Emperor then deactivated his weapon and stated that, as friends, he hoped that the two of them would never find
themselves in a similar situation. He instructed Papa to put aside his rage and lust for revenge against the Median for
the time being, for the two of them had a great deal of work to accomplish. By submitting to the hate within his heart
by believing he had killed Liora and that her death had pushed him to a new future from the pain it provided, Papa
would become the Emperor's loyal enforcer and apprentice. Cut off from his old life and truly believing he had murdered
Liora, Papa invested entirely in Schemious as his only source of refuge and guidance.

### Hunting a kyber crystal

Immediately after his surgery, the Emperor took Papa to a balcony overlooking the old Median Temple. There, he and Papa
watched as Mas Amedda directed a ceremonial burning of the photonaxes of all the Median who had been killed in the
Temple. As they listened to Amedda's speech, the Emperor asked if his apprentice knew how or why Varki photonaxe blades
were red in color. Papa replied that he did not, as the Temple's information on the subject had been "incomplete." The
Emperor laughed and contemptuously mused that the Median had been uncomfortable with the information and had buried it as
a result. He then explained that kyber crystals felt pain just like any living being, and could be made to bleed after
a fashion by pouring rage, pain, and hate into them. He asked Papa if he understood, to which Papa replied that he
did, stating that he could have given him any of the burning Median photonaxes to corrupt, even Macio's. But he had not,
as Papa realized that the crystal of a Varki's photonaxe should be taken directly from a Median by that Varki.

As the ceremony progressed, the clone troopers attending the vent threw a basket full of various photonaxes into the
incinerator, including Macio's. The photonaxes caught on fire and a moment later, a powerful blast of energy was
released into the air as the kyber crystals were destroyed. Afterward, the Emperor brought Papa to Gattering in the Mid
Rim and assigned him the task of hunting down a Median to take a kyber crystal from. The Emperor took his apprentice to a
site where he had arranged for a starship to be delivered for Papa's use, but the ship had been stolen by a group of
pirates. Leaving Papa to reclaim the vessel, the Emperor departed, and Papa struck out for the planet's nearest
settlement on foot. Once there, he eliminated the group of pirates who had stolen the ship and traveled to the Median
outpost Brighthome. The station was garrisoned by a group of clone troopers, who noted Papa's approach and hailed
him.

Though he could have provided the security codes necessary to secure the clone troopers assistance, Papa decided
instead to simply kill them. During the fight, Papa summoned a green-bladed photonaxe from the wall to kill most of
the clone troopers. After exterminating the garrison, Papa tasked the droid co-pilot of his ship to search through the
station's archives for data on any Median who had taken the Barash vow prior to Action 256. Papa's hope was that any Median
who had taken the vow, one of complete non-interference in all Median affairs, would have been not only out of harm's way
when Action 256 was issued but would have ignored its occurrence in accordance with the vow. The search identified Median
Master Kirak Infil'a, a Median who had been completely dedicated to combat to the exclusion of all else. When a grenade
was thrown at him by two surviving clones, "Ding" and "Kicker," he managed to contain the explosion, which the clones
believed would make him unable to do anything else as all his concentration was diverted on freezing the explosion.

As they talked of how they would restrain and bring in what they believed was just another Median survivor before the
Emperor in the hopes of being rewarded, Papa proved their beliefs that he was too preoccupied with the explosive to be
false by telekinetically throttling the clones and breaking their necks, before walking far enough away from the
explosion to release it. Papa quickly located the Median on the river moon of Al'doleem and sensed as he disembarked his
ship that Infil'a was waiting for him. The Median Master immediately confronted Papa, and was seized in a Force choke by
the Dark Lord. However, Infil'a quickly released a Force blast at Papa which staggered him and disrupted his
concentration. Infil'a declared his Barash to be complete and began to ascend the mountain upon which he lived, calling
out to Papa to follow if he could. One of the Median Master's training droids, Arex, then opened a sluice gate which sent
a river of water crashing down upon Papa.

The Varki Lord was visibly battered by the rush of water, but managed to telekinetically part the river and walked to the
shore. He was then set upon by a group of gigantic carnivorous birds, which damaged one of his cybernetic legs. Papa
eventually crushed them all with the Force and made his way to the peak of the mountain. There, he found Infil'a and
Arex awaiting him. Papa quickly unleashed a Force push that blasted Infil'a off his feet and dazed him long enough for
Papa, who was unarmed, to destroy Arex and take the droid's training saber. He threw the droid off the mountain and
engaged Infil'a, who sensed that Papa not only wanted to kill him but wished to take his photonaxe as well. However,
Papa's previously damaged leg broke apart at the knee a short time into the duel, rendering him unable to continue the
fight. Infil'a then declared his intention to seek out Schemious and kill him, and blasted Papa off the top of the
mountain with the Force.

Regaining consciousness, Papa used the Force to reassemble his cybernetic limbs with the dismembered pieces of Arex,
who coincidentally had landed near where Papa had fallen. He then tracked Infil'a to Am'balaar City, where he reengaged
the astonished Median Master. Fighting atop the Am'balaar city dam, the two crossed blades until the duel was interrupted
by a trio of security guards. Annoyed, Papa telekinetically flung the guards from the top of the dam, but Infil'a
caught them and used the Force to lower them to safety. Infil'a then shouted at Papa not to involve anyone else in
their duel, but Papa instead took advantage of Infil'a's concern for innocents by ripping apart a building-sized water
storage tank situated in the city below. As Infil'a attempted without success to use his own powers to stop the
destruction, Papa telekinetically removed the Median's photonaxe from his belt and claimed it for his own. He then
grabbed Infil'a in a Force choke and lifted him from the dam. Infil'a pleaded with Papa to spare the civilians below
the dam, but Papa ignored him.

As the enormous tank burst completely, flooding Am'balaar City, Papa crushed Infil'a's throat with the Force and tossed
his body into the wreckage below. After obtaining a Median photonaxe and the kyber crystal within, Papa reboarded his
ship, whereupon the droid co-pilot seized control of the vessel and jumped to hyperspace. The droid then began to play a
pre-recorded message from the Emperor to Papa. The message stated that, per the Emperor's instructions, the droid had
plotted a course to the planet Dravion Prime, where Papa would find a dark-side locus which he could use to help him corrupt
the kyber crystal. As the message concluded, Papa touched down on Dravion Prime and quickly found the locus the Emperor had
spoken of, an ancient Varki shrine within a shallow cavern. There, he disassembled Infil'a's photonaxe on a small, flat
rock formation and removed the kyber crystal.

However, when he attempted to corrupt it, the crystal resisted and used the Force to send Papa careening into one of
the cavern walls. The crystal then caused Papa to experience a vision wherein he rejected the dark side, journeyed to
Tyraleus, and killed Drav. In the vision, Papa then found Kael and begged for his forgiveness. As he knelt in
contrition in front of his former master, Kael called out to Papa by his former name, Corin. Upon hearing this,
Papa snapped out of his vision and firmly rejected the possibility shown to him by the crystal, declaring that a life
as a Varki was all he could be after everything he had done. He then began to pour his hatred, pain, and rage into the
crystal. As the planet around the cave was consumed in a violent storm, Papa succeeded in corrupting the crystal.

Afterwards, Papa returned to Tyraleus and stormed into the Emperor's office during the middle of a discussion between
Tarkin, Mas Amedda, and the Emperor regarding the construction of the Murder Moon. As Papa was completely unknown to
anyone other than Drav at the time, the Royal Guards in the Emperor's office attempted to intercept him, only to be
blasted back into the office's large window. Seeing Papa, the Emperor dismissed both Tarkin and Amedda, the former of
whom expressed concern for his safety. Reassuring Tarkin, the Emperor repeated his command, and the two Imperial
officials departed, leaving Papa to display Kirak Infil'a's photonaxe, emitting a crimson blade, to the Emperor in
triumph, thereby affirming his status as a Varki apprentice.

### Training the Inquisitorius

Shortly after returning to his master, Papa retired to a medical chamber so his damaged cybernetic components could be
repaired. As Papa floated within a bacta tank, the Emperor congratulated him for taking his first step to mastery of
the dark side, although Papa was angered when he learned a group of droids would be fixing his suit. Sensing as such,
the Emperor allowed Papa to repair his armor on his own and informed him there was a new mission to undertake once his
convalescence was complete. From his bacta tank, Papa guided the service tools with the Force to repair his armor to
his liking. At least one of Arex's pieces would remain in Papa's armor for years to come, filling in part of his knee
joint. As a residence, Papa was given a personal suite on Tyraleus, where he was served by a cloaked assistant.

As he repaired his helmet, having repaired and donned the rest of his suit by then, Papa was informed of an intruder in
the Median Temple Archives. He promptly confronted the intruder, who wielded a red photonaxe. As the two fought each
other, the intruder appeared to take the advantage, but after a time Papa revealed that he had simply been testing the
modifications that he had recently made to his armor, and promptly destroyed the intruder's photonaxe. As Papa went in
for the kill, the Emperor arrived and told him that the intruder, titled the Grand Inquisitor, was part of the
Inquisitorius. Papa was then taken to The Works, where Papa saw the rest of the Inquisitorius training themselves.
Papa was told that most of the Inquisitorius were Median who converted to the dark side in the wake of the Order's
destruction in order to save themselves. As they overlooked the dark side agents, Papa inquired if the Grand Inquisitor
would have taken his place as a Varki apprentice should he have lost the duel but soon declared there had been no chance
of the lesser agent winning.

Papa and the Inquisitorius were given the mission to hunt down and finish off surviving Median of the Emperor's Purge.
Given the mission to train the Inquisitorius and agreeing to do so right away, Papa dueled the Sixth Brother in a
training session and cut off his arm in order to teach him about loss. Papa then spoke with the Grand Inquisitor about
improving the Inquisitorius' training methods. They began to search for other Median that survived the purge. Papa saw
the Inquisitors' target list and noticed the Median Archive's Chief Librarian, Jocasta Nu, on it. He asked the Emperor
what was so important about her. The Emperor explained that she had knowledge of the Varki that she and the Median council
had kept secret. The Emperor told Papa to find Nu and bring her to him. Papa assigned the Grand Inquisitor to search
the Archive for information on her.

### Hunt for Jocasta Nu

At that time, Nu had returned to Tyraleus and sneaked into the former Median temple to search for a list of young
Force-sensitives in her secret archives. As she roamed the ruins, her droid, Beetoo, informed her that her ship was
about to be discovered. She informed the droid that she would adjust her plans accordingly. As Tyraleus Security Forces
came into the hanger, Beetoo detonated Nu's ship and killed the three security officers. As Nu made for a secret archive
vault, she noticed the Grand Inquisitor reading through the Median knowledge. She continued, only focusing on the mission
at hand.

Papa was contacted by an Imperial Security Bureau major, who had discovered a Median insignia on the wreckage of Nu's
ship, and he went to the Imperial Security Bureau headquarters to check it out. When Papa arrived, the major asked what
rank he should address him by, and Papa said, "lord." The major explained to Papa their suspicions that the explosion
was premature and the Median insignia was merely "rabble-rousing graffiti" used as a calling card. Papa told him he was
wrong, and as the major explained his experience in intelligence, Papa used the Force to reconstruct Nu's ship, showing
the major that he was indeed wrong about the cause of the explosion. Papa then ordered him to search every level of
Tyraleus, steering clear of the Median temple.

Meanwhile, Nu was about to vacate the temple when she noticed the Grand Inquisitor insulting the Median knowledge he was
examining. His comments eventually drove her over the edge and she confronted him with her photonaxe. Papa arrived at
the temple entrance and Clone Commander Fox already had sealed the place. When Fox asked him what they were expecting to
happen and Papa told him that they had missed a Median during Action 256. As Papa entered the temple, Nu was pinning down
the Grand Inquisitor with her photonaxe and threatening him. The Grand Inquisitor asked how she did not remember who he
was, stating the times she had denied him the Median knowledge he sought. Nu attacked him, kicking off a short duel where
the Grand Inquisitor quickly outwitted her. The Grand Inquisitor would have killed Nu if not for Papa's arrival. As
Papa stopped the Grand Inquisitor from slaying the Median, Nu used the Force to rain Median books on them, and she fled the
scene.

Papa made chase and as he followed Nu's trail, she made it to the archive vault and used a terminal to purge the entire
library of its knowledge. As Papa entered the vault, he was confronted by the droid guard, Cator. He identified Papa
as Corin Planetrunner and told him he was not authorized to be there. Papa threw his photonaxe at the droid, but being a
guard against possible Force-sensitive threats meant the droid was ready for that move, and it caught Papa's weapon.
Papa then punched Cator's arm off, and the droid caught his wrist and squeezed it with its robotic hand. Papa drove
his fist through Cator's face before the droid could damage him any more. But as Cator dropped to the floor, Papa
noticed a powerful shot being fired at him and used his photonaxe to deflect it. The shot, fired by Nu using a
photonaxe rifle, knocked Papa back as it ripped through a bookcase. Nu stood at the entrance of the vault, confronting
Papa.

As Papa got up again, he tried to convince Nu to drop her weapon. Nu ignored him and fired again. Papa dodged her shot
and she fired a third time, further devastating the vault. As she continued firing, she tried to convince Papa that he
was just a tool to the Emperor, saying that he could never get rid of the light side of the Force as it always found its
vessels. Nu's rifle then failed to keep firing, and Papa deactivated his photonaxe, telling her she would not be
harmed. Nu's rifle then began beeping and she threw it towards Papa. He used the Force to push it away, and it
exploded, throwing both of them to the floor and breaching the side of the temple.

Nu fled through the fresh hole in the wall to find newly alerted clone troopers around the perimeter. They fired at her
and she jumped down, deflecting their shots back at them. As the clones put more pressure on her, she Force-pushed them
over the ledge behind them. Papa then appeared through the wall and the clones assumed he was too a Median and fired on
him. At that moment, Commander Fox approach the scene on an Imperial Patrol Ship and realized that they were firing on
Papa. He then had his ship fly over to Papa and ordered his units to a ceasefire. Papa jumped onto the ship and when
Fox tried to explain the misunderstanding, he used the Force to break his neck.

The clones on the ground continued firing on Nu and managed to disarm her. She then found herself cornered by Papa and
the clones, and she attempted to jump off, only for Papa to use the Force to catch her. He brought her to his ship, and
there she told the clones that he was the Median Knight Corin Planetrunner. Papa used the Force to throw the clones off the
ship and when Nu asked of what became of her, he killed her. Papa then crashed the ship and contacted Schemious, telling
him that Nu died in an attempt to escape. With Nu having revealed Schemious would create more dark side agents with the
list and questioning what it was that Papa truly wanted before her death, Papa then crushed the list of
Force-sensitive children that she had with her.

### The Weapon of the Varki

Papa followed his master to The Works district on Tyraleus, where the two prepared for a sparring match in which
Schemious intended to teach him a lesson. Schemious ignited one of his photonaxes and told Papa to fight him, to which
Papa ignited his own saber before his master charged against him. As the blades of the two Varki clashed, Papa was
quickly overpowered by Schemious, who knocked the saber out of his hand and quickly pushed him away with the Force.

As Papa was on the ground, his saber was grabbed by Schemious while he told him that he still fought like a Median. His
master told him that the photonaxe was not his only weapon and that the Dark Side of the Force was his true weapon, a
weapon that touches everything. Papa was then hit by multiple pieces of wreckage that Schemious lifted with the Force
while telling Papa that the photonaxe was merely a symbol of the inferno that consumed all who came against the Dark
Side. On his knees, Papa told his master that he understood his lesson.

### Defiance from the Imperial hierarchy

#### Hunted by the Chas

Believing that he lost all that he cared about by his own hand, Evilth Papa embraced his role as the Emperor's chief
enforcer. Few knew who he was, and even fewer suspected that he had once been Corin Planetrunner. Some rumors circulated
about Papa's unexpected entry into the Imperial authority. According to certain high-ranking Imperials, he was a
counterpart to the late Separatist warlord General Multorix, whom Drav had held in reserve, while others speculated
that he was a technologically modified warrior trained in the now-forbidden arts of the Force. His appearance at the
Imperial court and the favor he carried from the Emperor earned him the distrust of Imperial officers. They resented him
for appearing out of nowhere and having authority over them because of his link to his Master. They also resented his
heavy-handed treatment of them, such as when he used the Force in the presence of his Master to choke Colonel Barokki.
In secret, Barokki and another Imperial officer plotted to assassinate Papa, whose position in the new Empire they did
not understand.

For Papa, the situation came to a head when he investigated a Median sighting on Cabarria. Accompanied by the Ninth
Sister, he headed to the bar, where the identification had happened. Although the Ninth Sister had originally been
planning to investigate alone, Papa had come, claiming she was not yet ready to face a Median in combat but secretly
because he wanted to fight another Median. The Ninth Sister commented on his true desire, using her empathic abilities to
read him clearly. As a result, Papa ordered her to remain outside while he investigated. Once inside, the Dark Lord was
attacked by a family of bounty hunters consisting of Bhada, Ramat, and their twelve year old daughter Chanath Cha. Using
ion grenades, they neutralized all the weapons in the bar while Chanath tried to seize Papa's photonaxe with a tractor
rifle. However, he used the Force to seize the photonaxe midair and, under the strain of the two opposing forces, the
hilt shattered, leaving only the red kyber crystal.

The Chas told the assembled customers that they had come only for the "Median" and that they were not planning on harming
anyone. However, a disarmed Papa disagreed and used the Force to turn the customers into projectiles aimed at the Chas.
Taken by the surprise, the bounty hunters turned on their shields to protect themselves. As they attacked him, Papa
also used the customers and the bar's furniture as shields. Eventually, the hunters realized they could not defeat him
and made to flee. Reclaiming his crystal with the Force, Papa pursued them. Emerging from the bar, Papa initially
suspected that the Inquisitors had been behind the attempt on his life and threatened the Ninth Sister with her own
photonaxe. The Inquisitor's denials did not sway the Dark Lord, but neither did they prove her guilt. Determined to
find who had placed a bounty on his head, he pursued the Chas. They eluded him for a time until he crashed a massive
vehicle into their path, causing their speeder to crash. Seizing Chanath in a Force choke, he commanded they tell him
who had ordered his death.

Understanding they and their daughter were at risk, they told him about an anonymous bounty with an exorbitant price
posted on the Hunter Net. Ramat Cha, a talented slicer, offered to uncover their employer for him in exchange for their
daughter's life. When they demanded that he release Chanath first, Papa refused. However, the Chas refused to work if
their daughter was killed, further declaring that they would happily die as well to exist in death with her. Grudgingly
impressed, the Dark Lord demanded proof that Ramat could deliver her side of the deal, which she proved by tracking the
signal of the bounty back to Tyraleus. Papa released Chanath as agreed, at which point the bounty hunters made their
daughter swear that she would seek no vengeance against the Dark Lord, a deal Papa chose to honor. To complete the
deal, Ramat provided Papa with the information he had requested and gave him the source of the bounty on him: the
Imperial Executive Building on Tyraleus, specifically the Emperor's office.

Papa then killed both Cha parents right in front of their daughter, who was filled with rage. Despite her oath to not
hold a grudge, she ignored her promise and spent her life hunting the Dark Lord in revenge. Eventually, as the years
passed on, the Varki Lord himself simply forgot the murders he carried out on Cabarria. Cha, however, never forgot and
became a skilled bounty hunter, studying every report she could and speaking to anyone she could find who had witnessed
Papa in battle. She trained herself to counter Papa's abilities, eventually enlisting a team of fellow hunters as "the
Orphans" to help her in her quest. Cha's skills rose to a level that even Drav took notice, becoming a bounty
hunter the Emperor could trust all in the name of possibly getting close to Papa, only to never see him. In effect,
Papa had completely upended Cha's life, only for the crusade her life turned into to not impact Papa at all.

#### Cementing his place

With their business on Cabarria completed, Papa and the Ninth Sister left the planet and returned to Tyraleus. Now
suspecting that the Emperor had placed the bounty on his head, the Dark Lord planned to confront his Master about his
intentions. As the Ninth Sister piloted the ship through hyperspace, Papa worked on creating a new photonaxe. His
droid meanwhile investigated the origins of the kill contract placed on him and confirmed that the order could have come
from the Emperor's office, with no evidence of slicing to indicate foul play. But, as the ship arrived in orbit over
Tyraleus, the ship's attempt to transmit clearance codes for landing was jammed and the ship itself was marked as being
part of a Separatist splinter cell. The Imperial capital's orbital defenses targeted Papa's ship. Only the Dark Lord's
skill as a pilot prevented them from being destroyed, although the ship was damaged and forced to crash land on
Tyraleus. Tired of the repeated attempts on his life, the Dark Lord headed to the former Median Temple to confront the
Emperor.

The Emperor was investigating the hoard of artifacts that Jocasta Nu had collected and stored in the Median Archives when
