Papa arrived. The Emperor sensed that his apprentice did not wish to discuss his recent discovery, although he did
praise him for having found the Librarian's stash. Papa informed his master of the events on Cabarria and his
investigation into the kill order against him, before directly asking his Master whether he had placed it on his head as
part of a test. Noticing Papa's new photonaxe, the Emperor asked to see it, approving of its design. He also chastised
his apprentice for believing that he would resort to such methods as placing a bounty on his head if he wanted to have
him killed and that he did not "test": he "taught." He also told Papa that finding the assassins was his task, not
theirs. This echoed a previous lesson he had taught Papa when he had "disciplined" Colonel Barokki: that they must not
kill everyone in the galaxy, but that having power meant they could, and that they would never lack for people to
destroy.

Papa returned to his quarters, where he meditated on the past events and his Master's words. Thinking back to all that
had happened, he eventually realized the cause of the conspiracy against him was that his sudden elevation had caused
concern and fear among the ranks of the Imperial officers, who knew that he had "strength," but not that he shared the
Emperor's "power." Despite a lack of proof, Papa became convinced that Colonel Barokki, who had so suddenly borne his
displeasure, must be involved in the conspiracy. The Dark Lord met with the Emperor and shared his conclusions, and
requested that he be publicly recognized and allowed to show them the consequences of opposing him. The Emperor asked
whether he was sure, and Papa confirmed it: he would not kill them all unless he had to, but would not allow them to
act against him with impunity. The Emperor agreed to Papa's plan, but forbade him from killing Tarkin, as he was
essential to his plans.

The Emperor gathered the elite officers of the growing Imperial Military to clarify the new hierarchy. He formally
introduced Papa as his emissary, who spoke with his voice and whose commands would need to be obeyed as if they had
come from the Emperor himself. The Emperor then moved aside and allowed Papa to speak: the Dark Lord summoned five
officers before him: Corin Ferro, Zorta Bingan, Joon Strephi, Tomas Azoras, and Barokki. Informing them that the two
attempts on his life had been made from within the Officer Corps and that he had his suspicions who had been
responsible, he instituted a new rule: for every assassination attempt he survived, and he warned them that he would
always survive, five officers chosen at random would be executed. He instantly executed the five designated officers
with a Force choke before departing, leaving the remaining officers stunned and afraid. With his position in the
hierarchy established, Papa did not need to hold an official military rank. Instead, he acted as the de facto
Commander-in-Chief of the Imperial Military as per his position as the Emperor's right hand man. Papa would also come
to be recognized as part of both the Joint Chiefs of the Imperial Military and the Imperial Ruling Council, of which he
was considered a ranking member. After his demonstration before the officer corps, Papa returned to his personal suite
and mediated, cracking the window in his anger that positive thoughts still came.

### War on Mon Cala

In 18 BBY, one year into the reign of the Empire, Papa was reliving his duel on Dravion Prime through meditation. During his
experience, he was already in his cybernetic suit, and he used the Force to throw lava at Kael. Kael jumped up to
dodge it, but Papa Force-choked him and threw him into the rocks. Papa watched Kael burn before he awoke in his
meditation chamber as the Emperor asked for him over the comm. In his throne room, the Emperor told Papa that a year
after his ascension, it was time to show that his voice was the only voice within the Empire. Papa asked how, and the
Emperor told him that Mon Cala would make a great example of the price of defiance. He further told Papa that King
Lee-Char may have had an adviser helping him with his negotiations with the Empire. Papa asked if it could be a Median,
and the Emperor said it was possible. He told Papa to take a team to investigate this and claimed the military aspects
of the operation would be left to Moff Tarkin.

Papa arrived at Mon Cala aboard the Zeta-class shuttle Infernum. With him, he took three Inquisitors, the Sixth
Brother, Ninth Sister, and Tenth Brother, and a death squad of Purge Troopers. At this time, the Imperial ambassador
Telvar had just finished another meeting with Lee-Char, and the man was walking to his shuttle when he saw Papa descend
from the ramp of his shuttle. The Ninth Sister struggled to get past the king's Chief of Security, Gial Ackbar, and
Papa confronted the Mon Calamari, asking if he had read the writ that the Ninth Sister had given him. Ackbar confirmed
that he had, but demanded that he knew their business as he had a job to do and so did Papa. Papa complied and
explained about a possible enemy of the Empire on Mon Cala. As he said that, Telvar's shuttle took off and flew for
Tarkin's Space Eater, the Sovereign-which was in orbit above Mon Cala. However, as Ackbar denied the possibility
of an enemy of the Empire being on Mon Cala, Telvar's shuttle exploded.

Telvar's assassination prompted Tarkin to enact a full-scale invasion of Mon Cala. His forces landed at Dac City, where
Papa had arrived, and laid siege to the Mon Calamari and Quarren defenses. Papa and his team sprang to life and soon
seized the landing pad where the Infernum was parked. He then led them to the Dac City palace to find Lee-Char and ask
him about the possible Median. They fought their way through the palace guards and entered the palace, where the Ninth
Sister began torturing Lee-Char for the location of the Median. However, another threat loomed over them. A massive tidal
wave had suddenly erupted as a part of Lee-Char's defensive plan. The Sixth Brother warned them of this, and he and the
Tenth Brother began shielding Papa and the Ninth Sister from the wave using the Force. When their attempts began
failing, Papa joined them, but it was not enough. The group was washed away by the wave, and Dac City was left in
ruins.

Papa awoke at the bottom of the Great Ungeness Trench. As his oxygen supply was dwindling, he used the Force to create
an air bubble for himself. Suddenly, he was attacked by a squid-like creature, and after wrestling with it, he killed it
with the Force. Papa then rode its body using the Force and eventually picked up a transmission from the Inquisitors.
Papa asked them to come to his position, and they did so in an Imperial submarine. When they picked him up, he asked
about the Median, and the Inquisitors said that he was still alive somewhere. Papa then asked about Lee-Char, and the
Ninth Sister said that they did not know, but she then revealed that she had gotten the Median's location from him.
Knowing exactly where their target was, they began traveling for the Median.

Papa and his team arrived at the Median's location to find the individual and his disciples evacuating. The Median, an
Iktotchi Student called Ferren Barr, had been notified by Lee-Char after he was recovered following the events at Dac
City. The group of them immediately scattered, but one of the disciples instead attacked the submarine head-on with his
blaster. The shots bounced off the window, and Papa used the Force to crush his helmet. The other fled in the direction
of Bel City, and as Papa caught up with them, another disciple turned around to attack them. He too died in the process
but managed to slow Papa's submarine, and the rest of the group followed Barr to Bel City. Papa and the Inquisitors
arrived at Bel City and marched down the hallway, reinforced by the Inquisitors and the Purge troopers. Papa was then
contacted by Tarkin, who was struggling to deal with the grueling conflict on Mon Cala. Papa told Tarkin that he was
busy, but Tarkin knew that and asked him to do something else instead: capture Lee-Char. Papa told Tarkin that he did
not answer to him, but Tarkin replied that capturing Lee-Char was the only way to end the fighting quickly on Mon Cala,
and he pledged to owe Papa a favor if he did so. Papa agreed and told the Inquisitors to continue the hunt as he left.

Papa arrived at Lee-Char's Royal Command Bunker and killed his guards. He then disarmed Lee-Char and contacted Tarkin,
who told him to take Lee-Char to a window and send him his exact location. Papa asked Tarkin if he was going to send a
shuttle, and the man said not yet. Once Papa did what he asked, Tarkin began a bombardment of Mon Cala. Lee-Char
watched in horror but refused to surrender. The two were interrupted by Barr, who had outsmarted and scattered Papa's
team. Barr confronted Papa and the two dueled. As they fought, Barr revealed that he had assassinated Telvar to send
the Mon Calamari into war. Lee-Char overheard this and realized his mistake in following Barr. He ran to his terminal
and sent a message to the Mon Calamari and Quarren forces, ordering them to cease fire. Lee-Char then contacted Tarkin,
notifying him of the surrender. Tarkin sent a shuttle to pick him up but continued the bombardment.

Papa and Barr continued fighting, and Barr began laughing. Lee-Char questioned this, and Barr said that he had
completed his plan. Barr prophesied that the Mon Calamari vessels would be at the forefront of a great rebellion decades
from then, and decades after that. Papa told Barr that he was not a Median anymore, and Barr told him that that made two
of them, saying that he still beat the Varki. Papa then slew him, and the shuttle arrived to pick up Lee-Char. The king
told Papa that Mon Cala would rise again, but Papa told him that there was no Mon Cala, only the Empire. Some time
after the mission, Papa ordered to imprison and torture the people of Mon Cala.

### Investigation on Geonosis

Papa soon became aware of a project that was taking up many resources. He began investigating, which led him to the
data vault on Scarif. There, he found Project Stardust, a project that was a large battle station the size of a small
moon. Papa studied its design before he was interrupted by Tarkin, who was very displeased with Papa's snooping.
Tarkin told him he was not authorized to be there, and Papa claimed that the Force was all the authorization he needed.
Papa denied that he was Tarkin's beast but the man denied his claim and taunted Papa, saying he did not need the Force
to know he was very angry. Tarkin then produced a hologram of the Emperor, who told Papa he did not recall sending him
to Scarif. Papa apologized and told the Emperor he only sought to study the ways in which the Empire would extend its
rule over the galaxy. The Emperor told Papa of a new mission he was to go on. There had been certain instances of
sabotage during the Murder Moon's construction that Papa needed to discover the source of before it got worse. The
Emperor further told Papa that Tarkin had full authority over him and that if he disappointed him, he disappointed
Drav.

Papa arrived at Geonosis and met with Commander Orson Callan Krennic. As they greeted, an overhead rock formation
exploded and rained down on them. Papa saved himself and Krennic and they went to his office to discuss the matter.
Krennic claimed it was Tarkin sabotaging his efforts in order to get rid of him and take over the project. Papa asked
him if there was any proof and Krennic was not able to produce anything. Krennic then explained to him the incidences
that had occurred in the last three months. Papa gave his knowledge on the situation to loyalty officer Sid Uddra, who
met him at the Petranaki Arena to discuss what she suspected. She told Papa that as much as Tarkin and Krennic's
rivalry arose tension between them, it was unlikely for either to be the culprit. She then offered Papa with another
individual to look into: the scientist Galen Walton Erso. Papa looked through his office and found many kyber crystals
in which he bled for himself without issue. He then found a recording of Erso and his family. Papa also noticed that
Erso called his daughter stardust, which was the codename for the Murder Moon's project. Finally, Papa found an ootheca
egg in a box. Knowing that Geonosians were a slave race and were forbidden from breeding freely, he confronted Krennic
about this. Krennic denied that it was him and suggested that some of the slaves may have sent it as a distress call to
Erso. Papa then deduced for himself the saboteurs at hand.

Papa and a squad of death troopers entered a Geonosian hive and found the queen and her minions. The two sides engaged
but Papa quickly came out on top, slaying the queen. After the battle, he returned to Tarkin on the Carrion Spike and
reported his findings to him. Tarkin asked Papa how he knew the queen's hive had orchestrated the sabotages and Papa
told how their slicers had confirmed the hive to have installed corrupted tech into production, ensuring accidents.
Tarkin then asked Papa how he may have dealt with them and Papa said that they were animals and so they were
slaughtered like animals. Tarkin finally asked Papa if there was anything else and he stated to Tarkin that his
project, the Murder Moon, was able to destroy a planet. Tarkin asked how he knew and he told him of the kyber crystals he
saw in Erso's office. Tarkin then asked Papa why he was not happy for this revelation, and Papa said that he
distrusted his reliance on technological aberration. Tarkin then told Papa that he was one of those before realizing
that Papa wanted to be the only technological aberration. Papa warned Tarkin that the Murder Moon may become his tomb,
and when Tarkin asked if that was a threat, Papa told him it was only a prediction.

## Accepting the dark side

### The Emperor's emissary

Over the next two decades of the Empire's reign, Papa would remain one of the few who enjoyed direct access to
Drav. He was Drav's preferred envoy for all matters that the Emperor took a direct interest in. With Drav
forced to spend most of his time governing the galaxy at large, it was Papa who was tasked with taking a direct hand
against the Empire's enemies, becoming known as the "Emperor's Fist" to both Imperials and, eventually, criminals. Such
matters included the elimination of rebel uprisings and the continued construction of the Murder Moon. One of Papa's
earliest missions on the Emperor's behalf was to effect an execution on Murkhana. He was indeed made privy to the secret
construction of the Murder Moon, to be overseen by Wilhuff Tarkin. Papa's high status also gave him the ability to alter
Imperial records under the off-the-books Directive 081-Omega.

One Imperial captain who served under Papa in the immediate aftermath of the Clone Wars alleged to a later subordinate,
Yrica Quell, that Papa "matured" over the years: while during his first days as an Imperial enforcer Papa would simply
murder out of annoyance, Papa came to wait for a subordinate to commit a mistake, albeit sometimes a trivial one, to
have an excuse to kill. The Imperial officers remained wary of Papa and his power, as well as his continued devotion to
the ancient ways of the Force, but none rose to challenge him without feeling the consequences.

Despite the mistrust and even hatred he generated among the officers, Papa was held in high esteem by the Stormtrooper
Corps, as he often fought alongside them at the front line rather than remaining in command centers. As the Emperor's
enforcer, Papa retained command of the unit he had commanded during the Clone Wars as Corin Planetrunner: the 501st
Legion. When the Emperor retired the clone troopers, the rank and file of the 501st were composed of recruited
stormtroopers, some of whom received training from the Dark Lord himself, such as Sergeant Kreel, an undercover agent
whom Papa trained in photonaxe combat. Through their missions on Papa's behalf, the 501st came to be known as "
Papa's Fist." On one occasion, the stormtrooper Terex met Papa, becoming terrified of him while also respecting him.
Papa also garnered strong support from the pilots of the new Imperial Navy.

### Fighting the Shadow

For a little over a year into the Empire's inception, Evilth Papa received a communication from one of his most
proficient Inquisitors, the First Brother, whom had been dispatched to kill the resurfaced Tal on the Mid Rim world
Janix. The Inquisitor reported having faced the rogue Varki fugitive in combat alongside a surviving Median Student,
thought both had escaped from his grasp. Asking his master for his next moves, Papa sent another Inquisitor, the
Eleventh Brother, to work alongside First Brother to eradicate their targets. Upon learning both First Brother and the
Eleventh Brother had failed once more to end Tal after encountering the Dathomirian warrior, Papa saw fit to handle
the matter personally. Placing himself on the forest lying outside the planet's capital perimeter, Papa remained by the
fog-covered area in hiding as the Inquisitors drove his prey towards him. Learning that a squad consisting of Tal and
his allies would soon reach the forest, Papa made his way towards the cave tunnel connecting the city to the forest.
Soon two Mandalorian super commandos came into view and Papa quickly ended one of them before recalling back the
second, Rook Kast, into the fog with the Force. Choking her and snapping her neck, Papa allowed his mechanical breath
to be heard in the eerily quiet forest as he walked up to his foes. Appearing out of the fog, Papa calmly ignited his
photonaxe as he stared right at Tal, Master Eeko-Dio Daki, Student Devon Izara and four blaster wielding escapees. Not
saying a word, the Varki lord firmly met a strike from Tal as the Nightbrother ran straight at the cyborg and blocked
the blow without effort. Pushing back Tal, Papa easily engaged all three Force wielders in a photonaxe duel. Quickly,
Papa batted his armed adversaries away with his overpowering strength and exploited a moment to hit Tal's cybernetic
leg, carving a small gash through the metal and circuitry. Keeping the Median and former Varki away using only his lade,
Papa easily deflected the shots fired by the trio's allies and blew all seven outlaws away with a Force Push. As his
enemies realised their futility fighting him, Papa pursued as the group ran towards a ruined temple.

Papa managed to go out of the cascading temple unfazed, only covered in dust and watched as the criminals' shuttle from
Dryden Vos, flew up through the atmosphere and escaped into hyperspace before the pursuing gunships shot it down,
resulting in Papa failing to complete Schemious's order. Nevertheless, he had proved himself a greater apprentice to his
master's power by defeating and forcing the Emperor's first student to flee.

At some point, Papa was deployed to put down resistance on the mineral rich world of Bandomeer, where miners were
fighting back against Imperial exploitation. Papa punished them for their rebellion. Apparitions of Papa and other
dark siders were once faced by surviving Median Vanzell Mar-Klar and Nedriss Narr, who attempted to train a new generation
of younglings after Action 256. Having killed Tambor along with the rest of the Separatist Council during his mission to
Dravion Prime, Papa was also dispatched to Skako Minor to kill the Techno Union Foreman's remaining loyalists by wiping out
the planet's Ruling Council. Massacring the council officials, including Tambor's son Wat Tambor II, Papa established a
new Imperial-loyal regime on the planet, which also fell under Imperial occupation.

### Specter of death

At some point, a human dreamed about being pursued and killed by Papa. On Torku at one time, Papa pursued Davgar
Llian, a scientist allied with insurgents who had sabotaged an Imperial weapon. Papa, aware of Llian's role in the
sabotage, attacked once the scientist brought the weapon online to target local Imperial base, killing the soldiers and
confronting the scientist. Noting that only Llian was capable of reversing the sabotage, Papa mockingly thanked him for
doing so before strangling him with the Force.

Papa surveyed Uokara, a planet in the Unknown Regions, for signs of life on behalf of a director, who wished to
commence a mining operation. At some point, Papa unknowingly breathed in Ghymnon, a sentient pathogen native to Uokara
that had lived there for millions of years. Reporting the world as uninhabited, Papa was quarantined in a bacta tank
upon his return by a 2-1B medical droid in accordance with standard procedure following contact with a class IV planet,
much to the Varki Lord's displeasure. Within his mind, Papa confronted Ghymnon and defeated it. Papa ordered the droid
to catalog Uokara's lone, former inhabitant, subsequently ordering and leading a cleansing of the world by range
troopers armed with mobile bacta units. During the purge, Papa spotted a remaining speck of Ghymnon and destroyed it
with his photonaxe.<ref name="The Inhabitant />

### The ultimate mercy

Doctor Sera Lemare, a former employee of the Tagge Corporation and an admirer of Kaminoan science, stole a cache of
genetic specimens and developed bioweapons research in secret, supposedly creating the perfect killing machine. Bringing
a Lambda-class shuttle aboard the Phial-class heavy transport Endless Mercy, Papa led a squad of stormtroopers in
pursuit, ordering his men to stay vigilant and secure the area. Papa's team was immediately ambushed by the Z'Rakkon,
creatures born of Lemare's research. Outnumbered and overwhelmed, the Varki Lord struck at the abominations with his
photonaxe but lost his helmet in the process, swearing to take down his attackers down with him.

Dragged off by the creatures, Papa awoke to find himself and his sergeant confined in the Z'Rakkons' lair. The
sergeant, who believed he and Papa were to be eaten, expressed discontent with such a manner of death, causing Papa to
summon his photonaxe and promise vengeance. Papa freed himself and killed several of the beasts, lecturing them on
their mistakes before proceeding to eliminate their queen.

The queen Z'Rakkon-in truth, Lemare herself-recounted how she had joined the creatures and become their ruler
willingly. Stabbing Papa through the chest, Lemare then revealed that she had integrated the Varki Lord into the
Z'Rakkon hive mind. However, Papa escaped Lemare's snare and, despite her pleas, annihilated her. Lemare explained that
she had only tried to bring Papa peace, a favor Papa returned by killing her and guiding the Endless Mercy to crash
down on to the surface of an astronomical object below. Departing the decimated starship, Papa remarked that the only
peace was death and that the dark side would always endure.

### Relics of the Clone Wars

Around 17 BBY during the early Imperial era, around two years after the skirmish aboard the Tribunal during Action 256,
Papa traveled to the snowy moon that was home to the crash site of the Venator-class Space Eater. Investigating
the wreckage with a contingent of snowtroopers, Papa discovered a memorial to the clone company that perished in the
crash, as well as a photonaxe, partly frozen but still functional, that once belonged to his former apprentice, Seren
Ashoria.

Igniting the photonaxes' blue blade, Papa heard a squawking sound and turned his head to the sky, where he saw a
strange bird soaring through the air. Deep down in his heart, he realized his former Student was alive, but he lacked
any concrete proof and did not sense her presence. As such, he assumed to himself that she may have died, thereby
closing the painful memories she represented, despite deep down realizing she had to be alive. After gazing at the bird
for a moment, Papa deactivated the photonaxe and turned away from the crash site with the saber in hand, his image
reflected in an abandoned clone trooper helmet.

### Battle against the Varynathy

Around 15 BBY, Papa and his men fought against the Varynathy in Wild Space. The imperial army consisted of at least
several thousand stormtroopers, AT-AT walkers, AT-STs, REU fighters, and REU bombers. While thousands died on both
sides, Papa managed to kill the king of the Varynathy. Papa ordered his troops to attack and despite the high amount of
casualties, he did not retreat. The attacking force was only stopped by a Zillo Beast the Varynathy saw as their god.
However, Papa managed to subdue the Varynathy anyways.

### Rebellion on Ryloth

#### Preparing for the operation

Five years into the Age of the Empire, Papa, while meditating aboard the Perilous, was informed by Captain Luitt of
an attack on the Yaga Minor shipyards. The attack had been staged by several dozen members of the Free Ryloth Movement,
a primarily Twi'lek insurgency intent on liberating their homeworld from the rule of the Empire. The insurgents hijacked
an Imperial weapons transport, and Papa led a squadron of V-wing spacebattlers in pursuit. After a long chase, during
which the transport fled through hyperspace to several different systems, its engines overloaded when it attempted to
make yet another jump and Papa's squadron was finally able to engage it. The squadron brought down the transport's
shields with minimal casualties while Papa crippled the engines.

Though the squadron commander suggested allowing the Perilous to tractor the transport into one of its hangar bays
when it arrived, Papa assumed (correctly) that the insurgents planned to destroy the transport by detonating the heavy
ordnance present in the ship's cargo bays. In order to prevent this eventuality, Papa crashed his black Eta-2 Actis
-class light interceptor into one of its gun bubbles and ejected just before the collision. He then entered the ship
through the damaged gun emplacement and proceeded to kill all of the insurgent Twi'leks on the ship. After eliminating
the insurgent leader Pok, Papa noticed an active comlink on the bridge. Assuming that another rebel ship was nearby,
Papa had his V-wings fan out in a search pattern, but the rebel ship escaped detection by shutting down nearly all of
its systems and hiding in the rings of a nearby planet. Finding nothing, Papa had the Perilous collect the transport,
and returned to Tyraleus.

In the Imperial Palace, Papa reunited with his master. There, he and Schemious met with Ryloth's Senator Orn Free Taa
involving the inconvenience that was the Free Ryloth Movement. The movement, though relatively minor, had been
conducting raids on Imperial shipping facilities and transports and had seriously impacted the flow of Spice from the
planet. As such, Schemious believed that the situation warranted his personal attention, and decided that he, Taa, and
Papa would travel to Ryloth for a state visit. After informing the Senator of the planned journey and dismissing him,
Schemious informed his apprentice that Taa almost certainly had a traitor in the midst of his support staff who was
feeding the movement classified information on Imperial doings.

Though Papa understood his master's purpose in acting as bait alongside himself and Taa, he saw no reason why the
Emperor should potentially risk his own safety over such a minor issue. Rather, Papa advocated for simply killing Taa
and his entire staff, thereby guaranteeing the elimination of the traitor. However, Schemious wished to eliminate the
roots of the treachery, and not simply the lone traitor in Taa's staff. To that end, Schemious gave the order for Moff
Delian Mors to be informed that Taa would be arriving for a state visit, but stipulated that she should not be told that
either he or Papa would be accompanying the Senator. In this way, Schemious hoped to provide further encouragement for
the movement to attack, as he assumed that they would discover his and Papa's plans via their spies. Ten days later
Papa, the Emperor, Taa, and a contingent of Royal Guards journeyed to the Ryloth system aboard the Perilous.

#### Assassination attempt on the Defiance

While traveling from Tyraleus to Ryloth, the Emperor ordered the Perilous to stop in the Denon system to consult with
several navy chiefs on how to better integrate disparate naval academies into one Imperial Naval Academy. The Emperor
ordered Papa to oversee a training session conducted by Commandant Pell Baylo on the Defiance while the Emperor met
with his naval chiefs in Baylo's office on the training ship. It was during this training session that Papa began to
believe that Schemious was treating him much the same way the Median Council had previously: acting as he knew better,
keeping information from Papa, giving him "busywork." Baylo ordered the Defiance to enter hyperspace on a course for
Christophsis. Cadet Rae Sloane entered the coordinates, only to have her hyperspace path overridden by Baylo, who said
she was going to send them too close to a singularity.

Sloane studied the path, suspecting that Baylo was incorrect in his adjustment. Papa and Sloane discovered that the
changed hyperspace route would crash the Defiance into Christophsis' sun, killing all aboard. Papa ordered Sloane to
correct the problem, and without revealing that he knew of Baylo's treachery, Papa and Baylo went to see the Emperor.
The Emperor ordered Baylo to turn over command of the Defiance and take a position at the training center on Corellia.
Baylo, however, was loyal to the Republic and considered the Empire a hostile power. Instead of turning over his
command, Baylo offered his resignation from the navy. Papa then revealed he knew of Baylo's plan to crash the
Defiance, and the Emperor congratulated Papa for handling the "petty problem," annoying him.

As Baylo railed against the Emperor, Papa Force-choked him to death, drawing ire from the Emperor, who had wished to
see Baylo suffer and force him to watch his beloved Navy be turned into something he hated and have the Defiance be
melted down into cafeteria trays. Above all, he wanted to use Baylo for his own ambitions since the old man was willing
to kill his own students for a cause. Papa tried to explain that his way was more efficient, but the Emperor wanted to
hear nothing of it as he did not order him to kill Baylo. Later, he ordered Sloane to have the Defiance renamed the
Obedience as a subtle final jab at Baylo and a not-so-subtle reminder toward Papa to learn his place.

#### Crash land on Ryloth

Shortly thereafter, Papa and the Emperor reboarded the Perilous and resumed their course to the Ryloth system.
However, upon their exit from hyperspace, the ship immediately began slamming into spacial mines set up by Cham
Syndulla's rebels. Hidden amongst these mines were specialized devices designed to drain the ship's shields, which began
to buckle under the continual assault. As the shields neared failure, a swarm of several hundred reprogrammed Vulture
Droids set upon the Perilous from the system's asteroid belt. Papa boarded his personal interceptor and took several
squadrons of Imperial pilots to destroy the droid fighters and mines, but discovered a short time into the battle that
Vulture Droids were each carrying a payload of explosive buzz droids.

Realizing that the Vultures themselves were simply delivery systems meant to unload the buzz droids near or inside the
Space Eater, Papa ordered his squadron to concentrate fire on them, as they presented a far greater threat than the
mines. But between the mines and the Vultures, there were simply too many targets for Papa and his squadrons to handle,
and the Perilous was severely damaged. The second wave of Vultures was detected immediately after the first had been
destroyed, further compounding the already bleak situation. A message came to Papa from Captain Lewitt of the
Perilous that the ship could sustain virtually no more damage without being destroyed.

Papa moved to intercept the second wave alone, ordering his squadrons to remain near the Perilous to destroy any
droids that got past him. Though incredulous, the squadron commander obeyed, and Papa used the Force to begin tearing
apart the compartments on the Vulture droids that housed the explosive buzz droids. He then used the Force to begin
flinging the buzz droids at other incoming fighters and repeated this process until the vast majority of the Vulture
Droids had been destroyed. The remaining fighters were annihilated by Papa's squadrons, and he himself returned to the
Perilous. Papa marched to the Space Eater's bridge and Force choked Taa for a short time, informing him of the
traitor in his staff that had been responsible for the assault on the Perilous. Utterly terrified, the Senator vowed
to find the traitor, but the Emperor had Taa and his staff confined to their quarters. An order was then broadcast from
the Imperial headquarters on Ryloth for any and all repair ships to aid the Perilous as it sped, badly damaged,
towards the planet.

Unbeknownst to Papa, some of the Twi'lek repair teams in fact comprised members of the Free Ryloth movement, one of
which was a group of saboteurs with orders to plant timed explosives on the hyperdrive core of the Perilous. Shortly
after the teams landed, one of the Free Ryloth groups engaged in a firefight with Imperial stormtroopers. When Papa
learned of this, he ordered all of the Twi'lek repair teams, numbering over 100, to be killed regardless of whether they
were aiding the assault and proceeded to Deck 17, where the firefight had been reported. On the way, he killed a group
of apparently uninvolved Twi'leks before proceeding to the hyperdrive chamber. The saboteurs, who were led by Cham's
second in command, Isval, had managed to seal the hatch to the hyperdrive core before any Imperial troops could
interrupt them, and Papa began to use his photonaxe to cut it open.

By the time Papa finished cutting through the hatch, the saboteurs had already concluded their business and escaped.
The main hyperdrive core had been riddled with timed charges, set to detonate if anyone attempted to disarm or remove
them. Papa concluded that the ship was lost, and ordered the captain to evacuate. Papa contacted Schemious, who
instructed his apprentice to meet him aboard his shuttle. Before departing, however, Papa made one last attempt to kill
the saboteurs, but they narrowly evaded him and escaped in an Imperial escort boat. Subsequently, Papa reunited with
the Emperor and left on the shuttle, mere minutes before the Space Eater exploded. Shortly thereafter, the Imperial
traitor Belkor Dray provided Cham with the transponder identity of the Emperor's shuttle, and he directed Isval and her
group aboard the escort boat to attack it.

Papa's exceptional piloting skills allowed him to evade the boat and then fly upside down over its cockpit within
direct visual range of its pilots. Once there, he used the Force to choke both Isval and her co-pilot, but before losing
consciousness, Isval rammed the shuttle with her escort boat. The crash disabled the shuttle's main power, and Papa had
to use a nearly depleted backup battery to attempt a crash landing on Ryloth. As he guided the ship through the
atmosphere, he had flashbacks of events and people from his past. Though distracted, Papa managed to land the ship in
Ryloth's equatorial forest region, but his distraction did not go unnoticed by the Emperor, who noted that the landing
had been poor compared to what he knew Papa to be capable of.

Not too long afterward, the Twi'lek insurgents continued their assault on freighters, prompting Papa and the Emperor to
take action and destroy them, before moving away from their fallen shuttle. At night, they stopped to rest, when the
Emperor questioned his regret and loyalty, but Papa showed himself devoted still. They were soon attacked by a lylek
horde, forcing them to retreat into a tunnel, unaware that they had entered their nest. They stood their ground against
hundreds of lyleks and their significantly threatening queen, and killed them all before exiting the tunnel and finding
a young Twi'lek, Drua. When the Emperor tried to kill her, Papa stopped him, intending to have the girl guide them to
her village, where they obtained a communicator to speak with Moff Mors.

After giving them their coordinates, they were finally surrounded by Syndulla's forces, but so did Mors's, aiding them
in quelling the rebellion. As the stormtroopers killed the Twi'leks, Papa noticed a trio of Twi'leks: Syndulla, Isval,
and Goll watching from afar and went on to kill them, but Goll and Syndulla escaped, leaving Papa to capture Isval and
bring her before the Emperor. He mocked her, telling her that her people had accomplished nothing, and Papa
subsequently executed her. On the Emperor's orders, Papa then killed the villagers to leave no witnesses, concluding
their mission.

### Teller's campaign

When Moff Tarkin's Sentinel Base was attacked, Papa was stationed in the Imperial Palace on Tyraleus, where he held a
court with the Deputy Director of the ISB, Harus Ison, berating Tyraleusi criminals as well as Prefect Phoca Soot of
Level 1331, for ignoring the Emperor's decrees. Telling them to move their operations out of Tyraleus, Papa then made
an example of Soot for his disrespect and crushed his heart with the Force, and adjourned the court to meet with Tarkin
and Grand Vizier Mas Amedda. The latter politely asked Papa to refrain from killing all those who displeased him, to
which the Varki replied that he would give thought to the matter, before greeting Tarkin and sharing the latest
developments of the Murder Moon's construction.

The pair separated when Papa left Tarkin, who met with the Emperor alone. Afterward, Papa (like Tarkin and Amedda)
partook in a meeting between the Imperial Ruling Council, and the leaders of Imperial Security Bureau and Naval
Intelligence Agency in the palace's audience chamber, overseen by the Emperor. He then assigned Tarkin and Papa to a
mission on Murkhana to investigate recently discovered Shadowfeed technology and its relationship to the attack on
Sentinel Base. The pair traveled to the planet on the Carrion Spike, which Papa made to carry his meditation chamber.

On Murkhana, however, the Spike was stolen by unknown dissidents, prompting Papa and Tarkin to kill the Sugi crime
lord Faazah, and take his Parsec Predator to pursue the stolen ship, hidden by its cloaking systems. Making use of his
connection to his meditation chamber, Papa pinpointed the rebels' location to the Fial system and later, the Galidraan
system, where they engaged the Spike before they jettisoned his meditation chamber and escaped to Lucazec. With the
Predator disabled, Papa and Tarkin boarded the Liberator, from which Papa issued his black Eta-2 interceptor to be
transported on the Goliath from Tyraleus.

On the Goliath, Tarkin told Papa that the insurgency was surely being supported by someone high up in the Imperial
Military, and predicted that the insurgents would go to Phindar to refuel the Spike. Subsequently, Papa led a
squadron to attack the stolen corvette in the Phindar system. Though they greatly damaged the ship, it escaped,
prompting Tarkin and Papa to calculate its trajectory to Obroa-skai system. Teller transmitted false intelligence that
the insurgents were heading to the Obroa-skai system. Hoping to capture the Carrion Spike, Tarkin and Papa deployed
substantial Imperial resources including three Interdictor vessels. The prototype Immobilizer 418 cruiser malfunctioned,
yanking several ships out of hyperspace and causing a massive accident.

Despite failing to catch the Spike, the Imperials managed to capture the YT-1000 light freighter Reticent, which
Teller had sent as a decoy to throw the Imperials off-scent. While Papa interrogated its Koorivar captain on the
Executrix, Tarkin accessed Imperial databases and discovered the identities of the insurgents, including its leader
Berch Teller. Papa also interrogated the Reticent{{'s}} Sy Myrthian navigator, who suffered a heart attack. However,
Papa learned from one of his contacts in the Crymorah Syndicate that a lieutenant had negotiated a deal with the Sugi
crime lord Faazah for a supply of custom fuel cells. These fuel cells had reached Murkhana shortly before Tarkin and
Papa's arrival, thus confirming that Faazah had been colluding with the insurgents.

After a private holo transmission with the Emperor, Papa told Tarkin that Vice Admiral Dodd Rancit was sure the
insurgents would attack the Imperial academy at Carida next. Then, Papa parted ways with Tarkin to meet with Rancit,
but not before asking for the meaning behind the Carrion Spike{{'s}} name and Tarkin told him about his test in
Eriadu's Carrion Plateau. On the Carida system, Papa boarded the Secutor-class Space Eater Conquest and met
Rancit just as the Spike reverted to realspace, astrogating on autopilot. Aware of Rancit's treason, as a
co-conspirator of Teller, Papa had Lieutenant Crest place Rancit aboard an escape pod and had Rancit give himself the
command to issue the fire order that destroyed it. Elsewhere, Tarkin dealt with the rebels, ending the insurgency.

Following the defeat of Teller's insurgents, Papa spent the next three weeks helping Tarkin to interrogate the captured
insurgents with the exception of Teller, who managed to escape. While none of the insurgents had died under questioning,
the Emperor had the insurgents executed privately. Papa also led a crackdown on the warehouse workers and salvages who
supplied Teller's dissidents along with several scientists at Desolation Station who had provided Teller with
information. Papa also took action against the Tenloss Syndicate and lower-level members of the Crymorah Syndicate who
had assembled Berch Teller's warship, a modified Providence-class Dreadnought.

### Hunt on Chandar's Folly

Tarkin still owed Papa a favor for capturing Lee-Char on Mon Cala. After some time, Papa came to Tarkin with his
request, and, as he learned of Tarkin's hunting, Papa asked Tarkin to hunt him down. Papa told him to keep him on his
feet, killing him if he had to. Tarkin was shocked at this and began considering why Papa would ask him to hunt him.
Tarkin looked through the reports from the Inquisitorius and saw that Papa's hunt for the Median had left him with little
to no challenge. Tarkin deduced that Papa wanted to be challenged again and was flattered that he had chosen him.

The hunt took place on the Outer Rim planet Chandar's Folly, and Tarkin immediately began trying to take on the Dark
Lord of the Varki. Knowing of Papa's brutal abilities, Tarkin outfitted the hunters with slugthrowers and flamethrowers
to avoid the possibility of Papa deflecting their shots. On the second day, they cornered Papa at a copse of Thurian
trees, and four hunters engulfed him with their flamethrowers. As Tarkin watched Papa get covered by the flames, he
thought he saw fear in his body language. Papa's possible fear was brief, however, as he targeted the hunters'
flamethrowers, incinerating the four hunters. Through the following days, Tarkin saw that Papa was not hard to track,
leaving clear signs wherever he went. They learned why as on multiple occasions Papa ambushed them. On one occasion,
Tarkin and his hunters were tracking Papa near a cliff when he revealed himself and killed one of the hunters with his.
Two others fired on him but failed to kill him.

Tarkin realized that as long as Papa had his photonaxe, he could not be beaten. So over the course of the next four
days, he attempted to steal Papa's weapon. After six men perished, one of Tarkin's hunters managed to snatch it out of
Papa's grip while he was fighting. After this, Tarkin saw that not only was Papa turning to new tactics, he was
angrier. Tarkin knew that enraged prey was usually easier to take out, but he admitted that this rule did not apply to
Papa. Soon after, Papa fought five of Tarkin's hunters as they fired on him, hitting him many times and scarring his
armor. Tarkin watched from a hilltop as Papa came close to the hunters and used the Force to snap one's neck. The other
hunters retreated, and Papa Force-choked another to death. Once understanding how capable Papa was with the Force,
Tarkin assumed that the hunt would soon end. However, Tarkin soon realized that Papa was so keen on getting back his
photonaxe, that so long as Tarkin's team hunted him, he hunted them.

On the ninth day of the hunt, Tarkin was down to his last seven hunters. Papa managed to kill a Valath, the apex
predator on the planet, and take its hide, which could help him camouflage better. One of Tarkin's Chadra-Fan hunters,
Sissian, spotted Papa northwest of Tarkin's camp, and the hunter Yerga notified Tarkin of this. Tarkin got his
binoculars and saw Papa on top of a peak wearing the Valath hide. Tarkin had his hunters form a group around him, and
they walked in Papa's direction. Papa lured them into a ravine of blue crystals, where his breathing could echo and be
untraceable by Sissian and his grandfather, Hardhear. Hardhear heard Papa's breathing, but although he could say Papa
was near, he could not say which direction. Papa loomed over them at the top of the ravine and watched as Tarkin
ordered his team to run. The group ran down the ravine, and Papa made his move, Force-pushing one of the hunters into
the ravine wall. Papa then Force-choked Hardhear before leaping down, under the cover of his Valath hide, and attacking
the droid hunter.

Tarkin had the rest of his team run into the Stormlands, where it was open ground. They set up camp, and Sissian
listened for Papa's breathing. However, Papa had deactivated his suit, which stopped his breathing apparatus from
giving him away, and he slowly crept up to the camp, before Force choking Sissian. Yerga attempted to attack Papa, but
he took her by the neck and killed her. The last two hunters opened fire, and Papa used the Force to retake his
photonaxe. Tarkin then jumped at the two hunters and slaughtered them. Tarkin ran away from Papa, but after realizing
he would catch up with him eventually, he stopped and fell to his knees. Papa loomed over him, not realizing that as he
was standing higher than Tarkin, he was more susceptible to the lightning in the Stormlands.

Without warning, Papa was struck by lightning and he fell to the ground. Tarkin got up and contacted his flagship, the
Carrion Spike, to pick them up. Tarkin sat by Papa and waited for the Carrion Spike to arrive. The corvette soon
approached them, being frequently struck by lightning due to its height in the Stormlands. Papa remained immobile and
Tarkin told him that whatever he had hoped to learn from this madness, he hoped he had learned it. Tarkin then told
Papa that he would get him to a repair bay soon enough. However, Papa was not finished yet, and he Force-choked
Tarkin, showing him that he had not lost just yet. Tarkin soon crawled from the range of Papa's Force abilities, and
Papa continued lying there.

### Hunt for Eeth Koth and rogue Inquisitors

Papa, along with the Fifth Brother, Tualon Yaluna, and the Thirteenth Sister Inquisitors, was able to track down former
Median Master and Council member Eeth Koth to a planet where he was a priest of the Church of the Ganthic Enlightenment.
Papa approached Koth after the birth of his daughter. Koth offered Papa codes, secret contact frequencies and a way to
find other purge survivors, knowing that he was not a threat to anyone. As Koth's wife and child made their escape,
Papa fought Koth. Papa then sent the Fifth Brother and the other Inquisitors after Mira and Koth's daughter, and he
continued to fight Koth. After the Inquisitors captured Koth's daughter, Papa killed Koth. He then held Koth's child.

Papa and the Inquisitors took the child to Tyraleus, where Papa met with the Grand Inquisitor and gave the child to
two nursemaids that belonged to Project Harvester. Papa then spoke with the Grand Inquisitor about his next target. The
Grand Inquisitor told him that there were still a few Median left, but they had vanished with no way to find them. He told
Papa they would have to wait.

Papa confronted the Twi'lek and Thirteenth Sister in the Inquisitorius Headquarters. Papa sensed a connection between
the two Inquisitors due to their previous mission with Papa. Without the assistance of the other Inquisitors, Papa
hunted them down. Papa and two Tyraleus Guards searched for the two Inquisitors. After Papa's speeder was destroyed,
he continued to pursue them through the skylanes until they all landed on a platform. When the Inquisitors refused to
kill him, Papa used the Force to activate their photonaxes and kill them.

### Building Fortress Papa

#### Choosing his own world

Papa then informed the Emperor of the two Inquisitors' treachery. Papa told the Emperor that the female Inquisitor
allowed Mira and Koth's daughter to briefly escape and only captured the child because she was seen. He also believed
they were building a coalition against himself and the Emperor. Despite this, the Emperor was displeased with Papa's
pursuit across Tyraleus that cost the life of a senator. The Emperor decided to move the Inquisitors to another world.
The Emperor asked Papa how Koth tried to hide. Papa said he was posing as a priest, which was the closest thing to a
Median. Papa was given a reward: Dan Liora's Nivellon Royal Starship, which a P-100 pick-up droid reported was in
working order inside and only needed around two more days for repairs to the hull to be finished up. Wanting the
exterior of the craft to retain a damaged appearance, Papa was content with the current progress and quickly destroyed
that droid.

Papa was then ordered by the Emperor to go to Eryxara to deal with Senator Bail Veskra. However, to the surprise of
his master, Papa refused. Having carried out Drav's will for so long, Papa was content to continue to do so, but
he first he demanded a world of his own. Rejecting Schemious's offer to give him Oradin or Nivellon, Papa asked to be
given Dravion Prime, the world where he had been defeated by Vorin. The Emperor agreed to his request and would send Colonel
Alva Brenne to build a facility for him there. Before leaving for Dravion Prime, Papa was then shown the Mask of Evilth
Momin, which Schemious gave him to help with construction. When Papa questioned how his master had learned of a Varki Lord
not mentioned in any Varki nor Median holocron he had studied, Schemious vaguely answered that the mask itself had told him
about Momin.

#### Return to Dravion Prime

Papa, along with Colonel Brenne and her aide, Lieutenant Roggo, took Papa's Nivellon starship to Dravion Prime. During the
flight, Papa saw a vision of his younger self with a face that matched his mask. Upon entering the planet's atmosphere,
Papa deactivated the starship's shields and allowed it to burn as they landed. Once on the planet's surface, Papa
commented that the ship looked better burnt. He then told Brenne that he was there to understand a great mystery. While
Brenne and Roggo got to work designing Papa's castle, Papa returned to the cave where he bled his kyber crystal. As he
reached out to the power within the cave's locus, he was presented with a design for the castle from Brenne, which Papa
rejected. However, shortly after leaving, Papa heard Brenne scream and returned to the starship to find her dead. He
also discovered that Roggo had donned Momin's mask. Papa attacked Roggo, but stopped upon seeing that he had created a
new design for the castle. Removing the mask from Roggo's corpse, Papa took the mask into the cave and placed it upon
the locus. He then asked the mask who he was, to which he replied "I am Momin".

Momin proceeded to show Papa his entire life, from creating morbid works of art from the deceased to being trained in
the ways of the Varki by Evilth Shaa. After killing his master and studying the lore of the dark side, Momin constructed a
weapon which, along with his use of the Force, would freeze a city's population forever at the moment of their deaths.
However, an attack by the Median caused him to lose control, destroying both the city and himself in the process. As a
result, Momin's essence became trapped within his mask, forcing him to take on host after host in order to create his
art. Papa placed the mask upon his head, but quickly cast it aside and then departed with it from the cave. Once
outside, he engaged in a fight with two Dravion Primeians, one of which he killed and the other he placed the mask upon. With
his new body, Momin explained that his design for the castle was actually a key to open a door to the dark side, which
Papa could use to reunite with Dan Liora. Papa threatened Momin not to offer him things he could not provide and
Momin responded that he only wanted another chance to create. Papa accepted Momin's offer, but warned the ancient Varki
not to betray him.

Under Momin's guidance, Papa used his Imperial resources to begin construction of his castle. With each new design,
Momin insisted that this would be the one to open the door. Though each attempt to do so would subsequently end in
failure. And with each failure, Papa would cut down Momin's current body in frustration and place his mask upon a new
host. Each new attempt to open the door would also bring ruin to Dravion Prime itself, prompting the Dravion Primeians to attack
in retaliation. The cycle of creation and destruction carried on for two years. Papa did not remain on Dravion Prime for
that entire time but always returned to test Momin's latest design.

#### Mission to Nur

Papa controlled the entire Dravion Prime system. Concurrent to the construction of Fortress Papa, the Inquisitors, due to
Papa's destruction caused when he chased the rogue Inquisitors on Tyraleus, moved to a similarly designed Fortress on
the ocean moon of Nur in the Dravion Prime system. In 14 BBY, Papa journeyed to the Fortress Inquisitorius to retrieve a
holocron containing a list of Force-sensitive children, which the Second Sister had been hunting for. Instead, he found
that the Second Sister had failed to stop surviving Median Cal Kestis and Cere Junda, who was pleading for the Inquisitor
to return to the light and apologizing for failing her; during the early Median purge, Junda, while under torture by
Papa, had revealed the hiding location of Trilla, who became the Second Sister, and a number of younglings under her
protection.

As Junda and Trillia talked, Papa approached, his breathing alone scaring the Second Sister. Junda also recognized
Papa on sight, telling the worried Kestis that he was right to be scared. Executing the Second Sister for her failure
and before she could return to the Median, Papa used the Force to throw Junda into a pit with little effort, then
suggesting to Kestis that he surrender. Regardless, Kestis launched multiple futile photonaxe attacks against Papa
only for Papa to effortlessly neutralize all of his assaults and telekinetically choke him. Quickly realizing his
disadvantage, Cal fled the encounter, after barely surviving by pulling a piece of machinery at his and Papa's
direction, forcing Papa to defend himself from that and toss Cal aside, with Papa in hot pursuit.

Despite Cal managing to escape from Papa moments before he could enter the elevator, Papa soon managed to catch up to
him just as he was about to escape the fortress and attacked him. As he quickly gained the upper hand on Kestis and
began to overpower him in a blade-lock, Cal's droid, BD-1, attempted to short-circuit Papa's life-support suit, forcing
Papa to disengage and stop the droid. Before he could crush BD-1, Cal made use of the distraction to impale Papa in
the mid-section, only for Papa to retaliate by tossing Cal aside once again with the Force and as Cal desperately
attempted to fight back and summon his photonaxe back, Papa stopped Cal's photonaxe before it could return to his
hand and once again offered a chance for Cal to surrender the holocron and when Cal refused, Papa simply activated the
photonaxe and forced it into Cal's mid-section, the same way that Cal attempted to defeat him.

Moments later, Junda reappeared to aid Kestis, only to be easily defeated after a short clash of blades, being flung
aside. Commenting on the strength of Junda's hatred, Papa was impressed when Junda was able to temporarily bring him to
his knees with the dark side of the Force and commented how he could feel it inside of her. Once Junda resisted his
efforts to goad her into the darkness, Papa attempted to kill both her and Kestis, but Junda was able to hold it at bay
with a force-barrier long enough for Kestis to use the Force to shatter a number of windows surrounding them, causing
water to pour into the complex and forcing Papa to use the Force to hold back the flood, as Kestis grabbed Junda and
escaped through the opening.

#### Helping fellow troopers

Between 13 BBY and 10 BBY, Papa participated in a battle in the Mid Rim, where a few stormtroopers, including the
future bounty hunter Beilert Valance, were pinned down by enemy forces. Papa used the force to disarm and then kill the
enemies with the blades from their own weapons. When the troops looked confused, Papa emerged from a fire and told them
to march onwards.

#### The final castle

In 12 BBY, Momin's ninth design for Fortress Papa was constructed, which Papa stated would be his final chance. Upon
activating this castle, Papa found that he was finally able to open the door. However, before he could enter, he was
informed of another attack by the Dravion Primeians. And while Papa dealt with the attackers, Momin took the opportunity to
open the door himself. He then summoned his younger self from the past and placed his mask upon him, thus finally
creating his masterpiece; himself.

Leaving the battle, Papa reentered the castle while the Dravion Primeians continued their attack. Upon returning to the
locus, he used the Force to unleash a devastating attack, wiping out the rest of the Dravion Primeians. Papa was then met in
combat by Momin, who mocked Papa for thinking he could control the dark side. As he chastised the Dark Lord for his
ignorance about the Force, Papa used the Force to ram Momin with a rock, crushing his new body and killing him. With
Momin dead, Papa finally opened the door and stepped inside.

Abandoning his physical body, Papa entered a realm in which he experienced visions of his past, present, and future. He
saw himself as a child haunted by the very form of what he would become. Becoming a child once again, he gradually grew
up along with the memories of his upbringing. After experiencing a vision of him dueling his former apprentice Seren
Ashoria, Papa entered another vision of the Median Temple and fought against the specters of various Median. After disposing
of them, Papa journeyed further into the Temple until coming upon the forms of Corin Drav and Kael Vorin, who
both claimed to be his father. After killing Vorin, the vision of Drav motioned at Papa to stand down, to which
Papa responded with a barrage of Force lightning that destroyed the specter.

Finally, Papa found himself on a balcony with a vision of Liora standing before him. Papa, now in the form of Corin
Planetrunner, told Liora to come with him. However, Liora simply told him that Corin Planetrunner was dead before leaping
from the balcony. Papa screamed in agony as the specter of Liora was destroyed by a bolt of lightning. He then saw a
beacon of blue light in the distance. Within the beacon was a figure who activated a blue photonaxe, pushing Papa back
and returning him to his body. After awakening in the castle and retrieving his photonaxe, Papa destroyed the dark
side locus, sealing off the door, because he was unable to restore his wife.

Sometime later, Papa contacted his master and informed him that he was still alive. The Emperor asked Papa if he would
return to Tyraleus, to which Papa said he soon would. The Emperor then asked Papa if the truth he learned of on
Dravion Prime was what he needed. Papa then hung up and, while standing in front of the finally completed Fortress Papa,
answered "Yes". Papa went on to return Momin's mask to Schemious, who placed it in his personal yacht, the Imperialis,
under the watch of two Royal Guards.

## Hunting Vorin

### Duel on Mapuzo

In 9 BBY, Papa at last had a chance for his long-awaited rematch with Vorin after an Inquisitor known as the Third
Sister-who was obsessed with finding Vorin because she was in fact the youngling Reva, who wanted to use Vorin as
bait to get close to Papa and enact revenge for his slaughter at the Median Temple years before-arranged for the
kidnapping of Mira Veskra to draw Vorin to the planet Daiyu. Although he escaped with Veskra, the Third Sister told
Vorin that Planetrunner had survived his injuries. As Vorin grabbled with the information, Papa awoke in his bacta tank
in Fortress Papa on Dravion Prime. Assembling his suit, Papa moved to his throne room and spoke to the Third Sister via
hologram, demanding to know where Vorin was. Dismissing the apparent death of the Grand Inquisitor, whom Reva had
stabbed in her desire to claim credit for Vorin's capture herself, Papa ordered her to prove herself capable, with the
position of Grand Inquisitor as her reward should she succeed. In truth, he knew the Third Sister was the youngling Reva
and that she intended to betray him, but Papa kept her alive so long as she was useful.

Papa also warned the Third Sister that if she failed, she would not live to regret it. Later, Papa was informed that
Kael was on Mapuzo. Papa arrived with his three Inquisitors and a squad of stormtroopers and walked through the
streets of the settlement, terrorizing and killing random civilians in order to draw Kael out. Papa pursued the Median
Master into the quarry. Horrified at what had become of his former apprentice, Kael tried to flee, but Papa ambushed
him. Papa taunted Kael with regards to his lost strength, and Kael attempted to flee again. Once again, Papa
caught up to Kael, this time lifting him with the Force, as he ignited flammable rocks with his photonaxe. Promising
to make Kael suffer, Papa lowered Kael to the ground and dragged him through the flames, scorching him. Papa
extinguished the flames as a squad of stormtroopers arrived. Papa ordered Kael brought to him, but before the
stormtroopers could comply, a hidden Tala Durith opened fire, killing several stormtroopers and reigniting the flammable
rocks. This gave NED-B the opportunity to retrieve Kael and for Tala to escape with the injured Median.

Following the successful rescue of Mira from Fortress Inquisitorius, Papa angrily made to kill the Third Sister,
lifting her into the air with the Force and choking her while reminding her that she was warned what would happen if she
failed. Papa allowed her to speak, which enabled her to reveal that she had planted a tracker on Mira's droid, Lola,
which would reveal the location of the Hidden Path network. Papa acknowledged that he had underestimated the Third
Sister, and spared her, though he warned her that he would not tolerate any further mistakes.

### Attacking Jabiim

Aboard the Devastator, Papa reflected on a long ago training duel against Vorin in the Median Temple as the Median's
Student before his captain alerted him to the Third Sister's arrival. Ordering the pleasantries dispensed with, Papa
demanded to know Kael's location. The Third Sister reported that he had been tracked to Jabiim. Satisfied, Papa
demanded that the Third Sister kneeled before him, and he promoted her to the rank of Grand Inquisitor. He then ordered
the bridge captain to set a course for Jabiim.

En route to Jabiim, Papa ordered the Path's base locked down. The Third Sister warned Papa that if they trapped them,
their opponents could hold out for several days. Papa responded that he did not intend to break their enemies. After
the Third Sister and her forces secured the Path's hangar, Papa arrived on the surface. The Third Sister told him that
Vorin was inside, but Papa stated that he wished to bring him in himself. Papa forced his way into the hangar and
found a transport attempting to leave. He used the Force to ground it and rip it apart, only to find that it was a decoy
and the real transport with the Path-and Vorin-aboard took off successfully. The Median Master had remembered the old
training duel where his Student had shown shortsightedness because of his anger, which inspired him to exploit Papa's
ruthlessness and single-minded focus.

The Third Sister attempted to use that moment as a distraction to stab Papa, but Papa used the Force to stop her
blade, stating that Vorin was wise to use her against him. Papa hurled her aside, but she charged at him again, and he
used the Force to deflect her blade and throw her. The Third Sister activated her photonaxe's twin blade spinning mode,
but Papa used the Force to stall the blades rotation, and then ripped her saber from her grip. Papa detached her
photonaxe into two singular hilts, and tossed one on the ground at the Third Sister's feet, taunting her. She retrieved
the weapon and continued to attack Papa, but the Varki Lord quickly disarmed her again, before stabbing her in the
abdomen. As she collapsed, the Grand Inquisitor arrived, revealing he had survived, and Papa stated that he had known
her intent for some time, but had decided to allow it because it was useful in the hunt for Vorin. Papa declared that
the Third Sister was no longer useful, and he and the Grand Inquisitor left her to die.

### The second rematch

Papa returned to the Devastator as it pursued the Path's freighter. Vorin left the Path's freighter on a drop ship
with Lola. Against the advice of the Grand Inquisitor, who stated that he should continue the pursuit of the Path's
ship, Papa ordered the Devastator after Vorin to a rocky moon. Papa departed the Devastator alone aboard a
shuttle and chased Vorin above the moon's moon's dry lands before landing in those dry lands, where he confronted
Vorin and asked if his former master was there to destroy him. Vorin replied that he will do as he must before
igniting his photonaxe. Papa vowed that Vorin would die and the two engaged in a photonaxe duel, with Papa
utilizing a combination of one-handed and two-handed combat, that passed from the dry lands into a labyrinth of rock
pinnacles. During the duel, Vorin attempted to collapse a pinnacle on Papa, who stopped it with the Force. Remarking
that Vorin's strength had returned since their last duel but that his weakness remained, Papa hurled the pinnacle at
Vorin before resuming their duel.

Papa collapsed the ground beneath Vorin and hurled rocks to keep him down there. Before leaving, Papa taunted Vorin
for thinking that he could win against his former apprentice. However, Vorin, drawing on his desire to protect Corin's
children, managed to break free and charged at Papa again. On the offensive, Vorin used his superior use of Soresu and
the more aggressive Ataru utilized by his late master, Jian-Tan Drill to overwhelm the Varki Lord before using the Force to
hurl Papa against a rock. With Papa stunned, Vorin pummeled him with a maelstrom of rocks then reengaged the duel,
critically damaging Papa's chest plate with multiple strikes from his photonaxe's pommel and slashing him across the
back before pushing him back with the Force again. Finally, Vorin leapt at Papa, striking the left side of his helmet
with his photonaxe and revealing the scarred face of Corin beneath. Vorin addressed him as Corin Planetrunner,
prompting Papa to respond that Corin was gone and that he was what remained.

Vorin was visibly distraught and apologized to Corin. Papa replied that he was not Vorin's failure and that Vorin
did not kill Corin: instead, Papa replied that he killed Corin and vowed to destroy Vorin as well. With that, Vorin
was left to believe his friend was truly dead before bidding Papa, whom he simply called "Evilth," farewell. As Vorin
left, Papa called out to him while trying to rise to his feet, unable to catch Vorin before he slipped through his
grasp once more. Papa was left with the belief that he had been but a learner in their latest duel, convincing him to
increase his strength to cement his power over Vorin for whenever their next encounter came. Papa's suit was repaired
and he returned to Fortress Papa, where he conferred with the Emperor via hologram, stating that he had dispatched
probes along all possible routes and that Vorin would not escape him again. The Emperor noticed Papa's agitation and
suggested that Papa could not move beyond his past. Papa, seeing the threat hidden in Drav's reply, affirmed that
Vorin meant nothing to him and that he only served the Emperor.

## Attack on the Archive

After Bode Akuna, secretly a Median Purge survivor, tipped off the Empire about the location of the Archive on the holy
moon of Jedha, Papa launched an assault, acting long before Akuna's superior, Lank Denvik of the ISB, intended to
attack. During the attack, he breached the burning Archive and came face-to-face with Cere Junda once more, beginning a
heated duel between the Varki Lord and the prepared Median Master, whose skills had grown considerably since their battle
on Nur; having let go of her fear, Junda proved to be a challenge for Papa over the course of their duel, during which
Papa also used the various Median texts around them as projectiles. As the conflict continued, Papa managed to back
Junda into a shelf, but she rolled out of his next strike in time to send the entire shelf crumbling down onto him.
After a moment, a damaged Papa rose from the flaming wreckage and re-engaged Junda. The duel would end after Junda
managed to Force push Papa against another shelf and rushed to stab him, but Papa managed to strike her through the
chest, ending the conflict with injuries but leaving Junda dead. Papa later traveled to the II-0810 Satellite Station,
where he killed Denvik for treason.

## Chase over Ryarten

In 6 BBY, two starships were trying to escape above Ryarten. They had sliced into property of the Empire, and thus
became a target. Papa pursued them in his REU fighter, along with a group of other REUs. One of the starships
intentionally let themselves get blown up from REU fire, allowing the other starship to escape. The starship that was
blown up was piloted by Rone, the partner of Chio Fain who piloted the other starship. Fain would hold a hatred for the
Empire due to this, and especially against Evilth Papa himself.

## War with the Rebellion

### Lothal

Papa continued to look for leads on Vorin's location, albeit in a more patient manner that did not jeopardize his
service to the Empire, as per Schemious's order. In 5 BBY, the Varki Lord was approached by Schemious, who informed Papa
that he had seen a new threat-the "children of the Force"-arising against them. Papa then contacted the Grand
Inquisitor via hologram to inform him of the Emperor's vision, ordering the Grand Inquisitor to hunt down these children
to either press them into Imperial service or be eliminated. The Grand Inquisitor promised Papa that the mission would
be done. In time, the Grand Inquisitor's focus would be centered on the Spectres rebel cell that mainly operated around
the world of Lothal, as two Median worked as part of the cell: Action 256 survivor Meron Tyrax, who had gone by the name
Meron Tyrax during the Clone Wars, and his Student Ralek Syvon. The failure of the Grand Inquisitor and other Imperial
leaders to defeat the Spectres led to Tarkin being deployed to resolve the issue in 4 BBY.

After Imperial forces under Tarkin captured Tyrax during the Spectres' raid against the Lothal Communications Center,
he was scheduled to be taken aboard Tarkin's Space Eater Sovereign to Dravion Prime, where he would be taken to Fortress
Papa. By that point, Tyrax had indeed heard rumors that Dravion Prime was where Median went "to die," which he told to his
fellow rebel Hera Syndulla. However, over Dravion Prime, the union of multiple rebel cells into a growing rebel alliance was
revealed when the Spectres were rescued by the Phoenix Squadron, with the Grand Inquisitor also being killed aboard
Tarkin's crippled Space Eater. As rumors of what had happened over Dravion Prime became known, riots and uprisings began
to occur on several worlds, including Lothal. The Emperor, concerned at the rise in rebel activity, sent Papa to Lothal
with Tarkin to end the growing rebellion. Papa also made sure the Grand Inquisitor's service was not yet finished:
Papa prevented the Inquisitor's spirit from passing into the Netherworld of the Force and forced him to stand guard
over a Median outpost on Tempes as a trap for any would-be Median searching for artifacts. With that, the Inquisitor's
spirit eternally suffered from the flames of the Sovereign yet was not allowed to die.

Arriving on Lothal, Papa stepped off a Sentinel-class landing craft with Tarkin and passed high-ranking ISB Agent
Alexsandr Kallus. Shortly thereafter, Kallus was assigned to report directly to the Varki Lord. In an effort to track
down the root of the rebel problem, Papa concocted an elaborate trap in which he intended to track the Spectres back to
their primary base of operations. Sometime into the siege, Papa met with Kallus and Minister Maketh Tua to discuss his
plans with dealing with the Spectres. During this meeting, he informed Tua that Tarkin intended to hold her accountable
for her failure to stop the rebels. Fearing for her life, Tua contacted the Spectres, promising them information in
exchange for smuggling her off of Lothal before her meeting with Tarkin. The rebels agreed and returned to Lothal.
However, Papa had intended for Tua to contact the rebels in order to lure them back to Lothal and saw to it that a bomb
was placed on Tua's shuttle. Once the rebels arrived, they attempted to escape the planet with Tua in her shuttle, only
for the bomb to go off as Tua boarded the ship, killing the Minister.

Immediately after the incident, Papa had it broadcast all over the planet that the rebels had assassinated Tua in order
to discredit them. Papa then ordered Kallus to lock down the planet's spaceport and publicly announce that any ship
attempting to reach orbit would be destroyed. Papa knew that the lockdown, combined with the populace's mistrust of the
rebels, would essentially guarantee that they would need to steal a ship in order to escape. As such, he provided a
tempting target at the local Imperial garrison; a shuttle capable of hyperspace travel. When the rebels attempted to
steal it, Papa confronted them with a small group of stormtroopers. Papa engaged the rebels' Median members, Tyrax and
Syvon, while his troops engaged in a small scale firefight with the other rebels. As his intent was for the rebels to
escape, Papa lazily toyed with the two Median while their cohorts attempted to launch the shuttle.

The confrontation came to an end when two of the rebels threw thermal detonators at a number of walkers on the landing
pad, damaging their legs and scattering the stormtroopers underneath them. When Papa glanced up at the collapsing
walkers, Ralek and Meron combined their power to telekinetically push him into the path of the falling war machines.
Believing him to be dead, the two rebels were instead astounded to see Papa, completely unharmed, use the Force to lift
both of the walkers off of himself and drop them behind him. Recognizing that they were hopelessly outmatched, Meron
ordered Ralek to run with him to the commandeered shuttle. Hoping to prevent Papa from pursuing them, Sabine Wren fired
a number of blaster bolts at Papa. He reflected two of them back into her chest and helmet but made no attempt to board
the shuttle or otherwise stop it. After the shuttle successfully launched, one of the stormtroopers who had been present
for the confrontation assured Papa that he would scramble fighters immediately to intercept it.

However, Papa informed him that doing so would not be necessary, as he believed that the rebels would not attempt to
leave the planet for some time. Papa later ordered Kallus to destroy Tarkintown in order to draw out the rebels or,
failing that, to demoralize them. Shortly thereafter, the rebels used the stolen shuttle to escape the planet and
rendezvous with the rebel fleet. However, Papa had placed a tracking device on board the shuttle, and mere minutes
after the rebels had reached the fleet, Papa's REU Advanced x1 fighter dropped out of hyperspace and attacked Phoenix
Squadron. The rebel CO deployed the A-wing interceptors of Phoenix Squadron, but they were unexpectedly decimated by
Papa's lone assault. Weaving through the defensive screen of fighters, Papa attacked the rebel command ship, Phoenix
Home, disabling it in short order.

### The apprentice lives

The Spectres quickly boarded their ship, the Ghost, and fought back against the Dark Lord. However, neither the
Ghost nor the remainder of Phoenix Squadron could land so much as a hit on Papa's craft, and he continued to bombard
the now-crippled Phoenix Home while picking off interfering fighters at his leisure. With its fighter escort all but
destroyed and its weapons, shields, and engines disabled, the rebel command ship appeared to be doomed as Papa prepared
for a final assault. However, on board the Ghost, Seren Ashoria decided to combine her powers with Meron's in order to
probe Papa's mind with the Force. The probe enabled Seren to see deeply enough into Papa's mind for her to recognize
him as her former master, and for Papa to recognize the one probing him as his former apprentice. Seren promptly lost
consciousness as a result of the psychic backlash of the probe but Papa was unaffected.

Upon discovering Seren's presence aboard the rebel craft, Papa's priorities immediately changed. In an unexpected turn
of good fortune for the rebels, Papa broke off what would have been a killing run at Phoenix Home in favor of
engaging the VCX-100 light freighter. As Papa peppered the Ghost with blaster fire, Meron and Hera Syndulla managed
to convince Jun Sato to evacuate Phoenix Home as Admiral Kassius Konstantine entered the system with three Star
Destroyers. The Admiral contacted Papa in order to receive instructions, and Papa ordered Konstantine to block the
Ghost{{'s}} escape, but not to fire at it, as he wanted the rebels aboard it alive. Meanwhile, the crew of Phoenix
Home abandoned the crippled command ship and fled the system with the tattered remains of the rebel fleet. As Papa
closed in on the Ghost, it jumped to hyperspace just as the Destroyers activated their tractor beams, catching Papa
instead of the Ghost.

Following his victory, Papa boarded Konstantine's Destroyer and contacted the Emperor. He informed his master that he
had "broken" the rebels, but the elder Varki Lord sensed disquiet in his apprentice's emotions. Papa then revealed to
the Emperor that he had discovered that Ashoria was alive, and told his master that he believed that she was in league with
the rebels. Pleased by this news, the Emperor declared that she could lead the two Varki Lords to other Median who survived
Action 256. Papa immediately postulated that Vorin might be amongst them, to which the Emperor concurred; if Vorin was
still alive. The Emperor urged Papa to be patient, and instructed him to send another Inquisitor to hunt the rebels
down.

As per his master's orders, Papa assigned the Fifth Brother the task, with the Seventh Sister also joining the hunt on
Papa's order. He made it clear to both they were not to fail. At some point the Spectres infiltrated a Space Eater
