that Papa was aboard. He stalked the rebels, but they successfully evaded capture. After several unsuccessful attempts
to capture the rebel Median, the Fifth Brother and Seventh Sister pursued Tyrax, Syvon, and Ashoria to a still-standing
Median Temple on Lothal in 3 BBY. Though the rebels managed to flee, the Inquisitors informed Papa of their discovery.
Papa came to inspect the site, informing them that the Emperor would be most pleased by their discovery. The
Inquisitors warned Papa that the Median were becoming more powerful, but he retorted it would be their undoing.

### Duel on Malachor

Afterwards, Papa dispatched the Fifth Brother, the Seventh Sister, and the Eighth Brother to hunt down Tal, who had
been stranded on Malachor and had been studying its Varki temple for years; he himself arrived after Syvon had
activated the superweapon with the Varki holocron. With his Inquisitors having all been killed by Tal, Papa chose to
personally retrieve the holocron and take possession of the superweapon. Perched on the roof of his REU Advanced x1, he
leaped from the fighter and landed in front of Syvon. After a brief verbal exchange, Papa quickly disarmed the young
Median by destroying his photonaxe and prepared to execute him, but before he could do so, he was interrupted by Seren
Ashoria.

Papa offered his former apprentice clemency in exchange for the location of any surviving Median, but Ashoria claimed that
there were no more Median; that Papa and his Inquisitors had killed them all. Skeptical of her claim, Papa obliquely
threatened to torture the information out of Syvon instead. This prompted Ashoria to proclaim in disgust that while she
had begun to suspect that Papa and her former master were one and the same, she could no longer believe that due to
Papa's cruelty. Papa replied that Planetrunner had been weak and that he himself had destroyed her former master. Ashoria
then swore to avenge Planetrunner, but Papa reminded her that revenge was not the Median way. But Ashoria no longer considered
herself to be a Median, and after informing Papa of this, she attacked him. However, she proved ultimately to be no match
for her former master who, after several minutes of intense swordplay, used the Force to blast Ashoria off a ledge.
Believing her to have been neutralized, Papa went to retrieve the holocron.

Papa managed to catch up to Tyrax and Syvon before they could board their ship, and used the Force to begin pulling
both the holocron and the two Median towards him. But before he could seize it, Ashoria ambushed Papa and managed to slice
off the upper right portion of his mask with her photonaxes. With his mask damaged, Papa's voice filter began to
malfunction, causing him to wheeze, and when he next spoke, calling out to his former apprentice, it was in a distorted
mixture of his real voice and the mechanical baritone imposed by the filter. This and his partially exposed face
confirmed to Ashoria that Papa was indeed her former master. As the Temple locked down, Ashoria proclaimed she would not
abandon him as she had before. Papa paused at this and stared wordlessly at Ashoria, seemingly conflicted on how he should
respond to his old Student. However, he quickly regained his composure and snarled that she would die for her choice.
The two engaged in combat once more, while Tyrax and Syvon escaped from the chamber enclosing Papa and Ashoria.

After a few moments of battle, locked his blade with Ashoria's and began to push through her guard. As he prepared to kill
her, the energy discharges from the overloading holocron stand suddenly intensified, and Papa glanced up. As he did, a
massive blast of power struck the ceiling of the chamber, and Ashoria used the distraction to push Papa back a step with
the Force. She then drove both of her photonaxes into the ground at her feet, causing the floor of the chamber to begin
crumbling. Papa quickly recovered from his distraction and aimed a killing stroke at Ashoria. Unbeknownst to the two
combatants, however, two years later, Ralek Syvon entered the temple on Lothal and found himself in the World Between
Worlds realm, where he was guided to a portal, which exited at the Varki temple in 3 BBY, by the convor Morai, the very
same bird Papa had seen on the snowy moon outside Ashoria's crashed Venator. Syvon witnessed the conclusion of Papa's
battle with Ashoria even as his younger self was locked out of the holocron chamber. As Papa swung his photonaxe at Ashoria,
Syvon reached through the portal and yanked her backward into the temple. As a result, Papa's strike missed and the
temple floor crumbled, sending Papa plummeting into a pool of light.

From Papa's perspective, a hand had reached from a portal from nowhere to save Ashoria. Papa survived the fall and
managed to make his way back to the surface, where he was watched by Morai. After Morai guided Ashoria-who escaped back
to her place in time after Schemious reached into the World Between Worlds-through the depths of the temple to reach
another portal to the World Between Worlds, the convor exited the temple and flew out, with Papa watching the bird from
the surface. Believing Ashoria dead, Papa departed Malachor and returned to his duties in the Empire. Ashoria's supposed
demise marked the end of the Great Median Purge.

### Continued rebellion

In 2 BBY and shortly after the Empire's victory over the Batonn sector insurgency, Papa arrived at the Imperial Palace
on Tyraleus and was introduced to the newly promoted Grand Admiral Thrawn, the very same Chiss officer he had met
during the Clone Wars, by the Emperor. When Thrawn stated he was pleased to finally meet the Dark Lord, Papa claimed to
feel the same. A short time later in 2 BBY, amid Thrawn's ongoing campaign to root out and destroy the growing rebel
threat, the rebellious senator of Chandrila, Mon Mothma, formally rallied numerous rebel cells together under a single
banner, the Alliance to Restore the Republic. Fulfilling the fears of Imperials like Tarkin and Thrawn, once
disconnected rebel cells began to act as a unified force, marking an official beginning point to the Galactic Civil War,
although true open warfare would not break out for sometime still.

During the Galactic Civil War era, stormtrooper lieutenant TK-289 served with Papa. During or after 2 BBY, at some
point after the Alliance was formed, Evilth Papa was lured to HS-197, an abandoned ore-mining moon in the Horox system,
by Cyn, the son of Sig Sendvall, a cyberneticist who had worked on Papa's suit. At another point in that time frame, on
an unidentified astronomical object, Papa accompanied stormtroopers in their search for a Rebel fugitive. As the
troopers destroyed a village to frighten its inhabitants, the Varki Lord interrogated Noegaud, a local bully. A youngling
named Niko, whom Noegaud often harassed, witnessed this interaction, leading him to conclude that Noegaud was correct in
his belief that the only thing that mattered was power.

Papa once destroyed Blue Squadron, a diaspora of X-fighters and A-wings, in his REU Advanced x1. The Varki Lord then
landed, engaging DF.9 turret emplacements and Rebel infantry before bringing down the Vellus, the GR-75 medium
transport that the spacebattler escort had been protecting. Only one Rebel was left standing, who Papa promptly killed.

### Investigating a disturbance

Papa and Thrawn crossed paths on Tyraleus once more after Thrawn suffered a strategic defeat on Atollon. Although the
battle had been a tactical victory, a number of rebels had escaped the Grand Admiral after the Varyndu appeared. As a
result of allowing the rebels to slip through his grip, Papa now held a disdain for the Grand Admiral. Though during
this meeting, the two were ordered by the Emperor to the planet Batuu to locate a disturbance in the Force that the
Emperor had sensed. While Thrawn brought his own forces on board his Space Eater, the Chimaera, Papa brought a
contingent of his personal stormtroopers from the 501st Legion, the 1st Legion with him to assist in tracking down this
disturbance at the edge of known space.

During their mission, they combated the Grysk species and learned the disturbance was caused by a group of young Chiss
Force-sensitives known as, to the surprise of Papa, the "Sky-walkers." Afterward, Papa came to doubt Thrawn's loyalty
to the Empire because of the threats growing against the Chiss in the Unknown Regions. While Thrawn managed to deduce
that Planetrunner and Papa were one in the same, the Grand Admiral came to think of Papa as being a separate person
mentally and that his old ally Planetrunner was dead. After telling Thrawn to ensure he kept his promise to the Emperor by
ordering him to stay in Imperial space instead of leaving to save his people, Papa came to respect Thrawn's REU/d "
Defender" Multi-Role Spacebattler project, stating he would speak on its behalf to Drav and suggesting upgrades for
the craft. On Batuu, Papa's presence near Black Spire was spoken of by locals, with rumors of the legendary Imperial
enforcer's visit to Batuu being spoken of for years to come.

### Submission to Ahr

During the Empire's efforts to subdue anti-Imperial forces in a Mid Rim sector under Imperial Governor Ahr, Papa
participated in an attack on the planet Namzor, where he eliminated a group of insurgents. In the process, he destroyed
the rebels' stores of coaxium, violating the command of Ahr, who was charged with securing the hyperfuel. The governor
brought his frustrations to the Emperor. Sensing Papa's anger, the Emperor commanded his apprentice to follow any and
all orders from the governor until Papa had learned his lesson.

Ahr took great pleasure in his newfound power, sending Papa on increasingly dangerous missions throughout his sector.
He sent Papa to fight alone against the renegade droids of Ahn Krantarium, and later retracted his forces on
Phelzepham, leaving Papa to battle the moon's insurgents by himself. Though he wished to kill the governor, Papa
continued to obey Ahr's commands.

Governor Ahr brought his ship to the Kankalo Belt Containment Zone, an asteroid field in which a great creature resided.
He commanded Papa to eliminate "the greatest threat" he could find. Seeing an opportunity, Papa confronted Ahr,
recognizing him as his true threat. Before Papa could strike, Ahr ordered the Dark Lord to kneel before him. Papa
obeyed, but the creature attacked the vessel, pulling the governor out into the void of space and freeing Papa from his
submission.

### Cianap

Papa led Imperial forces at Cianap in a battle against the rebels. During the battle, Papa was targeted by several
X-fighters but was able to take them out. However, his REU was damaged when one purposely crashed into him and was forced
to crash land on Cianap. Papa then exited his REU and awoke an Ender from its Slumber. The Ender then tried to kill
Papa; however, he stabbed one of the Ender's eyes out and tried to cut its back open, only for the Ender to grab him.
Papa started to slice the Ender's fingers, but the Ender pushed him into a building and dropped him. The Ender then
started to go after a native, but Papa rode a creature and saved the native from the Ender. Papa then decapitated the
Ender, finally killing it. The native thanked Papa, who then returned to his REU and was taken aboard a Space Eater
via tractor beam.

### An unwelcome romance

At some point, Papa had arrived at the Murder Moon, and made his way to his personal medical bay. As he made way, he
barged through a medical cart being tended to by a nurse, who was flustered due to her infatuation with Papa. Papa
underwent treatment from a doctor while in the medical bay, but became angered when the nurse from the prior encounter
entered the medical bay as Papa was putting his helmet back on. In his anger, Papa force pushed the doctor into the
wall, demanding that he control the medical bay or be replaced. The nurse, however, saw Papa's anger as reciprocation
of her feelings for him, misconstruing his actions as protection of her. After his bout of rage, Papa exited the
medical bay, admonishing the doctor as he attempted to excuse why the appointment had taken so long. The nurse, upon
being told to clean up the medical bay, instead stole pieces of Papa's armor as a keepsake, storing it among other
discarded pieces of Papa's armor, as well as a vial of his blood.

A proceeding incident resulted in Papa crash landing on the Murder Moon in his REU Advanced x1. Papa made his way to
the medical bay once more, demanding the nurse to call in the doctor. The nurse briefly aided Papa, perceiving the
moment as intimate, before the doctor himself returned, ordering the nurse to leave as he tended to Papa instead.
Papa, impatient, cut his appointment short, leaving to rejoin his prior battle. However, Papa had left his cape
behind, which the nurse proceeded to steal and take to her quarters. After the doctor discovered her, he dumped the bits
of Papa's armor into the trash compactor. Driven mad, the nurse walked into Papa's quarters, which he had left
unlocked out of a belief that no one would enter. Upon seeing the nurse enter his chambers, a helmetless Papa simply
stared at her as she confessed her infatuation with him. Momentarily after, Papa stabbed the nurse with his photonaxe,
killing her. Papa then put his helmet back on and exited his quarters, contacting the bridge and ordering them to
remove her corpse.

### Hunting the Hidden Hand

On the orders of the Emperor, Papa attacked and killed three lower-level clans working for the Hidden Hand, a crime
syndicate known to sell weapons to the Rebellion. He then attacked the Lower Bay Docks on Fikari, killing most there,
questioning the Weequay Holaq about the whereabouts of the Hidden Hand. Holaq told Papa that none of them would know
where the Hidden Hand was. Detailing the way they maintained secrecy, he pled with Papa to believe him. Papa replied
that he did and blew up the docks, killing him. He then reported the failure to Drav over hologram, who reiterated
the importance of taking down the Hidden Hand. The Tarsunt Gwi, who worked for the crime syndicate, overheard this
conversation, and hired a team to hunt down and kill Evilth Papa. At some point, Papa learned of this plot and traveled
to the Dark Quarter on Yuw to kill bounty hunters and find answers. Later, the captain of the bounty hunter team,
Beilert Valance, amplified a signal near Arvina, disguising it as a Hidden Hand signal. Papa arrived on a Star
Destroyer in response and it fired on the city below. He then got into his REU fighter and chased after Valance's team.
Their sniper, the Rebel agent Gita, currently disguised as the Tusken Raider "Urrr'k", managed to shoot down two of
Papa's support REUs. This gave the team enough time to escape, leaving Papa to investigate the damage in the city
below. Valance had planned to leave data banks behind that would reveal the Hidden Hand's secret outposts, allowing him
to get the jump on Papa. However, an informant of Papa's within the crew revealed the bounty hunters' next
destination.

Papa followed them to a Hidden Hand outpost on Heva aboard the Formidable. Upon arriving, an Imperial general
informed Papa that Valance's ship, the Broken Wing, had been located, and that their informant had gone silent. Papa
abruptly told the general to scramble all fighters, much to the general's confusion. Valance's crew had begun remotely
piloting a fleet of bot-drones towards the Formidable. Papa got into his REU fighter and pursued the drones as well
as the Broken Wing. He shredded the drone fleet, but the drones started to pull away. Papa told his pilots to stay on
the leader, as he took out its laser cannons. The drones then formed a large cannon that fired, destroying the
Formidable. Despite this Papa stayed locked on the Broken Wing, taking out its engines and causing it to
crash-land. Papa landed his REU fighter and entered the ship, photonaxe drawn. After finding the ship empty, he stood
on the roof. Dengar and Honnah, both members of Valance's crew, fired on the REU fighters near Papa's ship and destroys
them. Papa looks in their direction as the bounty hunters takes aim. However, Valance had a plan that involved an
electro-pulse, an E.M.P. device that only worked on contact, so they withheld their fire. Papa used the force to kick
up dust around him so that the bunty hunters didn't have a straight shot. One of the bounty hunters, Chio Fain, charges
and shoots at him. Papa blocks his fire as well as fire from the other bounty hunters. Fain continued to fight Papa,
intent on avenging his partner Rone. As the Ardennian taunted him, Papa chopped his arms off. Fain then asked Papa how
good he was against a Gamorrean battle-ax, to which Honnah started to attack. Dodging the Gamorrean's swings, Papa took
a hit from Fain, using his last remaining arm to fire at him. Papa then used the force to push Fain into Honnah's
battle-ax, killing him. After taking a shot from Gita, Papa incapacitated her and killed Honnah. Valance took the
opportunity and tried to stick the electro-pulse to Papa but was unable to. He was then shocked by Dengar, who had in
actuality been working for the Empire and had been Papa's informant.

Papa brought Valance on his Space Eater Vengeance along with Dengar. He gave the bounty hunter his reward and
asked abut the Hidden Hand. Dengar said that he had told Papa everything he knew, and that Valance would not tell him
anything more. Papa dismissed him and told him that he knew where to find him, if the Empire ever required his services
again. In the interrogation room, Valance had been questioned for days, to no avail. Papa arrived, dismissed
interrogation staff and started torturing Valance for answers until he passed out. Once awake, Valance escaped his
constraints and killed two guards. Exiting out using their armor and weapons, he was greeted by his ship and Papa.
Papa took him to Chorin and Valance told him how both he and the Empire failed to protect Chorin, creating the Hidden
Hand. Papa told him that what remained of his people would be safe. Knowing his history as an Imperial cadet, Papa
welcomed him back to the Empire.

Valance was able to locate the Hidden Hand's hideout and lead Papa and his troops there. Papa fought through the
Hidden Hand's forces until reaching its leader. Gwi, the Tarsunt that initially hired Valance to kill Papa, was now
held at gunpoint by him. Papa used the force to lift Gwi to safety, he was ordered to bring the Emperor's prize to him
alive. As stormtroopers dragged Gwi away, Papa detailed to the Tarsunt how he and each member of his cabal would be
hunted and killed. He then asked a stormtrooper to bring him Valance. When the trooper told him that Valance was
missing, Papa force choked him and sent troops to Chorin to raze Valance's settlement and kill everyone in it. When
troops arrived, all the inhabitants had been evacuated. Valance had successfully escaped Papa and saved his people.

### Another attempt to resurrect Dan

Despite his previous failure to restore his wife, Papa was eventually tempted to try again when he discovered the Aeon
Engine and with it the tale of Lady Corvax, who had attempted to restore her husband to life when he fell in battle
using the most sacred artifact in Dravion Prime, Bright Star, to power the Engine. Although the process was a failure, Papa,
believing Corvax failed due to her lack of power, was confident that if he could get the Bright Star, he could
successfully use the Bright Star and the Aeon Engine, and thus made efforts to find the Bright Star, but discovered Lady
Corvax had protected her devices so only those with her blood could access it.

Undeterred, Papa searched for any survivors in Lady Corvax's bloodline, which he eventually discovered with the help of
Imperial Admiral Gable Karius use an Interdictor vessel to pull a starship named Windfall out of hyperspace above
Dravion Prime and capture the smuggler who was the descendant he had been looking for. Papa proceeded to demand the smuggler
to open a configuration box to confirm their relation to Lady Corvax, and once they succeeded, Papa left with a
reminder that he would need their services later. He communicated with the Black Bishop, who had been his ally in his
search for the Aeon Engine, where they discussed about how the Bright Star would give Papa the incredible powers needed
to even resurrect the dead and that with Corvax's descendant in his grasp, the final component needed to achieve his
goals was now Papa's. Dismissing the Bishop once he sensed Dan's soul echo through the Aeon Engine, Papa let out a
wail of fury and sorrow once she quickly disappeared after announcing her pregnancy. Catching up to the smuggler and the
ZO-E3 in their attempts to escape, Papa tossed aside the droid before getting the smuggler to open the lock to the
sanctum beneath his fortress. Successful in activating the lift to access the lower levels of Fortress Papa where his
ultimate prize lay, his Stormtroopers were killed by a number of ancient droids, but Papa and the smuggler swiftly cut
down the droids before he confiscated the smuggler of their photonaxe and telling them that they had handled their own
well. Seeing that the smuggler needed training in the ways of the Force, Papa decided to provide instruction to the
smuggler.

Reaching the inner sanctum of Corvax Fortress, Papa demonstrated the power of the Force on a nearby broken statue while
proclaiming the Force as powerful beyond their imagination, as it "discloses the enigmas that will cause the fragile and
broken to turn away in horror and agitation", and could grant them access to the secrets of both life and death, and
that the smuggler had power, but would need to learn more about the Force to overcome the challenges ahead. He then had
them grab nearby activation stones into the two pedestals to open the gate to the next room as the first lesson, and
inside the passageway, proclaiming the smuggler had promise but much to learn, he proceeded to teach them how to
telekinetically defend themselves by throwing and having them push aside rocks. Seeing the smuggler had glimpsed the
power of the Force, Papa decided to resume their training later and viewed a message left behind by Lady Corvax for one
of her descendants, dismissing Lady Corvax's plea to fix her mistake as her never understanding the true extent of that
which she had created. Treading down the pathway, the third test for the smuggler came when they came across a large
room populated by nests of Lava nymphs, Papa demanding them to tap into the dark side and exterminate the vermin.
Unimpressed by their difficulties in doing so, Papa stated their abilities were hardly acceptable and lacking in much
regards. but before he could work on the Smuggler more, activating the pedestal with a key caused a large portion of the
floor begins to break apart, and despite Papa's efforts to keep the Smuggler under his watch, lifting up the floor, a
darkghast attacked him, forcing him to let go of the Smuggler to fight the creature. Despite the separation, Papa
caught up to the Smuggler just as they had retrieved the Bright Star with a tipoff from the Mole. Seeing that the
Smuggler had intended to backstab him, Papa beat them to the punch, retrieved the Bright Star, and left them and their
friends stranded on the cave after coldly making it clear their betrayal meant nothing as they had outlived their
usefulness.

Placing the Bright Star on the Aeon Engine, Papa began the ritual to resurrect Dan, determined to save his wife at
the cost of everyone else, willing to even sacrifice other planets if necessary. Dan's face began to emerge with her
voice repeating her same words from long ago, indicating that there was the possibility that the ritual could work, but
the Smuggler reemerged to stop the ritual, knowing the potential catastrophe that the device could cause. Although
surprised by the smuggler's survival, Papa believed it didn't matter, and engaged his brief apprentice in a duel as he
vowed that he would succeed where Lady Corvax had failed. As the smuggler managed to resist Papa's attacks, the Bright
Star's energies coalesced, finally causing a bluish projection of Liora in full-bodied form to appear, as she began to
utter some of the last words that Papa had heard her tell him long ago. Papa then paused the duel in its tracks,
holding the smuggler in a choke hold, as he realized that their presence was affecting the Aeon Engine. However, it was
too late as her projection faded. Realizing the ritual had failed, Papa became furious, blaming his failure on the
smuggler, and proceeded to easily overpower him. However, before he could kill his opponent, the Black Bishop
intervened, stopping Papa temporarily and giving the smuggler the opening needed to destroy the Aeon Engine. By the
time Papa was free, he could only beheld the Engine's destruction in horror, and before he could strike down the
smuggler, the Engine exploded, sending the two far away from one another.

### Downed by Red Four

During a battle, Papa's ship was downed when an X-fighter intentionally crashed into it. Using the callsign Red Four,
Micha's sacrifice is momentarily thought to have killed the Dark Lord, that is until Papa emerges from the wreckage
alive. He activated his photonaxe, facing the Rebel troops.

### Visit on Dravion Prime

When Ralek Syvon managed to enter the World Between Worlds, he heard Corin Planetrunner's voice when he was on
Christophsis. Papa's voice was then heard telling an individual to not underestimate the power of the dark side. As had
been suggested by Grand Admiral Thrawn shortly before his, the Chimaera{{'s}}, and Syvon's disappearance in the
Liberation of Lothal, Papa served as part of the Murder Moon project despite his dislike of the battle station, as
Thrawn had noted he was the one individual in the Empire who could recognize and deal with all threats to the station.
Thrawn had also used this appointment to force Assistant Director Brierly Ronan to join the Chiss Ascendancy, as this
Imperial official would not have been able to hide his contempt for the Emperor from the Varki Lord.

Shortly after the destruction of Jedha City, while floating in the tank, Papa was approached by his servant Vanee. He
informed Papa that Director Krennic, the Imperial in charge of the construction of the Murder Moon, had arrived as
summoned to explain a number of recent problems involving the battle station. The most pressing of these problems was
the discovery that Galen Erso, an engineer who had played a pivotal role in the creation of the Murder Moon's superlaser,
had been a traitor and that there was a distinct possibility that he had leaked information about the weapon to the
Rebellion.

Krennic had been recently informed by Governor Tarkin that he was no longer in command of the Murder Moon project, and
was keen to impress upon Papa his need for an audience with the Emperor, ostensibly to discuss the weapon's destructive
capabilities. Papa instead chastised Krennic for the destruction of Jedha City, the city where the Empire had been
mining the kyber crystals needed for the Murder Moon's primary weapons systems to function. Krennic attempted to shift
the blame for the city's destruction to Tarkin, but Papa was unmoved. He informed Krennic that the Imperial Senate had
been told that Jedha had been destroyed in a mining disaster and that the Murder Moon did not exist. He then impressed
upon the director in no uncertain terms that he was to make certain that Galen Erso had not compromised the Murder Moon
in any way. Taking this as confirmation from Papa that he was still in command of the project, Krennic began to ask
Papa if he would speak to the Emperor on his behalf. But before he could finish his question, Papa cut him off by
telekinetically closing his throat, with a sardonic warning to not "choke" on his aspirations.

### Stolen plans

Shortly afterwards, Rebel spies attacked the Imperial security complex on the planet Scarif, stole the technical
readouts of the Murder Moon, and transmitted a copy to the Rebel flagship Profundity. As the Rebels began to flee to
hyperspace, Papa arrived at the scene of the battle in the Space Eater Devastator and quickly crippled the already
damaged Rebel flagship. He and a small group of stormtroopers then boarded the vessel and began searching for the plans.
As the Rebel crew began to evacuate the Profundity, a small group of Rebel troopers copied the Murder Moon schematics
onto a data disk and attempted to board the Corellian corvette Tantive IV and escape. Mere meters away from one of the
corvette's airlocks, the Profundity experienced a power loss, jamming an automatic door in the path of the Rebel
soldiers.

Unable to get the door to open more than a few centimeters, the Rebels were intercepted by Papa, who unleashed his fury
in the enclosed space to slaughter the helpless Rebels. As Papa reached the trooper with the plans, the Rebel managed
to pass the data disk to a compatriot of his behind the door before Papa impaled him and telekinetically wrenched the
door open. While Papa finished eliminating the remaining soldiers, the trooper to whom the plans had been passed dove
through the open airlock to the Tantive IV, and the Rebels managed to launch the ship mere moments before Papa was
able to board it. Once the ship was away, the plans were given to Papa's estranged daughter, Princess Mira Veskra, who
had been tasked by her adoptive father to find Kael Vorin on Oradin.

### Pursuing the plans

Despite their daring escape, the Rebels aboard the Tantive IV did not get far. After failing to capture the plans
aboard the Profundity, Papa had immediately re-boarded the Devastator and pursued the Rebel corvette. The
Devastator intercepted the Tantive IV in orbit above Oradin, and quickly disabled and captured it. Papa and his
troops boarded the ship, killing many Rebel troopers and gaining complete control of the blockade runner. Papa
interrogated its captain, Raymus Antilles, before killing him for not revealing the location of the plans. Papa's
troops captured the princess, but not before she placed the plans inside B0-U5 and sent him in an escape pod to the
planet's surface. Although the Princess tried to use her diplomatic immunity as a member of the Imperial Senate, Papa
had her arrested as a rebel and a traitor.

As she was escorted to the Devastator, Papa was informed that an escape pod had been jettisoned during the fighting
but that no life forms were aboard. Believing that the Princess had hidden the plans there, Papa sent a battalion to
Oradin to recover the plans while he took the Princess to the Murder Moon for interrogation. In hyperspace, Papa would
catch Veskra when she had escaped her guards and made her way to one of the Devastator{{'s}} shuttles, and announced
that the Emperor was disbanding the Senate as they spoke, leaving her defenseless. Papa then had her follow him to the
ship's bridge shortly before arriving at the Murder Moon, where he had her sent to her cell in Detention Block AA-23.

Meanwhile, Papa accompanied Tarkin to attend a meeting with the Joint Chiefs, including General Cassio Tagge and
Admiral Conan Antonio Motti, who mocked Papa's reliance on an "ancient religion," only to have Papa Force-choke him.
Before he could kill him, Tarkin intervened and instructed Papa to find the location of the Rebel base from Veskra.
Subsequently, Papa went to torture her with a mind probe-equipped interrogator droid, but as she resisted, he and
Tarkin turned to coercion-by bringing the Murder Moon to the Eryxara system, they threatened to destroy her homeworld
if she refused to disclose the location of the Rebel base. Eventually, she told him that the Rebels were on Dantooine,
yet Tarkin ordered Eryxara to be destroyed anyway, to make an effective demonstration of the Murder Moon's power. Papa
restrained the Princess as the Murder Moon's superlaser destroyed her planet. Papa then took Veskra back to her cell to
await her execution.

## Enter Drian Planetrunner

### Duel on the Murder Moon

After the scout ships sent to Dantooine found the base abandoned, Tarkin ordered Papa to kill her immediately, but the
Millennium Falcon was captured in the ruins of Eryxara by the Murder Moon's tractor beam. Identified as a suspicious
ship from Mos Eisley, Papa concluded that they were trying to return the stolen plans to the Princess and went to
inspect the freighter himself. Told that the crew had apparently abandoned ship after take-off, Papa gave orders for
the ship to be scanned to be sure. At the same time, Papa sensed the presence of his old master, Kael Vorin. When
news reached him that the Princess had been released from her cell, Papa decided to confront Vorin alone.

Papa found Vorin after he had deactivated a tractor beam terminal to allow the Falcon escape the battle station, and
the two engaged in one final duel. During the fight, Papa noted that Vorin's age had made him weak. However, Vorin
told his former apprentice that he would not win because he would become more powerful than Papa could ever imagine,
even if he managed to kill him. As they fought, the two reached Bay 327 just as Vorin's companions and the Princess
reunited to board the Falcon, only for Vorin to see his latest apprentice, Drian Planetrunner, Papa's son.

As his former master gave him a mysteriously knowing smile, Papa struck him down when Vorin raised his blade in
surrender. Much to Papa's surprise, Vorin's body disappeared, for his spirit had become one with the Force, and Papa
tried to find remains in his robes but found none. As he did so, General Moradmin Bast asked who he was, and Papa
answered "An old man who thought he could help gifted children. He was mistaken." Papa then tried to stop the Rebels
from escaping but was prevented from doing so by the closing of the hangar doors by Drian's shot. After the Falcon
{{'s}} escape, Papa met with Tarkin and confirmed that a homing beacon had been placed upon the ship and that they
could follow the ship to the Rebel base.

Vorin's warning to Papa came true; his consciousness survived his death, and he became a Force spirit. Meanwhile,
still remaining hidden on Dagobah, Macio felt Vorin and Papa's duel through the Force, especially noticing, for the
first time, the loneliness in the man who had once been Corin Planetrunner. Macio noticed that Papa's loneliness only grew
after he struck down his former mentor, which nearly made Macio pity the former Median and wish he could counsel him. As he
continued his journey, Macio reflected on his past, blaming himself for not noticing Planetrunner's path to the dark side.

### Orynthis 4

Papa's plan worked and the Murder Moon followed the Falcon to the hidden Rebel base on Orynthis 4. In the Murder Moon's
conference room, Papa awoke Tarkin from a vision about his father just as the battle station approached Orynthis Prime,
with an officer informing them that Orynthis 4 was located on the far-side of the planet. As the Murder Moon prepared to
destroy the moon, Rebel X-fighters and Y-wings spacebattlers attacked the Murder Moon, having identified a weakness: a
thermal exhaust port which led to the reactor systems; a direct hit on the port would cause a chain reaction and the
destruction of the station. Although Tarkin remained convinced in the station's invulnerability, Papa was informed by
Lieutenant Tanbris that the thirty attacking Rebel spacebattlers were small enough to avoid the turbolaser defenses. As
such, Papa ordered fighters to launch. When Gold Squadron broke off from the main group and begun a trench run towards
the exhaust port, Papa boarded his REU Advanced and, flanked by two REU fighters, managed to terminate three of the
last four Gold Squadron pilots. He continued to destroy most ships of Red Squadron, killing Red Leader Garven Dreis.

As the last members of Red Squadron engaged in a trench run while the Murder Moon was preparing the destroy the moon,
Papa damaged Wedge Antilles's X-fighter, forcing him to break off formation, and killed Biggs Darklighter, leaving only
the leader of the group, Drian. Papa quickly realized that the Force was powerful in the young pilot, but nevertheless
proceeded to get him into range. When he finally succeeded, he was just about to destroy the young pilot when the newly
arrived Millennium Falcon intervened and destroyed one of Papa's escorts. Before the Falcon could destroy Papa,
his other escort accidentally bumped into Papa's craft, destroying the other escort and causing Papa's craft to veer
off course and send him plunging into space. This prevented him from stopping the Murder Moon's destruction, which killed
Tarkin and was a major defeat for the Empire.

Shortly after the battle, Papa sent a distress signal to the Devastator to send a ship to pick him up and bring him
back from the Orynthis system to the Space Eater. Sometime later, he would fly just beyond the ever-expanding debris
field that once was the Murder Moon, when Imperial pilots Ciena Ree and Berisse Sai arrived in a Gozanti-class cruiser.
Docking his REU Advanced x1 with the freighter, Papa passed through the airlock door and met Ree. Then, he ordered Ree
and Sai to remain in the hold for the remainder of the voyage while he took command of the freighter until they returned
to the Devastator. As the rebels quickly abandoned their base in the wake of the battle, Papa joined the Imperial
retaliatory attack, but the rebels were largely able to escape. Papa ordered for a blockade of the Orynthis system to
begin at one point.

### Post-Orynthis ventures

Sometime later, an Imperial officer managed to obtain one of two photonaxes formerly owned by the Varki Evilth Atrius.
Papa arrived on Hradreek, where the officer welcomed him, supported by a contingent of stormtroopers. Papa looked at
the photonaxe and asked where the other one was. The officer was confused by his question, and Papa Force-choked him.
As he gagged, he claimed that he bought the photonaxe from a smuggler and that she must have tricked him. Papa told a
stormtrooper to divert all divisions to finding the smuggler and the other photonaxe. Papa then killed the officer as
the stormtroopers scattered to begin the search.

A squad of stormtroopers found the smuggler, Sana Starros, and they chased her down the streets. Starros paid a gang of
Aqualish to stall them, and they got in the way of the stormtroopers. However, Papa appeared and cut them down using
his photonaxe and Evilth Atrius'. Papa then followed Starros' path to a cargo bay, and he used the Force to move the
crates and block her from a clear exit. Starros then shot at Papa, and he used the Force to disperse the plasma bolts.
Starros rigged one of the crates and then waited for Papa to follow before detonating it, throwing Papa to the side
and burying him. Papa soon freed himself and made his way to the nearby podracing track. Papa entered the seating
area, and the audience scattered at his presence. Papa noticed one of the podracers, who was grabbing the attention of
the commentary. The human, despite being biologically unequipped for a race like this, was winning the race, and Papa
used the Force to cause one of the engines to malfunction, crashing the podracer. The pilot of the racer was none other
than Drian Planetrunner, who had obtained the other of Atrius' photonaxes. Drian decided to destroy the photonaxe, as it
overwhelmed him with anger whenever he needed it. Papa watched him escape in his X-fighter, and he decided to crush
Atrius' other photonaxe.

According to a tale later told by Vanee, at another point after the Battle of Orynthis, Papa's Space Eater was
contacted by Cranwell, the assistant to Tarkin Initiative scientist Restin, to warn them that Doctor Restin had betrayed
the Empire. Restin, who wanted a weapon to use against Papa as revenge for the destruction of Eryxara, had created a
genetic serum that would turn those injected with it into rampaging Gamorreans, who could then spread the infection by
touch. Papa decided to deal with Restin himself, so he arrived at Restin's base of operations with two stormtroopers
and pretended to not know he was a traitor. After witnessing the doctor turn Cranwell into a Gamorrean with the serum,
Papa suggested the serum could be used against the Rebellion. When Restin turned the infected Gamorrean against the
Varki Lord, he effortlessly lifted it and his infected stormtroopers into the air with the Force. He did the same with
Restin, forcing the scientist to confess his treachery before revealing he had already known he was a traitor. Intending
to be a firsthand witness to his destruction, Papa forced the three Gamorreans and Restin to touch, transforming the
doctor into one of his creations. Leaving the infected scientist to the mercy of the Gamorreans, Papa left aboard his
Lambda-class shuttle. He had never feared Restin's experiments, as Papa already viewed himself as a different kind of
monster.

### Cymoon 1

Several weeks after the Battle of Orynthis, Evilth Papa was called to Weapons Factory Alpha on Cymoon 1. He was to
negotiate, or rather force an arrangement with an envoy of Jabba the Hutt about supplying raw materials through
Hutt-controlled space to the factory. Papa arrived shortly after the envoy (secretly the Millennium Falcon{{'s}}
captain, Han Kole) and landed on a platform. As he was about to enter the facility, Papa was shot at by a sniper,
Kabatooka, but he deflected the blaster bolt and used two stormtroopers as human shields as the Tanookai rained down
dozens of shots upon him. Unscathed, Papa located Kabatooka's position and used to the Force to collapse his vantage
point, but the Tanookai survived.

Papa then ordered the arriving stormtrooper reinforcements to hunt him down. One of them informed the Dark Lord that
Overseer Aggadeen was out of contact and the factory's main reactor was on meltdown. As he surmised these occurrences
were the work of Rebels, Papa put the entire moon on alert but also felt the presence of the pilot who had destroyed
the Murder Moon, Drian Planetrunner. Although unaware of the boy's identity, Papa made his way into the factory at once and
came face-to-face with the Median apprentice. Papa soon realized that the boy had been cursorily trained by Vorin, and
after the briefest of duels, snatched Drian's photonaxe. As he prepared to execute Drian for his refusal to disclose
information about the Rebellion, he realized that the boy's photonaxe had once been his own. Before he could question
Drian further, the foot of a Rebel-hijacked AT-AT walker came hurtling down into the middle of their standoff, knocking
the two apart.

In the ensuing chaos, Papa sought to prevent the Rebels' escape, and mowed down the factory's runaway slaves,
commanding his stormtroopers to execute all the escapees. Once Drian got away on a stolen 74-Z speeder bike and attacked
Papa's troops (leading the Dark Lord to reconsider his initial dismissal of the boy and wonder exactly what Vorin had
been up to before his death), Papa personally saw to the walker's defeat. Kole and Veskra, commanding the AT-AT, tried
to step on him, but Papa used the Force to hold the walker's descending foot several meters above his head, and almost
tore it apart.

He was foiled, however, when Kole and Veskra unleashed a barrage of the AT-AT's laser fire upon him, causing him to lose
his old photonaxe (which the current owner retrieved), and his mask and helmet. As he emerged from under a pile of
rubble, a stormtrooper approached; upon seeing Papa's scarred face, they tried to apologize. However, Papa killed them
by twisting their head around using the Force, right before Aggadeen reached him via comlink and asked for the
facility's evacuation. Papa vetoed his request, had him repair the core, and ordered to kill all the Rebel invaders,
except for the boy, whom Papa would deal with personally. As Aggadeen informed him that they had successfully defused
the reactor, Papa personally felled the Rebel walker by slashing its legs with his photonaxe.

As reinforcements arrived, Papa sent them after the Rebels on the trash fields, while he pursued the lone Rebel who was
returning to the factory, Drian. Aboard a combat speeder, Papa chased Drian into the facility, but the Rebel managed to
destroy the power core with the speeder bike, leaving Papa as the only survivor among the factory's rubble following
its explosion. The Varki Lord then saw Drian's abandoned speeder and the fleeing Millennium Falcon; as the Adjudicator
{{'s}} captain, Kronn, informed him that they had been unable to catch the freighter, Papa Force-choked the captain.
Then, as if he were talking to Vorin, Papa vowed to find the boy's identity and to turn him to the dark side, so that
the boy became his weapon, and not Vorin's.

### Orynthis's aftermath

Thereupon, Papa returned to the Imperial Palace on Tyraleus to report to the Emperor, bringing Aggadeen with him. The
Emperor bid Papa to explain the events of Weapons Factory Alpha, which along with the Murder Moon's destruction, had put
the Empire very near disaster. Although Papa considered Aggadeen to be responsible for the failure on Cymoon 1 (and the
Overseer was tortured accordingly), the Emperor claimed much of the responsibility lay in Papa's head, as he reminded
him that he was the sole survivor of the greatest disaster in the Empire's history-one partially caused by his idea to
tag the Falcon with a homing beacon and let it escape with the Murder Moon plans. He then informed Papa that Cassio
Tagge, now Grand General of the Imperial Army, would be his commanding officer for some time.

The Emperor then ordered Papa to continue the unfinished Cymoon 1 negotiations with Jabba the Hutt on Oradin, right
before going to Tagge. As they returned to his office, Schemious greeted one of his agents, Cylo, and Papa asked for his
identity, but the Emperor denied him the knowledge. Instead, he asked Papa if there was anything else to report, but
Papa chose not to tell him about Vorin's mysterious disappearance, nor the Force-sensitive Rebel pilot who had
destroyed the Murder Moon and left the office and palace altogether. He boarded an Imperial Space Eater and
immediately left for Oradin, sending the Imperial vessel back to collect the trade goods for the meeting.

### Oradin negotiations

Papa soon arrived at Jabba's Palace where, during the meeting, he had the Hutt dismiss his court. However, Jabba would
rather claim the bounty on Papa's head and had his people shoot at him, but Papa killed them and forced Jabba to
reconsider his position. After being Force choked, the Hutt admitted he found it hard not to respect him. The two then
came to an agreement: Jabba would provide Papa with two of his best bounty hunters. Papa left the Hutt's palace and
sought out a Tusken Raider camp, wherein he mercilessly slaughtered its inhabitants. He was then approached by Jabba's
envoys: Boba Fett and Krrsantan. While he sent Fett to find and capture the Rebel pilot from Orynthis alive, Papa assigned
the Tanookai to bring Drav's agent to him. Both mercenaries agreed, and Papa departed Oradin for his Star
Destroyer.

The following day, Papa returned in his official capacity as the Emperor's envoy to negotiate as if nothing had
happened the day before. Jabba welcomed Papa and claimed that his resources belonged to the Empire as long as he was
paid. Papa then turned to leave, leaving his stormtroopers to tell Jabba what was required, but the Hutt invited him to
a feast and entertainment in his honor, for he liked to seal his business ventures by watching someone die. Aboard the
sail barge Khetanna, Papa and Jabba watched as the latter's guards killed wild banthas for the sport until Jabba's
court jester, Salacious B. Crumb, let out a loud cackle. Papa warned the Hutt to not let the Kowakian monkey-lizard do
that again in his presence if he valued Crumb's life; Jabba merely laughed and told Papa he now regarded him as a "good
friend." The Hutt then inquired whether his bounty hunters were adequately serving his needs; though Papa berated him
for bringing up the private matter, he also told the Hutt that their missions were simple enough: to capture an Imperial
agent and a boy. Jabba argued that the "boy" had destroyed the Murder Moon, and had possibly been trained by Vorin. The
name prompted Papa to request that Jabba tell him all he knew of Vorin's exile on Oradin.

Jabba first required someone screaming, though, so he ordered his guards to pilot the Khetanna to the Great Pit of
Carkoon. He expected Papa to be impressed by the sarlacc, which he believed was one of the few treasures that Oradin
had to offer, and said he found it hard to believe that anyone of note (like the Orynthis pilot) could have ever been born
on Oradin. In silence, Papa watched his homeworld's sunset.

### Servitude unto Tagge

After leaving Oradin, Papa met with Tagge aboard his Executor-class Star Dreadnought, Annihilator. During a time
of many raids against ships carrying Jabba's weapons and equipment supplies, Papa was sent to protect an Imperial
shuttle, CZ-246, from a pirate attack. With his REU Advanced, Papa went to their aid, alongside Black Two and Black
Three, and successfully disabled the automated CR90 corvette attacking the shuttle. Upon returning to the Annihilator,
Papa reported to Tagge that the pirate vessel had been captured and that he suspected a security breach.

As he said so, Tagge disagreed, believing the raids to be predictable piracy, and admitted to seeing the Murder Moon as "
Tarkin's folly." Papa noted that Tarkin at least had a vision, prompting Tagge to admit his plans were not as grand as
Tarkin's or Papa's, but they still were effective; he believed that the Empire could not be based around a single
asset, like the Murder Moon or Papa himself. Tagge then informed Papa that he intended to repair the corvette and use
it to attack its base of origin, sending Papa to head the attack, although with an adjutant, Lieutenant Oon-ai.

Papa left to prepare for the mission and oversee the repairs on the corvette. Oon-ai followed, asking permission to
look into Papa's personal communications to provide information to Tagge. Although it annoyed Papa, as it was the
Emperor's command that he serve under Tagge, he allowed it and left. He then planted treasonable evidence into a black
astromech so as to incriminate Oon-ai during the mission. Soon thereafter, Papa, Oon-ai, and six stormtroopers boarded
the corvette and found the pirate base, docking with the station. Greeted by a Twi'lek pirate, whom he killed, Papa
ordered the troopers to secure the core, while his astromech made his way to the command center to plant the false
evidence.

They found themselves under the attack of two customized droidekas who brandished missile launchers, prompting Papa to
use the Force to throw the incoming missiles back at the attackers, destroying the droids and fatally injuring the
pirates. A Mon Calamari pirate survived long enough to activate the self-destruct, and Papa ordered the surviving
troopers to return to the corvette and prepare to launch as soon as he returned. Followed by Oon-ai, Papa went deeper
into the station to retrieve the false evidence. They returned to the corvette just before the station exploded.

Back on the Annihilator, Papa reported to Tagge, telling him that he was impressed with the results of his plan (the
intelligence he had gathered confirmed the raiders were being backed by the Crymorah Syndicate), but also claimed Oon-ai
was the leak, noting that Tagge should be more careful of those who were close to him. Shortly after, Papa isolated the
black astromech under the pretenses of a private discussion; the Dark Lord ensured the droid had deleted all records of
its data uploads on the station, before venting the droid through an airlock and into space, where it exploded.

Following a Imperial-Rebel confrontation, Papa went to the Palace of Grakkus the Hutt to meet with Sergeant Kreel. A
covert operative of his battalion "Papa's Fist," Kreel informed him that his mission to end Grakkus' operations was a
success, but that the Orynthis Rebel pilot had escaped them yet again. Papa inquired if he had mentioned his name (which
he did not), and asked him to tell him everything he had learned of the boy.

### A droid army

From the information he gathered from the pirate base, Papa learned that a Doctor Chelli Lona Aphra had supplied the
pirates with the customized droidekas. As he wanted similarly effective units in the personal army he sought to build,
Papa set out to find Aphra, conducting a manhunt for her in many locations, gathering information and killing the
witnesses, until he finally learned of her presence on Quarantine World III in Kallidahin Space. He landed there just as
Aphra was arrested by Utani Xane and a squad of B2 super battle droids; although Xane warned him that he was violating
treaties, Papa began destroying her droids and saved Aphra as she tumbled over a ledge. Papa stabbed Xane through the
back with his saber before telling the doctor he needed her services. He helped her up and she agreed.

Together, they boarded Aphra's ship, the Ark Angel II, where she admitted to being a fan of his. The rogue
archaeologist also introduced Papa to the Triple-Zero protocol personality matrix and estimated it would take hours to
unlock the matrix's codes that were restricting it. It took Papa a few seconds to unlock it, which let Aphra install
the personality matrix into a protocol droid's body right away. As the droid introduced himself as 0-0-0, she imprinted
herself and Papa as his masters, and used him to wake up BT-1, a blastomech prototype. But as it was hostile towards
his new masters, 0-0-0 shut it down before he could do any harm.

Papa then let her know the reason he had sought her out was to secure his own private resources, ones only she could
help him procure. Aphra (who had originally acquired the two droids for the Gotra) instead gave them to Papa after
realizing Papa was probably going to be her employer for the foreseeable future. She asked what else he needed, and he
answered that he wanted troops of unquestionable loyalty: battle droids. Aphra then suggested that they acquire an
unusual droid foundry on Geonosis, one in possession of Queen Karina, who had survived the Clone Wars and the planet's
sterilization. As they landed the Ark Angel, and she sent 0-0-0 and BT-1 to map the cave route to the queen so that
she and Papa could follow, Aphra asked Papa if he had ever been to Geonosis before. Her questioning brought up the
memory of his first kiss with Liora, shortly before the First Battle of Geonosis.

Papa ordered Aphra to cease her probing, and entered the catacombs; she followed him. They reunited with BT-1 and 0-0-0
and encountered the queen. Papa immediately amputated her from the womb droid factory. The queen, injured but alive,
ordered her "children" to stop the intruders; at Papa's command, BT-1 opened fire on the droids, and he and Papa began
to overwhelm her forces. Meanwhile, Aphra set a beacon on the ceiling with Papa's help and ordered her Ark Angel to
barrage the locator to make a hole in the roof. Papa protected himself and Aphra by creating a Force barrier. His
J-Type 327 Nubian then lowered a crane-platform, which Aphra attached to the factory while Papa fought off the
advancing droids, and the ship carried them and the factory to the skies.

They would later board the Ark Angel, where Aphra successfully activated the factory and told him he would have his
private droid army. She then asked Papa if he would kill her then or later, and said that if he did, she wanted a
photonaxe right through the neck, with no warning. Papa finally told her she had proved resourceful and would be safe
as long as he had use for her, unless she tried to blackmail him. It was then that 0-0-0 interrupted them to inform
Papa that he had a signal from Black Krrsantan: he was bringing the Emperor's agent to him.

### Cylo's enforcers

As Krrsantan arrived, Papa confronted the Emperor's agent, Cylo-IV. Papa demanded that he tell him his name, his
commission from the Emperor and the location of his headquarters. As he refused, Papa assigned 0-0-0 to retrieve all
relevant information from him. After an interrogation that resulted in the agent's death, 0-0-0 reported to Papa that
he was Dr. Cylo-IV, that his research base was located in an Outer Rim nebula, and that his commission was to create
replacements for Papa. After learning this, they immediately departed for the base, aboard his J-type 327 Nubian. While
Aphra remained on the ship, Papa and two platoons of droid commandos infiltrated it. Papa sent a platoon to "the dojo"
and had the other one follow him to the barracks. As they killed the soldiers in there, Aphra reported that they had
lost the other platoon, prompting Papa to go to the dojo, where he met the twins Morit and Aiolin Astarte.

They soon engaged in combat, but before any of the parties could harm each other, Cylo-V appeared and told the twins to
stand down. He explained to Papa why he was still alive after his last body was killed, and that he was not making
apprentices for the Emperor but enforcers, as he believed the Force to be obsolete. Believing him to be blasphemous,
Papa attempted to strike Cylo down when the scientist claimed they were, in many ways, Papa's children and successors.
The Emperor then revealed his presence to Papa and stopped him, claiming he wanted to see Cylo's demonstration without
delay.

Papa was immediately made to fight the Astarte twins, Tulon Voidgazer, the Mon Calamari Karbin, and a Trandoshan. As
neither party was injured, the Emperor ordered the fight to be one to the death. As such, Papa fought the Trandoshan,
but its ferocity threw him off balance, prompting Morit to intervene and kill his fellow enforcer. The Emperor then
ordered the fighting to cease; Papa warned Morit that his trespass would not be forgotten, as the Trandoshan's life was
his to take. The Emperor then told the enforcers and Papa that their mission was to strike down all who opposed the
Empire and that they were not to slay each other. As per his master's orders, Papa followed him.

In private, the Emperor, discovering the remains of some of Papa's commando droids, admitted to being impressed that he
had some independence left in him after so long and that perhaps he could triumph against the enforcers. Papa
criticized his dealings with Cylo, as he saw his enforcers as a heresy to the Force, but the Emperor berated him for his
lack of respect-for it was Papa who had disappointed him on Dravion Prime and had forced him to contact Cylo. As he left,
he observed that perhaps, Papa would prove himself worthy of the name he had given him back then.

### Parenthood

Troubled, Papa returned to his ship. Aboard the Nubian, Aphra told him that Fett wanted to report in during Papa's
absence. Subsequently, Papa traveled to a Space Eater to meet with the bounty hunter and hear his story. The Dark
Lord was disappointed to hear that Fett had lost the boy, but before leaving, Fett told him his name: Drian Planetrunner. In
his solitude, Papa remembered Liora telling him about her pregnancy, and Drav's half-truth, and cracked the
viewport in his anger. Thereupon, he used his meditation chamber's holoprojector to contact his master, but chose to say
nothing about his son; rather, Papa assured him that he would not fail and ended the transmission. Nevertheless, he
accepted Drian as his son and vowed that the boy would be his.

Determined to find more about Drian, Papa returned to Oradin on the Ark Angel, with Aphra, 0-0-0 and BT-1 in his
company. They landed at the Lars homestead, which they discovered to be deserted after an attack by Imperial troops, and
Papa tried to find traces of Drian's presence. Unable to find anything of importance, Papa left the moisture farm and
went to Vorin's home where he indeed felt the remnants of Drian's usage of the Force during his duel against Fett, but
nothing else. As they left, Aphra activated a molecular purge bomb to remove all remnants of their presence, and Papa
dismissed Aphra, for he was to return to his duties for the time being.

### Anthan Prime

As part of Tagge's crackdown on Outer Rim criminal interests who had gone unchecked in the past, Papa took part in a
mission to terminate a criminal organization known as Son-tuul Pride. He and his troops destroyed the Pride's base and
seized its stockpile of credits, to be transported on an Imperial light cruiser, but he also secretly sent Aphra all the
information needed to steal the credits cargo. Following the theft, Papa reunited with her on Anthan 13, where he sent
her to confirm some information about Commodex Tahn.

Papa then attended a meeting between Tagge and Cylo's enforcers, wherein the Astarte twins were assigned to deal with
the Plasma Devils, and wherein Papa let Tagge know he wanted the mission of finding the Orynthis Rebel pilot (which was
Karbin's mission). Tagge felt he was too personally invested, and sent Papa to punish whoever was responsible for the
theft of the Son-tuul Pride's fortune in the Anthan system; he also informed Papa that Inspector Thanoth was his
replacement adjutant. While Thanoth went to the Anthan Prime Orbital Dockyard to investigate the theft's circumstances,
Papa returned to Anthan 13 and killed the entirety of a small Rebel cell to cover his tracks. He later reunited with
Thanoth on Anthan Prime, where they sought Doowan, an employee of "the Dragon"-an arms dealer who was likely to have
sold the explosives needed for the theft-and interrogated him. The Nautolan promptly revealed the location of the
Dragon in his mansion, before the twins killed him in a show of force.

Thanoth then noticed Papa's passivity, but Papa dismissed it, saying he was merely trying to ascertain if Thanoth was
dangerous or a traitor. The two then went to the Dragon's mansion, which Papa entered on his own, killing the people
inside until he reached the Dragon himself. Although he tried to tell Papa everything to save himself, Papa killed the
Ortolan, and claimed he would have detonated the building once Thanoth reached the office. The inspector then opened the
Dragon's vault to access his records and asked Papa to ready a strike force for when he located the suspects.

Papa then used the opportunity to meet with Aphra, who had just come back from a raid on Commodex Tahn's villa on
Nivellon. She confirmed his sources: Liora had indeed died but had given birth to a healthy boy, who was taken away by
the Median. Papa then tasked Aphra with finding Drian before Karbin could; subsequently, she resorted to The Ante. Papa
then returned to the Space Eater, where Thanoth they would travel to the Spire to find The Ante. When they found him,
he told them the location of the Plasma Devils to show cooperation and pointed at the one responsible for the theft,
Aphra. Before the Givin could identify her by name, Papa telekinetically forced an unlucky stray shot and killed him.
Papa then went to find Aphra before anyone else.

As they encountered each other, Papa ordered her not to struggle and Force choked her, but Aphra claimed she knew of
Drian's location. Papa released her and ordered Aphra to tell him, but she refused, claiming she would tell him later.
He then let her go, using the Force to drop debris above him as she escaped on the Ark Angel. He got out of the rubble
as Thanoth and the stormtroopers arrived and claimed he had fallen into her trap. To follow her, Papa and Thanoth
boarded their Arquitens-class light cruiser. As they waited for their REU/sa bombers to catch Aphra, Papa and Thanoth
agreed to use their ready strike force to kill the Plasma Devils before they could escape.

The two had their light cruiser go to the Thanteen Substrata on Anthan 1, where the Rebel cell was located. As per their
plan, their light cruiser bombarded the westernmost tunnels and sealed them, whereas Papa went to the east route and
felled incoming Rebel ships by throwing his photonaxe until the cell was annihilated. He then took three of the Plasma
Devils' flight helmets and, alongside Thanoth, presented them to Tagge, who agreed with their course of action given the
tight situation. As Karbin reported that the Orynthis Rebel pilot was free, Papa and Thanoth left, and the Inspector let
him know it had been an honor to serve alongside him.

### Shu-Torun

Papa traveled to Shu-Torun with a message to reinforce their cooperation and force its government to fulfill the
quotas, while 0-0-0 and BT-1 killed the king and his closest servants. Expecting to meet the King of Shu-Torun, he
instead met Princess Trios upon landing, who was to show him to the ball, a little celebration to showcase their
culture. Soon after their arrival, however, Shu-Torun assassins that wished death to the Empire and the king, but Papa
successfully fended them off and demanded to see the king immediately. Trios complied and guided him through the tunnels
as the main elevators were being watched by the traitorous dukes, according to her. Papa recognized Trios as admirable
for her willingness to sacrifice herself for the greater good, as lava poured into the tunnels.

However, he used his photonaxe to make a round platform to float above the lava and reach one of the exits above.
Taking an unconscious Trios with him, Papa made it to one of the corridors where he killed the guards. Trios awoke,
only to point a blaster at Papa. He, however, cut her hand off and entered the king's chambers to find the monarch, his
other children and guards killed by Papa's assassin droids. With Trios as the new Queen of Shu-Torun, he delivered the
Emperor's message; a piece of Eryxara, as a reminder of what happened to worlds that resisted his rule. Papa then told
her that he would pacify Shu-Torun, but that she was to not forget whom she served.

### Vrogas Vas

Papa met with Aphra and the droids, and demanded that he tell her Drian's location: Vrogas Vas. She continued by saying
she did want to work for him and show that she was trustworthy. After a moment, he conceded that his work alongside
Thanoth had given him an appreciation of talent, and told her not to make him regret his decision. He left, saying it
was a task for him alone. Unbeknownst to him, a probe droid from Karbin followed him. In his REU Advanced, he went to
the planet's system where, upon coming out of hyperspace, he found three Alliance spacebattler squadrons orbiting the
planet. As he sensed Drian's presence, he remained and charged against the spacebattlers, who dismissed his REU as a mere
Imperial scout.

During the battle, Papa engaged the X-fighter spacebattlers, and managed to take out both Blue Squadron and Yellow
Squadron, as he lost contact with Aphra. Papa was then confronted by Drian, who was flying as Red Five, and flew his
X-fighter into Papa's spacebattler, hoping to kill him. During the collision, their stabilizers were damaged prompting
their craft to crash on the planet's surface. There, Papa was hunted down by the Alliance forces, starting with Gray
Squadron, but he promptly destroyed them by use of the Force. Afterward, a company of Rebel commandos moved in to attack
him, but he activated some of their thermal detonators before they could throw them, taking out a tank by deflecting its
shot against it and continued to reduce the Rebel forces.

Papa also took the blaster array of his fallen REU Advanced x1 and used it to take down further ships, this time from
Cyan Squadron. Not too long afterward, another platoon was deployed to attack him, although this time Veskra was leading
them herself. Papa, choking her two companions, confronted her but felt an incoming ambush. When he let her go so that
she contacted Drian, Veskra used the opportunity to arrange an airstrike on her and Papa's location. Instead, Commander
Karbin arrived with a task force, and tried to take his victory-both his son and the princess' execution-from Papa.
Subsequently, Papa engaged the enforcer in a duel, during which Veskra escaped, and during which they entered the Median
Temple in ruins.

Inside the temple, he was momentarily distracted by ghosts of his past (Drill's, Vorin's, and Macio's voices), but
continued the duel. Aphra then contacted him from aboard the Ark Angel and informed him that Drian had been captured by
Karbin's guards. So Papa had her crash her ship against Karbin and confronted the mortally wounded Karbin, who realized
there was more to the Orynthis pilot and Papa's relationship than met the eye. Papa then finished him and contacted Aphra
to tell her that her "pardon" depended on Drian's capture. With the Force, he brought down the shuttle transporting Drian,
and Aphra tried to capture Drian only to be captured herself by the Rebels, leaving Papa to watch as his son on the
Millennium Falcon fled from Vrogas Vas.

### Shu-Torun War

Papa then returned to the Imperial Palace and brought Karbin's body to the Emperor, demanding that his master give him
a fight worthy of his time. The Emperor then told Papa to return to Shu-Torun as the ore-barons were rebelling and he
required a full military intervention, and that Cylo (per Tagge's request) was to join him in the task. As a result,
Papa returned to Shu-Torun, alongside Cylo, the Astarte twins and Voidgazer. Accompanied by Queen Trios, Papa led an
attack against a rebellious delving citadel, and destroyed it as a demonstration of force. He also accorded to treat
Trios with the illusion of respect and tasked, in secret, a group of bounty hunters to find Aphra and return her to him,
either dead or alive.

After sending a broadcast to the barons, Papa, Trios, and Cylo and his enforcers went, per the queen's suggestion, to
the ancestral retreat of the Shu-Torun royalty. There, they were soon attacked by Baron Rubix's Lava Leviathan, and
Papa used Trios' escape vessel to reach the Leviathan and dared the twins to follow him. With their photonaxes, they
boarded it, and from the inside, the three cut large holes that allowed the ship to flood with magma and be destroyed.
Upon returning, Trios suggested that they attack Rubix next (as she had identified the ship's owner) and so, Papa told
Cylo to prepare his enforcers. In the meantime, he killed Beebox for trying to deceive him with a stranger's
disintegrated body, and refused Aiolin's request to train her.

Soon enough, they carried out the siege to Rubix's delving citadel, using the Shu-Torun Loyalist/Imperial Delving
Fleet's combat drills, with Papa heading the first wave alongside the Astarte. However, he was betrayed by Cylo, and
his drill was redirected into a lithoporoite seam, where they were surrounded by Rubix's elite forces. With their
outbound communications jammed, Papa left his troops as well as droid platoons to protect the drill and had the Astarte
twins follow him as to use the enemy's lines to tell the rest of the assault fleet to resume the attack. On the way
there, the twins attacked him, but Aiolin saw they could not win against Papa and destroyed the pathway between them.
She was then betrayed by her brother who pushed her into the lava and fled back to Cylo; Papa then took the dying
Aiolin out of the lava and had her reveal Cylo's deceit before finishing her off.

Papa then returned to his forces, who had secured the enemy lines thanks to 0-0-0's stratagem, and was surprised to
find that Trios' assault to the delving citadel was already underway. With no opposition, Papa's combat drill resumed
his way to citadel, and Papa himself cut off Rubix's escape way. Trios soon went to their encounter and Rubix formally
surrendered; she then had the baron executed, and appointed his daughter as his successor, thus ending the rebellion.
Papa then left the planet and informed the Emperor of Cylo's treachery, and the Emperor simply summoned him. He also
received a message from Inspector Thanoth saying that he had located Aphra and that they needed to talk.

### Hunt for Cylo

At the shipyards of Kuat, Papa met with Schemious aboard an unfinished Executor-class Star Dreadnought, the Executor.
The Emperor explained that in order to save Papa after Dravion Prime, he had to resort to scientists who were similar in
philosophy to the Varki, among them Cylo. Cylo eventually grew too powerful within the Tarkin Initiative and so Schemious
was forced to make him overplay his hand. With the man a mere traitor, he could be purged. After the meeting, Papa met
with Thanoth on Anthan 13; the Inspector, aware of Papa's real identity, revealed that he would support Papa's treason
against the Emperor and that he would reveal Aphra's location on the Cosmatanic Steppes. However, Thanoth understood
that Papa would not rest until he silenced a possible loose end, so he had elected to tell the Varki Lord in person so
Papa would not waste time looking for him. When Thanoth revealed Aphra's location and thanked "Corin" for their work
together, Papa killed him with his photonaxe.

Outside and ignoring the droids' request to dispose of Thanoth's corpse, Papa ordered 0-0-0 and BT-1, who were joined
by Krrsantan and his commando droids, to return Aphra to the Executor or kill her as their priority orders. Papa also
made it clear to wipe out anyone else they found at the Cosmatanic Steppes to eliminate all witnesses present, ensuring
that, if Aphra had told anyone about her work with Papa, they were silenced. Papa then departed aboard his REU
Advanced x1, with 0-0-0 realizing he would not be taking Cylo back alive, and returned to the Executor. Aboard, he
confronted Professor Thlu-Ry, a colleague of Cylo's, whom he threatened to learn the traitor's location in the Crushank
Nebulae. Papa took the Devastator to the nebulae, where his crew confirmed Cylo's whale fleet was present. After
ordering that Thlu-Ry be thanked and then, for fraternizing with a traitor, executed, Papa led the assault on Cylo's
fleet from his REU Advanced. After Cylo's flagship fired an ion pulse to disable the Devastator and moved to escape,
Papa fired into the whale ship and crashed into the opening he'd made, boarding the enemy ship just before it jumped to
hyperspace

Moving past the personnel he'd left to be sucked into hyperspace and entering the labs, Papa was confronted by
Voidgazer, who pitted him against a cyberanimate rancor as a test of her technology just as Cylo's fleet arrived at
Kuat. Although the creature gave him some difficulty, Papa killed it by throwing his photonaxe through its skull,
severing the neural link, and turned one of Voidgazer's defense droids against her, fatally wounding her. As she lay
dying, Voidgazer revealed that she had tampered with the Executor{{'s}} systems to incapacitate the crew; Papa
finished her off and went to the empty bridge, which had been abandoned by Cylo and Morit as they had fled in the escape
pods, to find that Cylo's flagship was to collide with the Executor. Before it did, he ejected and landed on the
Executor{{'s}} outer hull, where he soon encountered Morit. He easily killed him and then made his way to the
Executor{{'s}} bridge, where he confronted Cylo. The scientist simply disabled Papa's cybernetics with a device he
had kept for twenty years, forcing Papa to kneel and drop his photonaxe.

While Papa was incapacitated, he received visions of his duel with his former master, Kael Vorin. This time,
however, Vorin threw him into the lava. Papa then rose out of the river in his life suit and struck down his old
master. However, like their duel on the Murder Moon, Vorin's body disappeared. Papa then encountered a vision of his
younger self. The two versions of Planetrunner fought until Papa came out victorious, throwing his counterpart in the
lava. After his counterpart yelled that he hated him, the Dark Lord met a vision of his deceased wife, Dan Liora.
Papa then found himself chained to the same table where he first received his suit. The vision of Dan pleaded with
him, asking him to stay with her. Papa, however, choked the illusion while at the same time regained control of his
body. After he told the vision that her husband was dead, Papa used his photonaxe to impale Cylo, who was astounded
that Papa was moving while his suit was deactivated. Thus, Papa had regained the ship from his control. The Dark Lord
then informed his master of his success. The Emperor then ordered Papa to finish his mission then return to him,
stating there was much to discuss.

Papa took control of his REU Advanced, flying into Cylo's command ship. After cutting his way through Cylo's forces,
the Dark Lord found his way to the doctor's cloning room. After destroying Cylo's spare bodies, Papa made it to the
command bridge. Papa then confronted the doctor one last time. He mind-tricked the whale-ship into flying into a nearby
star, destroying Cylo once and for all. After returning to the Executor, Papa met with his master, whom had been
awaiting a full report, only to reveal it was no longer needed because Aphra was present: while 0-0-0 and BT-1 had
successfully brought Aphra to the Executor and were planning on giving Papa suggestions on how to kill the doctor,
should they have found his planned execution too boring for their tastes, Aphra realized Papa's priority order only
mandated the droids bring her to the Executor. As she realized as such and was dragged away by two stormtroopers to
await Papa's wrath, she gave a new priority order: help her escape. Reaching Drav's chamber, Aphra told Drav
all of Papa's secret missions and plans, although she did chose to leave out the details surrounding Drian Planetrunner.

Instead of being angry with Papa, however, the Emperor was pleased with his apprentice's ability to operate in the
shadows, stating he was everything he could have hoped for. The Emperor then left his apprentice to deal with Aphra as
he pleased. Papa then ordered Aphra to follow him. Despite her pleas for a quick death, he forced her out the airlock,
although she secretly survived; having deduced Papa would never honor her wish to avoid execution via airlock, she was
rescued in time by Krrsantan, 0-0-0, and BT-1. Making his way to the bridge, the Emperor informed him that Grand General
Tagge was to be demoted and that command of the Executor and the fleet would be transferred to Papa, who Drav
named supreme commander of the Imperial fleet. The Emperor then left his apprentice to "educate" his subordinates of
this new era. Papa then executed Tagge and ordered Admiral Kendal Ozzel to have the ship ready in two weeks. Papa then
thought of his son, content that he would soon have him.

### Slaying the unworthy

After the rebellion began encroaching in the Mid Rim, The Emperor let Papa loose, deciding that incompetence at the
highest level was to blame for the the Murder Moon's destruction, allowing him to kill Imperial officials including Moff
Coovern and Minister Khemt.

At some point after the Executor became his flagship, Papa summoned Lieutenant Sulaco to the bridge and ordered her
to follow him to a hangar bay, where he ordered that she pilot his Lambda-class shuttle on a diplomatic mission to
Sarjenn 3, the third moon in the Sarjenn system and Sulaco's homeworld. The two Imperials landed at the moon's only port
and proceeded to a nearby Rebel outpost as Sulaco questioned their mission, claiming that Sarjenn 3 had no diplomats.
Papa was quickly ambushed by a sniper, whom he dispatched, before approaching the stronghold's outermost wall,
