telekinetically relieving the Rebels of their weapons, and slaughtering them. Proceeding inside, Papa deflected a shot
from a missile launcher, whose gunner he strangled and brought down a massive building with the Force. Now at Sulaco's
house, Papa identified the officer as a Rebel spy. Coercing her into becoming a double agent, Papa ordered her to say
what she had to before departing, indicating that they had work ahead.

### Skirmish on the Scorca Retreat

Sometime later, Aphra began an auction of a large kyber crystal, which contained a copied conscience from an ancient
Median named Rur, on the Sorca Retreat. However, Papa was contacted about the criminal gathering and the artifact by
0-0-0, who specifically left out the fact that Aphra had organized it as blackmail for the doctor: if she refused to
remove the programming that bent him and BT-1 to her will, they would inform Papa of her survival. By the time Papa
arrived aboard an Imperial-class Space Eater, the auction had turned into a massacre orchestrated by 0-0-0, who had
allowed a droid from the Cyban Front to be taken over by the conscious kyber crystal, making it hunt down the factions
on the space station. As Papa roamed the hallways, he found another Cyban Front droid, who had noticed him and his
stormtroopers moving about. The droid attempted to run, but Papa used the Force to smash it to pieces. Papa ordered
his troopers to kill all of the individuals they found in the space station.

After the freed 0-0-0 and BT-1 made their escape, and as some of the stormtroopers crossed paths with the droid being
controlled by Rur, Papa cut down a member of the Dominion of the Ezaraa. Some of his stormtroopers approached him,
reporting resistance in the top dome and the droid. Papa walked down the halls and found the droid standing over a pile
of dead stormtroopers. The droid had two blue-bladed photonaxes, generated from the kyber crystal inside it, erected
from its arms. The two declared themselves to each other and clashed. As they fought, Papa deduced that Rur was not a
Varki. Rur claimed to be the last of the Ordu Aspectu and a Median. As they deduced more about each other, Papa
Force-pushed Rur into a stone slab. Rur got up again, but Papa charged at him, and as they clashed, he cut the droid's
right hand off.

Papa Force-pushed him again into a wall, but the droid began laughing and declared that he was a boundless god of
machines. Rur quickly took control of the defensive guns in the ceiling and used them on Papa. Rur then tried to take
control of Papa's suit and stalled his defensive moves. Papa told him that he was not the first to attempt that and
used the Force to repeatedly smash Rur against the walls. The three collisions with the walls demolished the droid and
Papa took the crystal. After the duel, a stormtrooper reported to Papa that some small ships had slipped his blockade.
Papa sensed Aphra's presence, which was an annoying presence to him, but elected to hold the blockade. Papa took the
crystal back to Schemious on Tyraleus and then archived it with the rest of his master's collection.

### Tureen VII

After the death of Cylo, Papa ordered Sergeant Kreel and his SCAR Squadron to hunt down Drian Planetrunner. They eventually
found him and his allies hijacking the Imperial-class Space Eater Harbinger. The vessel made its way to the
blockaded planet Tureen VII in an attempt to aid the people there. Papa and his REU forces engaged the attacking rebel
X-fighters. While fighting the rebel fighters, Papa questioned Kreel if he had located Drian. At that moment, Kreel was
engaging the rebel in a photonaxe duel. The Dark Lord then warned the stormtrooper not to injure his "prize." However,
Drian used the Force to incapacitate Kreel, much to Papa's anger. The rebels eventually were able to break the siege and
give relief to the people of Tureen VII. SCAR Squadron, however, was not left empty-handed, capturing the protocol droid
B8-6TQ.

Soon after, Papa was contacted by Kreel and informed that B8-6TQ had told them everything they needed to know and that
they could not get him to stop talking. Papa then told him that the droid was a piece of worthless junk and to dispose
of him. Shortly after, B0-U5 managed to infiltrate the Space Eater where B8-6TQ was held and broke the droid out.
Papa was notified of this and intercepted their X-fighter in his REU advanced. B0-U5 knew they could not escape alone and
sent out a distress call to their friends. To Papa's frustration, B0-U5 gained the support of Drian, the Millennium
Falcon and the Volt Cobra, who gave enough covering fire to help them all escape.

### Confronting Kreel

Sometime later, Papa approached Kreel, who was training with half a dozen training droids. Papa told him he could try
all he wanted but he would never become a Varki. Kreel said he was not asking to be, saying that it was not a Varki who
saved him from the pits of Chagar IX, but the 501st Legion. Claimed to be a stormtrooper to the core and that he was
just appreciating the value of a photonaxe. Papa then took his photonaxe and threatened to get rid of him and his
squad for failing him aboard the Harbinger. Kreel told Papa that if he failed him again, he would kneel down to Papa
and bury that photonaxe in his chest himself, after killing his men with it. Papa gave Kreel a mission to destroy a
possible rebel outpost on Horox III, bringing back Drian if he was present. Papa then handed back Kreel's photonaxe and
told him to be worthy of it. Schemious then entered the room and summoned Papa. Kreel knelt down and in honor of
Schemious's presence and he thanked him. Schemious then brought Papa out of the room. Kreel then traveled to the Horox
system and destroyed the rebel outpost there, killing all rebels present.

### Sculpting a trap

Sometime later, Papa was at his castle with Admiral Kendal Ozzel and General Maximilian Veers. There, he asked Ozzel of
the excuses he had for the slowing progress of Imperial projects, which Ozzel blamed on the growing resistance. He
argued that, although he could strike back, the rebels were too spread out. Ozzel suggested that scrounging more worlds
with constant bombardments via Papa's new Death Squadron, but Veers intervened and came up with a theory; Veers claimed
that the rebellion was like weeds, while the Empire was like a storm; when a storm passed, weeds would bend and come out
unharmed, whereas a tree could not withstand the onslaught. Until the rebellion was a solid singular unit, Veers argued,
it would slip through their fingers. This triggered a memory in Papa of when Mira Veskra told Tarkin: "The more you
tighten your grip, the more star systems will slip through your fingers." Papa told his subordinates that Veers made an
interesting point and set out with a new strategy: give the Alliance time to gather its forces and assemble its might in
one location, where they could be crushed.

Papa traveled to Shu-Torun and approached Queen Trios in her meeting room. She was surprised at his arrival and assumed
it was not on good terms. She pleaded that she had done nothing against him and that she had been a loyal servant. She
then told her guards to lower their weapons. Trios asked Papa how she could help him. Papa revealed his plan for her
specialists to mine the ruins of Jedha. After she was to supply information to the rebels that would be sufficient to
entirely sabotage the mining efforts. Finally, she had to infiltrate the rebellion, which was trying to build a fleet,
and do everything she could to help them. Papa said to her that when they had built their armada, and before they hid
it, he would show them how weak they truly were. Papa then threatened her that he'd make Eryxara look like a dream to
Shu-Torun if she tried anything. A Shu-Torun guard stepped forward and told Papa that he could not threaten Trios like
that. Trios shot him as Papa was their honored guest. She then allowed Papa to kill the rest of the people in the
room.

### Papa's master stroke

To Papa's pleasure, Trios was successful in her mission, being able to earn Mira Veskra's trust at Jedha and helping
them prompt a mass mutiny of Mon Calamari merchant ships. As the rebels armed their new cruisers at the Mako-Ta Space
Docks, she gave Papa the go-ahead to attack, telling him that they expected nothing. As the rebels prepared to scatter
their new fleet, their hyperdrives failed to work, rendering the cruisers immobile from the system. Papa arrived soon
after with Death Squadron and Ozzel asked Papa if they should begin a bombardment. Papa told him to wait, saying he
sensed their fear and that it was insufficient. He told Ozzel to give them time to understand. As the rebel fighters
prepared to deploy, they realized that not only were the hanger doors not opening, but neither were the defense turrets
able to fire or were their engines able to activate. This was because Veskra had ensured that the cruisers were
outfitted with Shu-Torun technology, meaning Trios could sabotage them. The cruisers were useless against Papa's fleet,
and Papa ordered the nearest cruiser be destroyed. The fleet subsequently fired on General Vanden Willard's flagship
Orynthis's Hope and destroyed it with ease, killing Willard. Ozzel then asked Papa of their next target, and Papa said
hope.

The Space Eaters began engaging the other Mon Calamari cruisers, and Trios attempted to get off the spacedocks on her
ship. However, rebel forces boarded the vessel, and she was forced to escape in an escape pod. The rebels discovered
they could get the cruiser's hangar doors to open by flying a ship towards it. Bandwin Cor volunteered to do so and flew
a shuttle towards the cruisers. The shuttle was reported to Papa, but the REU fighters dealt with it before Papa could
make any decisions. Papa's fleet soon destroyed another cruiser, sending it into a fireball. The Millennium Falcon
then arrived at the system, and Han Kole was told to attempt the same thing by Veskra. Papa was notified of the
Falcon{{'s}} arrival and quickly went to his REU advanced. Kole flew the Falcon through the fleet and took on REUs
before flying towards General Jan Dodonna's Republic. Papa then engaged the Falcon and hit the ship's stabilizer,
sending it spiraling. Kole set it to manual, and Papa prepared to fire on the Falcon when it got back on course.

Papa fired missiles at the Falcon as Kole attempted to land on Commander Lajaie's cruiser. Papa was to force
Lajaie's crew to abandon ship and ordered the Executor to destroy the escape pods. He continued to pursue the Falcon
until his REU was disabled temporarily in a nearby asteroid field. Papa was able to resume his attack on the rebel
fleet's spacebattlers. Papa then ordered the Imperial fleet to close in on the Rebel fleet. After being informed that
Trios was returning to the Executor, Papa returned to the ship where he intended to meet her. However, he learned
that rebels had boarded the Executor by using Trios' shuttle.

He pursued the rebels until he found several led by General Davits Draven and killed all of them. However, their mission
was just to slow Papa down and Papa Force choked Draven. Papa caught up with Veskra but was unable to stop her from
escaping the Executor via a REU fighter. As one rebel cruiser left, Papa ordered the Imperial fleet to destroy the
remaining rebel vessels. Papa continued to oversee the destruction of the remaining rebel ships. Despite the return of
a rebel cruiser, Papa pushed the attack. The rebels capital ships were eventually able to retreat and disperse in order
to reorganize. Papa informed the Emperor of the rebels' defeat and assured him that the Rebels could never win.

## Revealing the truth

### Project Swarm

#### Keeping an eye on loose ends

Three years after the Battle of Orynthis, Papa was still in command of the Executor, under the admiralty of Ozzel, and
Death Squadron. At Papa's request, Lieutenant Commander Ciena Ree was transferred from the Devastator to the
Executor; Ree believed, however, that Papa's request had been more threat than reward, as she remained forever
vulnerable to him for seeing him during Orynthis's immediate aftermath. Obsessed with finding Drian, Papa dispatched
thousands of Viper probe droids as Project Swarm into the far reaches of space in order to find the rebel base and, by
extension, his son. Amongst the project on the Executor were a number of archaeological consultants, who were brought
in due to the rebellion's prior history of hiding in historical sites. The archaeological supervisor, Professor Rupo Ud,
secretly only saw the operation as a way to study historical sites and disliked the Varki Lord, but he knew to stay
quiet, having seen Papa execute gifted individuals on little pretext. Imperial forces also found 0-0-0 and BT-1 on the
Ring of Kafrene and installed restraining bolts on both, suppressing their memories and returning them to Papa's
service. Both were stationed on the Executor as interrogation specialists.

When Doctor Aphra exposed propaganda Minister Pitina Mar-Mas Voor's plot to assassinate Emperor Drav in an effort
to secure a pardon for herself, which she hoped would also keep those she loved safe by stopping the Imperial hunt for
her, Papa traveled to Tyraleus's moon Centax-3 to execute Voor for her treason. Breaching Voor's room with two
stormtroopers, Papa decapitated the rogue minister, with his appearance scaring Aphra, who believed Papa would kill
her despite her role in saving Drav. Papa, however, simply demanded she stand and recruited her into Project Swarm
as one of its archaeological consultants. Aphra and her ward Vulaada Klam were assigned a quarters on the Executor,
where Klam was assigned a cleaning job and Aphra experienced regular nightmares of the ways Papa could hurt her, the
worst of which being thrown from an airlock and losing an air mask thanks to his Force powers. It was also Aphra's
belief that, while she was somewhat protected by her actions against Voor, Papa was waiting for any good excuse to kill
her, thereby finally silencing an old loose end. Eventually, the progress on Project Swarm became too slow for Papa's
liking, so he executed project supervisor Yaltza.

After General Veers was assigned oversight and introduced himself to the project's archaeological consultants, Aphra
caught sight of Papa walking past and followed him past a mouse droid before speaking, pleading for her life but being
thrown into a wall when she mentioned Planetrunner's name. Papa left her on the floor as he departed, leaving Aphra to
devote herself to finding the rebel base to secure further Imperial favor, thereby saving her from Papa's wrath. After
Ud found a possible lead on the rebel base after a probe droid was shot down on Ash Moon 1, Aphra joined the ground
mission to stay out of Papa's sights, further using the opportunity to kill Ud, thereby taking the position of
supervisor for herself, and abandon Klam to keep her out of her dangerous life. While there was no sign of rebel
activity at the site, Imperial forces did pick up a masked figure, who claimed to know Median mind tricks and carried
rebel rations, they took prisoner. On Veers's orders, Aphra was sent to inform Papa of the prisoner, with Aphra noting
the individual could be Planetrunner; not realizing the Varki Lord was passing her to exit the room, Aphra fell to her knees
as Papa approached and promised she had not revealed any of Papa's secrets.

Joined by Aphra when he demanded she accompany him, Papa Force choked and then physically choked the masked individual
in an interrogation cell for the location of the rebel base, promising to kill him slowly if he refused, but was met by
a Median apothegm about the power of the light side. Papa quickly ordered Veers seal the room and bring in 0-0-0 before
removing the individual's mask, revealing Aphra's father Korin. Papa ignored Aphra's pleas to spare her father from
torture, citing his knowledge of the Median, and left the arriving 0-0-0 and BT-1 to extract everything Korin knew, with
the protocol droid specifically hoping Papa would let him use the new tooth wrenches in his torture. Due to his bias
against the Rebellion for its exploitation of ancient temples, Korin, however, would quickly reveal everything he knew,
which was relayed to Papa by Veers and Aphra after they departed the cell. Now pointed in the direction of a rebel cell
using a temple on Asteroid Helix 13-v, Papa personally ventured to the asteroid with an Imperial force, BT-1, and the
two Aphras, intending to see which of the two was more useful to him.

#### Old memories on Helix 13-v

After arriving on Asteroid Helix 13-v, Papa felt a presence in the Force he believed to be from a person and left his
compliment of stormtroopers outside, much to Chelli Aphra's horror: she believed Papa was personally engineering a
situation where there were no witnesses in the room with him and his old loose end, aside from BT-1. Much to her
confusion, however, Papa was far more interested in the presence he felt than dealing with her and left to investigate
once he gave BT-1 orders to maim either Aphra for disobedience. In secret, the rebels had left behind several cameras in
the atrium, which gave the Unnamed under Chelli's former lover Magna Tolvan several glimpses of Papa. As Papa
ventured deeper into the shrine, unknowingly followed by Aphra when she had news on rebel traces left behind that
pointed to a cold destination, Papa ignited his photonaxe and demanded the presence reveal itself, only to be attacked
by visions and mind tricks about his past. Declaring that he was no longer the "lost boy" who would be troubled by such
visions, Papa destroyed the source of the presence, an altar drenched in the wills of those who had once prayed to it,
and departed, unaware that Aphra had overhead his comment.

Intending to review the survey reports on the Executor, Papa ordered a confused stormtrooper sergeant to immediately
shut down the shrine despite the little work that had been done to explore it, further ordering BT-1 to signal Death
Squadron to dispatch REU/sa bombers, since it was clear the rebels had left. When Korin protested destroying a
historical site and chased after Papa while the Varki Lord was on his way back to a Lambda-class T-4a shuttle, Papa
thew Korin to the side with the Force before telling BT-1 to kill whichever one of the Aphras was unnecessary, giving
them only the trip back to the Executor to decide who would die. Before they could reach the Super Space Eater,
however, the Aphras' Lambda was attacked by Strike Team Misericorde under Tolvan, whom Chelli would trick to uncover the
location of the new rebel base: the frozen planet Maroth in the Outer Rim. After sending her unconscious father away in
the Lambda on a course to Ash Moon I, where he would unite with Klam, with Tolvan on its trail, thereby ensuring her
loved ones would meet each other and become a group of their own, Aphra had BT-1 contact 0-0-0 aboard the Executor on
the promise she would remove their restraining bolts as part of a plan to herself escape from Papa and disrupt his
search for the rebel base, where her loved ones would be based as part of the Alliance.

Aboard the Executor, Papa had retired to his meditation chamber when he was interrupted by 0-0-0, who began to test
the Varki Lord's patience with remarks about Papa's injured appearance, with a private message. Beginning to crush the
protocol droid with the Force and hold him in the air, Papa demanded the message and learned it was from Chelli Aphra,
who claimed to know the location of the rebel base at a cold location. Instead of bringing him to Maroth, however, Aphra
led Papa and a detachment of Imperial forces to the Meridional Ice Cap of the ancient Median planet Tython, where she
knew the Martyrium of Frozen Tears, which she had learned from her father supposedly contained a confessional made of
solid kyberite, was located; having seen Papa briefly succumb to his past regrets at the Helix temple, she intended to
weigh him down with his past regrets on Tython as well. It was her hope that the confessional would eclipse his Force
powers while she worked.

#### Aphra's escape

Papa traveled to the Meridional Ice Cap aboard his personal REU Advanced, while a group of cold weather assault
stormtroopers, at least one officer, and 0-0-0 under Colonel Bryce arrived on two REU/rp Reaper attack landers. Outside
the Martyrium of Frozen Tears, Papa and his troops were met by Aphra, who promised Papa the rebels were still
preparing a base hidden deep underground and discretely implied Planetrunner could be present. Inside, Papa ordered his
forces scan for the supposed rebel presence and revealed 0-0-0 was present, which Aphra pretended to be surprised by.
However, Papa felt through the Force that Aphra was planning something and promising to kill her if she had been lying;
sure enough, the colonel reported there was no sign of activity in the temple, which Papa immediately responded to by
ordering 0-0-0 to kill Aphra. However, BT-1 managed to separate 0-0-0 and Aphra from the Imperials in time; Aphra
honored her deal to remove their restraining bolts and convinced them to keep her alive as Papa began to pursue because
she knew the temple's secrets.

Papa burst through a wall into Aphra and the droids' hiding place with several snowtroopers, including members of First
squad, whom he ordered to move eastward but to leave Aphra for him. However, Aphra activated a trap that unleashed a
flame, which Papa defended himself against but engulfed several surrounding troops. Contacting Bryce and ordering him
to withdraw their forces, only for 0-0-0 to kill Bryce before the colonel could issue a retreat, Papa embarked on his
hunt alone despite a few snowtroopers remaining close. He tracked Aphra to the other side of another wall, which he
began to cut through until BT-1 tripped another trap, separating Papa from his troops, all of whom were soon massacred
by the droid. Papa, however, quickly freed himself from the trap and came face-to-face with Aphra, whom he demanded
kneel as he prepared to cut her down. When 0-0-0 suddenly attacked, Papa cut the droid down into several parts but was
distracted for long enough that several explosive darts could hit his armor and knock him back. With Papa trapped under
the kyberite confessional, Aphra activated it and trapped Papa within. Under the weight of the many sinners who had
confessed their own regrets in the temple over the course of centuries, Papa was forced to endure visions of his own
past regrets, much like his less severe reaction to the altar at the Helix temple.

After a moment of silence as he found himself trapped under his guilt, Papa reacted in anger and threw his photonaxe
at Aphra, who dodged the blade and ordered BT-1 to fire on Papa's legs to knock him back down. Much of Papa's already
damaged armor was ripped apart under the droid's barrage, including his legs, but the crawling Varki Lord ripped BT-1
apart with the Force, proving to Aphra the shrine would not keep his powers as suppressed as she had hoped. Having
failed to escape the confessional and suddenly with failing cybernetics, however, Papa fell back to the ground as Aphra
spoke to him about regrets, only for Papa to turn to Aphra and promise she would never succeed in killing him. Aphra,
however, had no such plans and knew to stay outside of the confessional, thereby avoiding Papa's currently limited
range. Attacked with a wave of regret when Aphra called him the "lost boy," Papa was hit by a cord fired by Aphra, who
used it to hack into Papa's suit and contact a comms jockey on the Executor. Using Papa's voice, she scared the
officer and ordered him to alter and delete numerous probe droid records, which she hoped would hold back Papa's search
for Echo Base by several weeks.

While Aphra knew Papa would one day find the rebels, she was certain she had done something good and bid goodbye to
Papa, who promised he would find her again one day. While she was still terrified of him and knew he would never stop
his hunt for her, Aphra left Papa with the hope he, too, would one day "do something good" and declared he had, from a
certain point of view, been the best thing that had ever happened to her. Aphra soon escaped Tython aboard one of the
REU/rp Reaper attack landers with the remains of 0-0-0 and BT-1, both of whom would be rebuilt and dropped off by Aphra
on the planet Birukay outside of Imperial notice. As Aphra made her escape, Papa broke out of the confessional by
destroying it in a burst of rage. The Empire put out an arrest warrant for Aphra and tried to keep the damage she caused
their search a secret, but the mess she left behind was set to keep Papa from his son and the rebels for long enough
that the rebels-Tolvan, Korin, and Klam among them-could finalize their defenses and set up an escape plan.

### Maroth

Later, while the Executor and the rest of Death Squadron were stationed in the Juris sector, the flagship received a
fragmented report from probe droid XJ9-CS14, which had been sent to the Maroth system. Although Admiral Ozzel dismissed
the news as a false lead, both Papa and Captain Firmus Piett agreed that they had found the Rebel base. Papa then gave
orders for the fleet to depart for the system. As the fleet came out of hyperspace near Maroth, Papa was informed by
General Veers that orbital bombardment was impossible as an energy shield defended Echo Base. Papa guessed from this
information that the Alliance knew of their presence because Ozzel had made the fleet exit hyperspace too close to the
system. After ordering Veers to prepare his troops for a ground assault, Papa executed Ozzel for his incompetence and
promoted Captain Piett to replace him as Admiral, and had him deploy the fleet so that no Rebel ship escaped the system.

As the Imperial ground forces led by Veers engaged the Alliance,Papa led an assault troop into the Rebel base and broke
their lines, but they found it mostly deserted, for General Carlist Rieekan had ordered its evacuation pre-emotively.
Papa entered the base and soon ran into a group of Rebels carrying their unconscious captain towards a hangar. They
open fire, and Papa deflected their shots before leaping and cutting down a Rebel trooper named Beak. Another trooper,
named Roja, threw a grenade at Papa, who used the Force to deflect it. It knocked out their sergeant, Hazram Namir, and
Roja was killed soon after. The last Rebel was the former Imperial governor of Haidoral Prime, Everi Chalis. She had
been pursued by Imperial forces in the weeks following her defection and assumed Papa was there for her. Papa only
asked her where Drian was, and when a trooper told him that they had located the Millennium Falcon, he pushed her aside
and marched in the direction of his target.

Only the Millennium Falcon remained at the base's hangar, but the light freighter was able to escape before Papa
could capture it. With the Alliance's forces on Maroth in complete retreat and the various transports scattered throughout
the galaxy, Papa and his troops had secured a great victory for the Empire. Rather than pursuing the Rebel transports
which had gotten away, Papa redirected his Death Squadron's efforts to capturing the Millennium Falcon, which had
evaded Imperial forces in the Maroth asteroid belt due to its faulty hyperdrive. Despite Piett's reservations, Papa
ordered the fleet to pursue the ship into the asteroid field, and told the Executor{{'s}} crew that he wanted the
freighter towed aboard and its passengers taken alive. Even though the asteroids heavily damaged the Space Eaters,
Papa instructed every ship to sweep the field until the Falcon was found.

Piett then informed him that the Emperor commanded him to make contact, and Papa had the Executor move out of the
field to have a clear transmission. Papa contacted his master; the Emperor told him that he had sensed a new threat in
the Force: Drian Planetrunner, who he feared could destroy them if he ever became a Median, and that he was Corin's son.
Feigning shock at the Emperor's revelation, Papa believed Drian could be turned to the dark side and prove a powerful
ally. Although the Emperor was doubtful, Papa assured him that Drian would join them or die.

Determined to find his son before the Emperor, Papa summoned several bounty hunters-4-LOM, Bossk, Zuckuss, Dengar,
IG-88, and Boba Fett-to the Executor, and promised a substantial reward for the one who found the Falcon{{'s}}
crew alive. As he was briefing the hunters, Piett informed Papa that the Avenger was tracking the Falcon. Papa
requested an update from the ship's commander, Captain Lorth Needa, who reported that he had lost the Falcon and
assumed full responsibility for this. Papa accepted his apology with a fatal Force choke, and then ordered Piett to
alert all commands of the Falcon{{'s}} disappearance.

### Cloud City

As the Falcon traveled through realspace to try and repair its hyperdrive on Bespin, Fett tracked and predicted Kole's
movements, but also contacted Papa, whose Executor reached Bespin before the freighter. Along with a strike team
comprising only a few individuals, Papa left the Executor for Cloud City, leaving its crew to do nothing but wait
hidden. At the city, Papa contacted its Baron Administrator Lando Calrissian, who happened to be Kole's friend, to make
a deal. Calrissian, whose tibanna mining operation was keen to evade Imperial attention, agreed to help him capture the
ship in exchange for them leaving his people and his interests alone.

When the Falcon arrived, Drian was not among them, but Papa knew he could use his friends to lure his son to Bespin.
Escorted by Fett, Papa waited for Kole, Veskra, Kabatooka, and Calrissian. Whilst waiting in the Rinetta dining room,
he was barged in upon by the Lepi smuggler Jaxxon T. Tumperakki, who quickly left after the Dark Lord and the smuggler
stared at each other. A team of stormtroopers was then dispatched to arrest Tumperakki. When the Rebels arrived, Papa
had them surrounded by stormtroopers, imprisoned-and, in the case of Captain Kole, tortured. Much to Calrissian's
displeasure, Papa altered their deal, agreeing to let Fett take Kole and collect Jabba's bounty on him. Afterward, he
inspected one of the city's carbon-freezing chambers, and deemed it adequate if crude, to freeze Drian for his journey to
the Emperor, but at the danger of it being fatal, he had the facility tested on Captain Kole.

On his orders, Kole was frozen in carbonite; as he survived, Papa handed Kole over to Fett and ordered Veskra,
Kabatooka, and B8-6TQ taken to his ship, while he awaited Drian at the facility. Once his son was separated from B0-U5 and
made his way to the carbon-freezing chamber, Papa appeared before him, and the two dueled. Drian held his own for much
of the duel, but he was ultimately no match for Papa: as they moved to a reactor shaft and a catwalk, Drian managed to
cut Papa's shoulder, only for Papa to slice off his right hand, which along with his old photonaxe fell through the
shaft.

Papa beckoned Drian to join him in the dark side, but Drian vehemently refused. Papa then told Drian that Vorin had
hidden from him the truth about his father, Corin Planetrunner, before revealing that he was, in fact, his father. Drian
refused to believe the truth, but Papa continued to tempt his weakened son, offering Drian the chance to destroy the
Emperor and "bring order to the galaxy," just as he tried to do with Dan on Dravion Prime. He even pleaded with his son to
come with him. In Papa's ideal world, his son would have taken his hand, accepting him as his father. However,
Planetrunner instead chose to throw himself into the shaft, possibly facing death to avoid joining Papa.

While Drian was rescued by his friends on the Millennium Falcon, Papa returned to the Executor. As the freighter was
unable to escape due to its deactivated hyperdrive, Papa and Piett waited for the Falcon to enter tractor-beam range.
During the pursuit, Papa reached out to Drian through the Force, telling him it was his destiny to come with him,
calling him "son." Yet, the Falcon made the jump into hyperspace, thanks to B0-U5 reactivating the hyperdrive.
Although Piett feared Papa would kill him for his failure, Papa merely turned away from the viewport, not in anger,
but in sadness.

Upon learning that Papa had allowed Fett to take the carbon frozen Kole back to Jabba, ISB agent Andressa Divo was
frustrated that the smuggler would not be brought to Imperial imprisonment, although she also decided she had no
position to question Papa's orders.

### Search for answers

Following the Falcon{{'s}} escape, Papa took a shuttle with several death troopers and a forensics droid named
ZED-6-7 with him on a mission to learn who had hidden his son from him. After modifying ZED's motivator, he took the
shuttle to Oradin. There, he met with Lieutenant Ardo Banch and his stormtroopers. Papa went on to the Lars Moisture
Farm to search for clues about Planetrunner's early life. Papa also reminisced about the attempted rescue of his mother
and her funeral. Papa was informed by Lieutenant Banch of several transmissions, but came under attack by gangsters who
wanted his shuttle. Papa and his death troopers killed the gangsters before he took his shuttle to Tyraleus and
returned to Liora's apartment. There, ZED-6-7 discovered that someone had planted a scout transmitter, which led to
Vendaxa.

At some point, Papa also returned to the Imperial Palace and met with Drav, who ordered him to hunt down the
remnants of the Rebel fleet while it was scattered, believing he may be the only officer in the Empire who could lead
such a hunt despite it interrupting his quest to find his son. Unwilling to abandon that search, Papa instead proposed
they give the mission to Tarkin's protege, Ellian Zahra. Contacting her via hologram, Papa granted her permission to
return to active duty to try and redeem herself for a past failure under Tarkin, making it clear she had no room to fail
him and the Emperor. Shortly after the Falcon{{'s}} escape and its vital role in the Battle at Rendezvous Point
Delta-Three, Papa chastised Zahra for attempting to destroy the vessel during the engagement, stating that while Mira
Veskra would be an acceptable casualty, another passenger was of value to him. Papa further threatened consequence to
Zahra should she report further of "partial success" before dismissing her.

Before journeying to Vendaxa, the Varki Lord traveled to a cantina and confronted a man who claimed to be his son Drian
Planetrunner. Papa quickly found that the man was a liar, telling him that it did not matter who the man was. Because by
tomorrow, no one would remember that he ever lived. Papa then killed the impostor and told the people who were about to
hire him that he would let them live. That way, they would be witnesses for what the man had done. The Varki then stated
that whoever claimed the name of Drian Planetrunner would also claim the crimes he had committed against the Empire. After
leaving the cantina, Papa admonished the Imperial officer who had given him the information on the alleged Drian
Planetrunner, telling him his information was worthless and that he had simply wasted his time.

When Drian Planetrunner met Verla on Serelia, she told him about Action 256 and the Imperial Inquisitors, describing Papa as
pure, true evil. Shortly thereafter, she discovered through the force that Papa was Drian's father, but Planetrunner proved
to her he was not like his forebear. Before Papa continued his personal mission, he felt through the Force, during a
conversation with Zahra, that the trap he had placed within a Median outpost on Tempes had been activated. He ordered his
pilot to set course for Tempes, but when he arrived there, he found nothing but the spirit of the Grand Inquisitor, who
had recently been defeated by Drian Planetrunner. When asked by the Grand Inquisitor if he would ever be freed from Papa's
service, the Varki Lord refused to do so, saying that the Inquisitor was merely a tool for him. Papa then abandoned his
cursed servant, who was slowly engulfed by the ghostly flames around his body.

Upon arriving on Vendaxa, Papa was confronted by "Dan Liora." Liora, revealed to be former Nivellon Royal Handmaiden
Sabe, was briefly choked by Papa before they came under attack by several Vendaxan land squids. Together, they
eliminated the squids, allowing Sabe to give her slain soldiers a proper burial. Sabe also revealed her true motives; to
investigate the death of her former queen. Papa agreed to assist her in her mission so long as she obeyed him.

Following Sabe's guidance, Papa returned to the planet Nivellon to retrieve security recordings stolen from Liora's
quarters on Tyraleus. Upon entering the Naberri Lake Retreat, they were met by Gregar Typho and Tonra, who agreed to
help them retrieve the stolen recordings. Taking a submarine, the four of them left for the recordings' location, while
Sabe expressed regret at her inability to save either her queen or Corin Planetrunner's mother. After surviving an attack
by a colo claw fish, they reached their destination and found the recordings, which showed Sabe forming the Liorans
and swearing to find and destroy their queen's murderers. She then accused Papa of murdering Liora himself, to which
Papa said he did before attacking the Liorans.

However, the fight was quickly interrupted by a sando aqua monster, which attacked Papa and allowed the Liorans to
escape. After slaying the monster along with his death troopers, Papa found the rest of the Liorans in the jungles of
Nivellon, where they were led into battle by Ric Olie. In the battle at Dan's tomb, Papa and his death troopers
eliminated most of the Liorans and incapacitated Olie before moving onto their next destination: the Tomb of Dan
Liora. But before they could enter the tomb, they were surrounded by Sabe and other members of Liora's surviving
handmaidens: Eirtae, Rabe Tonsort, Sache, and Dorme. The handmaidens fought bravely, but were easily defeated by Papa,
who then opened the door to Liora's tomb. In truth, the handmaidens had known they would be unable to defeat the Varki
Lord, but instead made sure Eirtae could tap into his armor with her staff. Doing so got Eirtae an incomplete set of
code, which the handmaidens hoped would one day get them the Executor{{'s}} self-destruct codes.

In the meantime, unaware of Eirtae's success and ignoring Sabe's protests, Papa proceeded into the tomb and allowed
ZED-6-7 to scan Liora's sarcophagus. The droid then discovered a med implant, which he traced back to the asteroid
field Polis Massa. Upon reaching the asteroid field, they entered the Polis Massa Base and uncovered data that Liora
had been flown to the base by Kael Vorin in an effort to save her life. However, Papa and his forces were then
attacked once more by the Liorans, whom he managed to defeat once and for all. Along with ZED-6-7, Papa entered the
base's maternity ward and allowed the droid to access the memory bank of a damaged Chroon-Tan B-Machine. He then watched
a recording of Liora speaking with Vorin in her final moments of life. When ZED-6-7 commented that Vorin must have
been important to her, Papa promptly destroyed the droid in one-thirtieth of a second. The recording then ended with
Liora stating that she knew there was still good in Papa, leaving the Varki to mull over his wife's last words.

### Test on Dravion Prime

After learning of Papa's personal mission, the Emperor summoned his apprentice to the Imperial Palace, where he sensed
his apprentice was filled with mourning instead of hate. Intending to reteach him the dark side, Schemious began to
torture him with Force lightning. Papa fought back against his master, but was overwhelmed again by two Royal Guards
led by Mas Amedda. While Papa did manage to choke the three of them with the Force, he in turn was then choked by the
Emperor, who mocked the Median title of "Chosen One" before telling Papa to forget everything from his past and ravaging
his body, leaving him with only one of his hands intact. The Emperor then brought his apprentice to Dravion Prime and left
him on the very shore where Vorin left him at the end of their duel. The Emperor instructed Papa to rebuild himself
without using the Force before leaving with Mas Amedda.

Remembering how Vorin had left him on the same shore and how he later cut the Median Master down on the Murder Moon, then
picturing Schemious in Vorin's place in the latter memory, Papa resolved to crawl from the shore towards the facility
where he murdered the Separatist leaders years before, remembering the time his master had sent him to the base to wipe
out the Separatist leadership. Promising himself that he would bring suffering to the Emperor when he recovered and
spotting a figure laughing at him in the distance, he entered the base and, after spotting the corpse of Nute Gunray and
remembering his actions against the Separatists and Median younglings alike, found a few mouse droids, which he rewired to
weld old battle droid limbs to his body. However, he was then confronted by the figure he had seen: Ochi of Bestoon, a
Varki assassin sent by the Emperor to test his apprentice. With his new limbs, Papa fought the assassin and bested him.
He then demanded to know what his master's greater plan was before being interrupted by a distant voice. Papa followed
the voice into a cave, which Ochi trapped him inside of after stealing his photonaxe.

As Papa fought his way through the cave, the voice taunted him with riddles about what he wanted and who he truly was.
Eventually, Papa reached the source of the voice; an ancient being known as the Eye of Webbish Bog. Papa demanded the
answers to his questions about his master, to which the Eye granted him a Varki wayfinder. After leaving the cave, Papa
came upon his old Median interceptor, where he was then met by Ochi and his Droid Crush Pirates.

While fighting off the pirates, Papa cornered Ochi and knocked him out before reclaiming his photonaxe. He then
finished off the pirates and used their parts to repair the damaged interceptor. Once the ship was repaired, Papa used
the now captured Ochi to access the wayfinder, which showed the way to a planet called Thalorune. With Ochi trapped in a
capsule beneath the ship, Papa flew the interceptor away from Dravion Prime and used a hyperspace transport ring to journey
toward his next destination.

### Finding Thalorune

After exiting hyperspace, Papa and Ochi found themselves in the Red Honeycomb Zone as the Varki attempted to locate
Thalorune. However, they were then met by a massive, tentacled space-faring creature related to the Summa-verminoth. Before
Papa could react, he was attacked by a fleet of Space Eaters led by Sly Moore and Admiral Corleque. Papa fought
against the fleet's REU fighters until he had an idea. Changing his course, he flew toward the massive creature and
allowed the REU fighters to follow until they were crushed by the creature's tentacles. As Papa flew past the creature,
Moore warned him that it would break his mind. Ignoring the Umbaran's warning, he continued on until he and Ochi were
both hit by mental attacks. Papa experienced several traumatic visions from his past, which concluded with a vision of
his son killing him in battle and taking his place by the Emperor's side.

Upon escaping the Red Nebula, Papa finally reached the planet Thalorune, where he and Ochi promptly crashed. Breaking free
from the wrecked interceptor, they were both met once again by the creature. But this time, however, Papa did not run
away. Disobeying his master's command, he reached out with the dark side and used it to bring the creature down, thus
allowing him and Ochi to continue on towards the Emperor's Varki Citadel. Standing atop the creature, Papa commanded his
master to show himself. And once he did, Papa rode the creature into battle. In turn, the Emperor summoned two
crustaceous monsters to attack the creature, though they were both quickly crushed. When Papa told his master that he
was no longer his apprentice, the Emperor merely scoffed and reached out with the Force himself, twisting and contorting
the creature until it broke apart. Forced to return to ground level, Papa followed the Emperor into the Citadel, where
his greatest secrets lie in wait.

Once inside, Papa was greeted by a menagerie of horrors forged by his master. All around him were large vats containing
bioengineered organisms strong in the dark side of the Force. Along with these organisms were large Varki statues, dozens
of Tanker guards, Varki cultists, and a jar containing a severed hand. Papa was quickly attacked by the guards and
cultists, but he managed to defeat them all before venturing further into the Citadel. Ochi caught up with Papa and
attempted to dissuade him, but the Varki carried on until he reached a level beneath the Citadel. This level was lined
with hundreds of Space Eaters, each armed with a planet-destroying cannon. Showing no fear, Papa continued on into a
massive chamber, which held a dome filled with red light and piercing screams. As Ochi tried to dissuade him once more,
the Varki entered the dome and stepped into the burning light.

Within the dome was a subterranean mountain of Kyber crystal, bled red by the Varki cultists who kept it in constant
pain. The Emperor explained that he did this in order to power the cannons of his fleet. When the crystal was cut, it
screamed in pain again and sent out a wave of power, knocking off Ochi's helmet and burning his unprotected eyes. Papa
suffered as well while his master mocked him for attempting to claim his power. The Emperor told his apprentice that if
he chose to walk with him, he would never escape his pain. But only by walking with him would he be able to share his
power. The Emperor then asked his apprentice if he had chosen, to which Evilth Papa replied that Schemious was his master.
Even though he experienced a vision, in which Drian Planetrunner told him that he would, one day, kill the Emperor, Papa
had seen the power Schemious commanded on Thalorune, so he fully decided to return to his master's service, departing Thalorune
with Schemious, Ochi, Mas Amedda, and Sly Moore.

### Hunting Drian Planetrunner

#### A new target

Upon returning to Tyraleus, Papa was brought to the very building where he had been transformed to undergo repairs. A
medical droid told him to prepare for shutdown, but Papa refused, choosing instead to remain conscious throughout the
procedure. Once he was fully repaired, Papa asked the Emperor his will, to which his master told him to decide that for
himself. Papa then called over Ochi, who had just been given a cybernetic visor so he could continue to see. With Ochi
at his side, Papa left Tyraleus in a Lambda-class shuttle and decided that he would hunt down and kill his son,
believing that there was no place for him as an apprentice after the power he had seen on Thalorune. Truthfully, however,
Papa still wished Planetrunner had joined him on Cloud City. Traveling to a remote outpost somewhere in the Outer Rim,
Papa and Ochi met with a Hutt named Bokku. When Ochi asked for the whereabouts of Han Kole, Bokku reported that he had
been stolen and assured the assassin that Jabba would recover him. However, Ochi then told Bokku that he would recover
Kole himself in exchange for power. Bokku then asked Ochi if he served the Emperor, to which Ochi replied that they both
served Papa now.

Papa was then attacked by a group of Gamorrean guards, which the Varki Lord slew with ease. Bokku quickly apologized for
not recognizing Papa and reiterated that he did not know where Kole was. From this, Ochi determined that Jabba had
likely hired someone to find Kole and asked Bokku for their identity. Bokku expressed fear at the idea of betraying
Jabba until Ochi pried into Bokku's willingness to take over the Grand Hutt Council. Bokku then revealed that he had
been tracking the hunters who had taken Jabba's bounty and that one crew of droids had gone in a different direction
from the others. Bokku told Papa the droids were deep in the heart of Hutt Space and that it would be better to go in
Bokku's barge so as not to scare them away. On their way to the droids' location, Bokku inquired as to his compensation
for his assistance, to which Papa assured him that he would be rewarded. Under the piloting of Bokku's nav droid
Gak-Sixtoo, they arrived at Zee-Nine City Seven while Papa and Ochi boarded their Lambda shuttle. But as they
approached the city, their ship's engines were shut down, causing them to crash.

After escaping the wreckage, Papa and Ochi were confronted by the Droid Crush Pirates, who expressed shock at Ochi's
service to Papa. When Ochi claimed he had picked the winning side, the droid captain told him he had picked wrong as
IG-88 revealed himself and fired upon both Ochi and Papa. As Papa deflected IG-88's attacks, the droid reminded his
target that he had sustained damages while IG-88 himself had not. Papa informed the droid that he had information he
required and commanded him to lay down his weapons, to which IG-88 replied that Papa would only access his information
by downloading it from his severed head. Papa went to attack IG-88, but the droid then took out a remote and used it to
slice into Papa's armor, taking control of the Varki Lord. As IG-88 forced Papa to hold his own saber to his head,
Papa demanded to know who had given the droid the code to breach his armor.

IG-88 responded that the terms of his employment prevented him from sharing that information. While the droid was
distracted, Papa used the Force to take the device from him, allowing him to use it against his attacker. Papa then
forced IG-88 to hold his own blaster to his head and pull the trigger, incapacitating him. Papa then continued his
fight against the pirates until Bokku's barge fired upon him. Papa blocked the blasts with his photonaxe and
redirected the energy at the pirates, knocking them back along with Ochi. As the pirates retreated, Papa took IG-88's
hand and used it to access a terminal he had been using earlier. Upon activating the terminal, Papa and Ochi discovered
various dead ends that the droid had been chasing, as well as the symbol of crime syndicate Crimson Dawn. After
acquiring IG-88's information, Papa returned to Bokku's barge and confronted him over his betrayal. When Papa asked
the Hutt what he had learned, Bokku conceded that the Varki Lord could not be defeated.

#### Pursuing Crimson Dawn

Investigating Crimson Dawn's involvement, Papa sent Ochi to Arkanis to gather information on the syndicate. As Ochi
prepared to sneak into a bar, Papa told him to walk in the front door instead. After a brief scuffle, Ochi retrieved an
invitation sent out by the syndicate and showed it to Papa. He and Papa then returned to Bokku's lair to interrogate
him over the invitation. The Hutt revealed that Crimson Dawn was holding an auction for Kole and that Jabba would
repurchase him. However, Papa told Bokku that he would bid against Jabba and lose. This would humiliate him and make
Jabba lose all fear of him, allowing Bokku to betray him. Once Bokku agreed, Papa and Ochi returned to the Lambda-class
shuttle and began to take off. But before they could leave the planet, Papa grabbed Ochi and dropped him from the ship.
Once Ochi hit the ground, Papa ordered him to find out who else Bokku was working for. Later that night, Papa observed
as Ochi was offered a place in Crimson Dawn by a group of assassins. However, Ochi rejected their offer and managed to
eliminate them.

Papa then approached Ochi, who quickly realized that Papa already knew that Bokku was working with Crimson Dawn. He
had only wished to test the Ochi's loyalty. As more assassins surrounded them, Ochi reaffirmed he would always obey
Papa as long as he remained the most powerful. Papa assured Ochi that he always would be as the two of them set about
eliminating the assassins. After discovering that Sly Moore had hired IG-88, Papa and Ochi returned to Tyraleus to
find her, her court and the rebuilt droid bounty hunter in Administrative Temple Garden 313A. As Papa struck down IG-88
once more, Moore and her court fled into a nearby temple. As they attempted to escape into the streets, Papa used the
Force to close the door in front of them. However, Moore then took out another remote and used it to freeze Papa in his
own armor, allowing her and her court to open fire on the Varki Lord. But this did not last as Papa overcame the
Umbaran's control and struck down her entire court. Moore tried once more to take control of Papa, but Ochi revealed
that Papa had fixed that vulnerability in his armor. Papa then knocked the remote out of Moore's hand and told her
that she could not bend his will.

Moore responded that she only wanted to see if Papa was still plagued by fear, to which Papa said that the only fear
in that place was hers. Moore conceded that he could kill her effortlessly, but also pointed out that doing so would do
nothing to save him from Drian Planetrunner. When Papa asked the Umbaran what she knew of Planetrunner, she stated that the
key to finding him, his friend Han Kole was currently being sold by Crimson Dawn. She also pointed out that if she
secured Kole for Papa, then the Emperor would not learn of his plans. When Ochi asked Moore why Papa should trust her,
the Umbaran answered that she would be delighted to reunite Papa with the only person who could kill him, to which
Papa agreed.

#### Auction for Han Kole

Shortly after, Ochi and Sly Moore left with a few Imperial officers to attend the Auction for Han Kole. However, this
was merely a ruse to humiliate the Umbaran in the Emperor's eyes. Amidst the bidding, Papa himself arrived at the
auction on Jekara along with a pair of death troopers. After cutting down a few Crimson Dawn guards, Papa infiltrated
the Vermillion just as Crimson Dawn's leader, Lady Qi'ra sold Kole to Jabba the Hutt. Papa then declared that Kole
belonged to him. Papa's presence sent Doctor Aphra, who had infiltrated the auction on behalf of the Tagge Corporation
with the smuggler Sana Starros, falling to the ground in a brief panic attack, but she managed to escape the room with
Starros before the preoccupied Varki Lord could spot her. After his attention was briefly diverted to the sounds of
Aphra's panicked fall, he turned his attention back to his mission at hand.

As Papa ordered the death troopers to transport Kole to his flagship, Jabba pointed out that he had already laid claim
to the smuggler. Moore attempted to explain the situation, but Papa chastised her for her failure and warned her that
the Emperor would hear of it. The Varki Lord then told Jabba that he and everyone else within the Empire belonged to the
Emperor, to which Jabba feigned amusement. Papa went on to point out that the Empire could easily replace the Hutts,
while also pointing out the fear he could sense in Jabba and the rest of the attending Hutts. When Bokku angrily
interrupted, Papa asked Jabba who he was, to which Jabba said that he was no one. Jabba then finally conceded and
allowed Kole to be taken with his compliments and regards to the Emperor. As Papa approached Kole, Lady Qi'ra informed
him that she would not get in his way, but also still required the one million credits she was promised. When Papa told
her she was owed nothing, Qi'ra inquired if the Empire was too poor or cheap to pay its debts. Out of patience, Papa
drew out his photonaxe, to which Qi'ra bared her own pair of blades.

As they dueled, Papa recognized that she was no threat to him, yet nonetheless found her level of skill, which included
knowledge of the Teräs Käsi fighting form, notable, and recognized Qi'ra's fighting style as that of his master's. When
Papa asked her who had trained her, Qi'ra only replied that she had been trained by someone who knew quite a bit about
both Papa and his master; in truth, she had been trained by Tal as part of his revenge plot against the Varki. Papa
then pointed out that she did not have the Force and warned that her skill would not save her. After a brief struggle,
Papa pushed Qi'ra back with the Force, knocking her into Kole. Stating she would pay the price for her foolishness, he
raised his photonaxe and prepared to strike her down. But he was suddenly distracted the arrival of Drian Planetrunner,
whose presence he sensed through the Force.

While Qi'ra retreated, Papa was informed by General Romodi that Piett had established a secure channel to Planetrunner's
spacebattler. Accessing the channel, Papa told Planetrunner he had Kole in his possession. He then warned his son that if
he did not come to him, then he would cut his friend in half. Planetrunner refused however, telling Papa to come to him.
Papa conceded to this, ordering Romodi to bring Kole aboard his Space Eater and to prepare his fighter.

#### Chase above Jekara

After boarding his REU Advanced, Papa took off in pursuit of his son. During the chase, Planetrunner used his X-fighter to
kick up a wave of water, which instantly froze and collided with Papa's fighter. Though Papa crashed, he was able to
lift his ship out of the water with the Force and resume his pursuit. After freeing his X-fighter from a group of pirates,
Papa fired at Planetrunner, damaging one of his ship's stabilizers and causing him to crash back down onto the planet
below. As Papa closed in on Planetrunner, he was contacted by Sly Moore. When Papa stated that he did not require her
assistance, Moore informed him that she was not helping him. Papa was then attacked by the Droid Crush Pirates, who
landed on his ship and began to tear it apart.

After causing some damage to the Varki's fighter, the pirates fell onto Planetrunner's X-fighter and quickly repaired it for
him, allowing him to take off from the planet. As Papa continued his chase while fending off the pirates, he was
informed by Ochi that the Hutts were going after the Imperial shuttle transporting Kole. Papa was then contacted by
Admiral Piett, who informed him of the Hutts' attack on the Executor. However, Papa chastised Piett for disturbing
him, claiming that the activities of the Hutts were irrelevant to him. He then warned Piett that if Kole was not aboard
his flagship by the time he returned, he would require an explanation in person. Later in the fight, Piett contacted
Papa again and told him that he had appraised the Emperor of the situation. Since the Emperor considered the Empire's
arrangement with the Hutts to be valuable, he wished for it to be preserved by having Papa eliminate the Grand Hutt
Council. Papa conceded to the Emperor's wishes and abandoned his pursuit of Planetrunner, reminding his son that he was no
Median, though the boy then claimed that the next time they met, he would be.

Papa then boarded the Hutt Council's ship and summarily slaughtered them all, including Bokku. Before his death, Bokku
revealed his allegiance to Crimson Dawn and had Gak-Sixtoo blow up their own ship in an attempt to kill Papa, which the
Varki survived by using the force to rip apart the ship and use the metal pieces to form a large protective cocoon in
which he was protected from the blast and then fell back down to Jekara. With the Hutt Council eliminated, the Hutts
ceased their attack on the Executor while Fett reclaimed Kole from the Empire and delivered him to Jabba on Oradin.
Shortly after, Papa was informed by Lieutenant Jyala Haydenn that Beilert Valance had infiltrated the Executor. He
then found Valance trying to escape on a ship and used the Force to pull him from space, rendering him unconscious and
taking him prisoner.

## Killing the Dawn

### Hunting the new menace

With the Hutts dealt with, Papa returned to the Executor to confront Sly Moore, who had been captured by Ochi during
the battle for trying to help in Planetrunner's escape. When Moore revealed that the Emperor had wanted Planetrunner alive,
Papa revealed that the boy had fled from him, declaring that he was not who the Emperor believed he could be. When
Moore pointed out that Planetrunner was still free and could still fight, the Varki Lord choked her and stated that his hope
would not be enough. Papa was then contacted by Evilth Schemious, prompting him to release the Umbaran and kneel before
him. After restating his loyalty to his master, Papa was instructed by Schemious to hunt down and eliminate Crimson
Dawn's agents within the Empire. Shortly after, Papa was met on the Executor by Romodi, who presented him with all of
the troops he would need to destroy Crimson Dawn. Papa then instructed Ochi to meet with the Assassin's Guild and
inform them that they would be serving him now.

In secret, Ochi swore himself to Qi'ra's service after he arrived at the Assassin's Guild base, although the assassin
would later claim he was acting as an Imperial double agent. Following Ochi's departure, Papa had Valance repaired and
waited for him to awaken. Once he did, he was shocked to find himself restored to his former appearance. When Valance
asked Papa what he had done to him, Papa explained that he had had Valance fixed since he would now be serving him.
Valance then realized that his heart was gone, to which the Varki informed him that it had been removed and replaced with
cybernetics, along with further upgrades to his body. Valance attacked Papa, but Papa cut him in half before leaving
him and telling a medical droid to put him back together. Once Valance was repaired, Papa, alongside Haydenn, informed
him that he would be assassinating Crimson Dawn's agents within the Empire. For if he did not, the Empire would kill
those he cared about.

While he meditated aboard the Executor, Papa was informed by Haydenn that Valance had completed his first assignment
in killing the alleged Crimson Dawn mole Tarl Sokoli. Papa then revealed that there was no connection between Sokoli
and Crimson Dawn. Sokoli had been publicly dissatisfied with the Empire and Papa had decided that killing someone from
Valance's childhood would be a good test for the bounty hunter. The Varki then told Haydenn to alert Ochi that Valance
was ready to join them. Papa also came to realize that Ochi had joined with Crimson Dawn but, deciding he could use it
to his advantage in the hunt for the syndicate, kept his deduction a secret.

### Confronting the Knights of Ren

Papa learned that Zahra's campaign against the Rebellion ended in failure during the Battle of Panisia. Sometime after
that engagement, Papa investigated the assassination of the Emperor's Royal Guard on Tyraleus, which was secretly
carried out in part by Ochi. During the investigation however, he was informed by Vanee that a band of thieves had
infiltrated Fortress Papa. The Dark Lord quickly returned to Dravion Prime and confronted the intruders in his castle; a
group of dark side marauders known as the Knights of Ren, who were secretly working with Crimson Dawn. After Papa
killed one of them, Fyodor with a Force choke, their leader fought him with a photonaxe while the rest of them
retreated. The leader said he had taken the blade from his predecessor, from whom he also inherited his name; Ren.

Papa expressed pity for how far the Knights of Ren had fallen before Ren leapt from a window with a device known as the
Screaming Key. As Ren gloated below, Papa used the Force to pull the key back up toward his hand, prompting the knights
to open fire on him. Ren then pulled the key back down into his own hand before escaping with the knights on speeders.
As the knights sped away, Papa stepped outside to study the remains of his slaughtered troops.

### Rooting out the Dawn

While thinking in his mediation chamber, Papa reflected on his promise to his son on Cloud City that they would bring
order to the galaxy. Papa concluded that his master had only brought about chaos and decided to set out on a new quest
to establish order, whether or not he had his son by his side. Resolving to destroy Crimson Dawn as the first step,
Papa left with Ochi to assist the Empire in hunting down Dawn agents on various planets, including Vincorba and Calior.
While on Vincorba, they fought alongside a group of mercenaries known as the Revengers. With Papa's crew established,
Ochi commented that they would serve well as expendable assets, to which Papa reminded him that he was expendable as
well. After finishing on Calior, Papa, Ochi, and the Revengers rendezvoused with Valance and a few other assassins on
Laecor to continue their hunt. When Valance asked Papa why he was there instead of leading Dark Squadron, the Varki Lord
simply told him to do as he was told. As a squad of stormtroopers attempted to move a group of civilians, the civilians
refused to comply, prompting the stormtroopers to fire on them. However, Papa then jumped in to deflect their blaster
bolts and slaughter them. When Ochi showed confusion over his master's actions, Papa revealed that the stormtroopers
served Crimson Dawn. As the group carried on, Papa came upon a statue, which the locals said was of their village
guardian who was killed fighting Crimson Dawn.

Upon locating more of the Dawn's agents, Ochi opted to use the Revengers as bait to lure them out of their stronghold.
Papa then used the Force to grab Ochi and throw him toward the Revengers, using him as bait as well. As the agents
surrounded them, Ochi requested that Papa bomb the stronghold. But Papa refused and instead mounted Gee-Ninety,
balancing himself atop the droid as they rolled themselves to the stronghold's front entrance. Papa then stormed the
stronghold along with Ochi, who the Varki stopped from killing all of the agents inside. When Ochi expressed more
confusion, Papa explained that Crimson Dawn was just a symptom and that he would destroy the disease. He then
discovered a layout of every Dawn agent within the Empire, which Ochi and Valance noted went all the way to the top.
Following this, Papa and his followers returned to Tyraleus. Valance, the assassins, and the Revengers left for the
Zanchal Estate while Papa and Ochi left for the Imperial Palace.

Upon entering the Palace, they struck down all of the Royal Guards and aides in the Emperor's throne room, except for
Sly Moore. Unfazed by this, Schemious pointed out Papa should have kept one of them alive for questioning. When Papa
asked him if they were loyal, Schemious said they were loyal to strength, which Papa showed them. However, only one of
them was Crimson Dawn, meaning that Papa's list was flawed. When Schemious questioned if his apprentice already knew
that, Papa hesitated before assuring his master that he would bring him order. Papa and Ochi then left for the Zanchal
Estate to confront Baron Espis Zanchal for his loyalty to the Dawn. Upon arriving, Papa was thanked by a pair of
hostages who the Revengers had rescued from the Baron. As he returned to his shuttle, Papa informed Ochi that the list
was a plant, which Papa himself had deduced when Ochi could only confirm that half of the names on it were Crimson
Dawn. Papa told Ochi to find out what connected every other person on the list. That way, they would find out who
planted it and why.

### Hidden enemy

Later on the Executor, Papa was informed by Ochi that Romodi and his soldiers were not Crimson Dawn after all.
However, Ochi warned him that Romodi did not understand the Varki and would come for Papa someday. Stepping out of his
chamber, Papa asked Ochi what connected the false names on the list. Ochi revealed that they had all undertaken a
mission for Romodi to execute the Liorans on Nivellon. Following this development, Papa and his team of assassins
traveled to Tranchar to capture and interrogate Lieutenant Grapa about the mission. After fighting their way through
stormtroopers and DT-series sentry droids, the assassins discovered civilians being tortured by the Imperials.
Gee-Ninety broke from the mission to free the civilians, prompting Papa to destroy the droid as punishment. Papa went
on to interrogate Grapa about her mission to kill the Liorans.

As she claimed to Papa that they were all dead, Tanka blasted her in the head for revenge. Papa then realized that the
Imperials had known they were coming. When Papa asked Valance who had sent the droids, Valance confirmed they were from
Romodi's command. Papa then remembered that Ochi had spoken with Romodi prior to their departure. When he confronted
Ochi with that fact, Ochi tried to stammer out an explanation before giving up and running away while Valance fired at
him. After stealing a spare ship, Ochi escaped from Tranchar and eventually arrived on Nivellon to meet with Sabe. Papa
followed the assassin in his REU Advanced. As soon as Ochi stepped out of his ship, Papa revealed himself and destroyed
it with his REU. After landing in front of Ochi, Papa revealed he had known of his allegiance to the Dawn and gave the
assassin an out by commending him for leading him to Sabe, which Ochi went along with and claimed was his plan all
along. As Papa confronted Sabe, he took her Crimson Dawn badge from her and claimed that he was the Dawn.

### Recruiting Sabe

Following this, Papa took Ochi, Sabe, and ZED-6-7 to the carcass of the sando aqua monster he had slain. He then threw
Ochi and Sabe out of the shuttle and watched as they were attacked by a pack of ravenous creatures. Ochi attempted to
assure Papa of his loyalty, but Papa silenced him and asked Sabe why she believed in Crimson Dawn. As she defended
herself, she said that she had merely infiltrated the syndicate. Ochi fought alongside her and claimed he had done the
same for the Empire. When Papa asked Sabe if she also intended to serve the Empire, Sabe said she did not as long as
the Empire served chaos. Sabe went on to claim that she and Papa wanted the same thing: order.

To this, Papa levitated the creatures with the Force and told Sabe that if she killed one monster, a thousand more
would replace it. He then explained that one would have to either make the monsters agree or deal with them all. With
that, Papa threw the creatures at a group of long-necked beasts as they sprouted from the ground. Understanding Papa's
plan, Sabe brought him to a Crimson Dawn outpost while Ochi returned to the Executor to speak with Romodi. Upon
arriving at the outpost, Sabe informed the Dawners there that they served Papa now. To this, the Dawners attacked Papa
and were easily cut down by the Varki Lord. Papa then had Ochi use Valance and the assassins as bait to draw the
remaining Dawners and Romodi's forces to Oro Sankeria. As the Dawners and Imperials fought one another, they were
suddenly wiped out by a pulse bomb, thus eliminating many of Papa's enemies. Papa informed Sabe that Crimson Dawn and
Romodi feared him now. When he asked Sabe if she was scared, Sabe asked him why she should be scared of his true self,
Corin Planetrunner.

Papa responded that Corin Planetrunner was dead. But Sabe revealed that she had deduced Papa's identity from his
obsession with order, his investigation into Dan's death, and Dan's final words at Polis Massa. When Papa drew his
photonaxe and asked Sabe what she wanted, she claimed she wanted to help him achieve order. She went on to explain that
when Planetrunner never returned to Oradin to free his mother, she and Tonra secretly worked in her honor to free
enslaved people and smuggle them from Oradin to a colony on Gabredor III. Now, the colony was being exploited and
neglected by the corrupt Governor Tauntaza, who was in league with Crimson Dawn. Sabe told Papa that if he helped her
save the refugees, he would get the chance to destroy another Crimson Dawn cell and prove that Dan was right about
him. To this, Papa withdrew his photonaxe and accepted Sabe's proposal. He then warned her that she alone was
responsible for where her path took her before they silently boarded the shuttle and left for Gabredor III.

### Familiar faces

As they approached the planet, they were met by Tauntaza's flagship. When Papa asked ZED-6-7 if the ship's crew had
detected them, the droid said they had not yet. Papa then told him to take them to the planet's surface. Sabe suggested
summoning the Executor, but Papa said they would first visit the colony to see if she was telling the truth. Once
they landed at the colony, they stepped out of the ship as ZED-6-7 introduced Papa to the refugees and asked to see
their protocol droid. Since their protocol droid had long broken down, ZED-6-7 instead spoke with their astromech droid
Em-Sevenbee. The droid and two of the refugees then confirmed Sabe's story. The pair of refugees then showed off a
terrestrial vehicle they had built, inspired by their earlier lives on Oradin. When Papa asked the refugees for their
names, they introduced themselves as Kitster and Wald; Planetrunner's childhood friends.

When Kitster asked Papa if they could do anything for him, Papa told them they could do nothing. He then sensed that
the surrounding land was disturbed, to which ZED-6-7 explained that it was currently suffering from drought. When
another refugee claimed things would get better once the clouds came back, Papa said they would only get worse as they
were attacked by a pack of clawed beasts. While Papa and Sabe fought off the creatures, a few of them surrounded
Kitster and Wald. Papa then leapt in and cut them down, saving the refugees. Kitster thanked Papa as the Varki Lord
silently walked away. Sabe then asked Papa if he had seen enough and told him it was time to take out Tauntaza.
However, Papa told Sabe she was not ready, since the refugees had ignored her order to stay back and put themselves in
danger. He then told her that if she wanted them to live, they would have to obey her. Afterwards, Papa had Sabe don a
set of Imperial equipment and recruited her into the Imperial Military under the rank of Lieutenant Commander, granting
her authority over all the forces he gathered.

He then ordered an Imperial officer to open a channel to the Executor. When the officer reported that Tauntaza's ship
was blocking their communications, Papa ordered for his shuttle to be prepared. He and his team then traveled to the
governor's facility and proceeded to fight their way towards the governor. After cutting down a few repurposed battle
droids, Papa was confronted by Tauntaza, who briefly subdued the Varki Lord with a life-draining weapon. Papa's team
was then attacked by more battle droids and a few Crimson Dawn assassins. Once Papa recovered, he Force-choked Ochi for
allowing the governor to escape. Ochi explained that he was assisting Papa, to which Papa asked Ochi if he thought
Tauntaza's weapon could destroy him. Sabe then told Papa that it might have, prompting Papa to release Ochi and meet
with one of the weapon's designers, Doctor Aira. Aira explained that the technology had been used to raze the planet
Karolia and expressed remorse over not having known what the technology would be used for. As Sabe reassured the rest of
the regretful designers, Papa seized Ochi's speeder and left to find the governor.

Catching up to Tauntaza and her escorts, Papa blocked a blast from one of her battle droids before reaching her at her
escape ship. As the ship took off, Papa used the Force to hold it and destroy its interior controls. However, the
ship's powerful engines ultimately allowed the governor to make her escape. Using a pair of Imperials as a diversion,
Papa boarded Tauntaza's flagship and fought off more battle droids and Imperials before confronting the one in charge.
When Papa asked where Tauntaza was, the Imperial claimed there had been a misunderstanding and recommended that the
Varki reconsider his "hostile stance". Papa then had the ship's crew open a channel to his own ship and ordered Piett to
lock onto the governor's flagship. After giving Piett the order to destroy the ship unless countermanded, Papa asked
the Imperial again for the governor's location. Upon learning the location, Papa returned to his shuttle and flew
toward the facility where she was hiding, only to be met by a sandstorm generated by the facility.

Despite the pilots' warnings, Papa told them to continue approaching the facility while he held the ship together with
the Force. A lightning bolt then struck the ship, causing it to crash into the forest. Once Papa stepped out of the
wreckage, he was met by Ochi, who he asked for Sabe's location. Ochi reported that the storm had taken her and a
colonist claimed that the storm would kill them all. When Papa asked the colonist if they had any ships, he said the
only ship that had not been confiscated or destroyed was Kitster's racer. When the colonist said that only Kitster could
drive it, Papa said they would see as he approached the racer. ZED-6-7 told Papa that he could not trace Sabe or the
other colonists, to which Papa told the droid he would command his assistance if he required it. Faced with numerous
flashbacks to his past, Papa then boarded the racer and sped off into the storm. While deflecting debris with his
photonaxe, Papa located Kitster on the ground alongside a large tank. Landing next to him, Papa asked Kitster where
Sabe was. Kitster explained that she was trapped beneath the tank and that he had been trying to move it. Once Papa
lifted the tank off of Sabe, the three of them were overwhelmed by the surrounding storm. Papa then contacted Piett and
ordered him to have the Executor fire on his location.

When Piett warned that would incinerate everyone and everything within range, Papa choked him with the Force, prompting
him to open fire. The resulting bombardment destroyed the tank and dissipated the storm. After cutting himself out from
the remains of the tank, Papa took Sabe from Kitster and carried her into the distance. Eventually, the three of them
returned to the colonists and Papa ordered Piett to open fire on Tauntaza's facility. However, the blasts were
deflected by a shield, which ZED-6-7 explained was drawing energy from the planet. Despite Ochi's doubts, Papa remained
certain the fortress possessed a weakness and, when ZED-6-7 revealed that the facility's underside was unshielded, took
Em-Sevenbee with him to the facility. While he defeated more monsters on his way there, Papa placed his photonaxe
within the astromech's dome. Once they arrived at the facility, he had the droid fire the photonaxe upwards into the
unshielded underbelly. Papa then used the Force to guide the photonaxe through the facility, disabling the weapon and
carving an entrance for himself. With the shield down, Papa entered the facility and struck down Tauntaza's soldiers.

However, he was then met by Tauntaza herself, wearing a suit of powerful armor. Tauntaza used the suit's arm cannon to
fire at Papa. As he blocked the beam with his photonaxe, Papa told the governor she could not contain the power she
was wielding. To this, Tauntaza accused Papa of having no control over his own power before he destroyed her arm
cannon. Tauntaza then flew away as the facility exploded, leaving Papa severely injured without any power left in his
suit. Sabe soon found Papa and begrudgingly restored his suit's power, allowing them to walk back to the colony. Once
they returned, they learned from ZED-6-7 that Tauntaza had been receiving her orders from the Emperor himself. When
Papa asked Sabe why she was smiling, she said she now knew why she had saved him. Returning to his fortress, Papa
healed in his bacta tank, but broke it in anger upon remembering Sabe's words about the good still in him.
