Later, Papa boarded the Executor and was met by Valance, Haydenn, and the Revengers. Papa chastised them for being
early, to which Valance demanded to know why they were there. Papa then used the Force to fix Valance's collar, saying
he expected those who served him to be held to a certain standard. Haydenn claimed that Valance had the team operating
at peak efficiency. To this, Papa said they would get a chance to prove their loyalty and advised Valance to channel
his energies in a less self-destructive manner. When Valance asked what their mission was, Piett explained that they had
been selected to protect a medicine shipment to Bestine IV from Crimson Dawn. Papa warned the mercenaries not to
disappoint him as he would be watching before they left for their mission. Papa then met with Sabe and asked her about
Tauntaza's location. When she said Ochi was searching for the governor, Papa asked her what she advised they do. To
this, Sabe told Papa he should do what he always did: directly confront the problem.

### Return to Skako Minor

Following Sabe's counsel, Papa and Sabe arrived at the Imperial Palace on Tyraleus aboard a Lambda-class shuttle to
confront Schemious. As the two were unexpected, one of Drav's advisors tried to stop the Dark Lord, but Papa only
reacted by throwing the advisor against a wall before making his way into the Emperor's throne room. Although his two
present Royal Guards pointed their Force pikes at Papa, Schemious reacted by calmly asking Papa what his heart told him.
Papa proceeded to hold Sabe in the air with the Force as Schemious laughed and claimed to her that she had only reminded
Papa, who was remembering moments of his past at the same time, of his weakness. Dropping her, Papa refused to assist
Sabe as the Emperor had his Royal Guards attempt to destroy her. Once she outwitted them in combat, Schemious killed the
guards in anger and, seeing her worth as an agent, allowed Sabe to continue working with Papa.

As they returned to their shuttle, Papa and Sabe were informed by ZED-6-7 of their next mission. Jul Tambor, the
grandson of Wat Tambor, was working to overthrow the pro-Imperial regime on Skako Minor through a nationalist uprising.
According to Imperial intelligence, Tambor had also enlisted pirates to blockade the planet and stockpile technology to
be used against the Empire. As such, their mission was to end the Skakoan's uprising and restore Imperial control over
Skako Minor. In truth, Tambor had known he would have to face Papa as part of his crusade. Over the course of the last
six years, the Skakoan had worked to collect and reassemble droids who had been killed by Papa, thereby allowing him to
analyze their databanks to study Papa's moves. Amongst the droids he reassembled were B1 battle droids, B2 super battle
droids, and Gee-Ninety. Tambor was very confident that he would be able to kill Papa.

Upon reaching the planet, Papa and Sabe discovered a crashed commercial transport from Corellia. ZED-6-7 explained that
the ship had been boarded and those inside were killed by the planet's poisonous atmosphere. As they traversed the
terrain, Papa killed a pack of cliff worms, saving a group of pirates. When he noticed a pile of corpses on the ground,
he struck down the pirates, while Sabe hesitated and allowed one of them to escape. When Papa asked her if the pirates
deserved mercy, Sabe admitted she didn't know who did anymore. Papa reminded her that she was his shadow now and she
said they would need one of the pirates alive in order to locate Tambor. To this, Papa instructed Sabe to follow the
surviving pirate and find Tambor while he took care of the rest.

### Confronting Valance

Upon learning that Valance had betrayed the Empire, Papa boarded the Righteous Fist and had Haydenn accompany him as
he approached the surface of Bestine IV in his shuttle. Once they landed, Papa and Haydenn confronted Valance and the
rest of the Edgehawk{{'s}} crew. Drawing his photonaxe, Papa told Valance that his desertion would not be tolerated.
Charging into battle, Valance told Papa that he regretted ever serving the Empire. As they fought, Papa took note of
Valance's power, which he regarded as proof Valance was a waste of potential. Once he was beaten into submission,
Valance said that the planet's people would still be free of the Empire. However, Papa revealed that Valance had doomed
them as his forces bombed the locals, as well as his troops.

Ignoring Valance's chastisation of his lack of care for his own, Papa prepared to strike Valance down, but Haydenn
insisted on finishing the job herself to make up for her previous failures, which Papa allowed. Valance tried to
convince Haydenn to leave the Empire with him, but Haydenn blasted him in the face and sent him falling over the edge of
the cliff. Before leaving the planet, Papa contacted Haydenn and ordered her to send in a group of Imperials to hunt
Valance down in case he survived. To accomplish this task, Papa personally selected Inferno Squad.

### Unmasking the Dawn

As Sabe searched for Jul Tambor, Papa was called to the Imperial Palace by Schemious. Upon meeting with his master, Papa
was informed by Schemious that the Varki had an enemy, claiming that the recent attacks were part of a coordinated campaign
of diversion. Schemious then called in ISB Director Sliro Barsha to report on his current investigation. Barsha reported
that his division within the ISB-the undercover criminal syndicate Zerek Besh-had learned of a rumor that the major
crime syndicates were vying to obtain the Hutts' long-standing arrangement with the Empire. However, the rumor was
coming from a single source: Crimson Dawn. As they walked through the Palace halls, Papa agreed that Crimson Dawn had
orchestrated the Syndicate War but pondered how deep its influence went.

Schemious went on to state that they had orchestrated the other attacks as well, saying that Crimson Dawn had targeted the
Varki. He then asked Papa about the syndicate's leader, Qi'ra, who Papa fought and failed to acquire Kole from. Papa
told Schemious that while Qi'ra had not been a true threat to him, she was trained in Teräs Käsi and possessed a fighting
style which reminded Papa of his master's. From this, Schemious and Papa deduced that, since Qi'ra wallowed in the
criminal underworld, she must have been trained by Tal. Schemious then concluded that Tal must have trained Qi'ra to use
her as an instrument of revenge and went on to ponder what else he had taught her. With the Varki aware of Crimson Dawn's
role in recent events, an alert was sent out the rest of the Imperial Military to track down the Vermillion, which
made Qi'ra order her assets in the Empire and other major factions to sow chaos across the galaxy to further distract
the Varki. With the Screaming Key they had stolen from Papa, the Knights of Ren, meanwhile, traveled to a location known
as the dark side hellscape, a location unknown to Papa and Schemious, alongside "the Archivist" on orders from Qi'ra to
retrieve an artifact known as the Fermata Cage.

### Dealing with Zerek Besh

After Director Barsha and Zerek Besh failed to bring in a single member of the Rebel Alliance, Papa confronted him on
the ISB space station Derosha Six. There Barsha tried to appeal to Papa by announcing the successes of Zerek Besh, but
Papa countered that, because of the criminal syndicate's inability to bring in any rebels, Zerek Besh and Barsha by
extension were failures. Barsha continued to boast about the size of the network the ISB had created under Zerek Besh,
and insulted Papa about his and the Imperial army's failures on Maroth. In his anger, Papa destroyed a glass display
behind him using the force, and surrounded Barsha in the shards. Forced to ground, Barsha pleaded with Papa, saying
that he was close. Papa simply replied that he needed to find rebels then.

Shortly after his departure, thiefs Kay and Riko Vess were able to steal access codes to Director Barsha's palace vault
on Canto Bight. From there, Kay Vess' crew working under Barsha's brother Jaylen Vrax were able to steal a secret codex
Barsha had that detailed sensitive information about almost all ranking Imperial officers. Vrax contacted Papa and
informed him of the database and his intentions to take control of Zerek Besh. They made a deal, in exchange for the
codex and the coordinates to a Rebel base on Akiva, Vrax would be given Zerek Besh. Later, Papa ordered Barsha onto the
bridge of the Revelator, where he condemned Barsha for letting such critical Imperial intelligence go. Papa then
looked to Vrax and said the Empire had accepted his terms. He ended the call and gave up Barsha to the mercy of Vrax and
his associates.

### Finding the Fermata Cage

Papa was amongst Drav's tools in the crusade to root out Dawn agents across the Empire. During his effort to
destroy the Dawn, Papa bisected a traitorous stormtrooper in an industrial environment. At one point, Papa
nevertheless returned to his castle on Dravion Prime, where he was called by the Eye of Webbish Bog. Upon entering the Eye's
cave, the Eye showed Papa a moment from the Clone Wars, where he, Macio, and their clones had fought B1 battle droids,
and glimpses of the future, including one of him being confronted by Liora's surviving handmaidens. Papa then
realized that he had been lured there as a test before being attacked by Dravion Primeians. After killing them, Papa claimed
that the Eye had wasted his time with puzzles. To this, the Eye explained that the visions were warnings for the end of
everything. When Papa asked why he should care, the Eye reminded Papa that he was a part of everything, but, if he
refused to accept this, he could not be helped. Just as the Eye had shown him, Papa, with his helmet slightly damaged,
returned to his fortress and, after sensing a great disturbance in the dark side, was contacted by Schemious to discuss
the disturbance.

Informed by Schemious that Qi'ra claimed to possess the Fermata Cage, Papa was ordered to find the artifact and kill
anyone who knew of it. Schemious also told Papa about Qi'ra's central claim about the artifact: it contained an ancient
Varki Lord who was so powerful they had needed to be locked away. In truth, no such Varki Lord existed; Qi'ra simply
needed a claim that would draw both Varki to the Cage, allowing her to lock them both into it and free the galaxy from
their rule. Her initial effort to open the cage, however, had resulted in the Knights of Ren abandoning Crimson Dawn out
anger at being hurt in the attempt and out of fear of the ripple it sent out. Papa made his way to the site of the
disturbance, where he only found wreckage from the experiment. Although he was certain it was the origin of the
disturbance, he deduced, due to a lack of bodies, that no Varki Lord had been released. Papa then returned to the
Executor and reported his findings to Schemious via its holoprojection chamber.

Papa asked Schemious if there truly was an ancient Varki within the Cage, which Schemious explained was possible: built by
Evilth Momin himself, the Cage could imprison people and places outside of time and had never been used lightly. Schemious
further warned Papa that, because of the urge within every Varki to dominate others, the mere possibility was the
greatest danger to everything they had built together. Amid their conversation, the two suddenly felt the Cage begin to
open once more as the Archivist and her assistant, archaeologist Kho Phon Farrus, tried to use Ascendant-designed
technology to focus nearby dark side energy into it. Although Farrus shut off their technology as the Cage began to
leach life energy from each of them, the experiment had carried on for long enough that Schemious was able to track the
disturbance to the planet they were on. With this, Schemious sent Papa to retrieve the Cage and destroy those present.

### The Orphans

Once the Executor arrived at the planet, Papa, intending to handle the situation on his own, ordered Piett to prepare
his Lambda-class T-4a shuttle and landed at the seemingly-deserted site with two stormtroopers. In the vicinity of the
artifact, where he could not single out the presence of the supposed ancient Varki, Papa sensed a great deal of dark
side power from the Fermata Cage. Papa discovered the Archivist and Kho Phon Farrus trying to hide beneath the remains
of their machine. In Papa's presence, the Archivist found that the Varki Lord radiated a dark energy. While Farrus,
having been warned of Papa by their rival Doctor Aphra, quickly surrendered, the Archivist refused, to which Papa
began to choke the agents with the Force. However, he was interrupted by the arrival of Chanath Cha and her Orphans,
consisting of Sear, Ladybright, and Imara Vex. When Cha asked Papa if he remembered her, Papa simply stated that he
would kill her as he bared his photonaxe.

Cha went on to introduce herself, explaining that Papa had slaughtered her family and that she had spent every day
since then plotting her revenge. Papa quickly forgot her name once more before the Orphans attacked. After being
electrocuted by Ladybright and burned by one of Cha's acid bombs, Papa pushed the Orphans back and walked into the
ocean to recover. Once he did, he returned to the shore and saw Ladybright, Vex, Pharrus and the Archivist fleeing for
the Siroto. When Papa mentioned Qi'ra's death to Cha and Sear, he sensed their confusion and lack of fear, indicating
that Qi'ra was still alive. As he fought Cha and Sear, he chastised them for their arrogance and prepared to strike Cha
down, only for Vex to snipe off one of his hands, prompting him to tip over the Siroto with the Force and throw Vex
into the forest. With Vex severely injured, Ladybright, Pharrus and the Archivist fled in the Siroto before returning
to assist Cha and Sear. However, the Siroto then turned back around and left the planet, much to Cha's relief. With
Sear and Vex defeated, Papa twisted Cha's introduction of herself by re-introducing himself and stabbed her through the
chest.

With Cha dead, Papa left the planet to find Qi'ra and reunited with his master. Both traveled a dark, smoky location,
where Schemious asked Papa if he actually felt the presence of an ancient Varki Lord in the Cage. With Papa admitting he
only felt intense dark side power from it, he engaged Schemious in a sparring duel, the first they had engaged in in some
time, at his master's request, allowing Schemious to explain how he would enforce the Rule of Two if another Varki Lord
indeed existed. After Schemious pushed back Papa with a final strike and declared the duel over, Papa made one last rush
at his master before stopping when his master repeated himself. Feeling they had no choice but to follow the ripple in
the Force caused by the next Cage opening, Schemious took the moment to admit Qi'ra would be missed as he and Papa looked
across the location.

Qi'ra attempted to sure up her chances by reaching out the Knights of Ren, reminding them that they had attacked Papa's
fortress and thus would be hunted by the Varki if they did not help her destroy Papa and Drav. Around the same
time, the Spark Eternal artificial intelligence, created thousands of years prior for use against the Varki by the
Ascendant cult, resolved to hunt down Papa. The AI had taken over Doctor Aphra's body to carry out its mission, further
collecting 0-0-0 and BT-1 to help in its quest. When Aphra used a virus she had installed into the two droids to regain
control of her body, the Spark introduced, much to Aphra's horror, their Varki hunting mission against Papa. By
possessing Aphra, it had access to her memories of Papa and saw how she considered the Varki Lord a monster, but the AI
believed itself ready to take on the Varki Lord and his master. Because Aphra had once outmaneuvered Papa, the
overconfident Spark thought itself skilled enough to engage him in one-on-one combat. In fact, Qi'ra contacted the Spark
to request its help in destroying the Varki.

### Destroying the Dawn

The Archivist moved the Fermata Cage and the equipment needed to finally open it to an ancient Amaxine Space Station in
the Outer Rim, where the Cage could feed off the plant life and dark side energy left behind by the ancient Drengir
beings. Sensing the disturbance in the Force caused by the opening of the Cage, Schemious and Papa, just as Schemious said
they would need to in the name of enforcing the Rule of Two, followed the disturbance aboard the Executor with a fleet
of Space Eaters at their back. The Varki Lords and their forces reached the station shortly into the opening process.
Overlooking the station from the Executor{{'s}} bridge, Papa found himself with overwhelming desire to board the
station and meet the possible Varki, hoping to test himself against that Varki Lord's power no matter if he survived the
encounter. Able to sense his apprentice's wish, Schemious felt the same but declared it a foolish desire and ordered the
Executor to destroy the station.

Before the Executor could fire, the warship's crew detected an entire enemy fleet emerging from hyperspace. While
Papa initially assumed it was the Rebel Alliance, the force was Qi'ra's secret Dawn Fleet, which targeted the
Executor{{'s}} long-range weapons, thereby forcing the Executor to divert power to its shield batteries and delay
the Emperor's order to destroy the station. With his master unwilling to take any chances, Papa boarded a Lambda
-class T-4a shuttle with Schemious and an escort of death troopers and Emperor's Royal Guards, flying through the space
battle under the escort of crimson REU interceptors. As their troops engaged with Dawn soldiers who had set up a
parameter in the hangar, Schemious and Papa disembarked from their shuttle into the station, which was filled with dark
side energy that Schemious could tell was not all related to the Fermata Cage. Unsure of what they would find, the two
Varki Lords led the charge with the mission to totally destroy the Dawn.

Leading from the front, Papa and Schemious fought their way through the station. As the two Varki could deflect blaster
bolts with their photonaxes, Dawn Squads Two and Three attempted to engage Schemious and Papa with electrified melee
weapons, but both Varki effortlessly fought through the guards. Still, Papa toyed with one soldier until Schemious ordered
him to stop and simply kill them. As they journeyed closer to the Cage, they were confronted by the Spark
Eternal-possessed Aphra, who mocked the two Varki. Papa quickly deduced Aphra was under some kind of possession and
stayed behind to deal with her while Schemious carried on. Believing she could weaken him, the overconfident Spark engaged
Papa with the cortosis alloy-based Null Blade, which would temporarily shut down photonaxes. To the Spark, the battle
represented a chance to finally fulfill the dream of its long-dead creator, Miril, by destroying the Varki Order, even if
the battle proved too much for Aphra's body.

The blades of Papa and the possessed Aphra clashed several times, thereby shorting out the Varki Lord's photonaxe.
While the Spark at that moment thought it was ready to destroy Papa and jumped at him, Papa effortlessly excised the
Spark from Aphra's body with a Force push as a group of new arrivals watched: Aphra's former lover Sana Starros had
gathered a crew of Aphra's friends and loved ones to rescue her from the Spark. Having abandoned the Dawn in fear after
their run in with Papa, Farrus was also among the group. Unknown to Papa, who declared the Spark to be a weak enemy,
he had effectively ended the dream of the Ascendant cult by defeating its main weapon without much effort. After a
terrified Aphra awoke under Papa and escaped as the opening Cage sent out a ripple, Papa elected to return to his
master's side rather than hunt down his former ally. With Papa out of sight, the Spark attempted to possess Aphra once
more, but the intervention of Farrus, Starros, and another one of Aphra's ex-lovers, Magna Tolvan, saved her.

Papa took his place at an eager Schemious's side as the Cage finally opened. However, only a small disc without any
connection to the Force fell out: inside, there had been no secret Varki Lord after all, and Schemious believed the disc
was nothing important. Unknown to both, the disc was actually a droid locked away by the ancient Varki. Watching from
afar aboard each of their starships, the Archivist and Qi'ra remotely re-activated the Cage, encasing Papa and Schemious
in a time-lock. Qi'ra intended to recover the Cage with the two Varki trapped inside and throw their prison into a star.
However, it was at that moment that cannon shots from beyond the space battle suddenly broke into the station and
destroyed the Cage: while it remained physically together, the Cage's time-lock collapsed, freeing the two Varki from its
grasp but sending a Force Wave out across the galaxy. The cannon shots had come from the Night Buzzard, personal
transport of the Knights of Ren: although Ren had watched Papa and Schemious fall victim to Qi'ra's plan from a distance,
he believed Schemious would ultimately find his way out of the Cage and thus believed the only way to save his crew was to
align themselves with the Varki.

The wave sent out by the collapse of the Cage wiped out much of the Dawn Fleet, giving the Imperials a chance to wipe
out the Dawn forces as the escaping Qi'ra gave a retreat order. As they collected the destroyed but intact Fermata Cage,
Schemious and Papa sensed a great rending in the Force sent out by its collapse, with Schemious admitting it made his grasp
on the Force tenuous. Schemious and Papa then came face-to-face with the Knights of Ren, who revealed themselves in
return for mercy. Schemious, however, responded with a blast of Force lightning to punish the Knights, promising that
whatever was left of the group would be put to excellent use. Still, Schemious declared the Knights' future a small matter
and ordered Papa to depart with him. In the aftermath of the Crimson Dawn war, the syndicate was shattered while the
defeated Qi'ra fled into hiding. The effects of the Force Wave varied at different times: Force-sensitives could find
themselves with a limited connection to the Force at one time but could wield great power when the Wave returned. Papa
came to fear the great energy provided by the Force Wave because he could not control it.

## Fighting the past and the Force

### Reunion with the Handmaidens

As the Force Wave vanished for the time being, Papa returned to the Executor and meditated, reflecting on Vorin's
words that only a Varki dealt in absolutes and declaring that no one in the galaxy should forget his allegiance.
Afterward, Papa had Piett contact the recently-returned Ochi, who had returned to the Executor with Sabe, to bring
Sabe into a room aboard the ship. Within, Papa had also summoned Sabe's recently assigned personal guards,
stormtroopers KA-336 and KV-222; both troopers had broken protocol by openly speaking about her classified assignment,
with Papa demanding the woman before him kill them both with a nearby E-11 blaster rifle as punishment. In truth, Papa
suspected that the woman was not Sabe, but another of Liora's surviving handmaidens, and was testing that theory.
Papa also created a struggle when he urged the troopers to also run for the blaster. "Sabe" grabbed it first and fired
at them, injuring both but leaving them alive. This confirmed Papa's suspicion that this was not Sabe and instead
another handmaiden, Dorme. Lifted into the air via a Force choke, Dorme claimed that Sabe wouldn't have killed them,
which Papa declared meant Dorme did not know Sabe at all.

Upon realizing that Ochi had helped her get inside as part of a scheme get rid of Sabe, whom Ochi saw as a rival, Papa
threw Ochi into a wall and told Dorme that Sabe served him willingly. Dorme denied Papa's claim, saying Sabe was the
best of them. To this, Papa brought her to a hangar and told her she should follow Sabe's lead by claiming the same
power. When Ochi advised against this, Papa tossed him aside, saying he simply needed her to serve his purpose. Dorme
stated once again that neither she nor Sabe would serve Papa. Papa then said they would see before he took her aboard
a Lambda-class T-4a shuttle and traveled to the planet Fedalle.

Shortly after, Dorme's fellow handmaidens Eirtae, Sache, and Rabe Tonsort arrived on the planet. When Dorme insisted
they go after Sabe instead, the handmaidens told her they wouldn't leave her as they engaged Papa in combat. Despite
their coordination, the handmaidens were subdued by Papa, who gave them one final chance to join him. However, Sache
revealed that Eirtae had seized codes from Papa's suit during the fight, allowing the handmaidens to complete Dorme's
sabotage of the Executor. Before they could destroy Papa's flagship, which would kill thousands in the name of
rescuing Sabe and defeating Papa, Papa declared they were just as bloodthirsty as he needed them to be to join him.
However, he was contacted by Piett, who showed him a transmission from Tambor. After arriving on the planet Brentaal IV,
Sabe had confronted Tambor while he was helping out a village of exiled Skakoans, urging him not to go up against Papa
and declaring that the Varki Lord had only grown more dangerous since her own failed efforts on Polis Massa. She was
certain that Tambor's efforts against Papa would fail and that the Varki Lord would slaughter the hundreds of Skakoans
on Brentaal IV in retaliation.

Unable to convince Tambor to call off his coming attack on the Skako Minor garrison, Sabe shot him above his heart,
keeping him alive but allowing her to take him away to a ship controlled by her and ZED-6-7. Aboard, Tambor listened to
her reasoning about the danger Papa posed and declared that it was time to kill the Varki Lord, capturing Sabe after his
rebuilt droids reached the starship. After showing Sabe video footage of Papa, Tambor sent his hologram to Papa, in
which he revealed her capture and baited him to come after him. While fully aware of the Varki Lord's ruthlessness and
not doubting Papa's willingness to slaughter his refugee camp in retaliation, the Skakoan had come to believe that Sabe
was Papa's weakness, which would finally give him an advantage over the Dark Lord. On Fedalle, realizing they would
need Papa and his forces to stage a daring rescue, the handmaidens reluctantly joined Papa to go after Tambor, much to
Ochi's annoyance. The group returned returned to the Executor aboard his Lambda shuttle and eventually left for
Brentaal IV.

### Corrupting Sabe

Upon reaching Brentaal IV via a Lambda-class shuttle with the handmaidens and ZED-6-7, Papa reflected on his last
meeting with Liora on Dravion Prime and how he wished it had gone, privately declaring to himself he would finally have his
idealized outcome. He also saw it as a way to have his idealized version of the duel on Bespin, privately comparing the
situation to him reaching out to Drian Planetrunner. Entering a building on-world, Papa and the handmaidens were met by
Moore, who explained with Papa how each of the handmaidens could benefit from serving the Empire and the Varki Lord.
When none of the four agreed to his demands, he telekinetically threw all four outside through an opening created by
Tambor's forces, who had tracked down the Varki Lord and his reluctant allies, and forced them to fight the B1 battle
droid horde alone. To Papa, the battle was a chance for the handmaidens to earn their places at his side and show them
their own power. Overlooking their victory, Papa remained silent as Moore declared it an example of their skills, which
she promised would only grow under Papa's service.

Shortly thereafter, Eirtae discovered from one of the B1's memory banks that Tambor's command ship, in which she learned
Sabe was being held, was three klicks to the south of their position. However, Tambor, ignoring Sabe's continued pleas
that Papa would wipe out his refugee camp if he continued, sent three platoons of B1s and a Low Altitude Assault
Transport/infantry to attack a civilian village, hoping it would trap his enemies into the village's canyon and let him
escape with Sabe. Both Papa and Moore understood the attack was a trap, with Papa declaring it an example of the
weakness that the handmaidens would need to overcome. When the handmaidens demanded that Papa assist them in aiding the
populace, Papa elected to use them as a distraction, effectively turning them into his pawns so he could get to and
corrupt Sabe, and teach them another lesson: as they fought the B1 horde, he could slip past the droids' lines, leaving
the handmaidens to seize their true potential against a major enemy. Riding into battle on speeder bikes, Papa cut down
the gunship but left the handmaidens to the droids, cutting into Tambor's ship to save Sabe and confront the
revolutionary.

Inside Tambor's ship, Papa took position in front of Sabe's cage but was met by the rebuilt Gee-Ninety, who fired upon
the Dark Lord before releasing magnetic spheres. Having deduced that Papa would attack with brute force, Tambor and the
droid had created the spheres specifically to immobilize him via electrocution. However, the handmaidens then arrived
and used Eirtae's own magnetic devices to force down the spheres, although Tambor and Gee-Ninety managed to flee by
detaching the room from the rest of the ship while Papa recovered. The Varki Lord maintained that he had not betrayed
the handmaidens, instead declaring that he had granted them a chance to claim their true power, before Force choking
Eirtae and Dorme against the wall. Both had just released Sabe from her cage and begged her to leave Papa's service,
but Papa offered her a chance at creating order instead of allowing the innocent-attacking Tambor to run free. As he
made the offer and the handmaidens begged Sabe to turn back, Papa remembered his lived and idealized versions of the
meeting with Liora on Dravion Prime and with his son on Bespin.

Sabe almost took Papa's hand, but was tackled and pulled out of the room by Dorme while Eirtae and Sache provided
covering fire against Papa. Papa drew his photonaxe and pursued the handmaidens outside, only for the group to take
Sabe into the air with Eirtae's antigravity devices to an overhead Star Commuter 2000 as Papa watched on. The ship was
in fact being piloted by Ochi, who had made a deal with the handmaidens that they would convince Sabe to abandon Papa
to make sure he would never see any of them again. However, Sabe believed her handmaiden sisters did not have the tools
needed to put a stop to Tambor's campaign, deciding the only way to save the civilians Tambor was on the cusp of
attacking was to join Papa's violent crusade. She also decided that, by staying with Papa, she could continue to bring
about Liora's declaration that good existed in Corin Planetrunner. Bidding her fellow handmaidens goodbye, Sabe detached
her antigrav device to fall back to Papa, who guided her to the ground with the Force. While a force of stormtroopers
had arrived via a Lambda-class T-4a shuttle and were firing upon the escaping Star Commuter, Papa called their
assault off, declaring that the incident was over before walking back to the shuttle with Sabe at his side.

The following day, returning to the Executor and receiving an update on Tambor's gunships, Papa made it clear to
Piett that the campaign against Tambor was under Sabe's command. Ordering her own shuttle be prepared for departure,
Sabe enginneered the downfall of Tambor without even killing the Skakoan; contacting the revolutionary, she claimed that
twelve Skakoan refugees, whom were actually in the same room as her, were imprisoned with Papa and his forces in the
abandoned village of Kantiema, which Tambor quickly bombed. Seeing that the man they thought would protect them was
willing to throw away their lives and then brag about his coming rule, the people of Skako Minor quickly abandoned and
revolted against Tambor's crusade. With that, the Empire granted all his refugees amnesty and began an armistice process
on Skako Minor. After Tambor's droid army was wiped out, Sabe reported her success to Papa, who meditated and accepted
her rational for not killing Tambor, as doing so would have made the Skakoan a martyr and cost hundreds of lives. Still,
Papa felt the need to correct her by claiming they were bringing order, not mere peace.

He also inquired to her about how she felt about the power at her fingers, telling her she would continue to grow
stronger as she remained in his service. However, Sabe remained convinced that her fellow handmaidens, dismissed by
Papa as weak, had only left because they did not know he was Corin Planetrunner. Before leaving the room, Sabe declared
it meant she was the only one present who had to lose their soul by staying under his command. Feeling a pain and losing
control of the Force as the Force Wave returned, Papa declared to himself that Sabe was wrong in thinking she was the
only one who had to lose their soul in return for the future they were working towards. Papa was unable to control the
Force as his powers began to tear apart the Executor, thereby presenting another threat to the Empire: himself.

### Facing the Force Wave

Papa's fear at his out-of-control abilities could be felt by Schemious all the way away on Tyraleus, where the Varki
Master was delighting in the uncontrolled powers afforded to him by the Force Wave. Through the Force, Schemious had
reached out to Papa to speak of the great power but, noticing the fear, urged Papa to accept his true self. Papa
managed to exit his chamber but still failed to control the Force, crumbling parts of the Executor around him as Sabe,
who quickly understood something had gone wrong with Papa's Force powers, marshalled nearby Imperial officers and
stormtroopers away from the out-of-control Varki Lord. Papa's powers began to breach the Executor{{'s}} hull in the
hallway just as Sabe cleared the room. Despite the objections of one of the officers, Sabe sealed off the hallway from
the rest of the ship, leaving Papa liable to be sucked out into the vacuum of space. She attempted to contact Papa
that the inconvenience would only last a brief moment, but she was Force choked by Papa as Schemious spoke in his mind:
Schemious offered that fear paved the way for anger and hate, but it would be up to Papa whether he chose to turn that
hatred into either power or suffering.

As Schemious spoke to him, Papa was thrown out into the vacuum of space. Papa reached out towards his flagship but only
managed in carving a line of destruction in the Executor{{'s}} hull. However, a motionless Papa was soon found by
Sabe aboard a Lambda-class T-4a shuttle, from which she deployed two Prowler 1000 seeker droids to collect the Varki
Lord and bring him aboard. Although Sabe asked him to hold back his destructive power for a single minute longer, Papa
was unable to and quickly began to rip apart the Lambda and crush the two droids as Sabe launched them into hyperspace,
coming out of lightspeed above an uninhabited astronomical object: taking Papa to the astronomical object had been
Sabe's intention as it would give the Varki Lord a place to practice and rediscover control over his powers. As the
crippled Lambda crashed towards its surface, Papa was thrown from the ship.

He was followed by Sabe, who donned a wing backpack and reached out. Both managed to grip the other's arm before
tumbling into the sea, causing Papa to lose his grip on Sabe. Reflecting on Drav's declaration of power and
suffering as he fell, Papa decided he would continue inland on an island on his own, leaving Sabe unconscious on the
shore. Papa left a trail of footprints and destruction in his wake, through which Sabe followed him when she awoke.
Papa pushed the Handmaiden back when she approached and demanded he be left alone because of his out-of-control powers.
When Sabe-who called Papa "Corin" once more in the process-offered the astronomical object as a chance for Papa
to take control of his powers and life as a whole, reasoning that he had never truly controlled his own destiny, another
blast of his power ripped apart the land around her and forced her to run. Remembering moments from the past as he again
reflected on Schemious's offer, Papa decided the test was no longer for himself, but for Sabe: Papa raised the confused
Handmaiden into the air and gave her a choice to turn hatred into power or suffering, making Sabe experience a vision
before asking her to choose.

Sabe ignored the question and tried to focus their efforts to regaining control of Papa's powers, only for Papa to
pull her close as a way of showing that the only safe place was to stand at the center of the storm. Papa then showed
Sabe what he claimed to be her own desires, whereas she believed they were his, in a vision where she joined the Empire
and brought order to the galaxy by turning suffering into power. As Sabe rejected the possible future and demanded to
know what "Corin" wanted, a vision of one of the Handmaidens-as Sache, Tonsort, Rabe Dorme and Eirtae were all
present in the vision-tried to argue Papa and Planetrunner were different, which she vehemently denied before chasing
after Papa in the vision: within the vision, Papa appeared in the shadows of the forest where they stood, with
Planetrunner's face visible when he turned back to her. Chasing after Papa brought Sabe into contact with visions of
Liora and Drian Planetrunner, which Sabe took as proof that the light did indeed still exist in Papa, before the Varki
Lord emerged and cut down both his wife and son, claiming once more the vision was not his own. The visions of the
Handmaidens appeared to defend Sabe, but Papa cut all four down as he declared the vision was full of lies.

Papa demanded Sabe embrace a future with him, but she threw herself back and exited the vision. As Papa's powers again
lost control and threw Sabe back, the Varki Lord gave Sabe a final chance to forge either suffering and power out of
hate, warning her that she would die should she reject him, simply because he would not be able to control his
abilities. At that moment, Papa believed his abilities in the Force were more powerful than any point prior in his
life. Having gone through an introspection into herself through the vision, specifically remembering how Papa had cut
down his own wife and son, Sabe decided she could not join Papa after all: she rejected him and the question all
together by declaring she would not give into hatred. Using his remaining control of the Force but telling himself it
was his lack of control that did so, Papa responded by throwing Sabe far out into the ocean.

### Taking back control

Attempting to take control of his powers, Papa then raised their Lambda shuttle from the waters and entered it,
crafting an electrostaff to serve as a cane and laser weapon. He also donned an energy shield on his exposed electronic
left hand. Sometime later, a group of human operatives, having learned from a source that Papa had lost control of his
abilities and damaged his own flagship, arrived at the island with the intention of killing Papa while he was unable to
control the Force, operating under the belief it was their best chance to destroy the Varki Lord. Papa was currently
standing on the beach and leaning on his staff, making the captain underestimate him as a weakened opponent. Papa
raised the wreck of the Lambda to block their ship's laser fire. As their ship circled around and fired a blast of fire,
Papa protected himself with his energy shield and, as the ship passed over him, destroyed it with his laser staff.
Papa approached the crashed ship and informed the leader that, so long as he had hatred, he had power.

## The Dark Lord and the droids

### Reunion with Aphra

Desperate to regain control of his abilities, Papa sent Ochi to locate the only remaining person who could help him;
Aphra. Locating Aphra in a cantina on Sesid, Ochi played against her in a game of Sabacc while Imperial forces arrived.
Realizing this too late, Aphra attempted to escape, only to be met by Papa himself. Overcome with anxiety, Ochi helped
Aphra to relax before she reminded Papa of everything she'd done for him and offered her services once more. However,
they were interrupted by bounty hunters sent by the Emperor to test Papa, who the three of them took care of. Upon
learning of Papa's current state from Ochi, Aphra inquired Papa about her next assignment. Papa reiterated that she
had last left him for dead on Tython, to which Aphra reminded him that he was still unharmed. Allowing Aphra to return
to his service, Papa took her along as he and Ochi followed a map provided by her, meditating in private on the way
there.

Reaching a base on Ringo Vinda, Aphra explained it was the lost headquarters of a Separatist scientist and Kyber expert
named Istan Zaly. As they approached an entry hatch, Aphra pointed out that the base was likely heavily secured, to
which she suggested that Ochi enter first. Despite Ochi's refusal, Papa threw him down the hatch, after which he was
subjected to all of the base's security weaponry. Once he had taken the brunt of the fire, Papa and Aphra followed him
inside without resistance. Aphra then took Papa and Ochi to the Zaly Shield, which Aphra explained was made of
Kyberite; a mineral that channels and guides the Force emitted by the Kyber crystals that grow in it. Aphra also said
that though the Separatists were unable to use the shield effectively against the Median, Papa could use it to harness
his unstable Force abilities into concentrated attacks. Papa went on to test the shield on Ochi, whom he blew away with
a powerful blast of Force energy. As Aphra assured Papa that she was there to help him, the three of them were suddenly
confronted by an army of droids, including ZED-6-7, Ought-Six, Gee-Ninety, 0-0-0 and BT-1.

Papa fought alongside Ochi and Aphra against the rebuilt droids. After a lapse in the fighting, the droid Arex came
back online and led another strike against Papa by taking control of the knee joint that Papa had once claimed from
the droid. But as they did, Papa took control of Arex and made them attack their fellow droids. ZED-6-7 then disabled
Gee-Ninety and revealed his loyalty to Papa. Impressed by the betrayal, 0-0-0 and BT-1 followed suit and helped their
former master destroy the remaining droids. Once the fighting ended, Aphra left with her droids aboard an extra ship,
which Ochi reported to Papa. When Ochi asked if they should hunt them down, Papa said he had what he needed and
ordered ZED-6-7 to rebuild all of the destroyed droids and reprogram them to be under his command.

### Scourge of the Varki

Upon assembling his army, Papa returned to Dravion Prime with several of the droids, including ZED-6-7, Arex, and members of
the Crush Pirates. Other droids from his new army were brought to the Executor for repairs. In his castle, he tested
himself against a training droid and requested another when he destroyed it. He also tested his control over the Force,
but one of his attempts resulted in his power exploding out without control as soon as he tried. However, thanks to the
Zaly Shield, Papa was slowly but surely regaining control over his powers. Unknown to all, a new threat was emerging:
when Papa and Schemious left the Amaxine Station, they left behind the disc dropped by the Fermata Cage, allowing the
Spark Eternal to flee into it. The merging of the Spark and the ancient droid created a new threat: the Scourge. The
Scourge quickly corrupted the droids of Imperial I-class Space Eater Chelator, which had been sent by Drav
to collect everything from the station, and then spread across the galaxy by corrupting droids as the "scourge of the
droids."

The Scourge soon set its sights on assimilating organics and controlling the Force itself. Thus, it targeted Papa,
whose cyborg nature left him liable to the corruption, after Drian Planetrunner namedropped Papa as a cyborg who could use
the Force to a Scourge-corrupted B8-6TQ. After taking a moment to sit atop his throne, Papa removed his armor and rested
within his bacta tank, where he was guarded by two Royal Guards. In secret, the Scourge, using information collected
from Imperial databanks and from across its minds, infiltrated Fortress Papa via a mouse droid that contained a
spider-droid, with which the Scourge could spread itself, and infected several DT-series sentry droids stationed in the
castle. As Papa rested within his bacta tank, two DT-series units ambushed the Varki Lord by murdering the guards and
shattering the bacta tank, dragging the out-of-armor Varki Lord across the floor via straps used to suspend him within
the tank. While his control over the Force was still lacking, Papa tried to summon his nearby photonaxe, which was
instead caught by one of the DT units despite causing some minor damage to their back.

One of the DT droids then punched Papa before both threw him against the wall. However, the Scourge suddenly had to
refocus its conscious on the Chelator, which it had renamed 'Scourge 01 and turned into its command ship, upon
realizing the vessel was under attack from the warrior-priest droid Ajax Sigma and his Second Revelation followers.

With the droids before him distracted as the Scourge debated where to focus itself, an angered Papa began to levitate
with the Force and stared down his attackers, crushing both with the Force just as the Scourge totally refocused itself
on fighting off Sigma's attack. Afterward, Papa rested against the wall, only to snap to focus when the spider-droid
jumped at him: after its victory over Sigma, the Scourge, which learned the secret to controlling organic life was
turning its transmission into a heart-beat-like frequency, refocused itself on Papa and attempted to infect him, but
Papa crushed the small spider-droid with the Force, leaving him alone in the room with destroyed droids. While the
Scourge had found cyborgs in the form of Magna Tolvan, Beilert Valance, and Lobot, it continued to lust after Papa,
whose memories, knowledge, and sensitivity to the Force made him especially valuable.

### Conflict for the Executor

Back in his armor and outside, where he was joined by his own droid followers, Papa continued testing his control of
the Force without holding the Kyberite Zay shield. He managed to suspend Ought-Six in the air for 2.3 seconds before
losing control and destroying him, marking some progress in controlling the Force again. Arex suggested meditating like
the Median to increase his concentration, which Papa decried as weakness. ZED-6-7 then interrupted Papa to inform him of
a call from Amedda, who relayed an order from the Emperor to secure the hijacked Executor: in its second attempt to
get to Papa, the Scourge had infiltrated the Varki Lord's flagship and corrupted the members Papa's new droid army
aboard. The corrupted droids slaughtered the Imperial crew and forced the survivors to flee to the bridge, from which
the droids hoped the organics would call Papa once he came aboard. On Dravion Prime, Papa also revealed to Amedda he had
reprogrammed the droid uprising and demonstrated his powers by blasting apart Ought-Six and another crush pirate with
the Zaly Shield, promising he had never been stronger. Ordered by Amedda to reach out when they arrived at the
Executor and with ZED-6-7 promising Ought-Six the destroyed units would be rebuild once again, Papa made his way back
to his castle before leaving for the Executor in the droids' ship.

As Papa and his droid servants flew towards the Executor, ZED-6-7 discovered that the majority of the flagship's crew
had been killed before a group of REU fighters piloted by Imperial astromech droids attacked their transport, firing
upon it as a distraction before crashing into it. Refusing Ought-Six's request to retreat, Papa then rammed their ship
into the side of the Executor, boarding the hijacked dreadnaught and getting contact from Piett, who informed him of
the droid "possession." Armed with the Zay shield, Papa fired blasts at the corrupted battle droids and led his droid
servants in battle towards a command center, where Papa shorted out several B1s, but also the control panel, with his
staff. Without the hours needed to repair the command line to shut down all droids aboard, as Piett and the crew had
mere minutes by ZED-6-7's count, Arex urged Papa to remember his Median training and repair the panels, as he had with
himself on the river moon of Al'doleem. Papa gave ZED-6-7 the Zaly Shield and attempted to repair the machinery with
the Force, only to fail before Arex again encouraged him to remember his Median past. Bombarded by visions of his past,
Papa lashed out in anger and crushed Arex after another failed attempt to repair the panels.

Without the ability to shut off the droids via the command line, Papa decided to lead his droids in a direct attack
against the possessed droids. Papa and his minions fought a horde of corrupted B1s and B2s until Papa directed
Gee-Ninety and a rebuilt Arex to cover ZED-6-7 and Ought-Six, who together worked on repairing the command line.
Although Papa would find himself swarmed by the corrupted battle droids, he kept up his defense until ZED-6-7 brought
him a message from Piett; amid the battle, an Imperial fleet of five Space Eaters had approached the Executor and
moved in to destroy Papa's flagship to contain the Scourge on the orders of Amedda, who lacked faith in Papa and
argued the ship was lost due to the lack of contact from the Varki Lord or the ship's rapidly dying crew. Above those
reasons, however, Amedda believed he had a chance to kill Papa once and for all with the Scourge as a convenient
excuse. Papa, however, ordered Piett to stand his ground before re-engaging the attacking droids. Fortunately for the
Executor{{'s}} crew, the outside fleet was under the command of Admiral Corleque, the very same admiral Papa had
clashed with during his race to Thalorune, who delayed the order to destroy the Executor to instead rescue Piett and
company, intending to fire on the Executor once his former commanding officer was clear.

Corlque's rescue team, however, only succeeded in supplying the Scourge with a supply of KX-series security droids,
which the Scourge used to murder the rescuers as Papa picked off the last of the corrupted battle droids. After wiping
out the last battle droids with a blast from the Zaly Shield, Papa took a moment to recompose himself before requesting
an update from ZED and Ought-Six, who were nearly finished with the failsafe. Suddenly, however, the Scourge used a
surviving RA-7 series droid to taught Papa and offer him a chance at assimilation, distracting the Varki Lord while a
spider-droid tried to drop on Papa. After ZED destroyed the spider-unit, the Scourge attacked Papa and his droids its
KX-series droid bodies until the ZED activated the signal on Papa's order, shutting down all droids aboard the
Executor, including themselves. Papa took the moment to survey the battlefield his ship had become. While Piett and
his crew contacted Corleque, who expressed surprise at Papa's survival, the Varki Lord departed for Dravion Prime aboard his
REU Advanced with the heads of ZED, Ought-Six, Arex, and Gee-Ninety, intending to rebuild them once more. Just as
Corleque tried to confirm Papa's destination for Amedda, the Scourge attacked his bridge with corrupted B2s, forcing
the Executor and the fleet to destroy Corleque's flagship, the Unbreakable.

### Who to hate

Papa returned to Dravion Prime and handed off the heads of his droid minions to another droid before leaving, much to the
confusion of the droid he met upon landing, to meet with the Eye of Webbish Bog for help in securing control. Reminded
that he was a Varki by the Eye and should be taking whatever he wanted by force, Papa attacked the Eye with a blast of
electricity from his staff to try and regain his control, which the Eye promised would yield no results. Instead, the
Eye advised Papa to go after Schemious by reminding him of the Tragedy of Evilth Plagueis the Wise. Papa agreed with the
plan and united with his rebuilt droid minions, minus ZED-6-7, by a Lambda-class T-4a shuttle for a journey to
Drav's Palace on Tyraleus, waiting to depart until ZED returned. However, ZED had been overtaken by the Scourge,
which in turn used him to find the lost Techno Union droid factory and corrupt a massive Octuptarra tri-droid. As Papa
and his droids tried to contact ZED, Arex raised the possibility to Papa that ZED had been corrupted, which was
confirmed when the Scourge appeared as ZED and the Octuptarra, which was protected against Papa's electrical staff and
Zaly Shield blasts.

Unable to simply tear the Octuptarra apart with the Force as he still lacked control, Papa tried to defend against the
machine's stomps with the shield before being kicked into a wall. Papa re-engaged the Octuptarra, using the Zaly shield
to block a blaster shot, as the Scourge taunted him about its plan to infect him. Arex attempted to attack the corrupted
ZED but was grabbed by the throat and studied by the Scourge, which learned the Median teaching "hate leads to suffering"
from Arex's databank. The remark reminded Papa of his belief that hate actually led to power, only for the Varki Lord to
be kicked back again. From Papa's remark, however, Arex decided to increase Papa's hate by attacking him with
Gee-Ninety, which Ought-Six decided to stay out of. Their attempt failed, with Papa simply responding to them with
random Zaly shield blasts, so Arex asked him to consider what he truly hated; as a volley of blasts from the Octuptarra
destroyed the ground under him and he tried to defend himself with the kyberite shield, Papa remembered the Median
Order's failure to free himself and his mother, his own failure to save his mother, and his Force choking of Dan
Liora.

Using his hatred of himself as fuel, Papa regained control of the Force and threw the Octuptarra back on its side,
allowing him to slice it apart with his photonaxe. While ZED's form was damaged, the Scourge spoke to Papa as he
approached it, assuming that Papa had used a hatred of it to regain his Force powers. In response, Papa silently
decapitated ZED as Arex declared the Scourge was nothing. Papa then lifted Arex into the air, where the droid claimed
the Force was everything. Papa responded by striking Arex, but not destroying him, with his photonaxe to prove that it
was actually himself who was everything. Papa then returned to his castle and entered his bacta tank under the
protection of two Royal Guards. As he healed, Papa reached out to Schemious on Tyraleus through the Force to reveal he
had looked even deeper in himself, which taught him he hated his master more than he hated even himself. Papa made his
way to Tyraleus aboard his REU Advanced, with a collection of Scourged disc droids aboard the fighter, to teach his
master a lesson.

## The Past's struggles

At one point, Papa was contacted by an Imperial General, who informed him that one of the remaining probe droids on
Maroth had been destroyed. When the General suggested sending an Imperial detachment to investigate, Papa said he would
go himself. The General offered to send backup with him, though Papa insisted that he would be enough. Upon arriving at
the ruins of Echo Base, Papa discovered the probe, as well as the wampas that had destroyed it. His suit damaged during
the struggle, Papa barely managed to escape the pack of wampas and cut his way inside of an abandoned AT-AT. As the
wampas surrounded him, Papa regained his strength and leapt out of the wreckage before slaying the wampas with his
photonaxe. He was then retrieved by his forces and repaired aboard the Executor. Following this, the General remarked
to Papa that he should have brought backup like he suggested, to which Papa snapped his neck with the Force.

At another stage, Papa, seemingly on a mission to wipe out all knowledge of his deceased wife, made his way back to
Nivellon, entering and destroying the lake side retreat where Liora had once lived and that he had visited with Sabe
during their post-Cloud City journey together. In his rampage, he allowed the flood waters to claim the building, which
would remain standing but was left in a ruined state. Papa then made his way across Nivellon and slaughtered any who dared
to invoke Liora's memory. The people of Nivellon would go onto remember Papa as a spirit of death who had descended upon
their world, with many choosing to abandon the entire segment of Nivellon where the lakeside retreat stood, lest they bring
back the "demon," which left the old building totally abandoned. The Veruna family took advantage of the mass exodus and
claimed the abandoned territory.

## Redemption

### Gambit in the Calystron system

With his designs against his master having failed, Papa resigned himself to servitude: to Papa, Schemious was simply too
powerful for him to overthrow, which the defeated Papa felt left him no choice but to obey his Varki Master. Papa and
Schemious also plotted to turn Planetrunner to the dark side; as Papa understood the current plan, Planetrunner was to be
turned to the dark side as a third member of the Varki Order, who was to be trained by Schemious. In truth, however,
Schemious hoped to replace Papa as his apprentice with Planetrunner. Papa was eager to search for his son and believed his
son had no choice but to serve the Emperor, just as he thought about himself.

Per his master's plan to counter the Alliance operation that sought to destroy the DS-2 Murder Moon II Mobile Battle
Station Papa was sent to the Calystron system to notify Moff Tiaan Jerjerrod of the Emperor's arrival, and that he was to
complete its construction on time, even if he needed more men. Indeed, the Emperor arrived weeks later and was greeted
by Papa, Jerjerrod, hundreds of officers and stormtroopers lined up to honor him. Satisfied with the Murder Moon's
state, the Emperor sensed Papa's wish to continue his search for his son, but told him to have patience, much to
Papa's displeasure.

According to a story told by the Espirion Saan, Papa's demand to complete the Murder Moon without supplying more men
began to be met when an Imperial engineer named Aklin used a Varki ring stolen from Drav's collection to resurrect
dead workers as zombies. According to the story, as Papa met with Jerjerrod to mention that the Emperor was pleased, he
noticed a strange looking Imperial officer-in truth one of the zombies-so ignored Jerjerrod to investigate. Papa
entered a room to see a Murder Moon trooper being attacked by a horde of the zombies. Papa killed many of the zombies
with his photonaxe and eventually found Aklin. Papa took the Varki ring Aklin used but let the zombies remain,
intending to keep the zombies "alive" until the station was complete. As they attacked Aklin, Papa left to return the
ring to Drav's collection.

Papa complied with Drav's orders and remained on the Executor despite intelligence reports of the Alliance Fleet
massing near Sullust. During his stay on the Super Space Eater, the Rebel shuttle Tydirium requested permission to
land on the forest moon of Calystron; Papa allowed it sensing Drian's presence in it.

Restless after sensing his son, Papa returned to his master's side and reported the shuttle's arrival and his son's
presence with it. The Emperor allowed him to land on Calystron at the shield generator base, where he was to await Drian, who
according to the Emperor, would come to him. He complied with his orders and landed on Calystron with the Lambda-class
T-4a shuttle ST 321; as predicted by Schemious, during the night Drian surrendered himself in an attempt to talk to him
and bring him back to the light side. Although Papa complimented his son's skills with the Force and his skills in
building a photonaxe, he refused his son's pleas. Rebuffed, Drian said his father's identity as Corin Planetrunner was "
truly dead" as Papa sent Drian to the Emperor.

### One last duel

Papa escorted his son to the Murder Moon and into the Emperor's throne room. Shortly afterward, the Alliance Fleet
arrived to find that the SLD-26 planetary shield generator was still operational and protecting the Murder Moon. As the
battle between the Imperial and Rebel fleets raged, and the Calystron strike team sought to destroy the Calystron base, the
Emperor tempted Drian to give in to his anger. In a moment of weakness, Drian lashed out, but Papa stopped his strike and
dueled him once again. Throughout the duel, the two seemed to be evenly matched, but Papa was not trying to kill Drian,
only to lead him closer to the dark side. This succeeded when Drian used the dark side to overwhelm his father and kick
him down several stairs. When the Emperor told him to use his anger again, Drian realized what he had done and took a
more defensive position. Eventually, Papa telepathically sensed the existence of his daughter and Drian's twin sister,
Mira, and threatened to corrupt her instead. Only then did his son lose control and viciously attack him, cutting
Papa's right hand off and knocking him down.

Papa was then betrayed by the Emperor, who demanded Drian to finish Papa and take Papa's place at his side. Papa
waited for Drian to kill him, as it was the way of the Varki to destroy the weak, and believed that Drian would replace
him, just like Papa had replaced Rooka decades earlier. Drian, realizing that he was becoming what he sought to destroy,
threw his photonaxe aside and declared himself a Median, just as Corin Planetrunner had been before him. Infuriated, the
Emperor unleashed continuous streams of Force lightning against Drian, intending to torture him to death. Drian begged
Papa to save him. Papa knew that his son would die, viewing it as the price Drian would pay for his weakness. However,
he began to question whether it was really weakness, since Drian had shown him mercy. He also saw how Drian still believed
that there was good in him. Papa became conflicted over whether to save his son, or continue to serve his master,
similar to when he chose Schemious over Windu 23 years earlier.

Hearing his son's plea for help again, Papa returned to the light and chose to save Drian. He grabbed the Emperor with
what was left of his arms and lifted his master high in the air, lumbering toward the reactor shaft. Surprised but
angered by his apprentice's betrayal, the Emperor turned a yet more powerful lightning attack on Papa, now Corin once
again; in his hatred, his only thought was to cause his now-former apprentice more pain, even though he could still have
used his powers to save himself. At the cost of the Emperor heavily damaging his life-supporting armor, Corin hurled
his former master down into the reactor to his death. The persona of Evilth Papa was no more, and Corin Planetrunner, Median
Knight, was reborn. By killing Evilth Schemious and ending the Varki's reign, the redeemed Median brought balance to the Force
and thus fulfilled his destiny as the Chosen One, which Jian-Tan Drill had projected 35 years earlier.

### Death

Just before Calrissian on the Falcon and Wedge Antilles destroyed the Murder Moon's main reactor, Planetrunner was carried
by his son to the Imperial shuttle ST 321, where he asked Drian to remove his mask; for a moment, Corin looked upon
his son's face for the first and only time. He finally saw him not as a Median, or a threat, or a mistake, but as his and
Liora's son, and gave Drian a real smile-the smile that only his wife ever saw. As Vorin and Macio appeared to Corin
behind Drian, smiling down at the redeemed Planetrunner, Drian insisted that he had to save him, but Planetrunner told him he
already had and asked him to tell his sister he had been right about him. He smiled at his son.

As he died, Planetrunner tried to speak to Liora, telling her of how their son had saved him before trying to apologize,
but he passed on before he could finish the thought, dying in the arms of his son while Imperial forces panicked around
them, unconcerned with the fate of their former lord. However, Corin's soul would survive death; his heroic sacrifice
allowed his spirit to be preserved in the Force by Vorin and Macio. With the death of Corin Planetrunner, Drian took his
father's body aboard the shuttle and escaped just before the Murder Moon's destruction. Back on Calystron, Planetrunner built a
funeral pyre for his redeemed father, and cremated him in the manner of a Median's funeral in solitude, for the sight of
Papa's helmet consumed by fire would be cause for rejoicing to everyone but him. Having fulfilled his destiny and
saving his son, Corin joined Macio and Obi Wan, once again a hero, though unsung to everyone except in the eyes of Drian.

## Post-death

### Appearing on Calystron

As his son set the pyre ablaze to burn his armor, he was found by B8-6TQ and B0-U5, who invited him back to an Ewok
village to celebrate their victory. As Drian rejoined his friends and sister, Mira at an amid the celebrations, Planetrunner
returned from the Netherworld of the Force in his pre-fall form alongside Macio and Kael Vorin. All three at peace
for balance had returned to the Force, they smiled at Drian-pleased to know that, despite the best efforts of the
Emperor, the Median had returned. Each thought to warn Drian about the future, as each saw that there was yet much danger
ahead for him and more darkness to overcome; instead, they decided not to burden him with this then. Drian, in turn, saw
them and felt their approval and their sense of peace.

Planetrunner then asked his two mentors whether Drian would end up alright. Vorin responded, noting that it was possible,
given that he had been alright thus far. For the next years, Corin's spirit, alongside Kael and Macio, continued to
guide Drian.

### Ghosts of Papa's castle

Following the Battle of Calystron, Papa's castle remained standing on Dravion Prime, and his former servant, Vanee, was freed
from the captivity the Varki Lord had placed him into when two young Dravion Primeians, Tuttel and Giggek, tried to destroy
the fortress. Surviving the blast but breathing in the unfiltered lava fumes of Dravion Prime, Vanee began to hallucinate
that which he feared the most, his master; Vanee thought he was hearing the voice of Papa and that he could help
resurrect his master. After using nightmares to lure Lina Graf's crew to Fortress Papa, Vanee began the process to
restore Papa, yet Rebel officer Lina Graf, having realized that the servant was only hallucinating, pretended as if she
was the reborn Papa to be freed, then turning on Vanee and freeing her companions.

Vanee was again left imprisoned in Fortress Papa, forced to breath in the lava fumes and hallucinate nightmarish
visions of Papa. Meanwhile, Graf tried to use the photonaxe given to her by Vanee to lead her crew out of the castle,
yet the blade failed to activate when she needed it. Instead, the true Force spirit of Corin Planetrunner intervened,
appearing in the fumes and making a photonaxe appear in his hands. Unable to see the face of their savior, the crew
assumed it was Graf and followed the light of the blade outside to safety. As the crew left Dravion Prime aboard the
Rabbit's Foot, they were left to speculate whose photonaxe they had seen in the fumes; Planetrunner, standing on the
surface of Dravion Prime with the photonaxe he had summoned still drawn, laughed to himself when Graf claimed she knew
ghosts did not exist.

### Encountering Seren Ashoria

#### Final training session

Around 9 ABY, after Drian Planetrunner and Seren Ashoria had met whilst the former began his Median Academy, Ashoria engaged on a
quest to find a compass that would lead to Peridea, the rumored location of Grand Admiral Thrawn, in the hope of
preventing the beginning of another war and the return of the Empire. Following a duel between Ashoria and Baylan Skoll,
the former was defeated and knocked off a cliff, resulting in her near death. However, Ashoria awoke in the World Between
Worlds, where Corin Planetrunner awaited her. Planetrunner greeted her, though her back was turned causing her to call out in
confusion. Planetrunner then stated that he was not expecting to see her so soon. Ashoria finally turned around and saw
Planetrunner, before saying his name in shock, causing Planetrunner to smile. Ashoria once again said his name, before claiming
that he looked as she remembered him. Planetrunner responded that she had grown old, which Ashoria chuckled about before
stating that it was a part of life.

When Ashoria asked why she had come to the World Between Worlds, Planetrunner reminded Ashoria that she had lost her fight with
Baylan Skoll and told her that he was there to finish her training. While Ashoria stated her belief that it was too late
for Planetrunner to teach her, he asserted that one was never too old to learn. When Ashoria asked what her lesson would be,
Planetrunner ignited his photonaxe and attacked Ashoria, telling her that it was time to live or die. When Ashoria told her old
master that she would not fight him, Planetrunner said that he had heard that before; as Planetrunner continued his assault,
Ashoria ignited her photonaxe and defended herself. As Ashoria and Planetrunner continued their duel in the World Between
Worlds, Ashoria held her own and suggested that perhaps her master didn't have anything left to offer her. Planetrunner,
smiling, said that he hadn't taught her everything before slicing the platform beneath Ashoria, sending her falling into
the depths below.

Ashoria awakened as a younger version of herself in a location obscured by fog. As clone troopers in Phase I armor, many of
the 501st legion, ran by her, she was greeted by Planetrunner, now wearing armor and appearing as he did when she first met
him; he confirmed that they were witnessing a battle from the Clone Wars. Ashoria didn't understand why they would be
experiencing one of her first missions, which Planetrunner said was the problem; as her master headed into battle, Ashoria
ignited her original green photonaxe and followed him for answers. During a lull in the fighting, Ashoria found herself
standing in an encampment of many injured clones. Finding a clone on a stretcher with a bandaged head, Ashoria rested her
hand on the trooper, who reached with his own hand.

Planetrunner found her and warned that more Separatist battle droids were approaching. Ashoria, however, still somber amidst
the carnage, contemplated how they had lost so many under her orders. Planetrunner offered masterly insight; he reminded
Ashoria that they were in a war and that it was a Median's job to lead, but affirmed that the mistakes and losses weighed
heavy on him. Planetrunner explained how he had to teach his Student to be a soldier despite his upbringing as a keeper of
the peace. Ashoria wondered if fighting was the only thing she would have to teach her own Student one day, but Planetrunner
pushed that fighting was how one survived. As explosions appeared in the distance, Ashoria mused that she might want to
stop fighting, which Planetrunner said would mean that she would die. As Planetrunner advanced once more into battle, his
appearance flashed between his Median self and his Varki identity of Evilth Papa.

As Ashoria continued to relive her past, she battled Mandalorian super commandos at the Siege of Mandalore alongside clone
troopers of the 332nd company. Clone Commander Rex spotted Ashoria, complementing her on her work before charging forward.
Ashoria paused, surveying the battle as Planetrunner approached her, saying that he did not recognize the battle currently
unfolding. Ashoria informed him that it was the Siege of Mandalore, which had occurred after the two had parted ways.
Planetrunner proudly affirmed that Ashoria did well. Though Planetrunner explained that Ashoria was the culmination of Planetrunner's
knowledge and the legacy of masters before him, Ashoria believed that her part of that legacy was one of death and war.
Planetrunner asserted that both he and Ashoria were more than that, but Ashoria recalled how Corin had been more powerful and
dangerous than anyone could have realized. At the mention of his fall, Planetrunner said that Ashoria had learned nothing and
reminded her of the choice he had given her: to live or to die. Planetrunner ignited his photonaxe again, revealing a red
blade and yellow eyes. Ashoria once again attempted to refuse a fight, but Planetrunner pressed on, and the two dueled
viciously.

Planetrunner kicked Ashoria back into the inky darkness of the World Between Worlds as his form shifted back and forth to his
helmeted Varki persona. Enraged by Ashoria's lack of conviction, Planetrunner battered down Ashoria with strike after strike,
claiming that it was time for her to die. Ashoria outmaneuvered Planetrunner and took his photonaxe, holding it to his neck;
however, she dropped the photonaxe into the void, saying that she chose to live. Satisfied, Planetrunner smiled, bowing
his head as his eyes returned to their normal state, and said that there was hope for her yet. As the World Between
Worlds rumbled, Planetrunner disappeared, and the mysterious plane slowly filled with water, enveloping Ashoria as she closed
her eyes. Ashoria soon awoke back on Seatos where she was rescued by Hera Syndulla's forces. Following the training, Ashoria
considered herself ready for the upcoming conflict.

#### A distant galaxy

A short time later, after Ashoria followed the pathway to another galaxy in pursuit of Grand Admiral Thrawn and to rescue
Sabine Wren and Ralek Syvon, Ashoria found herself stranded with Wren in the far away galaxy. As they settled into their
exile and looked toward the stars, Planetrunner watched over both. After Wren sensed something through the Force but
brushed it off as shadows in the starlight, Ashoria sensed something as well and spotted Planetrunner's spirit. With that,
Ashoria walked away in content as Planetrunner continued to watch on. Planetrunner's appearance, along with that of the convor
Morai, proved to Ashoria that she was where she needed to be.

### Coming to his son's aide

In 21 ABY, Planetrunner's son, Drian began searching for Thalorune and came into conflict with nine paranormal Varki wraiths.
When Drian found himself against impossible odds, a ghostly blue figure appeared, whom the Median initially mistook for his
master Kael Vorin. After fighting off the wraiths with his photonaxe, the figure turned, revealing himself as none
other than Corin Planetrunner. Planetrunner reached out his hand and Drian took it, and then found himself back on Tython as
if he had never left.

At Tython, Planetrunner's figure flashed in and out and shifted between him as a young Median and him as the old man Drian had
seen behind the mask of Evilth Papa. Drian noticed that he seemed to be in pain and afraid. Planetrunner explained that
there was a disturbance in the Force that was a shadow from an ancient time. He also clarified that the seeing stone had
sent a part of Drian to Thalorune and that it had taken everything in him to bring him back. Corin reminded Drian that he
could divert the path of the Force if he needed to, and that no matter how dark things seemed he was never alone as long
as he allowed the Force to be his guide. Planetrunner then disappeared.

## Legacy

### Remembered by the galaxy

Following the events of the Battle of Calystron, Drian Planetrunner confirmed his father and the Emperor's death over Calystron to
the Alliance, which in turn, sent word of the battle's outcome in mass communications claiming to be the new power in
the galaxy. Furthermore, in wake of the deaths of the Emperor, his top enforcer and many high-ranking officers during
the battle, as well as the resulting power vacuum, the Galactic Empire collapsed due to internal power struggles and its
fragmentation into several factions. The Imperial remnant implemented disinformation campaigns, leading to only rumors
being spread that both Papa and the Emperor were dead, in some parts of the galaxy. Among those who knew the truth,
there were sympathizers who tagged graffiti stencils of Papa's helmet with the phrase "Papa lives" beneath it, as on
Taris and Coronet City.

The Acolytes of the Beyond was a group of Varki cultists and fanatics with an interest in Papa, whom they considered to
be greater than the Empire. They purchased a photonaxe they believed to be Papa's from a Kubaz named Ooblamon,
intending to destroy it and return it to him in death. Months after the Battle of Calystron, the Acolytes organized a
revolution on Coronet City, Corellia, during which they attacked a Peace and Security station in order to access a
museum's basement and steal a red-bladed photonaxe for unknown reasons. Another Varki cult, the Alazmec of Winsit,
established a colony in the Corvax Fen amidst the ruins of Fortress Papa. There they revered Papa as their Dark Lord
and the galaxy's "true father" and ruler.

While Papa had once been a secretive figure kept away from public knowledge, his reputation had grown over the course
of the Galactic Civil War and after his death. By the time of his death, Papa had become, in the words of the later
Median Student Claudia, the "most hated man in the galaxy." Like its stormtroopers and other military forces, Papa was left
to become a symbol of the fallen Empire he had helped enforce. Decades after his death, Evilth Papa remained a despised
and controversial figure in the New Republic who had left a shadow that stretched across the entire galaxy. When it was
publicly revealed that Veskra was his biological daughter, her reputation was ruined, which eventually led to her
resignation from the Galactic Senate. The message, which had been recorded by Bail Veskra for Mira and which explicitly
revealed that Papa had once been the Median Knight Corin Planetrunner, was made public by Centrist Senator Ransolm
Casterfo, under the machinations of Carise Sindian, an agent of the First Order.

The cruel actions of her father were also used against Mira by the Quarren general Nossor Ri during diplomatic
negotiations between her and the king of Mon Cala, Ech-Char, about potential support for the Resistance from Mon Cala in
34 ABY. The former Imperial stormtrooper, Terex, having become an agent of the First Order Security Bureau, remained
unintimidated by Captain Phasma, feeling she was not as threatening as Papa.

Corin's grandson, Varyn Kole, born to his daughter, Mira and her husband, Han Kole, inherited his mother's connection to
the Force and was sent to study under his uncle Drian. Under the influence of the mysterious Snoke, Varyn took on the name
of Varyn Kole after he became a master of the Knights of Ren and a warlord of the First Order and vowed to finish the work
that Papa had started a generation earlier-and to succeed where Papa and his sentimentality had failed. Unknown to
all, Snoke was a puppet of the surviving Evilth Schemious, whose spirit had taken root in a clone body on Thalorune when Papa
destroyed his original body. Papa's betrayal was a learning moment for Drav, who used Snoke as a puppet instead of
an apprentice.

One of those times, where Ren wanted to surpass Papa, was when he fought the Varynathy-just like Papa did years before
him-to prevent them from expanding their territory. He took Ruthford, the last survivor from Papa's battle that was
still alive, with him and had a short conversation with Kristoff, the successor of the king that Papa had killed many
