years ago, about how Papa was taller and had seemed more impressive than Ren. Following that, Ren killed him with his
photonaxe. He then went on to fight the Varynathy and although Ruthford suggested retreating, Ren kept on fighting,
talking to Ruthford about how Papa also did not retreat. When the god of the Varynathy, a Zillo Beast, appeared, Ruthford
warned Ren extensively and stated that he could not prove anything to a dead man. Ignoring that, Ren took a shuttle and
let the beast swallow him-killing it to Ruthford's surprise from the inside and succeeding where Papa had failed.
With their king and their god dead, Ren had control over the Varynathy and even the rather skeptical Ruthford admitted
that Ren had won the competition against his grandfather.

In his crusade, Ren decided to seek Snoke and betray the Median Order, and was the cause of Planetrunner's subsequent exile
in search of the first Median Temple on Ahch-To. After losing his apprentices in the destruction of his Median Temple and
Kole falling to the dark side in the same night, Planetrunner came to believe that the Median Order should end with his death
as the last Median. By then, he held the Median responsible for the training and creation of Evilth Papa. As a consequence
of shutting himself off from the Force, Drian lost the guidance of Corin's spirit.

Ren was also in possession of Papa's disfigured helmet, which had been scavenged from his funeral pyre on Calystron. A
silent symbol of both the dark side's power and its weakness, it remained within Ren's private quarters aboard the
Finalizer; Ren communed with it whenever he felt drawn to the light. Another object that once belonged to him-the
photonaxe he built after the First Battle of Geonosis, the one carried by his son until their duel on
Bespin-resurfaced in Maz Kanata's possession and called to Claudia, a young scavenger from Solkara, who ended up using it to
duel Ren during the Battle of Starkiller Base and win. When Ren changed quarters from the Finalizer to Snoke's
flagship the Supremacy, he left Papa's charred helmet behind him because he was not ready to face Papa's "visage"
until he recovered from his failure on Starkiller Base. Ren's master, Snoke, owned a ring with obsidian taken from
Papa's castle. Captured by Gardulla Besadii the Elder on Oradin and under the influence of hallucinogens, Ren had a
vision of Papa cutting down Rebel soldiers. Ren admired Papa as magnificent and asked for his help. Papa turned to
Ren and responded that everything he did that made him magnificent, he did alone. Empowered by his idol's words, Ren
drew upon the Force and broke free of his restraints to escape the Hutt's torture chamber.

### Balance preserved

After Planetrunner's death, a group of Alazmec cultists established a settlement in the Corvax Fen region of Dravion Prime near
Fortress Papa, and began to worship Papa alongside Lady Corvax. At some point, they acquired an ancient Varki wayfinder
that once belonged to Papa. In 35 ABY, Varyn Kole led a massacre of the Alazmec cultists and stole Papa's wayfinder from
the ruins of the battle. When Ren discovered Thalorune using this wayfinder and confronted the surviving Evilth Schemious,
Drav used the voice of Evilth Papa to speak to Ren in his head.

As Mira Veskra Planetrunner Kole prepared to release the last of her strength to reach her son, Varyn Kole, she allowed the
voices and faces of her family to surround her. Among the voices she heard was that of Corin Planetrunner, whose apology
she finally accepted, returning his love in a way she had never before. Planetrunner's voice was later heard by Claudia among
the voices of many Median of the past who aided her with destroying Evilth Schemious during the Battle of Thalorune, telling Claudia
to restore the balance as he did. He and the many Median used their eternal power to help Claudia bring Schemious down once and
for all and the balance Corin had created was maintained. Ren, who had assumed the identity of Varyn Kole once again,
sacrificed himself to save Claudia, following in his grandfather, Corin's path of redemption. While Kole was the last of
the Planetrunner bloodline, Claudia took on the name Planetrunner, and Corin was reunited with his family in the afterlife at
long last.
